It was a poisoned immortal fruit!

Xu Qing looked at Poison Monarch, then bowed deeply at the waist. “Your humble servant accepts the mission!”

He wanted the poisoned fruit!

Poison Monarch didn’t seem surprised. He thought Xu Qing to be much like himself. If you wanted to get stronger, break through, and reach higher heights, you could definitely ask a tiger for its skin! In this case, Poison Monarch was the tiger. At the same time, Xu Qing was providing a tiger skin to Poison Monarch. After all, the Immortal Paragon had ordered that no one infect Xu Qing with their karma.

That’s just going to make things interesting. Poison Monarch flicked his sleeve and started walking away. He blurred, as if he were becoming one with heaven and earth. Ultimately, he vanished, leaving behind a few words echoing about. “You’re on your own now, Xu Qing.”

After he was gone, everything went back to normal. Then a golden stream of starlight descended from above, wrapped around Xu Qing, and drew him up into the sky.

He rose up into the canopy of heaven and ultimately left the planet that housed the Department of Acquisitions headquarters. He didn’t resist. He allowed the starlight to guide him up. As the planet grew smaller and smaller in his view, his thoughts wandered.

Although the immortal fruit was poisoned, it was extremely fresh and of good quality. The downsides and upsides were clear to see.

Furthermore, Xu Qing wasn’t under the illusion that eating the poisoned immortal fruit would mean that the other party’s evil intentions would go away completely. Those evil intentions were related to personal progress, so it was almost certain that the two of them would clash again later. Rather than place his hope on the off chance that the other party would simply give up, Xu Qing preferred to take control.

Besides, he was well aware that he currently had a severe lack of cultivation resources. With a good excuse to work with, he was definitely going to be able to make some advancement. And thus, rather than worry about when the poison might flare up... he figured it would be better to just eat the fruit and grow stronger as quickly as possible.

It was similar to how, back when he had no cultivation base, and was stuck in that city that the broken face had just looked at, he ultimately chose to start practicing cultivation, if for no other reason than to get rid of mutagen more quickly. That same frame of mind applied here.

Besides, to a certain degree, Poison Monarch was right. The two of them really were very similar.

In any case, it’s still possible that I could deal with a poison flare-up if it happens.... Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed as the planet grew smaller and smaller, all while the Reception Universe as a whole filled his field of view. Eventually... the entire universe was visible to him, and the starlight took him completely out.

When he appeared in the starry sky, he caught sight of Sir Star Ring and everyone else. They were waiting for him.

Coming to a stop in front of them, he waved his hand to open the ring of holding. The Acquisitioner identity medallions flew out. They were gray pieces of jade.

Everyone took their medallion and sent some divine will inside. Light flared, which then turned into gray hundred-pocket robes. Everything around Xu Qing blurred as he also donned a hundred-pocket robe. From a distance, the group of 89 cultivators were all dressed alike, causing an indescribable air of prestige to surround them.

Looking very serious, Zhou Zhengli strode forward and bowed to Xu Qing.

“Greetings, Captain!”

The other ascendees, regardless of what they were thinking inside, also offered formal greetings.

That included Yuanshan Su. As for Hordeslayer and Rampart, they were about to join in when they realized Sir Star Ring wasn’t moving a muscle. All of a sudden, Hordeslayer and Rampart seemed to stand a bit taller. Xu Qing didn’t seem to care either way about any of it. Taking out the mission jade slip, he sent the mission information into the minds of everyone present.

Their first mission as Acquisitioners was to take place in the Helioterra Universe. They were to go there and search for resources![1]

There was something unique about the Helioterra Universe. It was not in the Nineshores Heaven! It was located in another heaven beyond heaven. However, that heaven beyond heaven was not listed alongside the eleven Immortal Lords! Put most precisely, this heaven beyond heaven belonged to a perished Immortal Lord. As a result, that heaven was masterless.... The name of that heaven beyond heaven had long since been erased.

After looking at the mission jade slip, Xu Qing was instantly shaken inside. He wasn’t the only one. Other ascendees, particularly Sir Star Ring and the other Shining Stars, all had odd looks on their faces.

In all of the Fifth Star Ring, there was only one place that matched that description.... It was, of course, the Aurora heaven beyond heaven!

Prompted by instinct, Li Mengtu and Zhou Zhengli looked at Xu Qing. Even Hordeslayer, Rampart, Yuanshan Su and Sir Star Ring... all looked in his direction. After what all of them had experienced in the historical reflection of the Aurora Immortal Palace, they had come to view Xu Qing as Young Lord Aurora. The entire event had left a deep impression on them. freewebnovel.com

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed as he checked the details of the mission. It said that to get to the Helioterra Universe, they had to take the mission jade slip to a teleportation facility, where arrangements had been made for them to teleport to their destination.

Because that heaven beyond heaven was masterless, it had become a public place. What was more, because of the historical events of the past, the nonhumans there had become quite rebellious by nature. After all, there was no heaven for them to be subordinate to.

When people from other heavens beyond heaven went inside, they would usually split up based on who backed them. Compared to other heavens beyond heaven, it was a wild and disorderly place, where everything was a complicated jianghu-like world.

It had countless universes within it, all sorts of nonhumans, and a mish-mash of organizations. There were also a host of god prisons. Because of that, it was considered to rank high among the heavens beyond heaven. Back in the day, Immortal Lord Aurora was considered to have peak battle prowess among the Immortal Lords.

Based on the description in the mission jade slip, the Helioterra Universe was on the edge of the heaven beyond heaven. It was administered by the imperial clan of the Helioterra race, who were known as Helioterrans. It had a total of thirty-one god prisons in it. Of those thirty-one prisons, the biggest was A29, and within it were imprisoned, for the most part, Altar Gods.

After everyone had familiarized themselves with the information from the jade slip, Xu Qing put it away. He swept the gathered crowd with his gaze, and then without a word, headed to the nearest teleportation facility, just as the mission had directed.

Zhou Zhengli and Li Mengtu exchanged a glance and then followed. Everyone else started moving with glittering eyes. And thus, the group became a stream of 89 beams of light that pierced through the starry sky.

As they sped by at top speed, the cultivators they passed mostly just frowned and got out of their way. These were obviously notorious Acquisitioners, and they were like tigers or jackals that no one wanted to get close to, let alone provoke.

Half a month passed.

In the depths of the Nineshores Heaven was an ancient planet that had a teleportation facility built into it. As Xu Qing and the others descended, Xu Qing produced the mission jade slip, and the portal filled with rumbling sounds. A powerful force of teleportation power caused majestic pulses to flow out in all directions.

Xu Qing and the others instantly disappeared. It took them five days to reach their destination.

When they reappeared, they were in an unfamiliar starry sky, and they were standing on an ancient and crumbling platform made of crimson stone. The platform was hot, but was rapidly cooling down. It took a huge amount of resources to use a teleportation portal that teleported you to another heaven beyond heaven.

The requirements for a cultivator to use such a portal were high. Someone without a sufficient cultivation base, would likely be killed by the process itself. One could not have any mental flaws either, as one could lose one’s mind and ultimately die.

When the group materialized, a few dozen people coughed up blood and immediately settled down cross-legged to recover. Some seemed dazed, as if they had been shaken down to their souls.

Only Xu Qing and Sir Star Ring appeared to be completely unfazed.

Thankfully, these were all ascendees. Based on everything they had experienced to get to this point, they were elite chosen both in terms of cultivation base and mental acuity. Even though some were affected by such a massive teleportation between heavens beyond heaven, they quickly recovered and began to study their surroundings with divine will.

There was very little light in the sky. The stars here were dim. The spirit energy was scarce. The place was truly a wilderness.

“So, this is the Helioterra Universe,” Xu Qing murmured as he stood on the stone platform and looked around. Then he glanced at Zhou Zhengli.

Zhou Zhengli understood the meaning of his glance. Stepping forward, he bowed and said, “Young Lord, everyone is aware of the mission and the parameters. I suggest we split up. Regardless of how we fare, we’ll pool our resources when we meet back up.

“If anyone runs into a situation too difficult to handle, they can use up some of their ringsource to call for help from nearby. If even that fails to resolve any sticky situation, then the young master can intervene. Of course, the premise is that the ringsource at hand is worth it. What do you say, sir?”

Zhou Zhengli looked at Xu Qing.

Xu Qing nodded. He wasn’t inclined to waste time and energy making complicated arrangements. Besides, he knew that everyone was after ringsource, so there was no way he could completely avoid people taking some for their own. It made more sense to give people some leniency in that regard.

“I’ll handle Prison A29. The rest of you can decide amongst yourselves where you want to go other than that.”

With that, Xu Qing blurred off into the distance. After he was gone, everyone exchanged glances. There was some brief communication, and then some people went off on their own, while others stuck together in groups of between three to five. And thus, they were like a cloud of locusts that dispersed in different directions.

***

In the depths of the Helioterra Universe was a galaxy in which floated an amazing imperial palace. There was currently a lot of singing and dancing going on in the palace.

Seated on the imperial throne was a red-skinned giant with two faces, resting his head on one hand. All of a sudden, a jade slip flew into the palace and stopped in front of the giant. There, it popped, producing the projected image of a figure who immediately prostrated to the two-faced giant.

“Your Majesty, an Acquisitions squadron from the Nineshores heaven beyond heaven just entered our Helioterra Universe!”

The two-faced giant didn’t look at the newly arrived messenger. He just kept watching the singing and dancing. “You know the drill. Make sure they find some ringsource. If these jackals know what’s good for them, they’ll take some scraps and then leave. But if they don’t know what’s good for them, then we’ll make sure they understand who’s really in charge of the Helioterra Universe.”

1. What I’m rendering as “Helioterra” is a reference to an ancient Chinese theory about the nature of the universe. There were two common theories, which are generally rendered as heliocentric theory and geocentric theory. In this case, “helio” refers to the sun and “geo” to the earth. I think you can get the meaning just on that, but to be absolutely clear, they were conflicting theories about whether the center of the universe was the sun or the earth. A third theory eventually came around that was a mixture of the two. I’m using “helioterra” because it mixes two words related to sun and earth. It also works in other contexts as you will see. ☜

Xu Qing was like a shooting star zipping through the starry sky, leaving behind a wake of distortions. The ripples of his passage were a result of his cultivation base, as well as the might of his immortal embryo.

In some respects, it was similar to the gods. It was just what happened when cultivation reached a certain level. Just as there were many ways for the weak to be vulnerable, the strength of the powerful was often a convergence.

Xu Qing had his destination locked in, but wasn’t going all out in terms of speed. He was taking time to study his immortal embryo, but at the same time, he was paying attention to the universe around him, this new heaven beyond heaven.

The events at the Fallen Immortal Moors were only a reflection of history.... And yet... the effects of Hordeslayer and Rampart acknowledging me as owner spread into the real world. Li Mengtu’s poison canon also gained something of an origin.... And in the Inkland, Starfire summoned a manifestation of the Hundred Flowers Palace.

It all goes to show that though the events in the reflection of history didn’t change anything in the real world, they did have some effect.

What’s more, I was given command over the Aurora Immortal Palace there! The immortal palace is the most integral aspect of a heaven beyond heaven. The most paramount location. That’s why the Aurora Immortal Palace only appears when there’s a spirit tide. The real immortal palace is most likely in this very heaven beyond heaven. If I call on my command of the immortal palace in this heaven beyond heaven....

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered, and his heart raced with curiosity. As he proceeded along, he sent out his divine will to try to find the immortal palace. It didn’t work. Perhaps it was because too much time had passed, or perhaps it was because the immortal palace had sunk into ruin. Eventually, he sighed and abandoned such attempts.

His destination was Prison A29. It was the biggest god prison in the Helioterra Universe, and it was also where the largest portion of ringsource came from.

As the captain of an Acquisitioner squad, it was only natural that he was able to take the biggest slice of cake. He wasn’t concerned with whatever danger his so-called subordinates got into. Nor was he concerned with where they got ringsource in the Helioterra Universe. Whether it was from god prisons or nonhumans, it didn’t matter to him.

If they ran into obstacles trying to collect ringsource, or got into conflicts with nonhumans, others would step in, if for no other reason than to get more ringsource for their own collections. Unless things really got out of hand, Xu Qing didn’t have any intention of interfering with anyone. He was completely and utterly focused on one thing.

I need to collect ringsource and upgrade my immortal embryo!

Eyes sparkling, and heart full of determination, he accelerated. He even took advantage of some teleportation portals he encountered. In that manner, he spent about ten days going halfway across the Helioterra Universe. That was when he reached his destination.

It was a red starry sky. The red color didn’t come from starlight. Rather, it came from a shockingly enormous red kelp plant! It had nineteen leaves, each of which was so long that it could wrap around a planet.

The nineteen leaves all met at the base, which was where a network of fine roots grew downward. The roots surrounded and were embedded into a huge sun, from which they constantly extracted nutrients.

Xu Qing looked at the kelp plant, his eyes shining.

A plant growing in the starry sky.... I wonder if my god vine could eventually grow into something like this.

Xu Qing cast his senses into the Sageheaven Pagoda, and the god vine that was part of it. The god vine was asleep, but based on its aura, it seemed like it would be able to wake up fairly soon.

Xu Qing looked back at the kelp plant. As he looked at it more closely, he realized that upon the nineteen leaves were spots of various sizes.

Each spot is a minor world. They’re all prison blocks! And the biggest prison block of all is in that sun.

As Xu Qing studied the kelp, it flickered with red light, and then a terrifying stream of divine will spread out from it. It locked onto Xu Qing, and it was so terrifying that it felt like he was dealing with an immortal.

Xu Qing’s eyes hardened. He could tell that this red kelp was not the prison. It was responsible for keeping the prison in check. He took out his Acquisitioner medallion, as well as his mission jade slip.

“I’m here on a mission from the Nineshores Heaven to collect ringsource!” reewebnovel.com

The divine will from the red kelp swept around Xu Qing and examined the medallion and jade slip. A moment later, it seemed to make a decision. The divine will retracted slowly, and one of the leaves slowly drifted up to Xu Qing.

He looked at the leaf, and then looked at the sun surrounded by the kelp plant’s roots. After considering the situation momentarily, he stepped onto the leaf and raced toward one of the spots on it. The spot grew larger and larger from his perspective, until it was a world. He pierced through the barriers of the world, and then rumbling sounds echoed out.

He landed on black soil. Everything was rotten and full of death as far as the eye could see. There was no wind, no spirit, no mutagen. Everything was barren and deathly. He studied his surroundings, looked down at the ground, and then, without an expression on his face, stomped his foot down.

“Wake up!” he said coolly. Rumbling sounds echoed out as a wind picked up, spirit filled the world, and mutagen turned into a tempest. It kicked up black soil in all directions, causing it to fill the sky, and obscuring Xu Qing himself.

If you could stand at a very high vantage point and looked down at that exact moment, you would clearly see... that there was a huge line on the surface of the ground. And that line was currently rising up, lifting the soil like a wave in the sea. And then the line parted, revealing an enormous, bloodshot eye. Īts eye had opened!

The black ground had merely been covering that eye, and once Xu Qing had stepped down, the eye had no choice but to open. As the tempest raged around Xu Qing, he stood unmoving, right on top of the pupil of the eye!

Īt looked at Xu Qing coldly, without happiness or anger.

“Inferior species. Slave.”

Xu Qing’s facial expression remained the same as usual. This was the eye of a Flawless God.

“You’re Flawless... relatively speaking,” Xu Qing said calmly to the eye of the god beneath his feet. Long ago, Xu Qing had encountered similar eyes back in the Revered Ancient mainland. [1]

Every eye he had seen had caused him to tremble as mutagen assailed him. In some cases, the gaze of such eyes made it feel like his flesh and blood were independent entities that wanted to separate from him. That was the result of the vast disparity in the levels of life force involved.

But right now, his gaze was calm and unruffled. In fact, the eye of the god seemed to be contorting and becoming increasingly bloodshot. This god was not like īt had been in the past. And even where īt was at īts peak, īt would still react similarly to Xu Qing.

Xu Qing lifted his hand to reveal his Acquisitioner’s medallion. The medallion served to confirm his status, and the rights that came with it. It also had the unique function of being able to extract ringsource. He held out the medallion and pushed it down in front of him.

The god’s eye contorted with greater intensity, and a sound like a howl rose up. Golden ringsource began to seep out of the eye. Every strand that was extracted caused immeasurable pain to the god’s eye. Eventually, after forty-nine strands had been extracted, the god’s eye became as gray as ash. That was the limit. The eye twitched as it began to close, to return to a state of slumber.

Xu Qing frowned.

That’s not very much.

The ringsource he had collected was hardly larger than the fist of an infant. It wasn’t nearly as pure as the ringsource he had collected from the Inkland. Naturally speaking, he would need far more than this to be able to make use of it.

With that thought in mind, his eyes flashed coldly. Then, instead of putting away his identity medallion, he pushed it down toward the closing eye of the god! It hit the eye just as the eyelids were about to meet!

The eye snapped open, and this time īt emanated a different type of fluctuation. It was the terror that intelligent beings experienced in the face of death! The terror didn’t last for long. Xu Qing held nothing back to extract many more golden threads from the eye.

This wasn’t just ringsource. This was pure life force! A cry of anguish echoed out for a time, before vanishing.... And then the eye of the god collapsed into ash, having been completely destroyed. Īts death caused even more ringsource to appear.

Because of all the ringsource, Xu Qing could sense the mark of Starfire on his arm trembling. Xu Qing took a strand of ringsource and put it above the mark.

“Want it?” he asked.

Starfire ceased trembling, and then a gravitational force sprang out of the mark. The ringsource was sucked in, and then Xu Qing heard a silken voice speaking in his mind.

“Thank you, Young Lord. You’re truly amazing.”

Face expressionless, Xu Qing hovered in place and began to absorb the ringsource. As the ringsource entered him, his immortal embryo glittered, and its aura improved. Eventually, Xu Qing’s eyes shone and he licked his lips.

Not enough, by far. I need much, much more....

Xu Qing burst into motion as he went to another minor world.

In that manner, time passed.

Xu Qing went to one minor world after another on the leaf. In every one, a god died to provide ringsource. And thus, his immortal embryo began to shine more and more brightly.

As far as Xu Qing was concerned, there was no advantage in leaving the gods alive. The mission jade slip had not left any instructions to do so. He collected every scrap that was available, keeping some aside for the mission, and taking the rest for himself.

Meanwhile, the other ascendees were in other locations doing their best to collect ringsource in whatever ways they could. Some they kept for the mission, but the rest... they used for their personal cultivation. Looking at them from a different perspective, they really did seem like jackals.

1. Some of the eyes Xu Qing encountered were in chapters 49, 369, 524.2, and 838. I believe there were others. These were just the first three I was able to easily find. ☜

When perspectives differed, so did attitudes and actions. It wasn’t a simple matter of good or evil. After all, good versus evil often played out even among members of the same species.

There was little need to mention hatred, fury, or ambivalence toward nonhumans. After all, their ancestors were gods. If the immortal revolution hadn’t occurred in the Fifth Star Ring, then they would be the ruling class. Humans would be slaves that they could take advantage of at will.

But the gods had been either slaughtered or rounded up and imprisoned. So the nonhumans were like fish on the chopping block. In some ways, it was like reincarnation.

It wasn’t possible to say who was wrong or right. It was only possible to say... that regardless of which species was in question, and regardless of whether it was immortals or gods, perspective determined everything. The weak were doomed to be devoured by the strong. Those who fell behind would lose the right to continue onward.

Cultivators did not live the way the gods had lived in the past. But that was a fundamental magical law of the higher star rings, or perhaps, of all living beings in general. Victims wouldn’t always be victims. And the victimizers wouldn’t always be victimizers. In the end, everything was cyclical.

It was a truth Xu Qing had come to understand back in the Revered Ancient mainland.

After everything he had experienced in the Fifth Star Ring, he understood more than ever how to deal with the gods here. It was all according to the laws that bound everything. It was just like the discarnate wills of obsession in the Heroic Immortal Tombs. That was how the Fifth Star Ring treated the gods, as well as the nonhumans.

In the end, it was the same with Xu Qing. And yet, based on his judgment, among all of those apathetic gods, there were some that were more human than most humans.

Unfortunately, these imprisoned gods were not among them. Xu Qing wasn’t some sort of loving philanthropist who would take time getting to know each and every god before deciding what to do with them. He had no qualms about draining the pond to get at the fish, and thus, it didn’t take long for him to reach the last minor world on the leaf.

The environment consisted of a viscous black sea. The sea was calm, but did not seem auspicious and peaceful. The water stank, and powerful mutagen roiled in all directions.

A head was buried in the seafloor. It looked like the head of a bird, covered with tentacles that constantly excreted a viscous fluid. Over time, that fluid had turned into a black sea.

When Xu Qing arrived, the mutagen kicked up into a frenzy. Huge waves rolled across the surface of the sea, and the head below looked up, eyes opening. Golden light shone up through the sea as the head looked up.

A strange sound that could shake the mind and heart filled Xu Qing’s ears. It became a host of thoughts that weren’t his own, growing in his head. As the intangible thoughts formed and took shape, they became strands of excreted black fluid that wrapped around his head.

The mutagen became a tempest that raged toward Xu Qing. The waves grew larger, and the entire world began to spin. The sea became the sky. The sky became the earth below.

And then... the black sea began to pour down like rain. And thanks to the power of the inversion, the head broke free! The world blurred as rumbling sounds filled heaven and earth.

A few breaths of time passed, whereupon a dense immortal energy erupted from the chaotic blur. Mountain-toppling, sea-draining force spread out, crushing everything and driving everything away.

Everything then became clear and bright. The mutagen began to dissolve within the immortal energy. The viscous sea vaporized. Xu Qing became clear.

He reached out with his right hand and grabbed a head that was vastly larger than his own body. His five fingers stabbed into the flesh of the head. Though there was a huge disparity in size, there was only one source of terror, and it was the head!

Īt was trembling! Golden strands of ringsource were extracted, and poured into the medallion in Xu Qing’s hand. Eventually, an anguished howl echoed out. The god’s head trembled, turned gray, and collapsed into dust.

Xu Qing hovered alone in midair, his gaze sharp as he looked around.

The marks sealing this place are on the verge of fading away.... That’s why the god was able to take the initiative. But the sealing mark wasn’t touched by the god. It seems to have been affected by something else. Something was helping īt break down the seal. It was giving īt a chance to break free of the prison. Was it nonhumans? Or was it... the jail itself accepting bribes?

Xu Qing had been a jailer in the past, so he knew full well how jailers could shamelessly seek personal gain.

He pondered that for a time, his eyes narrowing. Then he flew out of the minor world and appeared out in the starry sky. He looked at the red kelp plant. He closely examined the other leaves.

The kelp plant swayed.

Finally, Xu Qing said, “The gods in the other leaves are almost all dead. You... ate them, didn’t you?”

The swaying kelp leaves suddenly began drifting rapidly toward Xu Qing.

Xu Qing didn’t move a muscle. “The leaf you offered to me was prepared in advance for collection purposes, so that no one would realize you had been accepting bribes. Am I right?”

A terrifying will built up, aggressive and full of astonishing pressure. Cracking sounds echoed out in the surrounding starry sky, all while gruish symbols floated up, locking the place down.

Eyes narrowing, Xu Qing continued, “I have a good relationship with Young Lord Aurora. Check my aura. You’ll find I have command over the Aurora Immortal Palace. Immortal Lord Nineshores cares a lot about me. Surely you can sense the aura on this object.” Xu Qing took out the wooden slip that was the authentication token for the God Blood River ferry boat. “I’m also the 1st place ascendee. If I perish here, you’ll never get away with it.”

The kelp plant hesitated, and the terrifying will reached out to the wooden slip. The terrifying will trembled. The stream of will left the slip and surrounded Xu Qing. It checked him more thoroughly.

Xu Qing’s facial expression remained the same as usual. After the mirrored history of the Aurora Immortal Palace concluded, everyone else experienced lingering effects in the real world, and there was no reason to assume he wouldn’t.

Though he had not been able to sense the Aurora Immortal Palace in this heaven beyond heaven, he got the feeling it was because the immortal palace was in concealment. He might not be able to sense it, but that didn’t mean that this kelp plant, which was native to this heaven beyond heaven, couldn’t sense it.

In other words, he was trying to use a roundabout method to confirm his own identity! It wouldn’t matter if he failed, as his biggest protection was Immortal Lord Nineshores, as well as the fact that he was the 1st place ascendee.

And thus, he submitted to the inspection.

Moments later, he could sense great fluctuations in the will of the kelp. In fact, the actual plant itself was visibly shaking. Xu Qing’s eyes gleamed. He had guessed correctly!

The kelp trembled, and its aura became chaotic, as if it had come to a decision. Thanks to the deep inspection the kelp had just carried out, it realized that, hidden within this human was the ability to command the Aurora Immortal Palace. There was obviously some major karma at play. The command wielded by this human scared it.

And the reason was that it was subservient to the Aurora Immortal Palace! Although the Aurora heaven beyond heaven had no master now, the kelp’s status was the same as ever. And its actions really did constitute a crime. It was faced with a difficult choice....

However, that was when Xu Qing spoke again. “You’ve been keeping an eye on this god prison for countless years. Nobody will fault you for having an occasional snack when you get hungry.”

The kelp froze.

“And considering the food is almost gone, the fact that you left a whole leaf is really an expression of loyalty!”

The will of the kelp surged.

“After all, I came late. That’s not really your fault.”

The leaves on the kelp plant swayed back and forth, and the pressure reduced significantly. As far as it could tell, this human wasn’t joking around. He was being completely serious.

“Therefore, let’s just forget about the past. And now, I want to ask you a question. Do you... want to eat thāt?” Xu Qing pointed at the sun wrapped up in the roots.

The kelp leaves all twitched, and then divine will echoed around Xu Qing, like a deep voice.

“Yes!”

Xu Qing nodded. “Let me in. Protect me. And I’ll see... how we can split whatever’s inside!”

The kelp hesitated and checked Xu Qing’s aura again. Then the roots shifted aside to reveal a path. Before it was completely open, the kelp suddenly sent out its divine will to scan the area. It had sensed something.

“There’s no need to be nervous,” Xu Qing said calmly. “It’s a friend of mine. Let him in.”

The kelp seemed to consider his words, then created an opening in the sealing barrier.

Zhou Zhengli shot inside. He quickly looked around. Then, acting as if nothing unusual had just happened, bowed to Xu Qing.

“What is it?” Xu Qing asked.

“Young Lord,” Zhou Zhengli said respectfully, “some of the others have had no trouble collecting ringsource. Others ran into trouble, but everything has been easy to resolve.

“Unfortunately, something unusual happened with the Helioterran imperial clan. That’s why your humble servant has come. Young Lord, can you use your status here in the Aurora heaven beyond heaven... to crush those fools who think this place really has no one in charge??

“Of course, if you’re not inclined to help, your humble servant can always go ask Sir Star Ring to handle the situation.”

Xu Qing looked at him. There was no doubt that Zhou Zhengli was very intelligent. If it weren’t for the fact that Xu Qing knew he could turn into an adversary at any time, he would probably be very pleased with how he acted.

“Have Sir Star Ring deal with it,” Xu Qing said.

“Yes, sir, Young Lord Aurora!” Zhou Zhengli backed up and then hurried away.

When he was gone, the kelp re-sealed the area.

Xu Qing turned back to the roots. “Alright. Open it up. I’m hungry, and I bet you’re hungry too.”

Without any hesitation, the kelp continued to open the path into the depths of the sun. Eyes glittering, Xu Qing stepped onto the path!

Heatwaves buffeted Xu Qing’s face. Burning fire was all that could be seen in all directions. Heaven and earth was bright red and dazzling! Everything was made of fire, with the occasional burst of liquid fire here and there. The liquid fire would fly into the air and then explode, leaving behind streams of mysterious magical symbols. From a distance, it looked like an eternal rain of magical symbols.

When the symbols landed, they became crimson kelp plants that tried to grow, but unfortunately... couldn’t survive in the heat. They would eventually crumble into ashes that then became part of the liquid fire. There were only a very small amount that, by random circumstances, would manage to take root and grow.

It was a difficult process, and even while growing, they would occasionally burst into flames. Xu Qing only spotted a few here and there that managed to survive long-term. Most were severely withered, and looked like they might be incinerated at any moment.

This is only one small area of this sun. But even if you estimate mathematically, you can conclude that... not much kelp can survive here.

As he acclimated to the heat, he looked off into the distance and said, “Where are the gods locked up?”

He was asking the huge kelp plant that existed outside. A moment later, a vague response came from the will of the kelp.

“In the middle... immortal oath, so I can’t go in very deep, the kelp here... my will can help....”

The voice of the will came and went. It was clear that even the mighty kelp plant was afraid of this sun. Perhaps it was because of the immortal oath, or maybe it was something else.

Checks and balances of some sort? Or is it more targeted?

Thinking back to what he had experienced here so far, Xu Qing decided the first possibility wasn’t likely. So he would need to be more careful in case it was the second possibility.

With that, he started moving. He wanted to get a more complete picture of this sun, as well as whatever god was sealed in the middle of it. Only then would he start thinking about taking the ringsource.

In that manner, time passed.

A few days later, Xu Qing slowed down. Thanks to his cultivation base, he was quickly acclimating to the place. But even still, he needed to stop every so often and use surrounding bits of kelp to help the process. Only then would he continue.

After traveling for about half a month, he reached his limit and had to stop in front of a piece of growing kelp.

He hadn’t actually entered the central region, but his divine will could detect exactly where that spot was. When he sent his senses forward to that spot, his eyes hardened. By means of his senses, he could ‘see’ an astonishing sword there! It was stabbed right into the sun. The part sticking out into the open was a hilt like a huge mountain peak. It seemed likely that, on the opposite side of the sun, there was a sword tip piercing out in astonishing fashion.

The moment Xu Qing’s senses reached the sword, he came to a sudden realization.

There is no god imprisoned in this sun. Rather... īt is the sun! This sun is a god! Īt’s the type of god equivalent to a Lower Immortal. Īt’s... a True God!

Xu Qing’s pupils constricted as he looked down at the ground and the withered kelp in the area. He felt shaken.

That sword is what’s keeping the True God here. It’s sealing the god’s body! It’s stabbed right through the god, leaving the god in a state of neither life nor death. Apparently... īt can’t rely on īts true name to return!

To other gods, the kelp leaves suffice to serve as a prison. But to True Gods, the kelp is the jailer!

The kelp wants to use the True God for its own cultivation, even more than I do. That’s why it’s continuously dropping seeds here in the hope of establishing a firm connection. It’s all in the hopes of absorbing the god! All of the scattered kelp plants here are being used to try to absorb the True God’s ringsource....

Unfortunately, because of the environment and personhood here, there’s simply not enough of the kelp to absorb any significant amount of ringsource.

After a moment of thought, Xu Qing lifted his right hand to reveal the Acquisitioners medallion designed to absorb ringsource. He pushed it down toward the ground. He unleashed all of his cultivation base.

This was different from when he had absorbed the other gods. This time, his actions didn’t cause the ground to tremble. The sun didn’t even seem to react at all. Several strands of golden ringsource quietly rose up. However, there weren’t many of them. It was as if there was some profound force blocking ringsource. Though the extraction effort wasn’t a complete failure, it wasn’t very successful either.

Shortly after, Xu Qing stopped and looked up. Focusing his senses on the sword hilt, his eyes began to shine.

“The surface beneath my feet is like a shell,” he said out loud. “That means collecting ringsource here is going to be very difficult. The best place is going to be where the sword is stabbed inside! That’s essentially an injury to the god!”

His eyes narrowed. “If I really want to eat my fill here, that’s where I need to go all out.... In that case, it’s time to tap into everything you’ve prepared. Don’t hold anything back. And I won’t either. Maybe we’ll get an opportunity to really stuff ourselves. The alternative is that we make do with the little bit I got just now.”

Xu Qing stopped speaking and waited.

Shortly after, a withered kelp plant in front of him suddenly swayed, almost decisively. And then it reverted from its withered state into being bright red. It wasn’t the only one. All of the other living kelp on the sun transformed from being withered into a state of vibrant red. It looked almost like a host of red pāramitā lilies swaying in all directions. And they were moving toward Xu Qing.

Along the way, many of the kelp plants collapsed into dust. But as a group, they continued onward. In short order, Xu Qing was surrounded by a host of undulating kelp. He didn’t avoid the plants. They gathered around him in layer after layer over the course of a few dozen breaths of time.

Soon, Xu Qing looked very different. He was now a figure in a crimson suit of plant armor, several hundred meters tall. He was like a giant. Majestic life force pulsed from the kelp, filling Xu Qing and giving him astonishing levels of protection. This kelp had been building up on the sun for countless years, and each little bit of force it provided was now being pooled together into an astonishing reserve power!

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered brightly. He could sense that the kelp was really going for broke.

Without any hesitation, he unleashed five extremes, using the mutual restraining factors of the five elements to create a peak level of resistance. Then he used his space-time canon to summon overlapping universes. In that manner, he dispelled the pressure weighing down on the path in front of him.

Next, his immortal embryo glittered, making him like a person surrounded by flowing lightning. He shot forward. He headed... directly toward the huge sword he had just sensed!

As he neared, the pressure grew more intense, and the fire more terrifying. Xu Qing’s external kelp armor was sizzling and crumbling into ashes. He was fully aware that, acting on his own, he would never make it this far. And the moment the kelp armor completely went away, he would be incinerated.

After all, this was a True God!

But none of that could reduce Xu Qing’s resolve. He accelerated! His eyes flashed with a crazy look!

If Erniu were here to see, he would let loose exclamations of admiration, and would confirm that little Ah Qing had truly mastered the Way of the Ox.[1]

In that manner, time passed.

As Xu Qing hurtled onward with that crazy look in his eyes, and as the kelp armor bolstered him, he crossed a vast distance toward the central part of the sun.

Soon he spotted the actual sword off in the distance. The sight of it caused him to breathe heavily, and he trembled from head to toe. His soul and fleshly body were very close to catching ablaze. But the fire couldn’t do anything to the crazy look in his eyes. If anything, it grew more intense the moment he spotted the huge sword!

Acting on instinct, Xu Qing bit his tongue and spat out a mouthful of blood. He was using something akin to a blood escape art to get a burst of speed. About seventy percent of the kelp armor was gone, and the heat was incredibly intense. But he reached the sword!

Now he could see the area clearly. There was a massive ravine in the spot where the sword was stabbed into the surface. There was flesh trying to close up the wound and push the sword out. But the sword was incredibly tough, and couldn’t be moved. As a result, there was no way that the wound could close up. It was something of a deadlock.

The moment Xu Qing arrived, he felt a sensation of impending death. He knew that the kelp wasn’t going to last much longer, and that he had no way to stand up to the heat.

But... he also sensed an incredible reserve of ringsource within the wound!

Given what Xu Qing had seen, this ringsource was unprecedented. The only thing that could come close to comparing was the depths of the Inkland, which he couldn’t enter. This destined opportunity. This good fortune....

As the craziness in Xu Qing built, he sent an internal message with divine will.

“Cover me, Starfire!”

The mark on his arm immediately unleashed pure coldness. Shē was unleashing hēr god power to bolster Xu Qing. Not only was it buying time, it was also there to protect against any sudden malicious act by the kelp.

And thus, Xu Qing dropped into a cross-legged position, pulled out the Acquisitioners medallion, and pushed it down. Instantly, rumbling sounds echoed out as golden strands emerged from the sword wound.

It looked like a geyser!

Starfire was shaken to the core. The kelp plant was filled with excitement.

Xu Qing was going crazy!

The amount of ringsource was flabbergasting. After all, this was a True God! In the higher star rings, True Gods were like darling children, and were doted on by all of the natural and magical laws.

Starfire still felt the same. The main difference was that this True God was imprisoned, so if karma was sown, it wouldn’t be too problematic.

The nourishment brought to Xu Qing’s immortal embryo by the ringsource was unprecedented. By combining those elements, he would be able to complete his immortal embryo. And that would mean... that his cultivation base had broken out of Imperial Sovereign and into Quasi-Immortal!

The destined opportunity and good fortune at hand caused Xu Qing to go even more crazy.

When Xu Qing achieved major success with his immortal embryo, his space-time canon became full, and he gained even more control over space-time parallelism.

In the blink of an eye, he acquired a hundred worlds! One hundred worlds. One hundred versions of himself. And thus, he was able to devour even more ringsource. It was like a snowball effect.

Starfire and the kelp went even more mad, and went all out trying to snatch as much ringsource as they could. And thus, as the three of them worked as hard as they could, the first wave of ringsource began to weaken.

“Who has the outrageous gall to steal the god fodder of an immortal like me??”

A burst of killing intent swept out in all directions.

Xu Qing’s gaze hardened. As he watched, the silver light became a sealing mark. The sword and the sealing mark did not have the same origin, as if the latter were a postheaven construction. However, now wasn’t the time to sit around contemplating the matter. Starfire once again became a mark on his arm, where shē went all out to bolster Xu Qing. Xu Qing sped backward, just beyond the reach of the killing intent.

Even being just on the edge of the reach of the killing intent, it still managed to destroy many of his space-time bodies.

His true body coughed up mouthful after mouthful of blood. That said, he didn’t waste the blood. He used it to unleash various blood escape arts. Rumbling booms echoed out one after another as he teleported backward to safety.

Gasping for breath, he continued to flee. Eventually, he reached the exit point, where he dashed outside. Once he was hovering out in the starry sky, he managed to relax a bit. After checking himself, he scanned the ringsource he had stored in his parallel space-times.

Once I digest all of that, I should be able to reach complete success with my immortal embryo, and become a Quasi-Immortal! However, it’s going to be close. I’d rather have a bit more, just to be safe. And then my battle prowess would soar when I reached Quasi-Immortal!

Licking his lips, he looked deeply at the sun. The killing intent from just now was not something that a Quasi-Immortal would possess.

That was a Lower Immortal.... This place was set up by a Lower Immortal as a place to gather ringsource. It’s all being confined here.... When I came along to snatch a bit of it for myself, it unleashed that sealing power.

The kelp had answered honestly. Apparently, now that it got a good serving of ringsource, it didn’t feel the need to keep anything hidden.

Without dealing with that sealing, it will be impossible to continue absorbing ringsource. Unfortunately, I can’t quite resign myself to giving up now.

The message was a request for help, although it was worded very tersely. That just conformed to Sir Star Ring’s proud personality.

The Helioterran imperial clan in the Helioterra Universe had once possessed amazing innate abilities. Originally, their skin was half crimson red and half azure blue, and they had four faces, one looking in each direction. They had also been huge. At birth, they would be 300 meters tall, and by the time they reached maturity, they would be 3,000 meters tall. Some would even eventually reach a height of 30,000 meters.

Back then, their total population was vastly beyond most other species. In terms of cultivation, they didn’t have special techniques. They inherited legacies through soul and blood, and could automatically absorb the ringsource of the higher star ring. All of that was because their species descended from a True God!

Years ago, their species had conquered the Helioterra Universe, and had even spread their influence beyond that. In the past, they had been considered one of the central factors in the god cultivation system in the Fifth Star Ring.

Unfortunately... when immortals and gods waged war, the gods were eventually defeated. The immortals rose to power, and the Helioterrans’ glory became a thing of the past. Their True God ended up imprisoned.

And as a species, they withdrew from the war. In fact, they were one of the first species to surrender to the immortals. That was how they ended up surviving after the war ended. They were rewarded with the right to rule the Helioterra Universe, and were also allowed to have an imperial clan, which in the end was quite an honor.

There were similar imperial clans throughout the Fifth Star Ring, but all of them existed because of similar arrangements. That said, all such species in the Fifth Star Ring... had bloodline restrictions placed on them.

And thus, while the Helioterrans had once been dual-colored, their skin was now only a single color. And instead of having four faces, they had two. Their full-grown height was also limited. They could now grow no taller than 300 meters.

Something similar happened to their cultivation. Because of the limitations on their bloodline legacy, they lost their innate abilities. Eventually, they had to switch from the path of gods to that of cultivators. They had to learn to absorb spirit energy, and could only strive for immortal ascension, not godly ascension.

As generations passed, their two-face trait disappeared, and their numbers decreased. In the end, members of the so-called Helioterran imperial clan were mostly about 30 meters tall, and they only had one face.

But then the Aurora Immortal Palace went dark. The heaven beyond heaven had no lord, and finally, the Helioterran imperial clan had hope. Members of their species experienced ancestral awakenings, and they once again began to develop two faces. And they soon took over the universe.

Right now, in the depths of the Helioterra Universe, Sir Star Ring hovered outside of the Helioterrans imperial palace. Chains of order swirled around him, and his face was cold as he looked at the palace.

He was surrounded by countless Helioterrans, all of whom were 30 meters tall. They wore black armor, and pulsed with baleful auras as they glared coldly at him.

Directly in front of him, blocking the way to the imperial palace, were three figures. The three of them were over 200 meters tall, but not quite 300. One of them wielded a spear, one held a pagoda, and the last one had an enormous banner rising up behind him. Astonishingly, all of them pulsed with Quasi-Immortal auras.

Something like this could never happen in any of the other heavens beyond heaven. Nonhumans weren’t allowed to achieve immortal ascension. In fact, they weren’t even permitted to become Quasi-Immortals! But these three didn’t just emit Quasi-Immortal auras. They also pulsed with the fluctuations of the gods! They were cultivating the path of both immortals and gods!

As they stared at Sir Star Ring, the Helioterran with the banner at his back spoke in a raspy voice.

“Sire, you have fought with the three of us several times now, and every time it ends in a draw. What’s the point of continuing? You people came to this universe to collect a certain amount of ringsource. And yet, despite learning that we have an exemption medallion, you just keep pushing the issue. This... is just too much!

“We Helioterrans have a bottom line. Sire, I suggest... you not do anything to harm your own interests!”

Sir Star Ring’s expression was cold. He had been in this place for a while, but had only been able to fight up to this spot, no further. Any one of this group of three would be no problem for him to kill if he was fighting them alone. And if he had to fight two, he could wipe them out if he was willing to pay a heavy price. But three.... They worked together too well, making it impossible for him to make any headway.

In response to them, he coldly said, “It doesn’t matter to me if we get enough ringsource. It doesn’t matter to me that your species has broken the rules. It doesn’t matter to me if you achieve immortal ascension or godly ascension. In fact, it doesn’t even matter to me who you have backing and protecting you.

“The same goes for that exemption medallion. I just want... that lump of clay you have enshrined in your imperial palace!”

Sir Star Ring pointed directly at the palace off in the distance.

The imperial palace glittered, and a yellow lump of clay floated up inside of it, sending terrifying pulses out into the starry sky that contained the might of Heaven’s Principle!

“You want this?” said a cold voice from within the palace, its tone mocking. It was the emperor of the Helioterrans, who was 300 meters tall, pure red, and with two faces. “That’s the inheritance of Fourth True Monarch. You can’t have it.”

The emperor waved his hand, and the clay with Heaven’s Principle returned to him. Voice cold, he said, “Drive him away.”

The three Helioterrans who were blocking Sir Star Ring’s path suddenly surged with energy. It was very clear that they possessed, not just the will of immortals, but the will of gods. They started striding toward Sir Star Ring.

He was ready to fight this battle all on his own!

His canon of order could maintain a sense of order between himself and enemies. And his canon of balance could ensure that disparities between weak and strong could be smoothed out. The stronger his opponent was, the more his canon of balance could bolster him and improve his battle prowess. freewebnovel.com

Back when Xu Qing fought him, Xu Qing had to rely on his parallel universes and alternate versions of himself. That was how he had disrupted Sir Star Ring’s balance. From that, it could be seen how strong Sir Star Ring was.

Sir Star Ring didn’t say a word in response. Originally, he had been about to say something....

“Well, I suppose I could give it to you. Become an ally of the Helioterran Dynasty, and my personal vassal. Fight for us three times. And then... I’ll give you Fourth True Monarch’s inheritance!”

Sir Star Ring looked coldly at the emperor, as if he were looking at an ant. “You think that you, a nothing species full of bloodline criminals, are worthy enough to have me as an ally?”

The surrounding Helioterrans glared at him with fury, and their baleful auras surged.

Inside the palace, the emperor laughed coldly. “I’m not worthy?”

He extended his right hand and pointed out with his index finger. The starry sky surrounding the imperial palace distorted and blurred. The colors seemed to peel away, leaving behind only black and white. Within that black and white, a huge finger of ink appeared, which majestically pushed down toward Sir Star Ring. As it passed, the void shattered and the starry sky withered.

A grim look appeared on Sir Star Ring as he backed up at top speed, all while performing a double-handed incantation gesture. He was getting ready to go all out.

That was when a familiar voice echoed through the starry sky.

“You’re right. You aren’t worthy.”

Endless crimson light spilled out of nowhere, inundating the black and white, and causing the colorless region to turn bright red! Within that red was a leafy kelp plant. It had a total of twelve leaves, which swayed back and forth like whips. Then they lashed toward the finger.

A pop rang out. Unstoppable force surged forth, destroying the void and shattering the starry sky. The finger stopped moving and then dissipated.

The eighteen statues shivered and crumbled. The three Helioterran experts looked shocked as they were sent tumbling backward, coughing up blood like mad.

Inside the imperial palace, the previously composed Helioterran emperor had the same expression on both faces: astonishment. Then his divine will swept out, converging outside of the palace into the form of a face that looked at the huge kelp plant! And it was looking at... the young man in black standing on the kelp!

The young man had his hands clasped behind his back. His eyes sparkled like stars as he looked calmly at the face. Unsurprisingly, the emperor recognized the kelp! And because he recognized it, he was shaken to the core.

Prison A29... actually came with this guy?? This guy’s aura is clearly stronger than the fellow with the canon of order. Don’t tell me he’s actually the leader of this Acquisitioner squad?

This was a different heaven beyond heaven, so the Helioterran emperor wasn’t as up-to-date on the news from the Nineshores Heaven.

Meanwhile, Sir Star Ring did not suddenly feel calmer thanks to Xu Qing’s arrival. In fact, quite the opposite. And that was because....

Xu Qing has gotten even stronger!

Xu Qing was indeed stronger. Along the way, he had absorbed some of the ringsource stored in other space-times. As of now, he was only a tiny sliver away from achieving major success in the undying illusory reality of the immortal embryo! And because of that improvement, his canon was far mightier.

As he stood on the kelp leaf looking at the huge face of the emperor, he coolly said, “Hand it over.”

Xu Qing said the words very calmly from atop the kelp leaf. It almost sounded like his voice aligned with the principles of nature, making what he said completely and utterly reasonable. There was no need for any additional prestige. It didn’t matter that the only people present other than Sir Star Ring were the Helioterrans. In fact, the calmer he seemed, the greater and more intense the pressure felt by the Helioterrans.

This was the Fifth Star Ring. And humans reigned supreme!

Outside of the imperial palace, the members of the Helioterran imperial palace had grave expressions on their faces. A powerful enemy had arrived, and their hearts were sinking. They had already been convinced that Sir Star Ring was extremely strong. But now a second powerful expert had shown up, and they were shaken deeply.

Then there was the kelp plant! They were all fully aware that this was the true form of prison A29. The fact that this person had brought the kelp plant with him, and that it would fight for him... was profoundly significant.

They were all shaken with deep intensity. The Helioterrans were no longer glorious like they used to be. What was more, not one living member of their species had even witnessed that previous glory.

The current generation had all been born under the rulership of humankind. It didn’t matter that the Aurora heaven beyond heaven didn’t have a lord. In their bones, these nonhumans felt reverence for humankind. Because of the majesty of the Helioterran emperor, they temporarily managed to suppress that reverence. But in the end... the pressure from a truly powerful human expert was too much for them.

Xu Qing’s calm but forceful arrival, and the words he spoke that still echoed in their ears, caused all of them to once again recall their reverence for humankind.

Some of them instinctively bowed their heads. Deep in their blood, they were servants. Forcing nonhumans into servitude was an important tool used by humans in the Fifth Star Ring.

The Helioterran emperor knew that with absolute clarity. He said nothing. He looked at Xu Qing. And then... his forehead glittered as a command medallion flew out of it.

The medallion shone with gentle white light. Carved on its surface was the word ‘exemption,’ while the other side was inscribed with ‘Spiritlight.’

“Years ago,” the emperor said, “our species was viewed with favor by the Spiritlight heaven beyond heaven when we recognized one of their great leaders as our lord. Thus, we were given this medallion that provides exemption from any type of order or tax.”

The white light from the exemption medallion spread out over the imperial palace, which served as the entrance to the Helioterrans’ ancestral lands! The white light covered that entrance and cut everything off from it!

Xu Qing had heard about the exemption medallion from Sir Star Ring, but didn’t know much about it. But the fact that it was a gift, and that the Helioterran emperor had used it in the way he did, indicated that the medallion was very meaningful.

Along the way, he had asked Zhou Zhengli about it. Zhou Zhengli had already researched the matter deeply, and had been happy to offer Xu Qing a full explanation. There were some species in the Fifth Star Ring who, for various reasons, were awarded with exemption medallions. Normally speaking, when Acquisitioners encountered such species, they had no choice but to leave them alone.

However... Xu Qing’s eyes glittered as he looked at the exemption medallion, then pulled out the special mission jade slip that Lord Poison had given him.

“I’m here on orders from Immortal Lord Nineshores. My mission is to find a mysterious nine-colored ice that can extinguish the flame of a God Lord.” Looking coldly at the Helioterran emperor, Xu Qing continued, “This is a very important matter, and I suspect that your species has information. I’m going to perform an inspection immediately.”

The special mission jade slip glittered with pulses of light that swept out. When it contacted the white light from the exemption medallion, that light rippled. Then the white glow from the exemption medallion vanished. It no longer covered the imperial palace.

The surrounding Helioterrans were so taken aback that they couldn’t react. The emperor’s face fell; this completely surpassed anything he could have guessed would happen.

Normally speaking, all a species had to do was produce their exemption medallion, and the Acquisitioners would have to back down. How could he ever have predicted that this human would be on a mission like this? It seemed outright absurd to him! How could Immortal Lord Nineshores task someone with mere Quasi-Immortal battle prowess with collecting a type of ice that could extinguish the flame of a God Lord...?

In fact, he refused to believe it! And yet, the mission jade slip’s unique mark was truly one-of-a-kind! Most importantly, the reaction of the exemption medallion was clearly true and real....

The Helioterran emperor’s heart was pounding. That was because, even though his species had an exemption medallion, it obviously couldn’t defy someone on a mission directly from Immortal Lord Nineshores!

It wasn’t just the emperor and the rest of the Helioterrans who were visibly taken aback. Sir Star Ring’s gaze hardened as he looked at the mission jade slip Xu Qing was holding. Even he was caught by surprise by this turn of events.

Xu Qing stepped off the kelp leaf and strode toward the imperial palace. His every footfall caused the starry sky to tremble.

As he neared, the emperor’s face twitched. By the time Xu Qing had taken about seven or eight steps, the enormous projected face of the emperor had vanished, and he had emerged from the palace in his true form. He was 300 meters tall, crimson, with two gruish faces. And he pulsed with terrifying cultivation base fluctuations that formed an obstacle in front of Xu Qing.

Xu Qing stopped in place and looked at the Helioterran emperor. “You’re preventing my inspection?”

Eying Xu Qing, the emperor grimly said, “My species has no nine-colored ice.”

“The inspection will prove that either true or false!” The person to speak those words wasn’t Xu Qing. It was Sir Star Ring.

The emperor only sighed. He knew that he had miscalculated. With the wave of his hand, he caused Fourth True Monarch’s inheritance to fly out of the palace and land on his hand. His hope was to patch things up. If these people wanted this item, then... he might as well just give it to them. It was a precious treasure, but compared to what his species was really up to... it was better to just relinquish it. He was about to open his mouth to speak, when all of a sudden his face twitched.

Xu Qing’s gaze turned sharp as he looked in the direction of the imperial palace. At almost the exact same instant, the kelp sensed the same thing, and began to sway and emanate a threatening aura.

Teleportation fluctuations had suddenly begun to roll out from inside the palace. Someone was teleporting in!

The Helioterran emperor’s eyes narrowed and he waved his hand. The clay with heaven’s principle that he had been about to hand over returned to him, and he suddenly decided not to say the words he had been about to say.

“An emissary from our species’ patron is arriving. We’ll have to wait and see what the Helioterran patron says about all this.”

With that, the emperor turned and bowed in the direction of the palace. All of the other Helioterrans did the same.

The teleportation fluctuations grew stronger. Rumbling sounds echoed out as a huge pillar of light shot down from the starry sky and into the palace, sending out numerous shockwaves.

Xu Qing wasn’t unfamiliar with this type of teleportation. It was the same variety that had brought him from his own universe.

As the light descended, an aura very close to that of a Lower Immortal spread from the palace. The terrifying aura caused the starry sky to fold over itself as immortal energy took hold everywhere.

Anything related to gods would be rejected by this immortal energy. It was the result of an immortal embryo. This newcomer... was on the very cusp of transforming their immortal embryo and turning it into a mature immortal!

Sir Star Ring’s expression became very serious. Xu Qing frowned.

Everyone watched as the main door of the imperial palace swung open. Mountain-toppling, sea-draining force rippled out. It was like a volcano erupting with lava.

A middle-aged cultivator appeared, clad in a crimson robe, with a cold expression on his face. His every step caused the starry sky to tremble.

As he strode out into the open, the Helioterran emperor bowed deeply, and all of the other Helioterrans prostrated with deep respect.

“Our respects, Emissary!”

The terrifying aura of the emissary, plus the worshipful attitude of the Helioterrans, made for a very majestic scene.

The swaying kelp plant instantly sent a message to Xu Qing via divine will. “That guy has the same aura as the warden that sealed the True God’s wound!”

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed.

The man in the crimson robe looked around with an indescribably majestic gaze. When he noticed the kelp, his eyes glittered. Then he shifted his attention to Xu Qing.

“So, it was you that colluded with this traitorous plant to steal my Master’s god fodder?”

The Helioterran emperor blinked a few times.

Sir Star Ring’s expression turned grim, and the chains of order began to swirl around him.

Even as the canon of order stirred around Sir Star Ring, and the chains of order filled the void around him, Xu Qing’s gaze turned hard.

“Watch out,” he said, pointing in Sir Star Ring’s direction.

Sir Star Ring reacted with matchless speed, sending his chains of order out in front of him in a defensive array.

Unfortunately, he wasn’t quite fast enough. An astonishing force arrived before the chains. It was like planets shattering or universes quaking.

A deafening boom rang out as Sir Star Ring’s face went pale. Blood sprayed out of his mouth as he was sent spinning back like a kite with its string cut, his chains of order snapping and crumbling.

Astonishingly, in the spot where the chains had been shattered stood a figure. It was a blurry figure who was poised to pursue Sir Star Ring, only for Xu Qing’s finger to wave, causing space-time canon to form a sealing power. The figure was blocked.

However, that was only temporary. Xu Qing’s space-time sealing wasn’t strong enough to block the figure for more than a moment. Thankfully, that, coupled with the blockage of the chains of order, was enough to give Sir Star Ring a bit of breathing room.

As Sir Star Ring tumbled back coughing up blood, he unleashed his canon of balance, which gave him enough speed to temporarily avoid deadly danger.

The figure lurched to a halt in the starry sky. He was now fully visible. He was none other than the middle-aged cultivator with the crimson robe who had just stepped out of the imperial palace. Left standing behind in the palace was a blurry afterimage.

His true form had achieved incredible speed, appearing right in front of Sir Star Ring. If it hadn’t been for Xu Qing’s warning and assistance, Sir Star Ring would have been killed or, at the very least, sustained a grievous injury.

The cultivator turned to look at Xu Qing and coolly said, “You could see me moving? No wonder you have the gall to steal my Master’s god fodder.”

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed coldly. This was definitely the strongest Quasi-Immortal he had ever faced. As for his canon... it wasn’t very strange. In fact, it was downright simple.

Speed! He was capable of moving so quickly that he surpassed time itself! Canon wasn’t classified by strength or weakness. It was more about who could push it farther, and who could understand it more deeply.

“I originally wanted to kill this other guy so you would realize you can’t run, and should just return the stolen property. But since you blocked my path... then I guess I will kill you after all.”

Even as the middle-aged cultivator’s voice continued to drift out, he appeared only nine meters in front of Xu Qing!

That was a level of speed that surpassed the senses. He reached out with the intention of shoving his hand toward Xu Qing. As a result, he seized control of the space around Xu Qing, which became a vortex that erupted with a ripping force.

And yet, only an instant later, the middle-aged cultivator’s eyebrows shot up, and he made an exclamation of surprise. But he didn’t fall back.

Killing intent flared in Xu Qing’s eyes. He had long since been prepared to act. While his opponent was speaking moments ago, his canon of space had begun building up, and his canon of time had sowed chaos. Together, they formed space-time, and led to Infinite Timelessness.

When his opponent closed in and created that vortex, the ripping force encountered Xu Qing’s space-time. Without any fanfare at all, it was destroyed.

Xu Qing shivered, and blood oozed out of the corners of his mouth. But he still lifted both hands and went into an incantation gesture.

“Suppress. Freeze. Seal!”

Space was suppressed. Time was frozen. Space-time was sealed!

The starry sky around the middle-aged cultivator seemed to go rigid. All of the timelines solidified. The space-time they formed together was sealed, and everything around him seemed to become like amber.

At the same time, Xu Qing shone with silver light as he was made manifest as his nearly completed immortal embryo. He was massive, like the true body of a god towering within the starry sky. He lifted his right hand and spread his five fingers wide to represent the five elements. Metal. Wood. Water. Fire. Earth. The five extremes became ringsource, like five planets. He was not doing it to bolster himself, but rather... to bolster Xu Qing. He paid the price to strengthen Xu Qing. As a result, Xu Qing’s battle prowess swelled, putting him extremely close to the peak of Quasi-Immortal.

The immobilized cultivator slowly looked up at Xu Qing. Eyes shining with a strange, meaningful light, he said, “I think I know who you are. You’re that... Xu Qing!”

The middle-aged cultivator licked his lips, then lifted his own right hand, put it in front of himself, and pinched his fingers together. That action caused cracking sounds to ring out.

Space shattered. Time cracked. Space-time crumbled.

Then he relaxed his fingers, only to pinch them together even harder.

Sir Star Ring trembled from head to toe and coughed up a huge mouthful of blood. His balance, in the shape of scales, started crumbling. However, Sir Star Ring was an extraordinary individual, and thus, streams of starlight appeared around him. And every single stream was connected to a Star Ring Pagoda! By fully catalyzing their strength, he sent starlight streaming forth to sustain himself and slow down the crumbling of the scales.

That ensured that Xu Qing would be bolstered by balance for a bit longer.

The kelp’s leaves were shattering, and it was shaking violently. But the rips and tears in the leaves immediately sprouted little vines that snaked out and wrapped around the middle-aged cultivator. The sealing was being changed into a binding!

And yet, there was more. Starfire suddenly appeared in the starry sky, and hēr god altar became golden light. A divine likeness appeared, which unleashed full power. They were all trying to create an opportunity for Xu Qing!

This cultivator was truly astonishing in terms of speed and battle prowess. He was at the peak of Quasi-Immortal, just a step away from being a Lower Immortal! Although that one step would be incredibly difficult to complete, it was no exaggeration to say that when a cultivator reached this level, they were extraordinarily powerful. Strong enough to destroy all obstacles in their way.

And it had many applications. What this cultivator was revealing now was only a small portion of what it was capable of.

All of this takes quite a bit of time to explain, but in reality, everything happened in the time it takes a spark to fly off a piece of flint. An instant later, the efforts of Sir Star Ring, Starfire, and the kelp bought enough time for Xu Qing’s five fingers to fall all the way down. The starry sky shook.
