The difference was that he was not choosing the complicated route of parallelism. He was doing something far more direct.

It was something that Lower Immortals would comprehend, but not beings under that level, with the exception of people like Xu Qing, whose enlightenment had led him in that same direction. And as a result, Xu Qing was shaken by what he saw.

His path. His path....

Xu Qing had long been searching for a tenth extreme. He had worked hard, but hadn’t made any progress. But now he felt like he was in a dark world in which light had just appeared! Sadly, given the current circumstances, there was no time for thinking or planning. He had to put that inspiration aside for later.

Next came his true killing move!

A bell tolled. It was the toll of a bell that contained a scrap of God Lord power, something that could devastate all magics.

The starry sky went blank. The Quasi-Immortal cultivator shivered.

What appeared next contained heaven’s principle, parallelism, and the canons of Xu Qing's immortal body. It corresponded perfectly to his immortal embryo. It was... an iron skewer! And it wasn’t just one.

One after another, iron skewers emerged in parallel space-times. In total, there were 479 of them! Like shooting stars, they began shifting from being illusory to corporeal! Ultimately, all 479 combined into a single iron skewer at Xu Qing’s command.

He sent it out in a lethal attack! It shot right toward the middle-aged cultivator.

The cultivator fell back. He fled at top speed. He fled through time. He fled through space. He fled through the past, present, future, through fate and karma, through lineaments and memories.... He fled through everything!

But the iron skewer made from 479 skewers was guided by the tolling of the bell. Nothing could stop it.

It pierced space! It shattered time! It crushed past, present, and future! It penetrated fate and passed through karma! It devastated lineaments and memories! It passed through everything as it honed in on its target.

It caught up and stabbed him through the forehead. The moment it hit him, ripples spread out from his forehead, which turned into a surface of water. A blurry reflection became visible. Put precisely, it was a figure with its back turned away, a figure whose aura surpassed that of a Quasi-Immortal, and whose presence caused the entire surrounding universe to tremble.

It was an immortal! It was the middle-aged cultivator’s Master. This was a life-saving projection that had been implanted in him.

The figure looked over its shoulder. It cast a single glance at the iron skewer. That single glance caused the skewer to tumble off to the side, completely out of control.

Blood sprayed out of Sir Star Ring’s mouth. Starfire’s god altar destabilized. The kelp started crumbling. Xu Qing’s mind filled with rumbling sounds.

Taking advantage of the moment, the middle-aged cultivator finally managed to evade death. Retreating at top speed, he put distance between himself and his opponent. Though he was glaring at Xu Qing, his heart still pounded with lingering fear.

Then he said, “Emperor Helioterra. I command you and your species to help me. Attack!”

The emperor’s expression flickered, and inside he hesitated. If this were a simple matter of attacking a human, he wouldn’t think twice. But this emissary’s demand went beyond that. He wanted the Helioterrans to kill this human!

As the Helioterran emperor tried to decide what to do, Xu Qing managed to clear his head.

Looking at the middle-aged cultivator coldly, he said, “You’re out of chances.”

Xu Qing looked up into the starry sky. At that exact moment, the starry sky trembled, and a huge rift was sliced open. People emerged.

In the lead was Zhou Zhengli! Following him were Yuanshan Su, Li Mengtu, Sir Vilespirit, and more. All of the ascendees, Acquisitioners all, had come!

Another thing Xu Qing had done on the way was have Zhou Zhengli go out with orders for these people, just in case. If nothing else, Xu Qing would need them afterward to deal with the True God. Under Zhou Zhengli’s leadership, they had ripped open the starry sky to arrive here!

A tempest wind blasted out of the massive rift that had been torn open in the starry sky. It was as if a huge hand had ripped it open.

The entire void around the Helioterran imperial palace was shaking.

Cultivator after cultivator arrived, all of them pulsing with baleful auras. All of them had benefited to varying degrees thanks to ringsource. Clearly, Xu Qing wasn’t the only one to have made progress recently. The other cultivators had clearly done well. All of them had improved their cultivation bases since arriving. As a group, their battle prowess was far beyond anything from before.

That was especially true of Sir Vilespirit and Zhou Zhengli, both of whom had previously been at the peak of Imperial Sovereign, and were now just a breath away from a breakthrough. Li Mengtu wasn’t quite on that level, but he had still advanced significantly compared to before. Hordeslayer and Rampart were both in high spirits.

However, the person whose cultivation base had improved the most was Yuanshan Su. It was hard to say where she had gone to do it, but her immortal embryo was far stronger than before.

Because of all that, this group of cultivators was definitely capable of shifting the tide of this battle. Considering that all of them were ascendees, they had all survived countless deadly fights to get to this point. Even when acting as lone wolves, they were still dangerous. Now that they were here, their auras surged, and they were clearly ready for ruthless combat. They were a force no one would dare to take lightly.

Their gazes flitted to take in the Helioterran emperor... and the Quasi-Immortal cultivator!

All of the other Helioterrans were shaken, and suddenly got very uneasy feelings. The emperor scowled. This was the exact worst-case scenario he had wanted to avoid. Normally speaking, the chances of something like this were slim to none. Considering the emperor had an exemption medallion, he wasn’t worried about Acquisitioners showing up. At the very worst, he might have to pay them off to avoid trouble. That was why he had initially acted so fearlessly.

Yet none of his countless calculations could have prompted him to predict that Xu Qing would be on a mission for the Immortal Lord. That was the key to everything. Furthermore... his battle prowess was shocking, and he didn’t even seem scared of this emissary! In fact, he had seemed just on the verge of killing him!

What’s more, every single one of the people who just showed up, whether in terms of aura or just the sense I get from them, are obviously chosen.... This squadron of Acquisitioners is full of extraordinary individuals!

That thought struck fear into the heart of the Helioterran emperor.

Meanwhile, the Quasi-Immortal cultivator was sighing in his heart. He knew all about Xu Qing’s background. He had a very different identity than the Helioterran emperor, so he knew much more about what was happening in various heavens beyond heaven.

He had already heard that all of the new ascendees had become Acquisitioners. After all, the population of the heavens beyond heaven also included native cultivators who were born and raised there. In fact, they formed the majority of the population. Normally speaking, only ten percent of a squadron like this would be made of ascendees, as the ascendees would just replace people who were eliminated for one reason or another.

But this group of ascendees was different. On previous occasions, ascendees were usually sent out to different departments on different assignments. It was very rare for an entire group of them to be assigned to do the same thing. In fact, this was the first time in history that a group of ascendees had all been assigned to form a squadron in the Department of Acquisitions.

And thus, the arriving Acquisitioners caused the middle-aged cultivator to sigh. This was one reason why he had acted so decisively, and even gone so far as to demand assistance from the Helioterrans.

He knew that he couldn’t afford any delays. He needed to act quickly. It was true that he had an impressive background, and had even been on the path to becoming an Ascendee himself. But who here didn’t have an impressive background? And even those who didn’t, but still managed to get to the heavens beyond heaven, obviously had access to destined opportunities.

Thus, it didn’t matter that he was a Quasi-Immortal with a Lower Immortal Master. He knew full well that when dealing with a group like this... he might be able to provoke one or two of them individually, and could possibly even kill them. But if he had to deal with the whole group....

Not even his Master would dare to do that! So he quickly retreated to the imperial palace, where he would use the teleportation portal to go back home. He wasn’t going to worry any further about what was happening here. A fight like this... was not something he could win in a short time.

Another reason he chose to leave was that the situation was simply too unfavorable, and he was not confident he could solve it with force. And any slip-up could lead to his own death! So he decided to retreat.

Xu Qing was not surprised by his decision. Only a complete fool would fail to retreat in the face of so many opponents. That was especially true considering how close he had come to dying moments ago.

“But do you really think you can leave, just like that?” Eyes flashing coldly, he pointed out with his finger. “Send him on his way!”

Zhou Zhengli’s aura surged, and he replied, “Follow orders!”

Li Mengtu didn’t hesitate to attack. Sir Vilespirit blinked a few times, but he was familiar with how Xu Qing operated. Considering he wasn’t in danger of losing his life, he joined in the attack. Yuanshan Su didn’t hesitate to unleash her full battle prowess.

All of this had started because of Sir Star Ring, so he naturally went all out.

Hordeslayer and Rampart saw Sir Star Ring taking action. They were grateful to him, and they were in awe of Xu Qing, so they attacked with full force. Although they all had their own thoughts and considerations, they were united in the moment, so they all unleashed their cultivation bases and used their trump cards.

Nearly a hundred ascendees launched killing moves, which became like asteroids, combining into a shining force that shook the universe. It raged toward the Helioterran imperial palace with mountain-toppling, sea-draining force. Nothing could stop it. Even if the imperial palace had been made with more impressive materials, it couldn’t stand up to that force. In the blink of an eye, it shattered into dust.

It revealed the entrance to the Helioterran ancestral land, as well as the middle-aged cultivator, who had just been starting to blur away on the teleportation portal. His face fell, and blood sprayed out of his mouth. And as the teleportation was interrupted, his entire body distorted.

All he could do was willingly sustain injuries to use his Master’s mark to forcefully complete the teleportation. An instant later, he vanished.

Xu Qing looked at the spot coldly. He felt no regret. If the man was gone, he was gone. He was, after all, a peak Quasi-Immortal.

I’ll just kill him next time I see him. freewebnovel.com

Xu Qing looked over at the Helioterran emperor. So did the other Acquisitioners.

The emperor shivered deep inside. And then, without a bit of hesitation, he dropped to his knees and bowed to Xu Qing. Lifting up both hands, he held out the inheritance of Fourth True Monarch.

“Our humble species has erred,” he said loudly. “Please take this item to assuage your anger!”

The emperor was truly nervous, and was really out of options. He was about to continue speaking when Xu Qing waved his hand.

The clump of yellow clay flew into Xu Qing’s hand. After fiddling with it for a moment, he split it in half, keeping some for himself and giving the rest to Sir Star Ring.

“Many thanks for your help, all of you,” he said calmly. “I was given a mission by the Immortal Lord to look for a nine-colored piece of ice that can extinguish the flame of a God Lord. I noticed something suspicious about this species. I hope I can trouble you to inspect their ancestral land for me.”

The ascendees’ eyes lit up. They understood what was at stake, so it was with great enthusiasm that they shot into the ancestral land of the Helioterrans.

Xu Qing waited outside and continued to fiddle with the heaven’s principle clay.

The Helioterran emperor’s complexion shifted as his anxiety built. Unfortunately, he was in a completely powerless position right now. And then his face flickered even more dramatically.

Sir Star Ring had just emerged from the entrance to the Helioterran ancestral land, a quizzical expression on his face.

“We found something unusual. Something with nine colors. Do you want to take a look for yourself?”

Xu Qing actually looked surprised. “Are you serious?”

Sir Star Ring hesitated. “I’m not totally sure what it is. But I can tell it’s connected to the Aurora Immortal Palace.”

Xu Qing had a hard time believing that the pretext he had thrown out was actually true, and that the Helioterra Universe actually had the nine-colored ice that Immortal Lord Nineshores sought! If things turned out to be that simple, then the mission from Immortal Lord Nineshores was going to turn out to be little more than child’s play. What was more, he would need to completely rethink his judgment of Poison Monarch.

But no matter how he considered the situation, it seemed extremely unlikely that the nine-colored ice he sought was really here. With such thoughts on his mind, he put away the heaven’s principle clay he had been toying with. However, he didn’t immediately enter the Helioterran ancestral land. Instead, he turned to look at the Helioterran emperor prostrating to him.

The emperor’s eyes were wide with disbelief, and he was trembling. He was fully aware that if he didn’t provide a very clear explanation, then his entire species would likely be damned by myriad tribulations. This was something related to an Immortal Lord.... Not even his patron would utter a peep considering these circumstances.

Noticing Xu Qing looking at him, he immediately called, “Exalted one, this is a misunderstanding!! I know what this fellow daoist is talking about, and it’s definitely not the nine-colored ice referred to by Immortal Lord Nineshores. It’s a remnant of the Aurora Immortal Palace. In our species’ efforts to memorialize the Aurora Immortal Palace, we paid a huge price to fish a coffin out of the void!!

“It’s true that the coffin is made of ice, and it also has nine colors. But it’s not the thing you’re looking for!”

In his anxiety, the emperor wasn’t hiding anything. He explained everything openly.

Xu Qing’s face remained expressionless as he said, “I’ll find out one way or another by checking in person. Right now, all members of the Helioterran species, from the emperor on high to the lowliest member, will produce a drop of soul blood! Any who resist will be killed on the spot!”

Sir Star Ring bristled aggressively, as did the kelp plant and Starfire.

The Helioterran emperor hesitated only briefly. He was a decisive individual, and he knew that he couldn’t afford any more misunderstandings. It didn’t seem like this request was an attempt to wipe out his species more easily. It was more like... collateral. This person was worried about unexpected things happening in the ancestral land.

The emperor gritted his teeth, then reached up to his forehead and extracted some soul blood. He then indicated orders to be sent to the rest of his species. His heart was full of bitterness. The other Helioterrans quietly extracted their own soul blood.

The soul blood converged in front of Xu Qing. Waving his hand, he sent it to Starfire.

“You stay out here,” he said. “If anything happens to us inside, wipe out all of the Helioterrans.”

Starfire nodded gravely, collected up the soul blood, and then sent godly might out to cover the Helioterrans.

Xu Qing still didn’t feel completely confident that he had enough collateral, so he looked at the kelp plant.... He still didn’t completely trust the kelp. Eyes narrowing, he sent it a message via divine will, telling it to seal the Helioterran emperor and then go with him into the ancestral land.

The kelp seemed to be muttering to itself, but it did choose to send out a leaf, which became a sealing mark on the emperor. The emperor didn’t dare to resist.

Having done all that, Xu Qing took the kelp plant and the sealed emperor with him as he followed Sir Star Ring into the entrance.

The Helioterrans’ ancestral land was in a hidden galaxy. A bird’s eye view of the place revealed countless heavenly bodies and flickering natural laws.

One point of light stuck out to Xu Qing. He sent out his divine will, which caused the galaxy to expand rapidly in front of him. Larger and larger it grew from his perspective, and the process didn’t slow down. It grew immense, until ultimately, his view passed numerous planets and heavenly bodies. Then his gaze hardened.

In the very middle of the galaxy, in the spot he had noticed earlier, there were five enormous figures seated cross-legged. They were all Helioterrans. They were enormous and multicolored, with many faces, but they were all withered up. They were corpses. And they were the corpses of gods! Put precisely, these were god corpses belonging to the Helioterran species.

In the middle of the five corpses was a planet. It was completely frozen in ice. There was no life on the planet, only a coffin! And that coffin was made of ice that radiated a nine-colored glow. freewebnovel.com

A number of ascendees had gathered in that area, and their eyes gleamed as they observed the situation. None were making any moves.

“That setup is unusual,” Sir Star Ring said.

Xu Qing looked at it thoughtfully.

The Helioterran emperor quickly offered an explanation. “Exalted one, those corpses are gods that were members of our species long ago. After we surrendered to the immortals, we were assigned the mission of keeping thēir bloodline suppressed. Countless years have passed since then, and we’ve stuck to the mission the entire time. We’ve never wavered.

“The coffin is there to keep thēm more firmly suppressed. After all... if thēy were somehow resurrected, thēy obviously wouldn’t approve of our species. In fact, the first thing thēy would do would be to devour all of us.”

Sir Star Ring eyed the emperor of the Helioterrans. He had heard of similar situations before. The Fifth Star Ring was full of many species who were tasked with suppressing their ancestral gods.

“Interesting,” Xu Qing said calmly. “And you say you’ve never wavered?”

The emperor’s heart thumped in his chest. “Exalted one,” he said carefully, “what exactly do you mean by that...?”

Sir Star Ring looked at Xu Qing.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered as he realized what was going on.

To the cultivators of the Fifth Star Ring, the suppression of gods was important. That was why the star ring lacked mutagen and abounded with immortal energy. That was also why the species here couldn’t cultivate the path of gods. Because of that, old-timers would probably understand what they were looking at here. But more modern generations of cultivators would never have seen anything like it, and would have no idea what they were looking at.

But Xu Qing was not ordinary. He came from the Ninth Star Ring. In the Revered Ancient mainland, the gods wreaked havoc, and there were many species who outright worshiped gods. What was more, Xu Qing had personally witnessed multiple instances of godly ascension.

Whether it was the godchild of Crimson Mother, Empress Summer Departure, or that situation in the ghast hollow.... They all gave him similar sensations. And that was why he instantly realized what he was looking at....

This was obviously a godly ascension ceremony! However, based on what he could tell, this ceremony was incomplete. It wasn’t very impressive.

It’s been hidden.

Eyes narrowing, he waved his hand, and a band of silver light emerged from his immortal embryo.

Silver was the color of immortals. Gods absorbed ringsource and emitted holy golden light. That was why Xu Qing always saw gods covered with golden light. But when cultivators absorbed ringsource, they emitted silver light.

A stream of silver immortal light swirled in Xu Qing’s palm, and then he flicked his hand. The light shot into the galaxy, where it merged with some starlight, turning it silver.

The silver spread. It didn’t fill the entire galaxy. It just filled the galaxy’s starlight. Gradually, one stream of starlight after another turned silver. From Xu Qing’s high vantage point, it looked like a silver web spreading throughout the galaxy.

Then Xu Qing waved his hand to adjust it, and the different bright and dark spots in the web shifted, until it revealed an astonishing spell formation. The spell formation was just as large as the galaxy itself, and it connected all of the planets. In the middle of all that were the five corpses and the ice coffin. They formed two forces, one on the inside and one on the outside. In that manner, a huge convergence of ringsource was created.

When the Helioterran emperor saw what was happening, his face went pale. Sir Star Ring also reacted with visible surprise.

Then Xu Qing spoke. “Originally, this was all designed for the suppression effort you mentioned. But you used that as the foundation to build something much bigger. You created a godly ascension ceremony. Unfortunately, it’s not complete. Because of that, the godly ascension won’t work. Do you have an explanation for this, emperor?”

Xu Qing turned to look at the ashen-faced emperor.

Trembling from head to toe, the emperor dropped to his knees. “Exalted one, I would never dare to allow my species to attempt godly ascension. All of this was set up... to purify the blood of our species.”

The emperor didn’t dare to hide anything further. How could he ever have guessed that this secret attempt at godly ascension in the Fifth Star Ring would be identified so easily?

“That’s not important,” Xu Qing said. He reached out and clenched his hand into a fist.

A cracking sound rang out through the starry sky. Silver light flared from the spell formation as several key sections were broken. The ceremony was thus crippled.

“Sir Star Ring,” said Xu Qing, “you can lead people onto the planet now. Take that coffin. And have everyone prepare to absorb the ringsource that will come as a result.”

Sir Star Ring nodded and flew toward the planet.

Xu Qing waited quietly. Before long, he watched as the planet of ice trembled. Then a huge eruption of ringsource swept through the galaxy. The ceremony had been destroyed.

Afterwards, Sir Star Ring and Zhou Zhengli returned, dragging with them the nine-colored ice coffin.

Xu Qing knew what it was as soon as he laid eyes on it. No one else would have any idea what it was, because it hadn’t been in the reflected history of the Aurora Immortal Palace. But Xu Qing had possessed Young Lord Aurora, so his memories contained information about it.

“After Young Lord Aurora was born, his parents put him to sleep until after the gods had been subjugated. And to do that, they created a coffin. It does look like it’s made from nine-colored ice, but this is probably not the item Immortal Lord Nineshores is looking for.”

Xu Qing put the coffin away and turned to leave. He didn’t care if the emperor’s explanation was the truth or not. Nor did he have any need to collect any of the ringsource from this place. With Zhou Zhengli around, Xu Qing was confident that the other ascendees would be able to collect it, all while keeping an appropriate amount for themselves. They would definitely benefit a lot.

This matter is concluded. We also have enough ringsource for our mission. So next... we’re going to the real feast that occurs after the banquet is over. The True God!

With that, he turned to leave the Helioterran ancestral land.

A day later, outside the crumbled Helioterran imperial palace, the emperor prostrated with a bitter expression on his face.

The other Helioterrans flanking him were ashen and visibly weak. The three who had previously blocked the path of Sir Star Ring had blood oozing out of the corners of their mouths, and seemed incredibly dispirited. Their cultivation bases had declined! They were no longer Quasi-Immortals, but rather, had fallen down to the Imperial Sovereign level.

Close examination would reveal that they weren’t the only ones who had been affected like that. The other Helioterrans had all experienced a decline in cultivation base to varying degrees. And based on their soul fluctuations, the decline... was permanent. It came from their souls and their blood! Their bloodline had been pared down and their souls had been restricted! freewebnovel.com

Even the emperor himself had been affected. Although he was still a Quasi-Immortal, it was a constant struggle for him to stay in that level. Unfortunately, this situation wasn’t likely to change. That was because his extra face had withered up. His ancestral awakening had been interrupted!

And yet, the other Helioterrans still chose to defer to him, despite the resentment they felt in their hearts. A group of people was flying past them in the starry sky.

They were the ascendees. In the lead was Xu Qing. They were leaving.

***

The Helioterrans’ ceremony was about purifying blood and stockpiling ringsource. But the ascendees had taken the stockpile and split it up according to the quota established by Xu Qing.

Zhou Zhengli took the lead in handing over twenty percent of what he had collected. Li Mengtu and the others quickly followed suit.

As for the Helioterran imperial clan... Sir Star Ring used his powers of order and his canon of balance on them. In doing so, he ensured that the bloodline would remain impure.

Given the Helioterrans’ errant behavior, if events here had affected other heavens beyond heaven, it would have been necessary to report the matter, and the species would likely have been wiped out. Instead, their bloodline had been pared down. As a result, it didn’t matter what got reported at this point, the actions of Xu Qing and the other ascendees conformed perfectly with big human organizations in the Fifth Star Ring.

No one could blame them for doing anything wrong. Besides, their actions fell in line with what everyone expected from the Department of Acquisitions.... In fact, this entire thing seemed to be something of an assessment.

Even the Helioterrans realized that. They knew that in terms of a squadron of ascendees like this... their species didn’t measure up in battle prowess, background, or anything else for that matter. Their species was simply unlucky to have clashed with people like that. If the squadron had felt like simply exterminating them as a species, they would have had nowhere to run to.

Humankind was paramount in the Fifth Star Ring. So when all was said and done, they were actually a bit relieved at how things had ended. The fact that their species could continue living was a blessing on its own. Things had been wrapped up.

Now Xu Qing led everyone back to Prison A29. Along the way, he explained to the rest of the squadron what he had learned about the True God sun, and also what he planned to do.

When everyone realized that the kelp plant was actually the jailer in charge of A29, and that there was a chance they could extract ringsource from a True God, they started to get excited. They had already collected enough ringsource to meet the qualifications for the mission. And all of them had managed to build up significant personal stockpiles. But... they all still needed a lot of ringsource.

As a result, their eyes began to shine brightly. The recent experience of working together to invade another species and split the loot had caused all of them to warm up to each other significantly.

And they all approved of having Xu Qing as their leader. Considering that Xu Qing had a peak level of battle prowess, and was leading them to get more ringsource, their approval grew even stronger.

They soon arrived at Prison A29. The True God sun was still in the same spot. The kelp had come with Xu Qing as its true form, but hadn’t dared to be derelict in duty, so it had left behind a clone to keep an eye over things in the prison.

Upon returning, Xu Qing suppressed his anticipation, quickly scanned the area to make sure nothing unexpected had happened while he was away, then turned to the ascendees.

“Now we go forward with the plan to collect the ringsource!” Xu Qing said.

Sir Star Ring and all the others had been informed of the plan on the way. Now that they were present to see and sense everything personally, their eyes were shining with anticipation and determination.

Without another word, Xu Qing shot toward the sun. The kelp clone’s roots wriggled aside to make an opening, all while the true form provided a boost to everyone as they followed Xu Qing.

Zhou Zhengli, Sir Vilespirit, Yuanshan Su, and Li Mengtu were among them. Before long, the Acquisitioner squadron had entered the sun like a pack of hungry wolves.

***

Time passed. Three days later, the sun started trembling, and the kelp plant outside swayed back and forth violently.

It lasted for seven days. Rumbling echoed out into the starry sky, thanks to the violet ringsource fluctuations from the sun. Apparently, the sealing mark had been broken. A few more days passed. The sun was starting to get less fiery and hot. It was even shrinking. Apparently, there was going to be another eruption of ringsource.

However, that was when an intense stream of divine will swept through the interior of the sun. It turned into a voice.

“All of you... that’s enough!! This fodder is mine to take away. You have ten breaths of time to get the hell out of here. Any who remain after that will die here, and neither your Masters nor your backing organizations will have any cause to blame me!”

The thunderous voice shook the entire Helioterra Universe. Countless galaxies and planets shook, and all living beings trembled.

Even Xu Qing and the other ascendees were stricken with fear. After all, they had invaded this True God sun. Coughing up blood and facial expressions flickering, they fell into retreat.

By the time the ten breaths of time had passed, they were outside of the sun. The moment they appeared out in the starry sky, a huge vortex opened up beneath the True God sun. It looked like a gigantic mouth. Then a gargantuan hand stretched out, grabbed the sun, and dragged it into the vortex.

The kelp had no choice but to loosen its grip via the roots, otherwise it would have been dragged inside as well.

All of this takes some time to describe, but from the moment the ascendees appeared out in the open to when the vortex and hand appeared, only an instant passed. Then the hand dragged the sun into the vortex, and they all disappeared.

It was as if nothing had ever been in that spot. The only thing left behind was the quivering kelp, as well as Xu Qing and the ascendees, all of them scowling. Everyone seemed to be at a loss for words.

After going inside, they had encountered some difficulties breaking through the two sealing marks from before. But things had generally gone smoothly, and they had managed to absorb quite a bit of ringsource from the True God. Unfortunately... when they opened the third sealing mark, something unexpected happened.

There was an eye in the third sealing mark! It was the eye of an immortal, and it was the true form of the sealing mark restraining the True God sun.

The moment they spotted the eye, it opened and unleashed a terrifying tempest-like will. None of them had been able to stand up to it. There was no doubt as to its identity. It belonged to the Lower Immortal who was responsible for the entire situation.

Clearly, he had once been a minor government official in the Aurora heaven beyond heaven, and upon learning from his apprentice that something was going on, he erupted into a fury.

And he had given them ten breaths of time to leave. Not being willing to leave the True God sun behind, he had paid a heavy price to take it away. Apparently, the Lower Immortal hadn’t been able to do anything else but that.

And there wasn’t anything Xu Qing and the others could have done either. They weren’t strong enough to challenge a Lower Immortal. All they could do was sigh and leave.

The kelp plant looked confused. The prison it had been guarding... was gone. The gods in its leaves had been taken away by the warden. Now it had no mission left in this world....

In response to Xu Qing’s suggestion, it left with them.

Eventually, they ran into an asteroid field. There, they all selected asteroids where they settled cross-legged to work on digesting the ringsource they had taken. They would leave the universe in a month. Though they had only taken the ringsource from behind two sealing marks, that was still a significant amount.

Half a month went by quickly. The asteroid field drifted quietly through the starry sky.

During the time that passed, the ascendees all improved their cultivation bases and battle prowess thanks to the ringsource. Their auras were now much fiercer than before.

When the seventeenth day came... a magnificent aura suddenly spread through the floating asteroid field. The aura was so strong it threw the asteroids into chaos.

Space-time rippled. The five elements merged. The natural law of the universe stirred, converging into a dazzling, multicolored display. Deafening rumbling sounds echoed out, like the thump of a heartbeat or the crash of heavenly thunder.

Everyone was shaken deeply. Even as they sat there cross-legged, they opened their eyes and looked in the direction of the disturbance!

On an elliptical asteroid someone sat cross-legged in a black robe, with violet hair flying around him. He was shining with bright light and pulsing with explosive immortal energy. He was none other than Xu Qing!

Sir Star Ring’s eyes shone brightly. He’s breaking through to Quasi-Immortal! That energy. Those fluctuations....

Sir Vilespirit’s expression was grave. Yuanshan Su seemed stunned. Li Mengtu was already scanning the area for threats, as he took it upon himself to stand as dharma protector for Xu Qing.

Hordeslayer and Rampart seemed nervous and even scared. They had their own ideas about what this meant. If Xu Qing became a Quasi-Immortal, then all he had to do was lift his hand, and the two of them would become immortal swords that would excitedly rush to his call.... And thus, their anxiety was building.

That was when Zhou Zhengli’s eyes narrowed with determination. Standing, he flew over to an asteroid near Xu Qing and sat down cross-legged. Looking stern, he said, “What are the lot of you doing? Stand as dharma protectors right now! And if any of you are thinking of trying to pull some sort of fast one, let me just remind you—” Zhou Zhengli’s eyes shone with a mysterious light “—that this heaven beyond heaven has a name. Remember what it is? The leadership positions in the other heavens beyond heaven are filled.

“All of you understand what that means. So, regardless of what the lot of you are thinking, I can tell you that my goal is to seize a leadership spot in this heaven beyond heaven without a lord! Although the chances are small, they do exist. Considering the possible benefits... I’m willing to take a chance. And that’s why anyone who poses a threat to my chances will be considered an enemy!”

This was the first time Zhou Zhengli had openly stated his ambitions. Although no one could be absolutely sure that he was telling the truth... there was no doubt that his words stirred the hearts of everyone present.

Hordeslayer and Rampart suddenly weren’t feeling very scared. After initially looking stunned, their eyes shone. “Leadership spot?”

Hordeslayer and Rampart were moved. The brothers exchanged a glance, and then simultaneously looked over at Sir Star Ring.

Sir Star Ring’s face was completely expressionless, but he had turned his back to Xu Qing’s asteroid, indicating he was going accept the role of dharma protector. The two brothers’ spirits lifted. Sword energy soared up. Astonishingly, they chose to transform into two ancient immortal swords that glittered in the starry sky as their points shifted to face outward. They were also positioning themselves as loyal guards, watching over their master.

Zhou Zhengli smiled in response, all while his eyes glittered in a way that was both obsequious and amiable.

Sir Vilespirit snorted coldly in his heart, all while musing that these two swords had cultivated themselves into insanity. He also wondered why a Lower Immortal had taken people like that as apprentices, and how they had reached a similar level as himself. However, that was all inside. When he noted Zhou Zhengli’s actions, his eyes narrowed. Then, after some consideration, he closed his eyes.

Zhou Zhengli smiled again and then turned to look at Yuanshan Su. As far as he was concerned, Yuanshan Su was very important. Although it seemed on the surface that she wasn’t very strong—a far cry from Sir Vilespirit and Sir Star Ring—the reality was that she had exceptional battle prowess. And whether it was things he had learned about her in the past, or her behavior in the Aurora Immortal Palace, he knew that there was more to her than met the eye.

In fact, upon analyzing everything that happened in the Aurora Immortal Palace, there was no doubt that if Xu Qing hadn’t been there, she would have been the one to survive the longest. That was especially considering that she was... a female cultivator. And she was a very pretty female cultivator. As far as Zhou Zhengli was concerned, there was every reason to believe she would eventually become an astounding phoenix among women. Therefore, his gaze was filled with respect.

Yuanshan Su said nothing. She just settled into her role as dharma protector.

Zhou Zhengli looked away. As for the rest of the Acquisitioners, considering that the strongest among them were clearly siding with Xu Qing, it only lent further weight to their approval of him. Soon, the people who had harbored ill intentions quashed them. Everyone acted as dharma protectors.

In that manner, time passed.

The immortal energy fluctuations coming off Xu Qing grew stronger. The immortal energy spread out into the starry sky, eventually provoking a reaction from the universe’s magical laws.

At the same time, his immortal embryo began to manifest outside of him in the manner of a divine statue. It was fully 300 meters tall and looked like a god.

Xu Qing looked very dramatic as he sat on the asteroid. A terrifying aura spread off him, becoming a tempest in the starry sky. The surrounding cultivators backed away to avoid the tempest, but at the same time, they were paying close attention to the situation.

From ancient times until now, whenever an Imperial Sovereign became a Quasi-Immortal, it was a very grand occasion. After all, Quasi-Immortals... were still immortals! And the term ‘immortal’ was inherently marvelous.

Although most of the people present understood what would happen when an Imperial Sovereign rose to a higher level, they were still riveted on what was happening. That was because... watching this process would give them deep insights into what was to come for them in the future. Although things wouldn’t be exactly the same, at least they would get a general idea.

Sir Star Ring was paying very close attention. After all, this was the person who had served him up his first defeat. And Xu Qing had also killed him. He was very curious to see how his Quasi-Immortal upgrade went. The most important parts of a Quasi-Immortal upgrade are the nine bursts and the immortal foundation! Nine is the limit for the bursts. How many will he get?

There were others wondering the same thing, especially Zhou Zhengli. In fact, among this group, no one was paying closer attention than him.

As everyone pondered the situation, Sir Vilespirit suddenly said, “Ladies and gentlemen, who of you is willing to make a little wager? How many bursts do you think Xu Qing will get? Zhou Zhengli, I know you’re fond of him. Are you willing to put your money where your mouth is?”

Everyone looked at him with curious expressions. After blinking a few times, Sir Vilespirit continued, “I haven’t achieved my own breakthrough, but I do know that when an Imperial Sovereign becomes a Quasi-Immortal, they have to place their immortal embryo outside of their body and grow it in bursts. Ordinary Quasi-Immortals can only achieve three external bursts. Those who reach five are rarer, and any who achieve seven are considered chosen.

“As for eight bursts, well, people like that are as hard to find as phoenix feathers or qilin horns. And nine bursts... would make you a Lower Immortal! What about you, Fellow Daoist Yuanshan? How many bursts will you bet on?” He looked at her.

“Eight!” she replied coolly.

Sir Vilespirit smiled and looked at Sir Star Ring. Sir Star Ring ignored him. Unconcerned by that, Sir Vilespirit turned to look at Zhou Zhengli.

“Nine, of course,” Zhou Zhengli said with a faint smile.

“Now we wait and see what happens,” Sir Vilespirit said with a smile.

Li Mengtu frowned and was about to say something, when all of a sudden, he looked thoughtful. Then he looked at Zhou Zhengli and said, “The number of bursts isn’t as important as the immortal foundation!

“The bursts determine the strength of the immortal embryo. But the immortal foundation determines how far you can walk on the path of immortals! Every new Quasi-Immortal has to have that immortal foundation. It’s the foundation for their later immortal ascension!

“The foundation cannot be illusory. It must be corporeal. And it can’t be modeled on one’s canon. Some people prepare it in advance, but some people have more complicated plans.... I wonder what Xu Qing’s immortal foundation will be like.”

Li Mengtu’s words echoed through the starry sky for all to hear. Everyone responded with thoughtful looks. They all knew that the immortal foundation really was very important for one’s future.

Even Sir Star Ring, who had not participated in the talk of making a wager, was looking at Xu Qing in the tempest, and was thinking back to his own breakthrough. Originally speaking, he should have achieved nine bursts. But thanks to his conflict with Xu Qing, he had been unable to complete the breakthrough in the fifth world. After going through a lot of setbacks, he ultimately decided to go through with the breakthrough on the outside. And he had achieved eight bursts. In the end, he had died and been born again. That was when he finally achieved the last burst, and perfected his status as an immortal. But thinking back to everything that happened, he was still shaken.

Of course, the whole reason I picked the fifth world to begin with wasn’t just because the surroundings would help me achieve nine bursts. My real goal was related to what came after that, the immortal foundation.

I wanted to follow the path of Fourth True Monarch. I hoped to find his remains in the fifth world, and then incorporate them into my immortal foundation. So what is Xu Qing’s immortal foundation going to be like?

When he thought back to his fight with Xu Qing, he remembered the bell he had used. There was also that extremely sharp iron skewer....

Hordeslayer and Rampart shivered in sword form, then backed up. However, not feeling very confident in their position, they backed up again. All of a sudden, they were feeling a bit afraid.

Just as they did that, and as the tempest raged, Xu Qing on the asteroid emitted loud rumbling sounds. As the deafening sound spread out, the 300-meter immortal embryo that he had placed outside of himself, which resembled him in all respects, suddenly glittered with bright light.

“It’s starting!’ Li Mengtu murmured, his heart filling with anticipation.

The light became blinding as the 300-meter immortal embryo erupted with terrifying power. The rumbling grew louder. Then the 300-meter immortal embryo grew by tenfold. Astonishingly, it reached 3,000 meters in height, and the aura it emitted struck everyone with fear. This was the first burst!

But things weren’t over yet. The 3,000-meter immortal embryo let loose terrifying fluctuations again as it again grew by tenfold. It was now at 30,000 meters! Next came the third burst. 300,000 meters! After that was the fourth burst. 3,000,000 meters!

The process continued and showed no signs of weakening. In fact, it grew stronger. Soon, a 30,000,000-meter figure struck fear into the hearts of everyone.

“Xu Qing’s bursts are all tenfold increases!”

“Tenfold.... Normally speaking, they’re usually twofold or threefold!” freewebnovel.com

“We’re only up to the fifth burst!”

“It’s only the fifth burst, and yet... he’s already surpassed the vast majority of Quasi-Immortals!”

As everyone reeled... the bursts continued! In the blink of an eye, the sixth burst occurred. 300,000,000 meters! That alone went to show what kind of reserve powers Xu Qing had built up.

Everyone backed away further. Xu Qing’s immortal embryo really looked like a god. As it sat cross-legged in the starry sky, it seemed holy, and caused the hearts of all observers to pound.

Rumbling echoed out along with the seventh burst. The eighth burst followed instantly.

30,000,000,000 meters!

Although it wasn’t as big as an entire galaxy... compared to it, the planets in the area were like grains of rice.

The other ascendees had backed away a great distance. As they looked at Xu Qing’s immortal embryo, they were shaken to the core. Sir Vilespirit was dumbstruck. Zhou Zhengli’s eyes were shining with excitement. Sir Star Ring’s expression had not changed, but his pupils had constricted. Yuanshan Su remained silent. Everyone else felt tempests raging in their hearts.

As everyone reacted with different degrees and types of shock, Xu Qing’s external bursts seemed to stop. But that only lasted a moment. Finally... a heaven-rending, earth-crushing boom ripped through the starry sky as Xu Qing’s terrifying immortal embryo experienced another burst!

The ninth burst!

The starry sky went dark. A figure comparable to a galaxy towered in the starry sky. The surrounding planets were no longer like grains of rice. They were like dust.

Everyone was struck senseless.

Then the galaxy-sized immortal embryo shrank down rapidly, causing a host of afterimages to linger in the starry sky. Soon, it was back to normal size, and it fused with Xu Qing’s true body until they were one.

This was what he really looked like. The external bursts... portrayed the immortal embryo’s sphere of power. What that meant was that Xu Qing’s divine will... had a range as large as a galaxy.

“Unheard-of...” Sir Star Ring murmured, his scalp tingling.

Everyone else was flabbergasted.

“This can’t be! Normally speaking, this should be completely and utterly impossible. Tenfold bursts... all the way to the limit. The ancient records don’t even talk about this kind of thing happening!”

“Xu Qing’s reserve powers were obviously deep, but they couldn’t make this happen!”

“This surpasses any normal categorization!”

“There must be other karma at play!”

Sir Star Ring had previously been the number one Shining Star. He came from the Star Ring Pagoda, and was unusually knowledgeable. But after being temporarily stunned, he realized that something was off. He could admit that there was a disparity between himself and Xu Qing. But the disparity shouldn’t be this big! All of a sudden, he trembled inwardly as something occurred to him. It was a speculation that caused him to turn and look at Zhou Zhengli.

Sir Vilespirit soon came to his senses. So did Yuanshan Su and the others. And they all looked over at Zhou Zhengli. They were all thinking back to what Zhou Zhengli had just said.

As for Zhou Zhengli, he looked very excited. “It’s because... we’re in the Aurora heaven beyond heaven! It’s because... he sowed immense karma with this place. Someone actually gave him this heaven beyond heaven! That’s why... this heaven beyond heaven without a lord welcomed him with open arms!”

***

Somewhere in the Fourth Star Ring, in lands where gods proliferated, an old boat was soaring through the starry sky. It was a marvelous boat that the will of gods couldn’t detect. There were two people in it, both of whom had astonishing cultivation bases. As long as they were careful, they could safely traverse the Fourth Star Ring.

“He has it now,” a gentle voice said in the boat. The person who had just spoken was none other than Young Lord Aurora.

Next to him was a young woman who was his wife. Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix. Upon hearing her husband’s words, she laughed softly. “I knew it. I could tell that you gave him more than just the immortal palace.”

Young Lord Aurora looked affectionately at his wife. “He did us such a favor that an immortal palace wasn’t enough. I gave him the entire heaven beyond heaven.”

What had once been the Aurora heaven beyond heaven was trembling. The events that had just played out had attracted the attention of high-level entities. Streams of divine will that low-level cultivators couldn’t even detect emerged from other heavens beyond heaven, and focused on the heaven that had been without a lord for many years.

At the source of the disturbance, Zhou Zhengli’s words shook everyone, including Sir Star Ring, Yuanshan Su, Sir Vilespirit, and all the other ascendees. All of these people were chosen, especially Sir Star Ring. Whether in terms of battle prowess or knowledge, they were at the peak in their generation. And therefore, all of them were instantly able to recognize the logic and accuracy of what Zhou Zhengli had just said.

There was only one way to explain... how Xu Qing’s breakthrough had given rise to such a monumental tempest. It was a welcoming cry from this heaven beyond heaven. It was a blessing from it! That was the only way something like this could happen when an Imperial Sovereign became a Quasi-Immortal!

With nine bursts, an immortal embryo became like a galaxy! With nine bursts like that, one had to wonder what the coming immortal foundation would be like....

With such thoughts on his mind, Sir Star Ring’s eyes glittered. It seemed that everyone else was thinking the same thing.

That was especially true of Zhou Zhengli, whose expression was one of pure anticipation. Few people understood his canon. And those who did know about it only knew what he wanted them to know. Sir Vilespirit was the only one who understood it more deeply.

The reason for that had to do with the substructure of Zhou Zhengli’s canon. His canon... was actually quite similar to that of Immortal Lord Nineshores. It had to do with secrets!

That said, his canon explored a different direction. It was about foresight!

In the reflected history of the Aurora Immortal Palace, I had premonitions about everyone. There was one exception... I couldn’t foresee anything about Xu Qing. It was as if he didn’t even exist within the range of my foresight.

Because of the unique nature of my canon... if I worked hard enough, I could even make it work on an immortal. Though I couldn’t make any changes, I could at least struggle to see some traces. I wouldn’t dare touch them, of course.

But Xu Qing... is even more unique! There weren’t even any traces of him within my foresight. In the end, I left the Aurora Immortal Palace and waited outside in the hopes of catching a glimpse of him....

Zhou Zhengli thought back to the moment when Xu Qing had stepped back out into the Fallen Immortal Moors. Upon emerging, he had looked at Zhou Zhengli. When that happened, Zhou Zhengli didn’t betray any reaction on his face, but his insides were thrown into chaos.[1]

Even then, there had been something empty about Xu Qing that had struck fear into his heart. And then... just when he was about to look away, his foresight caused him to hear a faint voice.

“He has it now. He did us such a favor that an immortal palace wasn’t enough. I gave him the entire heaven beyond heaven.”

Those words struck him like lightning. He had been able to tell that the person speaking those words had intentionally let him hear. They had been very thought-provoking to Zhou Zhengli. And as he analyzed them... he realized that he needed to seize this opportunity that no one else had any clue about!

That was why he had chosen to continue to address Xu Qing as Young Lord. That was why he had delivered 1st place to Xu Qing on a platter. That was why he had been obsequious from the moment they reached the Nineshores heaven beyond heaven, all the way to now.

“And now... it’s time to bear witness!” Zhou Zhengli murmured in anticipation.

Everyone was waiting!

As they looked on, Xu Qing’s eyes opened as he sat cross-legged on the meteor. They were clear and full of enlightenment. So... that’s how it is....

During the bursts, he had come to realize that Young Lord Aurora had given him, not just the immortal palace, but the entire heaven beyond heaven. At the moment, he could clearly sense that the fluctuations of this heaven beyond heaven had formed a resonance with him. It was waiting for him.

He looked up at the surrounding starry sky. Xu Qing had originally been planning to use his space-time hourglass as his immortal foundation. After acquiring the nine-colored ice coffin, he had considered using that instead, as it was both mysterious and extraordinary. But in the end, he had decided that the space-time hourglass was more fitting. It was a space-time treasure, after all.

He hadn’t even considered using the violet crystal. After all of his experiences through the years, he had come to know more about the violet crystal, but also knew... that it was not something he could alter.

At the very least, I need to become an immortal before I try altering it in any way.

But now... Xu Qing knew that nothing else could be as suitable as the starry sky he was looking at. Therefore, his eyes shone with determination.

Slowly rising to his feet, he looked out at this heaven beyond heaven, and then threw his hands wide as if to embrace it. His divine will rumbled out, filling the galaxy he was in. And from that point... he started calling out to the starry sky with the goal of... taking this heaven beyond heaven!

The entire heaven beyond heaven, including all of the universes, galaxies, and planets all began to tremble. There were innumerable species, including the Helioterrans, who suddenly felt an indescribable pressure weighing down on them. And to their astonishment, they felt fear coming out of nowhere.

It was as if heaven had been lost... but was now coming back! The lord had gone, but a succession was taking place!

A tide began to flow in the starry sky, starting from the edges of the Aurora heaven beyond heaven, and moving toward Xu Qing. As it converged, great rumbling sounds echoed out everywhere. As deafening sounds rang out, as countless species trembled, and as Sir Star Ring and the others reeled....

The starry sky over Xu Qing was covered up! Dazzling and pulsing with immense pressure, a spectacular immortal palace... descended, replacing the starry sky overhead.

The immortal palace was pure jade, with ornate decorations. It had countless structures conforming to an ancient architectural style, and though it looked rather old and dilapidated, ravaged by time, there was nothing else that existed in this heaven beyond heaven that was more paramount than it! freewebnovel.com

This was... the true form of the original Aurora Immortal Palace! It represented the will of this heaven beyond heaven! It was glorious, majestic, and astonishing!

The moment it appeared, the hearts of the onlookers raced, and their minds felt blank.

Zhou Zhengli looked elated. He knew he had gambled correctly! Quickly ducking his head down, he dropped to his knees and prostrated to Xu Qing!

As the Aurora heaven beyond heaven joyfully welcomed the Aurora Immortal Palace, the starry sky trembled. And then the palace turned into a spectacular beam of immortal light.

It shot toward Xu Qing. It poured into his head, into his body, and into his immortal embryo! Dazzling, prismatic light glittered in the starry sky.

And then a deep, rumbling sound echoed into the hearts and minds of all the living beings in the sea of stars.

The immortal palace had a lord! It was Xu Qing’s immortal foundation! With that immortal foundation, he could control... this entire heaven beyond heaven! He had become an unheard-of Quasi-Immortal!

Opening his eyes, Xu Qing spoke in a voice that sounded like heaven itself. “Hear my decree!”

From this moment on, this heaven had a new name.

Green Heaven![2]

1. Xu Qing came out of the immortal palace in chapter 1184. ☜

2. The name of his heaven takes the Qing character from Xu Qing’s name and adds it to the word for sky or heaven. This has a number of implications. Normally speaking, this set of characters means “clear skies” or “blue skies.” At the same time, those two characters are part of a longer idiom that means something like Great Lord Clear Sky, and colloquially refers to “a just and incorruptible official.” Many readers made jokes/comments in Chinese like “oh, it turns out Xu Qing is the origin of the idiom” or something like, “Xu Qing turns out to be Great Lord Clear Sky.” But there are obviously multiple layers of wordplay in the name of this heaven that can’t all be conveyed in English. I originally wanted to translate it as Clear Heaven, because it made me think of the ‘clear skies’ meaning. However, later wordplay makes it clear that the meaning is ‘green’ (while also referring to Xu Qing’s name). ☜

In the many heavens, there was a voice of admiration that said, “It is good.”[1]

There was a profound gaze full of something very wondrous. There was a paramount will, tranquil and calm. Thoughts converged peacefully, ultimately revealing a secret known only to the speaker.

“It is time for the Aurora Heaven to turn the next page of history, and let the next generation begin a new epoch. Aurora, you were exceptionally talented to be willing to give up everything. Your son was exceptionally broad-minded to be willing to abandon all.... Considering that father and son were both like that, I... simply cannot measure up.”

***

The will of the many heavens was not perceived by the masses. As of this moment in the Green Heaven, as the Aurora Immortal Palace became an immortal foundation and fused with Xu Qing’s immortal embryo, his aura skyrocketed. It became stronger and stronger, until it was so stunning it left its mark in the entire heaven beyond heaven.

Eventually, as everyone looked on in astonishment, an indescribable pressure emanated from Xu Qing, something that caused everyone to instinctively feel the urge to bow to him. It was a sensation similar to what gods gave off. After ringsource reached a certain level of density, it would provide a natural majesty to the lord of a heaven beyond heaven.

The majesty caused Sir Star Ring to bow his head without even thinking about it. He, who had the legacy of Fourth True Monarch, also had karma tied to the Aurora heaven beyond heaven. And now that karma was converging on Xu Qing.

Yuanshan Su trembled and tried to exercise self-restraint, but failed. The scenes from mirrored history flashed in her mind, and all of a sudden, Xu Qing became... Young Lord Aurora. Li Mengtu looked somewhat dazed as he thought back to his identity in the reflection of the Aurora Immortal Palace. Sir Vilespirit instinctively took a few steps back and put aside all thoughts of disloyalty.

If they reacted in that way, there was little need to mention the other ascendees. All were shaken to the core.

But the largest tempest was in the heart of Zhou Zhengli. His eyes shone as he produced a piece of metal that he squeezed his hand down onto. The metal pierced his palm, causing blood to flow out. He also bit the tip of his tongue.

Then he activated his canon. After sending the blood from his tongue into his eyes, turning them bright red, he sent the blood from his palm into the piece of iron. And then he activated a secret magic.

Using that secret magic, he looked at Xu Qing! Everything he had said before was true. He really did want to assist Xu Qing. He really did want to make a bet. And he really did know secrets. At the same time, he really did want to follow Xu Qing into the future, where he would make even more immense gains.

That said, although all those things were true, he had another objective. And that was... to get a clear view of Xu Qing! He wanted to see Xu Qing in his foresight.

Even if it was an abstract image. Even if it was blurry. Even if he just saw a bit.... He wanted to do everything he could possibly think of to catch that glimpse! That was his dao.

As soon as he looked at Xu Qing, a premonition of foresight filled him, deep and intense, until it formed an obsession.

I have seen. Seen the dao. My canon can break through. And my cultivation base can break through!

Zhou Zhengli knew that, ordinarily speaking, his powers of foresight couldn’t do anything like that. And thus, he had waited. He had been waiting until this moment, when Xu Qing was breaking through. At that moment, a tempest raged, heaven and earth sang, the starry sky shook, and the Green Heaven was radiant!

The moment an Imperial Sovereign became a Quasi-Immortal was like the opening of a closed door. Even if it was only a small opening, it was possible to get a clear view of the world beyond.

And so, Zhou Zhengli took advantage of this moment to open that door. And... he saw through the crack! When he did, he shook from head to toe, and his mind filled with a sound like heavenly thunder. His eyes, nose, mouth, and ears... gushed with blood.

Yet he was laughing. It was an excited laughter. Within that excitement was an extreme level of fear.

An unfamiliar star ring.... An indescribably terrifying broken face.... And on top of that face is a throne... Sitting on the throne is a person.... He’s looking at me. He’s....[2]

Zhou Zhengli shook as his aura skyrocketed. Because of what he was seeing, his canon was also rising to great heights. His cultivation base had previously been just on the verge of reaching Quasi-Immortal.

What he had lacked wasn’t ringsource, but canon. But right now, his canon was improving, and his immortal embryo was erupting. He was now rising to the level of Quasi-Immortal.

A thick fog was building up around him, which was a manifestation of his canon, and contained the same secrets as his dao. Because of it... no one could see his breakthrough. However, the other ascendees could sense what was happening, leading to even further astonishment.

Xu Qing didn’t care. He opened his eyes. They seemed to contain rivers of stars. Universes. His eyes held whirlpools of stars. It was extremely majestic.

The entire heaven beyond heaven was full of rumbling sounds. Countless species dropped to their knees in their ancestral lands. Everyone was shaking.

And that was because... when Xu Qing opened his eyes, a pair of eyes appeared within the heaven beyond heaven, above the heads of all living beings and all inanimate objects. They looked down on the Green Heaven! They were Xu Qing’s eyes. By means of his authority over the immortal palace, he was looking at all things. It was a gaze of omniscience.

Xu Qing saw countless things. He saw all the universes in the heaven beyond heaven, as well as all the species, the god prisons, and the resources. After a moment, he sighed in his heart.

He retracted his gaze.

The Aurora heaven beyond heaven had been without a lord for years, and thus, the local species had descended into chaos and disorder. Weak species had long since been wiped out, while the strong species eventually developed karma with other heavens beyond heaven.

As for the god prisons... there were varying circumstances with the wardens and jailers. For the most part... most were unsupervised. There were no longer any god prisons with True Gods in them. After all, ringsource was the first thing people would want to seize. And of course, it would be taken away to other heavens beyond heaven.

In some ways, the Helioterra Universe was like a microcosm of the entire heaven beyond heaven.

It seems that the Helioterra Universe had a True God imprisoned because of that Lower Immortal. For whatever reason, he didn’t feel like expending the effort to take it away, so he left it here.

Xu Qing didn’t say anything. All the things that had been taken away... weren’t necessarily lost forever. He could theoretically take them back. Unfortunately, he would need to be a lot stronger to deal with such situations. And he needed time. Right now, he didn’t have either of those things.

After some thought, his eyes glittered. Then he spoke coolly, in a voice that filled the Green Heaven.

“In one hour, these heavens will be sealed. During that time, any species that wishes to leave may do so. I won’t force you to stay. However, though you may leave, you may not take any resources with you!”

It seemed meaningless to Xu Qing to force species to stay behind if they had backers in other heavens beyond heaven. The past was the past, and it had nothing to do with him.

What he wanted was a heaven beyond heaven that was devoid of chaos. If a lot of species left, this place would also be empty of life. But... at least it would be pure. It made a lot more sense to just let the species leave than try to force them to stay.

He then opened up the right to leave. Before long, many species had contacted their backers and were starting to leave.

Time passed by.

Although an hour wasn’t much time, it was enough for them to teleport out. The time limit arrived. The immortal palace within Xu Qing trembled. His voice echoed out.

“Heavens, be sealed.”

Light flowed through the heavens, spreading out from Xu Qing, moving at incredible speed through all of the universes. After the entire heaven beyond heaven was covered, the right to leave was closed. The starry sky was sealed. From then on, unless someone was given the right by Xu Qing, they couldn’t leave this heaven beyond heaven!

Around this time, the fog around Zhou Zhengli began to dissipate, and a figure emerged, step by step. He was no longer an Imperial Sovereign. He was a Quasi-Immortal.

And yet, he still had the same obsequious smile on his face as he bowed deeply to Xu Qing.

“Congratulations, Lord of Green Heaven!”

Everyone present, regardless of what faction they sided with, or what their background was, rose and bowed. It was a way of showing respect and approval of the entire heaven beyond heaven.

Xu Qing looked at Zhou Zhengli. A moment later, he coolly said, “We can leave now.”

Though he had the immortal palace as a foundation, and owned this entire heaven beyond heaven, they were reserve powers for Xu Qing. He still had an official assignment as an Acquisitioner.

Xu Qing waved his hand toward the starry sky. Ripples flowed out as a path emerged. He stepped onto it. Everyone else cleared their minds and followed.

That included Zhou Zhengli, although he followed closely behind Xu Qing. As he looked at Xu Qing in front of him, a tempest continued to rage in his heart. He just couldn’t stop thinking about what he had seen.

The person seated on that throne, the one looking at me... was him!

Ducking his head, he hurried forward resolutely.

***

And thus, they walked along the path through the starry sky. The path bolstered them so that every step they took spanned universes. Eventually, they reached the far end of the heaven beyond heaven. They left. When they emerged, an unfamiliar starry sky met their eyes.

This was the space between heavens beyond heaven, and it was known as the Heavenless Zone. Normally speaking, the Heavenless Zone was a barren waste. But perhaps because of the Aurora heaven beyond heaven being without a lord for so long, powers from other heavens had spread to here.

The result was that it was a bustling place, with galaxies full of life and civilization.

All of a sudden, the kelp plant sent out some divine will. “There’s a god prison here with a lot of ringsource!”

Xu Qing turned to look in that direction. Sir Star Ring and everyone else did the same, their eyes shining. They had not yet eaten their fill. They were still inclined to continue their travels.

Now that they could sense the god prison, their hearts stirred with anticipation, and some of them turned to look at Xu Qing. This went beyond their mission description.

Xu Qing pondered the situation.

“There’s a lot of ringsource there,” Sir Star Ring said. “And maybe even nine-colored ice.”

No one said anything, but their anticipation built.

Xu Qing thought about it. “It’s not a good idea to use the same excuse too many times.”

Everyone stood there silently.

Then Zhou Zhengli’s eyes glittered, and he quietly said, “Well... what if there was a prison break to deal with?”

2. I’m sure some of you will want to check back to chapters 965 and 465 to the ‘chair’ reference. I’m not saying it’s the same thing, but I’m sure some of you will want to check the wording. Note that in those chapters, I used the word ‘chair.’ I was very tempted to use ‘throne’ in those chapters, but did not, because ‘throne’ is a different set of characters.
