The Calm Holiness God Prison was in the Heavenless Zone in between the Aurora and Spiritlight heavens beyond heaven.

It looked like a statue of an enormous spider. The prison was inside the statue, while the outside had numerous palace structures. From afar, the palaces looked almost like nails, and they seemed to serve a sealing function. freewebnovel.com

The statue itself was pitch-black and as large as a planet. It was located inside of a dusty whirlpool of stars, and by means of its eight long, furry legs, it would slowly absorb the scattered ringsource that floated in the Heavenless Zone.

The prison had been located there for thousands of years at this point. It was originally constructed when seventeen imperial clans from different universes in the Spiritlight heaven beyond heaven pooled their resources. All seventeen of those clans still had controlling interests in the prison.

The gods inside had been collected by various means, from theft to purchase. In fact, many of the imprisoned gods were originally from the Aurora heaven beyond heaven. They were almost like trade goods that the Spiritlight clans had managed to get their hands on one way or another.

It had been constructed in the Heavenless Zone because of the unique characteristics of the prison. The gods inside of it had to be kept conscious to a certain degree. They couldn’t be put into deep states of sleep. As such, it was not possible to build the prison in one of the heavens beyond heaven, where there was strong immortal energy everywhere. Were the prison in an environment like that, the gods would have slipped into deep slumber.

The purpose of it all was to study the undying qualities of the gods. The results were then sent to the Spiritlight heaven beyond heaven, and were also recorded in reports in the Nineshores heaven beyond heaven.

This also meant that the two heavens beyond heaven had joint jurisdiction over the place. That was why construction had been authorized to begin with. Because two heavens beyond heaven had jurisdiction over it, and because of the special research going on there, the Department of Acquisitions had no authority there. In recent years, no Acquisitioners had been sent there on a mission. That resulted in the place being very peaceful and quiet.

The place was staffed by two wardens, as well as thousands of cultivators from the seventeen clans that had built the place.

At the moment, the sound of music and revelry drifted out of the biggest palace on the surface of the spider statue. Nonhuman servants were dancing and singing. There were even godslaves who had the blood of gods running in them, who were currently performing on very ancient musical instruments. There were also servants in chains serving fine, ringsource-infused alcohol.

There were a few dozen cultivators present, two of whom were human, and the rest of whom were nonhumans. All of them were having a wonderful time.

As for the two humans, one was an old man, the other was middle-aged. The former was from the Spiritlight heaven beyond heaven, while the latter was from the Nineshores heaven beyond heaven. They were the wardens of the prison, and they were currently toasting each other and chatting merrily.

“Day after day, year after year, the two of us really do have carefree lives, Daoist Brother.”

“There’s no end to the ringsource, we have servants attending to our every need, and we’re far, far away from the war. This place is like a paradise.”

“Hahaha! Living the quiet life. That’s really the way to live.”

They had been on duty here for about three hundred years, and things had been quiet and peaceful the entire time. They had benefited a lot, allowing them to reach the mid Quasi-Immortal level. In fact, they were very close to the late level.

“Unfortunately, all good things come to an end eventually. We only have one sixty-year-cycle left, and then our term in office will end. We’ll have to part then, and who knows when we’ll run into each other again.”

“Let’s not worry too much about the future. We might as well just enjoy ourselves in the moment.”

Laughing, they raised their drinking vessels in another toast. The surrounding nonhuman prison guards smiled and joined in on the toast. Everyone was about to drink when, all of a sudden, a wind swept in from outside, filling the hall. It instantly cooled the bustling atmosphere inside.

An ethereal nonhuman came in with the wind, eventually converging on a spot inside and transforming into a graceful female cultivator. Bowing, she said, “Exalted Wardens, we’ve detected the auras of roughly a hundred humans outside the prison. They’re getting closer as we speak. The guards on duty outside told them to stop, and even activated the prison’s defenses. But—”

All of a sudden, a deafening boom interrupted her. The defenses had been shattered. Next, a powerful aura swept in from the outside. The cultivators in the hall reacted with surprise. The two human Quasi-Immortals frowned, then suddenly blurred and disappeared. They reappeared a moment later outside. When they saw the clothing worn by the intruders, their expressions turned grim.

Numerous streaks of prismatic light were shooting toward the prison, pulsing with extraordinary auras. They moved with seemingly unstoppable momentum.

Eight individuals arrived with mountain-toppling, sea-draining force. They slammed down right in front of the two wardens, causing the statue to tremble. A blast of wind spread out in all directions, all while more streams of light arrived.

The nonhuman prison guards were arriving now as well, and they looked like they were ready to repel an invasion of enemies. Whether in terms of the number of people arriving or the level of their cultivation base, this was a shocking development. What was most noteworthy was that the arriving cultivators’ expressions were unperturbed and even cruel.

The one in the middle pulsed with a vile energy; he was the most terrifying of the group. The group immediately spread out into formation. It seemed clear that this group of cruel cultivators was a team of some sort, and they were waiting for something. It was the same with the fellow with the vile energy.

More beams of light were falling onto the statue, all in formation. When they had all arrived, one final stream of glittering light appeared, pulsing with an aura that seemed to be that of a Lower Immortal.

The nonhuman cultivators seemed astonished, and the two wardens were visibly taken aback. In the face of the mountain-toppling, sea-draining aura, they instinctively fell back a few paces.

“Lower Immortal?”

“No, it’s not.... But this aura....”

They struggled to control their breathing as the terrifying beam of light slammed into the ground.

It resolved into the form of a young man. He wore black clothes and had long, violet hair. As for his aura, it was terrifying and soul-shaking.

The entire prison was trembling. As the prison guards and the wardens trembled in fear, the cultivator who had arrived first, the one with the vile energy, stepped forward.

“I’m Sir Vilespirit,” he said in a raspy voice. “My exalted lord received a secret message indicating that a prison break is underway here. We came to get the situation under control.”

The prison guards grimaced. The two wardens looked fearfully at the cruel cultivators and the young man in black. However, they were still hesitating.

“As the Department of Acquisitions knows,” one of the wardens said, “this prison is under the joint jurisdiction of Nineshores and Spiritlight. There is no uprising at the moment.”

Standing next to Xu Qing was Zhou Zhengli, who smiled warmly. “I take it you’re one of the wardens, sir? Be at ease. We’re only here to inspect things. If there’s no uprising, we’ll just leave.”

The two wardens were about to start yelling angrily, but then they looked at Xu Qing and hesitated.

That was when Sir Star Ring stepped forward, bristling with a baleful aura. “We have a duty to perform. There’s no need to waste words. Everyone, follow me inside. Inspect everything thoroughly!”

Ignoring the prison guards, he led the way into the statue. A nod from Xu Qing was all it took to ensure that dozens of ascendees followed him.

The prison guards’ auras were in chaos. As for the wardens, they gritted their teeth and prepared to take action.

That was when Zhou Zhengli cleared his throat softly. Just as had been planned, the ascendees either unleashed unique energy fluctuations, took out identity medallions, or made loud exclamations.

“Our Master is the Lower Immortal known as Blue Mallard!”

“The director of the Department of Acquisitions is our teacher! Some people call him Poison Monarch!”

“Our bloodline goes right back to Old Man Talisman Sage!”

“I have an agreement with the Chen Clan to serve as a dao seed!”

“I was made a disciple of the Human Immortal Sect!”

“I’m in a dao contract with the Divergent Mountain Heaven!”

Many voices and numerous beams of light from identity medallions shook the starry sky. The warden’s faces fell.

In any system that exists over many years, a framework will come to exist that contains multiple branches of support. Unless someone in that system has heaven-defying strength, they would have no choice but to obey the rules of the framework. And it would be almost impossible for them to affect the branches. After all, the branches of the framework would be outstanding and powerful. What was more, after the passage of dozens or even hundreds of generations, those branches would become inherent parts of the system and its rules.

In the Fifth Star Ring, the eleven heavens beyond heaven were the eleven strongest branches. Within those heavens beyond heaven were numerous powerful organizations that both protected their own home and benefited from it. They could also be considered branches. And they were like gigantic vortexes that exerted powerful gravitational forces that affected all of the living beings in the Fifth Star Ring.

Given that, why would any cultivator want to trifle with them?

After Zhou Zhengli cleared his throat and the ascendees spoke, their words became like incisive divine abilities and daoist magics that struck the prison guards deep in their hearts. They were like boulders tossed into the sea! Every word left the listeners shaken to the core. Combined with the light of the identity medallions, it caused the nonhuman guards to feel like they were being struck with repeated tidal waves of shock.

Such backgrounds. Such affiliations.... Even the two wardens started to feel completely powerless.

This group was made of a host of silkpants! And in terms of cultivation base and talent, they obviously surpassed ordinary silkpants.

People like this had to be ascendees from the Immortal Capital! Although there were only a few orthodox sects in the Immortal Capital, the reality was that the entire place was like a tangle of dragons and snakes, in other words, a hodgepodge of good people and scumbags. It was essentially a breeding ground for all the heavens beyond heaven, a place that was a mix of darkness and light.

Someone might go unnoticed there for a long time, but after they reached their potential and left the Immortal Capital, they would quickly attract attention and be recruited.

The two wardens were fully aware of how that worked. Yet they were still puzzled by something.... Ascendees were normally split up. They were never grouped together into one squadron. Yet right now... the two wardens felt completely powerless in the face of these people. The wardens couldn’t compare to them in battle prowess. And these people had backgrounds that weren’t even necessary to mention.

And they’re actually Acquisitioners....

Both wardens felt deep bitterness.

Sir Star Ring was leading a few dozen ascendees right into the prison inside the statue. The mission was already underway. Sir Vilespirit, Yuanshan Su, Hordeslayer, and Rampart split up. Some went in on their own, others led some ascendees with them. Li Mengtu went inside as well. They went to different areas to divide up the work.

Soon, only a dozen or so people were left outside. Xu Qing didn’t need to do anything. After some thought, Zhou Zhengli decided to stay with him.

The kelp plant... did not go into the prison. It circled around the statue and took over the defenses. It also unleashed its majesty and used its divine will to help the ascendees with their search.

As the prison guards and the wardens watched the buzz of activity, they got the feeling this wasn’t the first time this squadron had done something like this. And that was true. After working together in the Helioterra Universe, they had learned to work in smooth coordination.

As everyone entered the prison, Xu Qing sat down cross-legged to work on his cultivation base and think about what to do next. He knew that their actions were going to cause some sort of backlash, and that he would be held accountable. He could think of different ways to deal with that, but the simplest was to find the nine-colored ice.

That said, considering everyone called on their backgrounds, I won’t be held solely accountable. Everyone made the decision together.

***

Time passed, slowly but surely.

Zhou Zhengli also sat down to meditate. As for the ascendees who had remained outside, they settled down cross-legged, but didn’t close their eyes. Instead, they kept watch over the prison entrance. They obviously wanted to go inside as well. However, according to the plan, there needed to be a watch outside at all times. Thus, duties had been split between everyone.

As the wardens and guards looked on grimly, someone suddenly flew out of the entrance. It wasn’t one of Xu Qing’s squadron. It was a nonhuman guard.

Kneeling in front of the two wardens, he said, “Exalted ones, they... they went inside and actually did start searching for something. But after noticing the imprisoned gods... they started interrogating them! And in the course of the interrogations, they started extracting ringsource. There are already a few dozen gods who have been completely drained of ringsource! If this continues....”

The guard hesitated.

Meanwhile, the two wardens scowled and looked over at Xu Qing.

One of them said, “Fellow Daoist, this is a private prison run by seventeen clans from the Spiritlight heaven beyond heaven. Given that we fall under the jurisdiction of two heavens beyond heaven, any theft here will be thoroughly investigated!

“We have been on duty here for years now, and we know the place like the backs of our hands. There’s definitely no uprising going on. You’re just using that as an excuse to take ringsource! This is both outrageous and amateurish!”

Xu Qing said nothing. Zhou Zhengli was the one who had come up with this idea. The ascendees who had remained on the outside weren’t thin-skinned. They had come here for ringsource, and thus, their expressions didn’t waver.

Zhou Zhengli, meanwhile, looked very solemn as he nodded and said, “That makes a lot of sense, exalted ones. My fellow squadron members are acting a bit boorishly. I’ll see what I can do. Fellow Daoists, can you please head inside to oversee things?”

The ascendees who had been waiting outside got to their feet with somber expressions on their faces.

“I was just going to suggest that!”

“They’re acting completely out of line!”

“We’ll go in and get things under control!”

The ascendees flew at top speed into the entrance.

The two wardens could see that something fishy was going on. Inside, they were more furious than ever, but they knew their battle prowess was insufficient to do anything. Then they exchanged a glance, and each could see the determination in the eyes of the other. They quickly had a conversation via divine will.

“These people are far too presumptuous! This matter must be reported up the chain of command!”

“The Department of Acquisitions offends people all the time. But this is pushing things too far!”

“You and the seventeen monarchs should report this to the Spiritlight Immortal Palace. I’ll gather everyone else and report it to the Nineshores Immortal Palace. These people might have impressive backing, but actions like these will definitely be punished!”

The two wardens immediately took out jade slips and started filling them with information.

Meanwhile, the Acquisitioners continued their work. Inside the prison, more and more ringsource was being gathered, and the prison guards couldn’t do anything to stop it from happening. After all, the spell formations in the prison were designed to work against gods. They didn’t work against cultivators, and especially not against human cultivators.

At the moment, in an area in the depths of the prison that hadn’t been discovered by Sir Star Ring and the others, there was dense mutagen isolated in an area surrounded by glittering god talismans. If one looked at that area, they would see only a sea of fog.

Astonishingly, there was an altar in the depths of the fog. It was constructed from the bones of gods, and there were four figures seated cross-legged around it. Thēy had gruish bodies, undulating tentacles, and emitted the fluctuations of gods. The four gods were using godly authority to communicate with godly voices.

“Our secret plan has been kept under wraps by those inferior species for a long time now....”

“His Majesty even implanted the two human Quasi-Immortals with his will, ensuring that they have no idea what’s going on.”

“In that case... how did anyone find out the truth??”

“It doesn’t seem like the intruding humans have sensed us. Nor do they seem suspicious.”

“They haven’t found us, but at the same time, they’re coming deeper and deeper.”

“That’s true. My divine will indicates that they’ve already started interrogating many of my people, and have drained them of their essence.”

“If things continue like this, they’ll inevitably find us!”

“Therefore, instead of sitting around waiting to be discovered... why don’t we beat them to the punch?”

The four gods sat there silently for a short time.

“His Majesty hasn’t returned. All we’ve done is issue the call. We’re not ready yet either. If we take action now, before His Majesty is back, then we’ll be in a position of weakness.”

“But if we don’t act soon, then any chance for return will be lost.”

“We’ve been preparing for years now.... Where did things go wrong? How could we have been noticed?”

The four gods again fell into silence. This sudden inspection had caught thēm completely by surprise. What was more, thēy could hear the increasingly chaotic sound of the humans interrogating the prisoners, and it caused thēir hearts to pound.

If thēy just had a bit more time to carry out thēir plan, thēy would succeed without a doubt. Not only would thēir lord and master return, but also thēy could use that momentum as a way to get out of the Fifth Star Ring. But now....

“There’s no point in sitting around thinking. I agree that we should take action now!”

“I second the motion!”

Golden light flared off the four gods as thēy joined thēir godly voices together in agreement. And then thēy reached out toward the altar. The altar rumbled loudly and let off a terrifying pressure. A golden tempest then swept from the altar up into the prison above.

Somewhere in the middle section of the prison, Sir Star Ring and the others were collecting ringsource from a god who was just on the verge of being squeezed dry.

That was when a deafening sound filled the prison, and then mutagen erupted everywhere. The entire prison suddenly went dark. Howls echoed out everywhere. The gods were rioting!

Sir Star Ring realized immediately what was happening. He was initially stunned, but then his expression turned grave as he cast his senses out. He immediately noticed the rising pillar of golden light. He also detected the aura of awakening!

They’re actually rioting? Sir Star Ring almost couldn’t believe it. But he knew it was a serious situation, so he immediately sent someone to report the matter to Xu Qing.

***

An incense stick of time passed.

Atop the statue, the two wardens were in the middle of preparing jade slips to send to their respective heavens beyond heaven, to request that Xu Qing and the others be punished.

Xu Qing sat there cross-legged with his eyes closed. Suddenly, his eyes opened, and he looked down suspiciously.

At almost the exact same instant, two people flew out of the entrance. One was a prison guard, the other was an ascendee. They both seemed similarly anxious as they flew to their respective camps and made reports.

“Exalted one, there actually is a prison break going on!”

Upon hearing that, Xu Qing turned to look at Zhou Zhengli. Zhou Zhengli was visibly surprised.

The furious guards who were waiting outside were similarly stunned. As for the wardens, their minds were reeling as if they had been struck by lightning. Instead of preparing jade slips, they just stood there, sweat dripping down their faces and their hearts full of incredulity.

There really was a prison break! Before anyone could react, the ground trembled as golden pillars of light shot up. Mutagen began to build up everywhere.

The two wardens instinctively looked toward Xu Qing, and by now, the dissatisfaction and anger in their hearts was almost completely gone. They knew full well how serious a prison break was.

“Exalted one!” they said urgently. They were still suspicious of why Xu Qing had shown up, but given the gravity of the situation, that didn’t matter. What mattered was stopping the prison break!

Xu Qing slowly rose to his feet. His cultivation base erupted, causing terrifying pressure to weigh down on the statue and dispel the light and mutagen. The statue rumbled. Then Xu Qing spoke in a grim voice.

“We’re taking control of this prison. Zhou Zhengli, send orders down the chain of command. Tell everyone... to immediately crush this god riot!”

The spider statue that held the god prison was shaking violently. A total of thirty-three golden pillars of light had shot up from within it, bringing with them intense mutagen and the pressure of the gods. This was the Heavenless Zone, where there was no immortal energy. As such, there was nothing to stop the mutagen from spreading rapidly. At the same time, godly fluctuations began to spread from inside the statue. Everything was devolving into chaos.

Xu Qing’s expression was calm, and his voice was as cold as a winter wind blowing from the Nine Serenities underworld. It filled the god prison and echoed in the starry sky, instantly calming the hearts of the prison guards and the wardens.

The wardens didn’t care what Xu Qing had been up to. Right now, his calm demeanor filled them with hope. Without any hesitation, they strode forth, bowed to Xu Qing, and handed over their jade slips, which gave them authority over the prison. They were obviously fine with him taking over.

Xu Qing wasn’t one to waste words. He took the jade slips, then took control of the prison, activating all of the spell formations and sealing marks inside. Then he looked at the wardens.

“Is there a True God imprisoned here?” he asked them.

Before the sudden development, they wouldn’t have given him an answer. But now they didn’t hesitate to offer a full explanation.

“There’s a desiccated corpse that’s being purified....”

“It’s the statue’s true form....”

Xu Qing’s gaze sharpened as he looked at the statue. The statue had attracted his attention when they arrived, and having heard what the wardens just said, he changed his mind about going inside. He immediately issued new orders.

“The two of you go report this matter to the heavens beyond heaven. Position guards at all the exits. Don’t let any gods out!

“Kelp plant, you suppress that god light. Send your roots into the prison to help them keep the gods under control. And have your true form contain the statue. You’re our second line of defense.

“Zhou Zhengli, you go into the prison. Have all the fellow daoists in there get the gods under control and also find out what started the rebellion. You should all be fine as long as you don’t run into a True God.

“Now, as for this True God statue....” Xu Qing’s eyes glittered with cold light. “I’ll deal with it!”

“Yes, sir,” Zhou Zhengli said, and he flew into the prison to relay the orders and get to work. He had his ways of dealing with gods.

Xu Qing paid him no further heed. Given what Zhou Zhengli was capable of, he was confident that he would do a good job.

The two wardens were also following through with Xu Qing’s orders. One of them was reporting the matter, while the other was sending the guards to positions by the exits.

The kelp plant appeared in the air, and its twelve leaves grew huge as it covered over the prison and blocked the golden light, sealing it. Its massive true form appeared in the starry sky, and it wrapped around the statue, all while sending roots down, some to block the golden light, and some into the interior of the prison.

Everyone had their assignments, and they were following through in an orderly fashion. And thus, time passed.

The surface levels of the prison were being methodically put under control by Zhou Zhengli.

That said, things didn’t go perfectly smoothly. For instance, right now, the howling of the gods rippled through the previously quiet prison. The howling came over and over again, and it stirred the ringsource and caused godly authority to converge. The riot in the prison had reached a critical point.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered as he rose up into the dome of heaven, settled cross-legged, and then looked down at the statue of the god. Circulating his cultivation base, he unleashed his Quasi-Immortal power.

Terrifying might spread out. The void rippled, everything blurred, natural laws transformed, and space-time was affected. Then, in response to his thoughts, his immortal embryo appeared externally.

It started out only a few meters tall, but it rapidly grew larger, until it seemed to fill heaven and earth. It was just as large as the statue, and it emanated a holy sensation. In its core, dazzling light stirred, bolstering the immortal embryo, and making its immortal might even more weighty.

Within that dazzling light at its core was an immortal palace! It seemed extremely ancient, but boundlessly paramount. And it was connected... to a heaven beyond heaven! It was the Aurora Immortal Palace!

The arrival of the immortal palace made Xu Qing’s immortal embryo even more majestic. It was no longer illusory, but almost completely true and real. And the aura it emitted could topple mountains and drain seas. It descended toward the prison statue.

Cracking sounds rang out from the prison as the mutagen it was emitting was suppressed. It couldn’t spread out at all. The howling of the gods was wiped away.

At the same time, Xu Qing’s might filled the statue, spreading through the entire prison, going from the top to the bottom, level by level.

However, Xu Qing had only just taken action when his eyes started shining. His immortal embryo’s hand lifted and went into an incantation gesture. Powerful streams of ringsource converged as the immortal embryo rapidly grew stronger. An iron skewer appeared next to Xu Qing, thrumming as it powered up. It emanated a sense of sharpness that seemed capable of piercing anything and everything. The canon of parallelism erupted, causing innumerable space-times to overlap around Xu Qing. All of it could be referred to as supernatural phenomena.

And anyone who looked up at the scene would feel like they were observing the many heavens. In fact, the space-times all had enormous versions of Xu Qing’s immortal embryo in them, so that it looked like innumerable immortal spirits descending from the many heavens. It was only natural that there was also terrifying pressure weighing down.

The guards posted at the exits, and the two wardens, were shaken to the core. The former were trembling from head to toe. They were nonhumans who had been conquered by humankind, and the aura Xu Qing was emitting right now made them feel like they were looking at an immortal.

The two wardens struggled to control their breathing, as the sensation they were experiencing was far more profound. It felt to them exactly like being in the presence of a Lower Immortal.

He’s not a Lower Immortal, but that majesty is so close to that level....

Both of them were sighing inwardly with reverence. From what they could see, Xu Qing and his squadron would have no trouble suppressing this rebellion by acting both inside and from without.

They were right. The gods in the prisons had all been locked up, and despite their attempt to rebel, they hadn’t really been prepared. Their haphazard attempt had fallen short in many respects. Before long, the godly aura shrank down, and things started to get quiet.

However, Xu Qing did not relax. In contrast, his gaze grew sharper, and he continued to gather energy. The reason was that he could sense there was a deeply hidden aura of awakening in the statue. It was not his first time sensing something like this.

Back in the outer sea of the Revered Ancient mainland, Eldest Brother and I worked with Yu Liuchen as bait, all to help hīm on a fishing expedition.... Specifically, hē was fishing for a returning True God! What I’m sensing now feels just like that![1]

Even as that thought occurred to Xu Qing, the statue that made up the god prison started trembling, and a seemingly unstoppable force erupted from inside. Beams of golden light shot out of the statue, and the kelp’s leaves couldn’t contain them all. The aura of a god began to rise high. They became like pillars of mutagen.

Chanting sounds drifted out of the statue, and they could distort the mind. Everyone who heard them reacted with shock. The ground started shaking, and then figures began shooting out of the various exits. They were the ascendees, including Sir Star Ring, Sir Vilespirit, Li Mengtu, Yuanshan Su, Hordeslayer, and Rampart. All had serious expressions on their faces, and all were wounded to varying degrees.

Zhou Zhengli was in the lead. “Milord! We got most of the rioting gods under control. But thēy had started a ceremony that can’t be reversed. Thēy’re trying to wake up a True God!’

Even as Zhou Zhengli’s words rang out, the spider statue shivered and then released a deafening rumbling sound. Deep cracks spread out over its surface, and then the previously closed spider eyes seemed like they would open. A tugging force appeared out of nowhere, which turned into a true name. That true name became part of the chant, and soon it became obvious that a specific name was being called out!

“Bimo Si!”[2]

“Bimo Si!!”

“Bimo Si!!!”

True Gods were undying. As long as the name of a True God existed and was remembered, then even if that god perished, thēy could return. And right now, a True God that the cultivators of the Fifth Star Ring had suppressed... was returning!

As the spider statue continued to crack, the cultivators flew off it, their expressions flickering dramatically.

Xu Qing looked very serious. He was thinking back to what happened with Yu Liuchen....

Meanwhile, outside of the prison, in the dusty void of the whirlpool of stars that surrounded it, everything was rumbling. The Heavenless Zone rippled and distorted as mutagen sizzled. And then a cold voice rang out that all of the cultivators present could hear.

“I am Bimo Si....”

The minds and hearts of the cultivators were thrown into chaos by the polluting sound of the voice. Many began to bleed from their eyes, ears, nose, and mouth. Their flesh seemed like it wanted to peel off their bodies, and countless random thoughts in their minds began to converge into one singular thought. That was the might of a True God!

Yet before the True God could finish speaking, Xu Qing’s eyes filled with battle spirit.

Years ago, Yu Liuchen, who was a mere Altar God, conspired against a True God.... If hē could do that, then considering my current battle prowess... then maybe I can deal with an extremely weak True God who’s in the middle of returning!

Killing intent grew strong in his eyes. He shoved his hand out! His immortal embryo glittered. The iron skewer shone brightly. Overlapping space-time went wild. He had powered up and was now going all out!

1. Xu Qing and Erniu went with Yu Liuchen to the outer sea starting in chapter 998. ☜

2. Bimo Si: This is a strange name invented by the author. It’s possible the author intended for it to be something akin to a daoist name or martial nickname, but on a gut level, it seems to me to be a proper name. Normally speaking, Bi is a surname, so the name could be Bi Mosi. However, the combination of the first two characters Bimo has a meaning in Chinese culture. It’s the name of a shamanistic folk religion and also the name of the shamans who perform the rituals and rites of that religion. Because of that, I’m going to isolate Bimo as the surname. I don’t think it’s supposed to have any connection to the actual religion. It seems to me sort of like using “Voodoo” in the name of some fantasy character simply because it sounds cool. Si has many meanings, none of which seem important here, so I’m not even going to list them. ☜

Meanwhile, inside the Heavenless Zone, as the god prison trembled, and the aura of a god proliferated... numerous streams of immortal will were converging in the starry sky from all directions, and none but immortals could sense them. They were patrolling immortals from the Nineshores and Spiritlight heavens beyond heaven! They had sensed the disturbance, and had come to reestablish order.

However, the moment their immortal wills took shape... a calm voice spoke to them.

“Let him try. And let those of this generation experience what a True God is like.”

The streams of immortal will replied in a shaky voice.

“We shall follow the Nineshores Immortal Decree.”

***

Thanks to the godly aura, the Heavenless Zone was shaking violently.

Everyone was backing away from the prison and putting up their defenses, including the two wardens, Sir Star Ring, and everyone else. It was the same with the kelp plant. They knew full well that they weren’t facing an ordinary god right now. This was... a returning True God!

True Gods were equivalent to Lower Immortals! In fact, in their gruish nature, they were more astonishing than Lower Immortals! After all, the gods were the former rulers of this higher star ring, and as a result, they could naturally absorb ringsource. That meant that they were much better adapted to exist in higher star rings than cultivators! Furthermore, they were eternally indestructible. Thus, when cultivators faced a True God, it was only natural that they would experience incredible pressure weighing down on them.

Everyone present knew that, taking in the Fifth Star Ring as a whole, the return of one True God wasn’t very consequential. It wouldn’t take much effort in the grand scheme of things to deal with such a True God. In fact, the Immortal Lords wouldn’t even need to take action. They could just issue a decree to have Lower Immortals deal with the situation.

But... to personally witness the awakening of such a god, and directly feel the terrifying aura that came along with it, was still a monumental thing.

The terrifying fluctuations distorted the soul, and caused everyone present to tremble to the core of their being. Everyone was backing away as quickly as possible.

With the exception of Xu Qing! In fact, he wasn’t just refusing to back down. Instead, his battle prowess was raging, and his cold eyes were fixed directly on the statue of the spider....

He lifted his hand, and his energy erupted. The iron skewer had been powering up, and now it glittered brightly. At the same time, all of the layers of space-time around him thrummed, and the immortal embryo behind him shone dazzlingly. He was going to try to slaughter a god!

Even as he took action, the huge spider statue shook violently! The will of awakening was exploding! Golden light shone off the eight limbs as the spider statue started moving.

Golden light was the hallmark of the gods, and as it shone, the spider placed its legs in front of it like a shield. It was a shimmering screen of gold! Behind that shield, and behind the spider legs, the statue’s eyes opened. They emanated cold apathy, and even stronger golden light, which spread through the starry sky like a sea.

The godly aura grew stronger. The chanting grew louder.

The name Bimo Si became deafening. Hē was quickly returning!

At the same time, Xu Qing dropped his hand down.

The iron skewer shot forth, piercing through the starry sky, its immortal light shimmering, all while unleashing terrifying fluctuations. This was a weapon that had been created by a Lower Immortal, and it brimmed with Xu Qing’s Quasi-Immortal power! The attack also included his canon! And it was backed by the might of the Aurora Immortal Palace and the associated heaven beyond heaven! Furthermore, it contained heaven’s principle!

Whether in terms of the materials it was constructed with or the power that filled it, the iron skewer was a superior product. Where it passed, the void shattered, and the starry sky filled with a succession of black holes. It was so sharp that it could conquer every obstacle!

In short order, it appeared right in front of the golden screen protecting the spider. It stabbed into it! An intense rumbling sound spread out!

But... it wasn’t able to pierce all the way through. It was blocked by the golden light. The statue was the desiccated corpse of a True God, and was essentially a carrier. This True God was not asleep any longer, but was in the process of returning. As such, it was no surprise that the golden shield hē generated was terrifying. In fact, not only did the iron skewer fail to pierce through the golden light, but actually, the golden light seemed like it wanted to devour it.

However, that was when a bell tolled.

As Xu Qing began moving forward, he took out a bell that contained a scrap of will from a God Lord. Its tolling caused the starry sky to shake. Cultivators and gods could both be affected by the sound of that bell. To varying degrees, their internal functions all slowed down.

It also affected the golden light! It suddenly seemed to stagnate.

The might of the iron skewer intensified, and it pushed forward with mountain-toppling, sea-draining force, and a will of destruction. Pushing all the way through the golden light, it shot toward the forehead of the statue.

It moved with incredibly explosive speed and stabbed into the forehead! The spider statue trembled....

The cultivators off in the distance watched, their minds and hearts trembling, as cracks appeared on the spider statue.

And then... it exploded violently.

That said, nobody relaxed. After the statue exploded, the aura of a god didn’t disappear. The sensation of a return was still present, and the chanting still echoed in the area. It was as if what had exploded was only the surface-level veneer of the returning True God.

A terrifying power suddenly arrived from the void. As it passed, the starry sky trembled, and all living beings writhed. It was the power of a god! It was pure power, like a starry sea, something that surpassed heavenly might. As it swept along, the godly chanting grew louder, and then... the entire region began to fold like a piece of paper.

However, the senses of the cultivators told them that the folding wasn’t taking place in this starry sky. It was as if space in this area had two different levels.

The first level was where all the living beings existed, while the second level contained only the crumbled statue. What was folding was in that separate, higher level! In other words, it didn’t affect any of the living beings present, only the rubble of the statue. It didn’t involve a single fold. In the shortest of moments, there were innumerable folds.

Then the rubble of the statue disappeared. The godly aura from moments ago, along with the power of return and the chanting, all disappeared. The folds went away.

It was as if nothing had just happened. The starry sky went calm. Everyone looked around in shock. It was too gruish, to the point where everyone had to wonder whether or not a Lower Immortal had suddenly arrived and put an end to the return of the True God.

But it didn’t take long before people realized that something else was happening.

No, that’s not it. The god. Īts fleeing!

Considering that Xu Qing was in the thick of things, he realized it before everyone else. Almost as soon as the folding began, the layers of space from his canon of parallelism began to descend. Using space-time canon and the power of overlapping universes, he suppressed everything in the area.

As a result, time went backward in this part of the starry sky, and then... all of the Xu Qings in the various space-times performed incantation gestures and tapped into their canon.

Things were... reversing! The folds were unfolding! However many folds had occurred, that many unfoldings were occurring!

To the sense of the onlookers, it was as if everything was flowing backward. The godly aura that had disappeared came back. It was once again possible to hear the godly chanting.

The power of return came back! The rubble of the statue... was visible again!

However, its appearance had changed. It was no longer the same substance the statue had been made of. Instead, the rubble took the shape of numerous white balls. They looked like flesh with white fur on it. However, the fur was so long that it was more like white hair, and as the hair swayed, it almost looked like tentacles spreading out.

All pieces of the rubble were like that. Each ball of hair emanated a soul-piercing sensation that inflicted bitter pain onto all non-gods.

Xu Qing’s face was pale as even his soul was affected. But then his immortal embryo stepped forward, enveloping him. And it grew even larger as it reached out with its hand. That hand was like an entire starry sky!

An immense buildup of power existed in that hand as it slammed down! It was a vicious slap!

Inside the immortal embryo, the foundational Aurora Immortal Palace glittered brightly. The light it emanated filled the entire immortal embryo, making it incomparably holy. The immortal embryo’s hand was similarly majestic.

As the hand slapped down, it filled the void and blocked everything. All of the remnants of the statue with the floating white hair suddenly stopped in place.

This was not just the hand of an immortal embryo, this was the crushing power of the Aurora Immortal Palace!

The hand fell.

That was when strange things happened. The various streams of hair swaying around the statue rubble suddenly stretched out and connected to each other.

A huge spider web formed in the middle of the starry sky, right beneath the hand of Xu Qing’s immortal embryo. The spider web was astonishing. It filled the starry sky, and was made of white hair!

Every point of intersection was a piece of rubble from the statue. Except, the rubble had changed. Now, each piece was a severed head with an anguished expression on it! They were the heads of men and women, old and young, cultivators and gods. They were all of the victims slaughtered by this True God. All living beings hē had cut down had been unable to flee in soul form. Hē had come to control them for all eternity, as they had become part of hīm!

And now they had emerged to block the hand of Xu Qing’s immortal embryo.

When the two made contact, there was no rumbling boom. Instead, there was a sensation of resonance that swept through the starry sky like a tempest. Where the tempest passed, planets crumbled, and asteroids were rendered into dust.

There was also a powerful backlash. As a result, the hand of Xu Qing’s immortal embryo was pushed back, and it even looked like it might collapse.

All of the onlookers seemed astonished.

Blood sprayed out of Xu Qing’s mouth, and his gaze became razor-sharp. In his view, the gruish and majestic spider web was almost completely golden! And he could tell that when it was indeed completely golden, the return would be complete.

I’ve already unleashed my strongest level of power, but I still can’t stop this thing from returning. And this is a weakened True God....

Xu Qing looked on silently. He was aware that Yu Liuchen had been dealing with a True God that hadn’t actually returned. Clearly, this situation right now was very different. He knew full well that even if he gave up right now, it wouldn’t change anything.

Even if this True God really did come back, it wouldn’t be some major event in the Fifth Star Ring. It seemed entirely likely that Lower Immortals had already been dispatched to deal with the situation. In fact, he got the feeling there were already Lower Immortals in the vicinity!

However, the fact that they hadn’t taken action yet.... Well, it meant he might be able to get some more ringsource! If he could suppress this True God in the process of returning, then he could continue to extract ringsource. Maybe he could even build up a big stockpile for future use.

Having reached the conclusion that this was definitely the best idea, Xu Qing’s eyes glittered.

I still have something to try!

He released the full power of his ringsource. Immortal energy surged, bolstering his immortal embryo, and causing the rebuffed hand to grow stronger and bigger. Tapping into the power of his authority, he catalyzed the Aurora Immortal Palace. It filled the immortal embryo, causing the hand in the starry sky to reach ten times its previous size. It was astonishingly majestic. Once again, it descended!

This time, it was not a slap. The five fingers were splayed, like columns in the starry sky. And the hand reached out to grab the spider web!

The moment the hand touched the spider web, blood sprayed out of Xu Qing’s mouth from the backlash. The hand seemed like it might collapse at any moment, and the effect actually spread to the entire immortal embryo.

Yet there was a crazy look in Xu Qing’s eyes. His immortal embryo was in chaos, but it was still being powered by the Aurora Immortal Palace. Immortal light shone dazzlingly from the palace, becoming a sea of brightness that stabilized all the weakened parts and cast brilliance into the surrounding starry sky.

Xu Qing was fully tapping into the power of the Aurora heaven beyond heaven. It turned into... an unprecedented long-range teleportation! And the range encompassed the entire surrounding galaxy!

Astonishingly, he was turning this place into a battlefield on which to battle the True God! He was taking the carrier body of the True God and teleporting it into his own heaven beyond heaven. Once there, he could use the entire might of the heaven beyond heaven to suppress the returning True God!

The power of teleportation surged. Deafening rumbling sounds echoed out, covering everything. And then Xu Qing, the immortal embryo, the hand, and the spider web all disappeared!

***

Meanwhile, in the Heavenless Zone, the immortal wills that could be detected by only immortals, were all shaken. Then they shifted their focus to look at... what had once been the Aurora heaven beyond heaven!

***

In the Nineshores heaven beyond heaven, in the very middle of the Nineshores Immortal Palace, amidst countless structures, was the Nineshores Immortal Tower, which rose high above all else. Standing there was an incredibly majestic figure. He wore a robe of blue and had his hands clasped behind his back as he looked off into the distance.

“Bimo Si was known far and wide in the Fifth Star Ring as the god of pain, with godly authority that could inflict extreme pain on all souls and convert it into personal power. The Immortal Paragon once said that this god’s illusion was only partly false. Some of it contained truth! Well, Xu Qing. I’ve given you an opportunity. Will you seize it and turn it into good fortune?”

In the past, it was the Aurora heaven beyond heaven. Now it was the Green Heaven!

Within it were numerous majestic universes, one starry sky after another, and countless planets. They had originally emanated bright, dazzling starlight. But then, in an instant, the entire heaven beyond heaven, including innumerable planets, all went dark. It was as if the light had been sucked away.

In the middle of the seemingly never-ending heaven beyond heaven, in a location that most low-level cultivators could never reach in a lifetime, was a massive black hole. That black hole had come into being out of nowhere!

Above the black hole was a vast, ever-expanding spider web! It was made of white spider silk, and the nodes where the silk connected continued to expand outward, along with the roiling aura of a True God.

At the same time, as that godly aura spread, all the heads in the spider web were calling out the same thing.

“Bimo Si!”

“Bimo Si!”

“Bimo Si!”

Sound was inherently shapeless. But the spider web had bestowed it with the will of a god, causing it to become strands of godly authority that converged in the middle of the web.

A figure was being revealed there! It was half person, half spider! At the moment, about seventy percent of the body of the figure was the color gold!

The chanting grew increasingly intense, causing the returning aura to strengthen. The might of a True God was flooding this starry sky.

Xu Qing’s immortal embryo towered over the spider web, its face awe-inspiring and its eyes glinting coldly. Astonishingly, its right hand contained a massive immortal palace that shone with dazzling immortal light. In the form of the immortal embryo, Xu Qing’s gaze focused on the figure forming in the middle of the spider web.

His hand fell. The immortal palace rumbled.

The black hole was beneath the spider web, and the hand was above it. The attack came from above and below, and the entire heaven beyond heaven stirred. The web would be crushed!

The half-person half-spider figure suddenly looked up, and the gaze of the spider met Xu Qing’s gaze. It was a connection of gazes but also a clash of souls and a convergence of ringsource.

The moment the connection occurred... Xu Qing’s vision flashed with light.

Things went back to normal an instant later. Nothing had changed. The immortal palace was still there, descending to crush the spider web.

The half-person half-spider figure struggled, but hē had not yet fully returned, and was not strong enough to fight back against the weight of an entire heaven beyond heaven. But in hīs defiance, hē fought back with godly authority and godly might.

Xu Qing trembled. Blood sprayed out of his mouth. His fleshly body and soul began to rip apart. But ultimately... he was unleashing what his foundation was capable of, by using the power of a heaven beyond heaven.

He was paying a huge price, but the result was success. Deafening rumbling sounds echoed out as the half-person half-spider figure was shoved down into the black hole.

It was over. That was when exhaustion flooded into Xu Qing. He quickly sat down cross-legged atop the black hole that contained the suppressed god, and absorbed the ringsource flowing out. It nourished him, and at the same time enabled his immortal embryo to grow further.

He forgot about the passage of time. He forgot about his Acquisitioner mission. He focused fully on cultivation.

The benefits were astounding. His cultivation base rose from early Quasi-Immortal, higher and higher. In almost an instant... ten years passed.

When Xu Qing opened his eyes, his cultivation base had reached the great circle of Quasi-Immortal. He felt like he was at the peak. It was like omnipotence. And as a result, when he opened his eyes, they were initially blank.

He quickly recovered. Upon realizing that ten years had passed, he remembered about his Acquisitioner duties. After all, to cultivators like Xu Qing, ten years of cultivation didn’t count for much.

I still have time. Next up, I need to arrange to get back to Revered Ancient!

Having reached this point in his train of thought, Xu Qing’s eyes glittered with determination. He stepped out of the heaven beyond heaven, and when he appeared outside, he was in the Heavenless Zone where the spider statue had been.

The statue had disappeared. The prison was no longer there. The wardens and prison guards were long gone.

However, Sir Star Ring and the others had not left. They were waiting there. Upon seeing Xu Qing, their expressions flickered.

They left together. Upon returning to the Department of Acquisitions, they handed in their mission. After that, they were given a host of additional missions. As a result, their squadron became well-known throughout the Nineshores heaven beyond heaven.

Before long, they were transferred to the front lines of the war. Their squadron quickly began to perform meritorious services on the battlefield between the Fourth and Fifth Star Rings. They even captured a goddess. That goddess was the daughter and only child of a God Lord![1]

Because of all the services rendered, Xu Qing’s prestige skyrocketed. What was more, word spread that the Aurora heaven beyond heaven now belonged to him. It took no time at all for Xu Qing’s name to ring in the ears of countless cultivators. freewebnovel.com

Although it seemed like time was passing slowly, to Xu Qing, it was speeding by. Eventually, he got a mission that led to an encounter with a God Lord from the Fourth Star Ring! Although he was capable of fighting Lower Immortals, he couldn’t possibly win a fight like that. The other cultivators in his squadron all died. He was seriously injured to the point where he nearly died. He fled into space-time, but was chased. Eventually, he chose to enter the chaotic sea of space-time. Within that boundless chaos, he disappeared.[2]

Although he managed to escape death, he suffered grievous injuries in the chaotic sea of space-time. He lost consciousness and then drifted through the chaos into the depths of space-time. He had no idea how much time passed before he woke up.

It took a lot of struggle, and some luck as well, but after experiencing countless setbacks, he managed to free himself. He eventually got back to the point where he had left. He emerged into the world.

Upon returning, he found that the war still raged. But then... a terrifying truth became evident when he returned to the camp. It was a truth that caused him to tremble with disbelief.

He found that from the time he had gone missing until now... a thousand years had passed! That truth filled him with extreme anxiety, perhaps even dread. He immediately left the battlefield and used the means he had at hand to leave the Fifth Star Ring and return to Revered Ancient. He didn’t dare to wonder what Revered Ancient would look like. A thousand years had passed.... He had missed out on a thousand years.

Soon, he hovered in the dome of heaven above Revered Ancient.

His face fell.

Revered Ancient looked very different compared to how he had left it. Gods were everywhere. Humans were extinct. Empress Summer Departure was nowhere to be seen.

He went to his former haunts in the lands of humans. He went to the entrance to Brilliant Heaven, only to find... that the entrance had collapsed. He went to the continent of South Phoenix. He went to the Sea of Endlessness. Huang Yan had perished.

Xu Qing took it all in silently. Then a sigh echoed in his ears. It was a familiar sigh. He turned and saw an old woman standing next to him.

She looked vaguely familiar. Floating next to her was a frail butterfly.

“Before Master withered into death,” the old woman said in a hoarse voice, “she said that you promised to come back in time. A thousand years have passed. You’re far too late. So... what exactly is the point of coming back now?”

She had once been the apprentice of the palace lord of the Summer Immortal Palace. She had been... a little butterfly.[3]

1. The term “goddess” being used here combines the character for god and female. In the context of this novel, it more specifically means ‘daughter of a god.’ I’m using the common rendering “goddess” for a few reasons. First of all, using ‘daughter of a god’ or ‘god daughter’ becomes very clunky. Second, I have not used ‘goddess’ for any of the female god characters in the novel. All such female gods are simply just called gods. When this term comes up in future chapters, it will always retain the meaning ‘daughter of a god.’ ☜

2. The chaotic sea of space-time was previously mentioned in chapter 1170. ☜

3. There’s an additional relevant line of text regarding the little butterfly in the next chapter, so I’ll save my customary links to past chapters for then. ☜

The wind in the Revered Ancient mainland carried a familiar humidity. It came from the depths of the Sea of Endlessness, and from the mutagen that filled heaven and earth. It was very different from the Fifth Star Ring.

Upon sensing it, Xu Qing opened his mouth to speak. And yet, even though his lips quivered, no words came out. Everything around him seemed somewhat blurry. Perhaps it was the distortions caused by mutagen, or maybe just the general influence of the gods.

The only thing that seemed clear... was the decrepit old woman in black clothing standing next to him. The wrinkles on her face seemed like ravines etched by time, hewn out by wind and rain and fate.

Of course, he remembered that little butterfly. Back then, she had been a young woman. There had been tension between the two of them, until... she took him to the Summer Immortal Palace for the first time. That was when he had met the old palace lord, who was, of course, human.[1]

Despite all those memories existing in his head, Xu Qing felt like they weren’t completely real.

“Master once said,” the old woman continued, “that people who have not experienced excruciating pain can never understand such a feeling. It’s like... they can’t even believe it. They will even go so far as to trick themselves into believing that nothing ever happened. And that’s because after excruciating pain is absolute nothingness.”

She smiled bitterly. “I watched the catastrophe strike. I saw everything go away.... That’s when I understood what Master meant. After experiencing all of that, a thousand years passed, and I still haven’t left this place. And now, today, I’ve run into you.... I just hope that one day, you can leave.”

The old woman turned bitterly and made her way off into the distance. She looked bleak, desolate, and infinitely lonely.

Looking at her retreating figure, Xu Qing suddenly said, “What happened to my Master...? My Eldest Brother...? Plumdark and Ling’er, and... what about all my other friends? My fellow apprentices and... everybody. What happened to them?”

People who knew Xu Qing would hardly recognize his voice at that moment. It was as hoarse as the grating of infinite grains of sand. He hardly dared to ask the questions he had just asked. But he did ask them, his voice hoarse and trembling.

The old woman stopped in place, her back to Xu Qing. She was quiet for a long moment. When she spoke, her voice seemed to contain the flow of history, like a reed flute echoing in time.

“A thousand years ago, that ancient immortal came looking for something. He started with humankind. When he saw the statue of Grand Emperor Swordsage, he waved his hand, and most of humanity was wiped out. Empress Summer Departure was strong, but to him, she was like a child. He erased her mind and turned her into a godslave.

“Your Master didn’t do anything at first. To him, humankind wasn’t very important. He only cared about those people close to him.

“That ancient immortal left South Phoenix alone. There was karma between him and your Master, so he carefully avoided it. But eventually, your Master came out of seclusion. He stood up to the ancient immortal, and tried to stop him. And that was because... the thing sought by the ancient immortal was that Eldest Brother of yours!

“Your Master fought for him. Your Eldest Brother eventually returned from Brilliant Heaven with a peak Quasi-Immortal cultivation base. But that wasn’t enough to change anything. Your Master died in the fight, and your Eldest Brother went mad. He became the sacrificial object the ancient immortal sought.

“In the end, your sect was wiped out. Your other Elder Brothers and your Elder Sister were not spared. South Phoenix sank into the Sea of Endlessness, and they all... became corpses.

“After that, the ancient immortal left and Brilliant Heaven stirred. The gods therein awoke. Emperor Ancient Spirit took advantage of the opportunity to rise to prominence, and Revered Ancient descended into chaos.[2]

“I vaguely remember that Plumdark you mentioned. She ended up homeless and miserable, and eventually perished as fodder for the new gods. I also remember Ling’er. She was devoured by Emperor Ancient Spirit to get at the destiny aura she had. As for everyone else you knew, they died over the thousand years that have passed.”

Xu Qing bowed his head.

The old woman didn’t say anything further. That was how things ended for everyone Xu Qing knew.

The wind blew from off in the distance, harsh and desolate. It kicked up the dust and lifted Xu Qing’s hair, but it couldn’t take away the infinite heaviness in his heart. That was how things ended for everyone he knew.

The old woman sighed. As she disappeared into the wind, she said one more thing. “If it weren’t for that thing you left underneath Revered Ancient, I would have assumed you died out there.”

She quietly shook her head, and then, in all her lonely bleakness, she disappeared over the horizon. From the look of it, now that her Master was gone, she had the responsibility of carrying on the mission of the Summer Immortal Palace. Unfortunately... she wasn’t sure if there was any point to it anymore. But that was the dying wish of her Master. And so, she disappeared into the blurry world.

Time passed.

Xu Qing just stood there for a long time. He wasn’t really sure how he felt. It was as if his thoughts had gone still. Everything had paused. Even his soul. He listened to the sound of the wind. To him, it sounded like sobbing. Even whimpering.

Endless pain filled him, like the rushing of the tide, overwhelming. Everything started to turn as red, as tears of blood filled his eyes. He opened his mouth to murmur something, but only blood spilled out. He staggered backward.

So, when pain becomes excruciating enough, it turns into nothingness....

He couldn’t even weep. He had lost everything. His heart was a black hole that could devour all. Within that black hole was endless emptiness. Xu Qing felt like it should be familiar to him. It was similar to being in the chaotic sea of space-time. But he didn’t want to think about that.

Within his heart and mind, the old woman’s parting words echoed over and over again. Her words became like sparks that started gathering in his eyes.

“Your Eldest Brother went mad. He became the sacrificial object the ancient immortal sought.”

“I also remember Ling’er. She was devoured by Emperor Ancient Spirit to get at the destiny aura she had.”

“Empress Summer Departure.... He erased her mind and turned her into a godslave.”

“If it weren’t for that thing you left underneath Revered Ancient....”

The sparks raged. Xu Qing suddenly looked up.

Maybe Eldest Brother didn’t actually die. Maybe Ling’er made a clone of herself. There’s also hope for Empress Summer Departure. Plumdark might have reincarnated.... There are still paths to choose from.... What’s more, everything she told me was hearsay! It might not even be true!

Xu Qing’s eyes blazed as if with fire. And I did leave something behind.

Xu Qing looked up, and his eyes seemed capable of piercing the deepest depths. His divine will spread out. He looked at all the ruins. He looked at the familiar yet unfamiliar world. He looked at the gods everywhere.... And his heart cried out. His soul trembled. Eventually, he got a response, although it was so weak it seemed just on the verge of being extinguished. It was coming from the Sea of Endlessness.

Xu Qing suddenly vanished.

***

In the silt deep beneath the surface of the Sea of Endlessness, a host of sea snakes wriggled along. They pulsed with fluctuations of intense godliness, and if one examined the sea snakes closely, it was obvious that each one had a gruish ghost face on it.

Deep within the silt was a dead body. Rather, it was half a body, as everything beneath the waist was gone. The upper half of the body was riddled with wounds. There wasn’t much flesh left on it, and it really looked no different from a decaying corpse.

Apparently, hē had been sealed here, and despite being nothing more than a desiccated corpse, it was still possible to detect the fluctuations of god magic coming off of it. Because of that god magic, hīs body was slowly reverting from a god state into that of a mortal. The process wasn’t far from being completed. The sea snakes would occasionally come here to devour some of the flesh off the corpse.

If things continued on like this, then it wouldn’t be long before the dead body disappeared completely.

But then, in the calm, dark depths of the seafloor, things stirred. It was as if space were being broken open. The mutagen in the area, and the pressure of the sea depths, were instantly wiped away. freewebnovel.com

A figure stepped out of nowhere. It was none other than Xu Qing.

As he walked along, all things on the seafloor trembled. Even gods went still. He reached the silt and the sea snakes. His gaze caused the sea snakes to shake violently. The silt seethed, and the buried body was revealed.

Upon laying eyes on the corpse, Xu Qing’s chest quivered. This corpse was his god clone. However, the soul inside of it was like a candle flickering in the wind, just on the verge of being extinguished. Xu Qing could see from the horrific injuries on the clone’s body that... the god clone had fought in the catastrophe.

If I absorb this god body into myself, the fact that we’re of the same origin means that I’ll be able to experience what the clone experienced! I can verify everything!

Heart pounding, Xu Qing neared the corpse and lifted his right hand to absorb it. However, just before he took action, he shivered. He looked more closely at the mangled body, a strange look in his eyes.

This god body actually comes from the broken face.... Its soul could be destroyed, but the flesh could not. Also, how could it be sealed here so easily with a god magic?

Pupils constricting, Xu Qing suddenly looked up, out of the Sea of Endlessness and into the canopy of heaven. Up above... there was no broken face!

Earlier, this hadn’t seemed strange at all to Xu Qing. But then he thought back to everything he had experienced, including the encounter with the God Lord, and he realized he could only remember certain key details. He didn’t remember everything that happened. Even right now, the Revered Ancient mainland was a blur. All those things were like reflections in a mirror.

As Xu Qing came to that realization, he suddenly spoke.

“Aurora Immortal Palace. Heaven beyond heaven! Crush!”

Wild colors flashed in heaven and earth. The Sea of Endlessness filled with rumbling sounds. In the Revered Ancient mainland, lands shook and mountains were rocked. The entire world was quaking. Massive cracking sounds rang out. It was as if a heavenly palace were crushing down onto it from outside!

Everything Xu Qing could see suddenly popped like a bubble! It became dust, roiling out in all directions. A starry sky replaced it. Starlight shone as the might of an immortal palace erupted.

The illusion was erased, and the truth was revealed! The world changed dramatically!

Xu Qing could see everything clearly. He wasn’t in the Revered Ancient mainland! He was clearly in a heaven beyond heaven! There was a corpse in front of him, but it wasn’t his god body. It was clearly... a True God that was half-person half-spider!

The True God wanted Xu Qing to willingly fuse with hīm! In that manner, the True God could switch bodies and return by means of Xu Qing’s husk!

But Xu Qing had woken up. It resulted in an instant backlash for the True God, especially considering the immortal palace was crushing down and the heaven beyond heaven was bolstering Xu Qing. The True God’s face distorted. Golden blood leaked out, and a cry of anguish echoed in all directions.

“How did you wake up??”

Xu Qing looked at him, flames of fury raging in his eyes as he looked at hīm. He had never been more furious in his entire life!
