Xu Qing had spent his youth wandering in misery. He had experienced the suffering of the human world. And he had survived it all thanks to his tenacious desire to keep on living.

Those experiences had made him cautious by nature. He would seek revenge over the smallest grievance, and had learned how to coldly slaughter his enemies. It had also fueled his thirst for knowledge, and had caused him to endlessly yearn for light and beauty. He was not the type of person who would casually open his heart to others.

His life had experienced twists and turns. But overall, things had been better than they had been in his youth. Slowly but surely, he had opened up his heart.

Unfortunately, though his path was like a blooming flower, it also came to be like a wilting flower. As he grew up, and as his heart opened, his world became filled with people.... He was moved in the depths of his being.

Also within him was a storm that could be called nothing other than fury! The first time he raged with fury was when Sergeant Thunder died. The next time was when Grandmaster Bai was murdered. It happened again when his own older brother had killed Master Sixth, and he had learned the truth about Peerless City. The fourth time was when Grand Emperor Swordsage perished.

Today was the fifth time.

Now that he was awake, he could see the many flaws in the illusion he had just experienced. But his feelings had been real. Now he knew what it was like to lose everyone he cared about. He had felt the pain, and he had felt the emptiness which followed. Now that he was awake, the intensity of his anger was equivalent to the intensity of the pain he had experienced. And now, he felt no need to respond to the words spoken by this True God who was still in the process of returning.

His aura, his bloodshot eyes, and the intense fluctuations rolling off him, became a pure killing intent that filled him, filled his immortal embryo, and filled the Aura Immortal Palace. It erupted!

The starry sky trembled. Ripples flowed through the heaven beyond heaven. In this starry sky, Xu Qing’s immortal embryo was boundless. The Aurora Immortal Palace was clear within it, and all of that heaven-shaking, earth-shattering power was unleashed onto the half-person half-spider god!

Rumbling sounds echoed out that surpassed everything from before. Boundless immortal light shone from the immortal palace. As it fell, the returning True God tried to dodge. Unfortunately... hē had not yet returned, and was very weak.

At the same time, the backlash from hīs arts of godhood brought pain to hīs soul. Hē could not hold back from screaming in anguish. The full weight of a heaven beyond heaven was not something that hē, a weakened True God, could stand up to.

Because of all those various factors, there was no possible way hē could escape. The majestic immortal palace crushed down. The True God trembled under the force of the blow. Hē shrank down, golden blood spraying out. Cracks spread out across hīs body, and pain swept through hīm like storm winds.

Hē wanted to fight back. But Xu Qing’s fury could not have been greater, and he would not give this god the chance to fight back.

The light of the Aurora Immortal Palace flared again, shining into the starry sky, and drawing even more power... to launch another crushing blow!

Rumbling sounds mixed with the scream of the True God. The True God’s fleshly body was crumbling even more. The spider half of the body was almost completely pulverized, and was leaking large amounts of ringsource. Hē continued to struggle, trying to use the escaping ringsource to fuel a god magic.

But Xu Qing had very nearly died just now, so there was no way he would let his guard down. He took a step forward, entering the Aurora Immortal Palace, where he sat down cross-legged in the main hall. In the outside world, the Aurora Immortal Palace was an illusion, but in this heaven beyond heaven, it was true and real.

Once seated inside, Xu Qing commanded full authority as the lord of this heaven beyond heaven. His cultivation base was insufficient, and he was not skilled enough to truly restrain a True God. But... the immortal palace itself was the most deadly weapon he could wield! He needed no divine abilities. No daoist magic could match the fury that raged in his heart right now. It was... pure violence!

In response to his very thoughts, the Aurora Immortal Palace once again smashed down onto the returning True God.

Once. Twice. Three times....

Xu Qing was venting his rage!

Ear-shattering rumbling sounds echoed out that drowned out the shrill screams of the True God. The god’s body was full of cracks. And then, another anguished scream echoed out as the spider half of the body collapsed into fragments.

Left behind was the person half of the body, whose gaze was extremely weak. However, pain in the fleshly body or the soul was not what this True God feared the most.

What hē feared... was the black hole below! It was a prison formed by the power of this heaven beyond heaven. If hē fell into that prison, then coming back again would be nearly impossible!

As the immortal palace smashed down on hīm again and again, hē got closer and closer to the black hole. At that critical juncture, hīs eyes suddenly lit up. Golden fire erupted from within them, incinerating everything around hīm as it flowed over his body.

Astonishingly, hē was choosing to burn up his own body! Hē was self-destructing! Erasing the carrier would indicate that hē had failed to return. But at the same time, it would wipe out all traces of hīm! And that meant that hē might be able to return sometime in the future. But if the carrier body remained, and was stuffed into the black hole, then hē would have no such chance.

Therefore, hē didn’t hesitate for a moment to try to incinerate his carrier. Hē even ignited the large portion of godhood that had returned. It didn’t matter how heavy a price hē paid if hē could eventually return in the future. If there was one thing the gods didn’t lack, it was time. Hē could keep waiting! freewebnovel.com

Hē carried out the incineration with incredible decisiveness. It was so quick and violent that it seemed impossible to stop. In the blink of an eye, the flames raged to the extreme, and hīs body became incredibly weak.

Unfortunately, hē had underestimated Xu Qing!

As Xu Qing sat cross-legged in the immortal palace, glaring at the burning True God, the coldness in his eyes grew incredibly intense. He knew that True Gods were undying. As such, he had not attacked with the goal of killing this god. Instead, he wanted the god to experience excruciating pain!

And thus, it went without saying that he wasn’t going to let the god escape.... That was not the ending he wanted!

Xu Qing lifted his hand and said, “Be sealed!”

The Green Heaven trembled. Countless stars, galaxies, and universes all responded to his control by means of the immortal palace. The entire heaven beyond heaven... enacted a sealing! The heaven beyond heaven was completely cut off from the outside! He was making this heaven beyond heaven a gigantic prison!

Of course, it was part of a higher star ring, and True Gods were undying. The fact that as long as the true name existed, a True God could leave and come back was an expression of the love toward them shown by the higher star rings. They were like fish swimming in the sea. So this isolation wasn’t complete. It was like a fish net that, though spread wide, still had holes in it.

However, Xu Qing was not limited to this one method. All of a sudden, something flew out of the immortal palace and hovered in the starry sky outside!

It was an hourglass! In the reflected history of the Aurora Immortal Palace, Xu Qing had acquired... a space-time precious treasure! Contained within it was a two-hour time period that transcended this space-time! It could add an additional two hours to any point in time. And whatever happened inside could not be erased. It would exist beyond space-time and beyond the timescape! It could not be limited by any other space-time!

If someone who controlled space-time canon used it, then they could make that time flow normally, or more quickly or slowly. The limit was two hours.

After the hourglass appeared, a cracking sound rang out. The hourglass broke open, and the sand inside shone with a five-colored glow. As it spread, the burning True God, along with hīs body and godhood... was covered by the sand!

It added an additional two hours to hīm! It was a two-hour period that did not have any karma. Nor was it part of this space-time! Because Xu Qing controlled space-time canon, he could slow down the departure and the incineration by a significant amount. In that instant, the world suddenly had an additional two hours!

If the closing of the heaven beyond heaven was like the casting of a fish net, then the space-time sand was a way to slow down the fleeing fish! It ensured that the god could not escape quickly! And it drew out the period in which hē was weak!

This development caused the starry sky to tremble as the will of a true name echoed out with incredulity.

Xu Qing stood up in the immortal palace. His eyes were extremely cold as he stepped out into the starry sky, where he appeared in front of the weak god, who was now experiencing one breath of time that lasted for two hours.

“You like inflicting pain on others?” Xu Qing asked. It was the first time he had spoken during the fight, and his voice was as cold as ice. “Well, then you can enjoy it for a bit.”

Xu Qing waved his hand, and a coffin of ice appeared. It was a nine-colored coffin that pulsed with frigid energy. It was Young Lord Aurora’s ice coffin, which Xu Qing had taken from the Helioterran imperial clan! Immortal Lord Aurora and his wife had prepared the coffin for their son, and had sealed him inside as an infant. The coffin would freeze the fleshly body and the soul. And also time. It was only natural that objects made by Immortal Lords were astounding.

Xu Qing tossed the coffin toward the burning True God. Once the god was inside, he sealed the lid, which became solid ice! The True God, who was burning and not fully returned, was trapped inside. Time was also sealed inside!

To a certain extent, it meant that the True God was stuck in a state of partial return. The god could not leave, nor could hē return. It was like... being stuck in space-time amber!

From now on, the god would be stuck in burning pain that had no end. The undying nature of this True God was no longer a blessing to hīm from a higher star ring. It was a curse! At the same time, hē would provide a constant flow of ringsource. It was almost like hē had become a spirit stone!

There was no door to life. There was no path to death. There was no way to depart. There was no means to return.

Thus was the pain of this True God. Hē was frozen in an ice coffin, sealed in time by the space-time hourglass, hīs karma ensnared by the heaven beyond heaven. Stuck halfway between returning and departing, hē was like a special spirit stone that emanated ringsource. All hē could do was descend into the burning pain, hīs soul torn apart as hīs godhood and ringsource was slowly sucked away in what amounted to pure torment.

Out in the starry sky, Xu Qing looked coldly at the ice coffin. His fury was finally subsiding. The end this True God had experienced was the best kind of torment to inflict on hīm. Since hē enjoyed pain, hē would personally feel a lot of it.

It’s too bad I don’t have Yu Liuchen’s godly authority of telling stories....

If he had that godly authority, then he could draw out time even further. He could tell a story of pain upon pain for this True God, and ensure that his time spent sealed in ice was one of even greater mental torment. At the same time, he would be able to extract even stronger ringsource.

There’s no rush.

Xu Qing retracted his vision, then went over and sat down cross-legged on the ice coffin. Closing his eyes, he began doing some breathing exercises. All of his pores opened, and ringsource from the coffin poured into him.

The ringsource was strong and pure, and as he did breathing exercises, it flowed into him. Once inside, it reached his immortal embryo and provided profound nourishment. The immortal embryo began to emit a soft glow that illuminated the surrounding darkness, and caused the innumerable universes, galaxies, and planets in the heaven beyond heaven to be a bit brighter. They were still recovering.

As light pulsed off Xu Qing’s immortal embryo, the immortal palace that served as his immortal foundation reacted similarly.

In that manner, time passed. A month went by.

Xu Qing opened his eyes. A mysterious light shone therein as he looked down at the coffin floating in the starry sky. The coffin had originally emitted strong ringsource. But it had diminished quite a bit, and had gone from a raging river to a trickling stream.

That was no surprise. The special spirit stone made of a god would last for a long time and would provide a lot of ringsource. But it wasn’t going to all come out at once. Absorbing it slowly but surely would be the most beneficial thing for Xu Qing.

During his month of breathing exercises, he had made some significant cultivation progress. His immortal embryo had become more stable, and its aura and pressure had increased. The immortal palace that served as his immortal foundation, plus his status as the lord of this heaven beyond heaven, ensured that his aura was far closer to that of an immortal. He was now very close to the peak of early Quasi-Immortal.

On the outside, cultivation speed like that would provoke instant jealousy among others. It was incredibly fast. After all, the Quasi-Immortal level was about the process of going from an immortal embryo to a mature immortal. And it required terrifying amounts of ringsource. Becoming a mature immortal... was the sign of the Lower Immortal level!

Unfortunately, it was too slow for Xu Qing. I need more of these True God spirit stones....

Licking his lips, he stood and looked off into the distance. He was thinking about what he had seen in that illusion.

Now that I think about it, there were some very strange aspects to that illusion.... His eyes glittered mysteriously.

In the illusion, it had taken him ten years of secluded cultivation to reach the peak of Quasi-Immortal. Although his memories didn’t contain all the details of how that happened, he could clearly remember what it felt like to reach that level. There was something especially noteworthy....

If I really did spend ten years of secluded cultivation here, it’s hard to say if the ringsource coming from the ice coffin would be enough to reach the peak of Quasi-Immortal. But it would definitely be enough for late Quasi-Immortal. It seems safe to say... that the illusion was at least logical on a theoretical level....

Even as the thought occurred to him, his mind filled with a haze.

On an instinctual level, he wasn’t willing to take that route. He was not going to stick around here in seclusion. For one thing, he didn’t want things to end up like they had in the illusion. What was more, sitting around in seclusion was the slow path to making progress.

There was another reason. Xu Qing knew full well that if he wanted to break out of the Quasi-Immortal level and step into Lower Immortal, he needed more than just ringsource to transform his immortal embryo. He needed to push his canon to a higher level!

And I need my tenth extreme!

He currently had no direction to pursue when it came to his tenth extreme. He hadn’t even done that in the illusion.... After some thought, he put the ice coffin into the black hole. The black hole would absorb the ringsource and keep it stored for later use.

Looking thoughtful, he turned to leave. But then he stopped in place all of a sudden. His eyes glittered.

“Wait. No!”

I must have made some progress with the tenth extreme in the illusion. After all, by the time I got back to Revered Ancient, my cultivation base was... not Quasi-Immortal. But I can’t remember the details.

He frowned. Now he was more doubtful than ever about the illusion. Unfortunately, without more detailed information to go on, he had no choice but to suppress his doubt and leave the Green Heaven.

***

Meanwhile, outside of the Green Heaven, the streams of immortal will began to disperse. Before leaving, they couldn’t help but glance back incredulously at Xu Qing emerging from the Green Heaven.

They would remember Xu Qing. It would be impossible to forget what they had just seen. The lord of the Aurora heaven beyond heaven, with a Quasi-Immortal cultivation base and battle prowess close to that of an immortal, had crushed a returning True God. A stunning achievement like that was enough to raise the eyebrows of them all.

One by one, they left.

***

The figure standing in the highest tower in the Nineshores Immortal Palace nodded. Since he seized the destined opportunity... and accomplished his Acquisitioner’s mission, then... there’s not much point in him staying in this star ring.

“Send orders to the Department of Acquisitions,” he said. “The squadron of new ascendees will be converted to a Transporter squadron. Just like all the other squadrons, they’ll take what they collected as Acquisitioners and transport it to the battlefield. They don’t need to come back. They’ll move in directly to the star ring’s god barrier formation.”

In response to Immortal Lord Nineshores’ words, the tower trembled, and then an official decree was sent from the Nineshores heaven beyond heaven.

***

Poison Monarch was in the Department of Acquisitions. As he sat there cross-legged, his eyes opened. New orders had come in from Immortal Lord Nineshores. He checked the orders, whereupon his expression flickered. After looking off into the distance, he sighed.

Is the kid lucky? Or is he unlucky...?

Poison Monarch didn’t want to simply give in like this, but the orders were from Immortal Lord Nineshores, and he didn’t dare to work against them. Sighing, he made the arrangements.

***

Xu Qing left the Green Heaven and returned to the same spot in the Heavenless Zone.

The prison was gone. However, the guards, the wardens, and Sir Star Ring and the ascendees were all waiting to see how things ended. A month had passed, and they were all feeling uneasy. After all, it shouldn’t have taken an entire month for a True God to return after the process had been started in the way it had.

Therefore, when they saw Xu Qing, they relaxed a bit. That was especially true when they realized that he was obviously stronger than in the past. Zhou Zhengli was the first to step forward and bow.

“Congratulations, Your Majesty. You have crushed a True God! There is truly no end to your virtuous achievements!”

Everyone else rushed to pay respects. All of them were shaken to varying degrees. The ascendees had personally witnessed Xu Qing becoming a Quasi-Immortal. They had sensed the majesty of his immortal embryo, and the fact that he was lord of a heaven beyond heaven. Now he was very nearly as strong as an immortal. They had also watched him teleport a True God away, and then calmly return.

Even top chosen couldn’t avoid being astonished to see him make such rapid progress and reach such great heights. freewebnovel.com

Sir Star Ring looked quietly at Xu Qing and sighed in his heart. The difference between them was only growing larger. However, that feeling didn’t last for long before it turned into a motivating force.

Xu Qing looked around at everyone. Upon seeing that the wardens and guards were still present, he relaxed a bit.

Things were already different from the illusion. After all, in the illusion, he had come out to find the warden and guards gone. But then, even as such thoughts entered his mind, and as everyone was bowing to him, something happened. Before he could say a word...

The ascendees’ identity medallions all vibrated. New orders came from the Nineshores heaven beyond heaven, conveyed through the Department of Acquisitions.

“There are new developments in the war outside the star ring. There is a huge demand for ringsource. All Acquisitioner squadrons are to personally transport the ringsource they have collected to the front lines as Transporter squadrons. There shall be no delays!”

All of the ascendees reacted with visible surprise.

Transport it ourselves to the front lines?

Hordeslayer and Rampart were trembling with astonishment. Yuanshan Su frowned. Li Mengtu’s expression flickered. Sir Vilespirit’s pupils constricted. The ascendees all reacted in different ways.

The war had always been something far, far removed from them. None of them had ever imagined... that they would see it so soon! That was especially true considering that their cultivation bases would make them like drops of water in the ocean. They could die at any moment.

Maybe they would run into Godfire gods, or Altar Gods. They might even encounter True Gods! Based on their previous understanding, the war with the Fourth Star Ring was being waged between God Lords and Immortal Lords. It was a war between gods and immortals. It was a war between opposing sides. It was a war of complete extermination of species!

Zhou Zhengli looked gravely at Xu Qing. Sir Star Ring’s heart sank as he did the same. All of the cultivators did the same.

Xu Qing, meanwhile, felt somewhat dazed. He was yet again thinking about the illusion he had experienced thanks to that True God. In the illusion, he had gone to the front lines! The difference was that, in the illusion, it had happened ten years later. In reality, it was happening a lot sooner. Ten years sooner.

Why did it happen that way in the True God’s illusion? Was it a coincidence?

A dour look filled Xu Qing’s eyes.

Each of the thirty-six higher star rings were like massive, independent star charts. The interior of every star ring was boundless. But viewed as a whole, the higher star rings were actually connected, and they made an even larger, irregularly shaped ring that would astonish anyone who could see it.

In the middle of the gargantuan ring formed by the thirty-six higher star rings, there was a vast, black sea of mutagen! The enormity of it surpassed all other things.

Its name was the Primeval Sea. It was a mysterious, unimaginable place. In the middle of it was a place that only God Paragons could enter, and even then, they would do so with great caution. It had thirty-six main streams which led to the thirty-six star rings. And within each star ring, there were even more tributaries, and they formed that which the cultivators and the gods called... the outer seas!

The war between the Fourth and Fifth Star Rings was being fought on the border between those two locations. It was a place that was part of the Fifth Star Ring, but at the same time, part of the Fourth Star Ring.

Neither the gods nor the immortals were willing to back down, so the war had dragged on for years in a deadlock. Neither side could do much to the other, and for the most part they had held back from taking the fighting to the level of the God Lords.

But then a new God Lord appeared in the Fourth Star Ring! That God Lord was deployed to the front lines, and the tide of battle instantly shifted. Immortal Lord Deepgloom had met his match for the first time in his life!

The fighting reached a point where it surpassed the level of mere daoist magics and god magics. The fight between the God Lord and the Immortal Lord was something that ordinary gods and immortals couldn’t even see clearly.

Even True Gods and Lower Immortals couldn’t fully comprehend a fight between a God Lord and an Immortal Lord. They could only vaguely sense what was happening. That was because the core of a battle on the level of God Lords and Immortal Lords came down to momentum!

To the cultivators in the war, Immortal Lord Deepgloom provided the momentum. He surpassed the heavenly daos, and was part of the determination of the Fifth Star Ring itself. His will was paramount on the battlefield. As he stood there, he represented the unique energy of immortal cultivators, which could drive away mutagen! If all of that mutagen were to be driven away, and replaced by immortal energy, then the situation with the war would completely change.

In fact, if the day came when the mutagen of the Fourth Star Ring were to be driven out, and replaced by immortal energy, then.... Without mutagen, without the aura of the gods, well, the gods... would be like fish out of water. No matter how they struggled, they would basically end up the same as the gods in the Fifth Star Ring. That was the line of research the Fifth Star Ring had been pursuing in their hopes of subduing the gods.

The aura of the gods was mutagen. It was poison to cultivators, and could infect all things. Immortal energy was the aura of immortals. It was anathema to gods, and could harm them without even touching them. That was the source of a powerful momentum.

Of course, the God Lord was aware of that. So when the new God Lord arrived at the front lines, the result was boundless mutagen spreading everywhere. It overwhelmed everything, including the immortal energy.

And thus, the war between the Fourth and Fifth Star Rings, viewed from the highest of levels, was a conflict between a God Lord and an Immortal Lord. It was a clash between mutagen and immortal energy. And both sides were trying to build up their own momentum! freewebnovel.com

Even if the gods didn’t follow the conventions of war and went on the offensive, it wouldn’t change anything. In order to fundamentally do anything, they needed to affect the clash between mutagen and immortal energy. The mutagen in the Fourth Star Ring was very strong, but so was the immortal energy in the Fifth Star Ring. If either side tried to invade the other, they would become much weaker. And thus, they nibbled away at each other, each side trying to build up momentum to create a critical moment.

Therefore, both gods and immortals in the Lord level were extremely important in the war. As Lords, they could both consolidate and fight over momentum. Because no one else could understand a fight between a God Lord and an Immortal Lord, all they saw was a swirling mass of immortal energy and mutagen.

As for the cultivators, they were watching to see their Immortal Lord gain the upper hand. When that happened, the immortal energy would spread and drive away the mutagen. The moment that happened, they would rush out to plant special dao flags from the Fifth Star Ring. The dao flags would mark an area as being occupied with immortal energy, and it would signify an expansion of Fifth Star Ring territory. Then, orders would be given to advance into the territory of the gods to destroy their foundation. It was a snowball effect, as the more territory fell, the more momentum they built up. That, in turn, supported the Immortal Lord, and shifted the tide of battle in his favor.

However, the same thing happened on the side of the gods. When the God Lord gained the upper hand, the cultivators were prevented from planting dao flags. In fact, dao flags could be destroyed, and mutagen would spread far and wide.

The end result was that, viewed from high above, the field of battle was an interchange between black and white. The black was the mutagen. The white was the immortal energy. It was like a black and white ink painting that was constantly shifting and flowing back and forth. That was how war was waged between the gods and immortals.

The war was about momentum. Every attack influenced the field of battle, and the two armies’ actions influenced the battle between the Lords.

It was very intense. Deaths occurred constantly. That was just what happened when the strong clashed with the strong.

In the rear echelon of a battlefield that was as wide as countless universes, over a hundred squadrons from the Department of Acquisitions were arriving at a teleportation portal.

One of them was the same squadron that had caused some trouble for Xu Qing and the other ascendees back to the planet that was the home base of the Department of Acquisitions. Upon materializing, they looked around with very serious expressions. Then, under the cold gazes of the warriors guarding the teleportation portals, they hurried off into the distance.

The Acquisitioners were now Transporters, and their mission was to disperse through the battlefield and deliver ringsource to the eastern theater of the war. There was a desperate need for ringsource there!

The light of teleportation faded away, and Xu Qing appeared with his squadron. An unfamiliar starry sky stretched out overhead, and the atmosphere was somber. The immortal energy was scarce, and it was even possible to see wisps of mutagen floating here and there.

Many of the ascendees felt out of sorts. To most of them, war had been some distant thing. Though most of them had experienced a lot of fighting in their lives, virtually none of them had experience in war. They could even hear occasional booms coming from the front lines, or indescribable roars coming from other universes. Chaotic fluctuations rolled through space, and there was a unique and sinister coldness that only death could bring....

Most of the ascendees were in a daze. Instinctively, they looked around to take in their surroundings.

However, before any of them could see much, a warrior cultivator on guard duty yelled at them.

“You lot, hurry up and get on with your delivery!”

The voice boomed louder than thunder into the hearts and minds of the squadron. It contained a mountain-toppling, sea-draining force, like a tempest that could crush anything in its path.

Everyone was visibly taken aback. It was the voice of a Lower Immortal!

Xu Qing’s pupils constricted. He was no stranger to war. Though he had never fought in a war this massive, he was naturally more prepared mentally for what war was like. He immediately flew off the teleportation portal. The other cultivators in the squadron followed.

The closer they got to the battlefield, the more dangerous things would get, and by extension, the more they felt the need to stick together as a team. That was just how human nature worked.

Xu Qing had the strongest battle prowess of them all, and his status was far above theirs. Sticking close to him was their greatest chance of surviving.

As for Xu Qing, his heart was sinking. As he sped along, he looked off into the distance, and took time to sense his surroundings. He was more sensitive to mutagen than the rest of them, and he could sense that the mutagen was getting stronger as they made their way forward.

If they need ringsource so badly... then why don’t they send stronger people to deliver it? That would be much more efficient. Why send people as weak as us to the front lines?

The more he thought about the situation, the less it made sense. And as he felt the mutagen getting stronger, his speculations went wild. After a while, he had a theory.

Around the time that the theory coalesced in his mind, he heard a whistling sound behind him as Sir Star Ring, Zhou Zhengli, Sir Vilespirit, Yuanshan Su, and everyone else caught up to him. Eyes narrowing, he looked at them.

Sir Star Ring’s expression was grim as he said, “Xu Qing, my canon senses are telling me that the order in this area is fractured. Everything is chaotic. Something isn’t right!”

Sir Vilespirit licked his lips and added, “As all of you know, I’m different from the rest of you. My canon isn’t the result of enlightenment. I have a special canon treasure. My broken sword. Well, whenever I’m about to run into a deadly crisis, it gets very excited. And right now, it’s more excited than it’s ever been!”

Zhou Zhengli looked extremely serious. After Sir Star Ring and Sir Vilespirit were done talking, he lowered his voice and said, “Your Majesty, it doesn’t make sense for us to be sent here. I have a theory. Is it possible that we—” He glanced around at everyone “—are bait?? It’s not that our squadron is being targeted specifically. Rather, the Acquisitioner squads are being sent here with ringsource... to turn them all into bait!”

Everyone scowled. Xu Qing’s eyes glittered. That was the exact same theory he had come up with!

“Right now,” he said, “we’re in cultivator territory. If we’re being thrown out as bait here, it implies....”

He trailed off, only to have his sentence finished by Yuanshan Su.

“It implies that something big is about to happen here!” she said. “They want to lure out any gods that are hidden in this area, all to make sure things here are more stable after that event occurs!”

In response to Yuanshan Su’s words, they all exchanged glances. Everyone had different opinions on the matter.

But in the depths of his heart, Xu Qing knew one thing for certain. He had come here to the Fifth Star Ring to find resources to grow stronger. Therefore... he had to abide by the rules of the Fifth Star Ring. He had become an Acquisitioner and then a Transporter. And here he was on the front lines. He had to accomplish his mission.

Of course, the more he understood about the battlefield, the easier it would be to accomplish his mission. And also... the easier it would be to defend himself.

With that thought in mind, he said, “Everyone, keep your guard up. We’re going to split into smaller squads and advance in a staggered formation. Be ready to back up other squads at any moment. Zhou Zhengli, you handle the particulars.”

“Yes, sir,” Zhou Zhengli said. He knew the individual members of the squadron much better than Xu Qing, so it didn’t take him long to split up the more than eighty people into five smaller squads. Then they split up into a staggered formation. He also arranged for about a dozen of the fastest and stealthiest cultivators to spread out both ahead and behind to keep the main group informed of any sudden developments.

Sir Vilespirit and some of the others with canon treasures used those treasures to surround the group with a powerful concealing aura. At the same time, Xu Qing hoisted a banner that covered the group with an additional layer of concealment. In that way, they hoped to keep their passage as unnoticed as possible.

With those arrangements made, they started moving forward. Their caution was rewarded as their journey went on.

Half a month went by. During that period of travel, which included the use of teleportation portals, things went smoothly. Given the unknowns and the fact that they all felt something strange was going on, they took a more roundabout route toward their destination. Thanks to their efforts at staying concealed, they were able to travel smoothly and consistently.

At a certain point along the way, Xu Qing spotted a dao banner. They were behind the front lines of the eastern theater, which meant they were in cultivator territory. As a result, each universe had a dao flag planted in it.

In terms of appearance, they came in the form of a planet-sized altar, atop which was a silver war banner. The war banners were the dao flags of the Fifth Star Ring, and they emitted a constant stream of very pure immortal energy, as well as a mighty pressure that would cause all living beings to tremble.

With a dao flag in place, a given universe would have a constant supply of immortal energy. Mutagen wouldn’t be able to affect that area, and all things related to gods would be suppressed. It went without saying that large numbers of cultivators always gathered around the dao flags.

Xu Qing and his squadron passed through over a hundred universes, which meant that they saw the same number of dao flags. Some were large, some were small, depending on the size of the area they affected.

The dao flags served another function. They ensured that the forces of the cultivator army could communicate quickly and effectively. As they continued on their journey, Zhou Zhengli maintained communications, especially with other squadrons on missions similar to their own.

Time continued to pass. Another half a month went by.

As they advanced, Xu Qing and his squadron got passing glimpses of many universes. Eventually, they left the rear echelon of the eastern theater and entered the staging areas in the middle of cultivator territory. After they passed through the staging areas, which was made up of hundreds of universes, they would reach the front lines of the eastern theater.

Unfortunately, once they entered the staging areas, Sir Vilespirit’s broken sword started getting even more excited. And Xu Qing could tell that the mutagen levels were much higher than previously. freewebnovel.com

As they proceeded along quietly, Zhou Zhengli’s expression suddenly flickered. “Your Majesty, one of the Transporter squadrons I was in contact with disappeared.... Either they got cut off from communication, or... they ran into a deadly situation!”

The squadron members looked even more serious than before.

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed. “The bait is working. They hooked a fish.”

He didn’t need to issue any special orders. All members of the squadron were even more careful after that. They made sure to mask their spirit power fluctuations, they kept proper distance between each other, and they made sure to make the most effective use of their concealment techniques.

Every time they went through another teleportation, they made sure to exercise more caution. Occasionally, they would sense something strange, and would avoid a teleportation portal. They didn’t hesitate to take the long way around if it seemed safer. Of course, they all kept their cultivation bases rotating at peak levels.

A month went by.

Either they had been lucky up to this point, or all of their caution had paid off, and their concealments had not been penetrated. Everything went smoothly. Unfortunately, Zhou Zhengli kept getting news about dangerous situations.

The majority of the Transporter squadrons had been ambushed by that point! Some squadrons never had a chance to send out distress messages, and were simply wiped out. Some held on for long enough to ask for help before communication was cut off, making it impossible to determine what happened to them in the end.

Regardless, it quickly became clear who was doing the ambushing. Naturally, it was gods!

However, these were not gods from the front lines. Instead, thēy were spies who had somehow hidden themselves in the eastern theater. Thēy had been so deeply hidden that, normally speaking, thēy would never have revealed themselves. But now thēy were taking the initiative to target the various Transporter squadrons moving through the area. It was as if there was a huge spy network covering the entire eastern theater.

Despite how cautious Xu Qing and his squadron were, after months of safe travel, they eventually ran into some gods.

The first person to notice something unusual was Sir Vilespirit, who was scouting on the right flank. He was already a peak Imperial Sovereign, and was very close to being a Quasi-Immortal. By relying on his broken sword, he was confident that he could fight a Quasi-Immortal. What was more, he had puppet arts to rely on. As a result, he never scouted alone; he had two puppets with him at all times. That made him a particularly reliable scout.

As for his broken sword, it had a mysterious origin. Its karma was inextricably linked with Sir Vilespirit, so that when it suddenly got excited, and he felt himself shaking, he didn’t hesitate to fall back.

The moment he did, the aura of a god ripped through the void. Gods appeared out of nowhere, unleashing a mountain-toppling, sea-draining tempest. Dense mutagen and godly might instantly raged forth.

Although Sir Vilespirit’s two puppets fell back with him, they also unleashed attacks at full power. Unfortunately, they couldn’t deal with this many gods. The puppets shivered as they withered up and were destroyed.

Sir Vilespirit coughed up seven or eight mouthfuls of blood. Relying on his broken sword, he managed to survive the initial attack by the gods. Pupils constricting, he continued to fall back, all while sending a message to Zhou Zhengli.

“I ran into some gods. Seven Altar Gods and twenty-three Flawless Gods!”

Mutagen roiled in his wake as he fled. Terrifying godly fluctuations swept toward him to overwhelm him. He was just on the verge of being overwhelmed. His eyes were bloodshot from the sensation of deadly crisis that filled him.

Then someone blurred into position next to him, grabbed his shoulder, and threw him back.

Just before the wave of mutagen and godly fluctuations were about to sweep over the newcomer, he threw his left hand out in front of him.

“Crush!”

That single word caused space-time to rumble. Overlapping universes appeared, turning into a crushing bout of space-time. It blocked the path of the mutagen. When the collision occurred, raging shock waves swept out in all directions. After, the new arrival stood there tall and straight, while the tempest of mutagen collapsed.

Revealed in the spot where the tempest had collapsed were thirty gods, all of whom looked different, but all of whom were terrifying. Thēir eyes were all locked onto the person in front of thēm.

He had long hair, a black robe, and exquisite facial features. As he hovered there, his aura was immeasurably close to that of a Lower Immortal.

That aura caused all of the Flawless Gods to shift nervously. The seven Altar God’s eyes glittered with golden light.

At the same time, whistling sounds echoed out from behind Xu Qing. Chains of order swept out in all directions as Sir Star Ring arrived. Numerous huge trees soared through the starry sky, as if an endless forest had arrived. Atop the tallest tree in the forest stood Yuanshan Su, her eyes cold. There was also a gigantic eye hovering in the starry sky, within which, seated cross-legged, was Zhou Zhengli. At the same time, poison spread out, along with killing intent. The canon of other ascendees joined the mix, creating a massive pressure. There was also an enormous kelp plant, whose gargantuan body spread out to lock down the entire area.

It looked less like these gods carrying out an ambush and more like Xu Qing and his squadron hunting gods!

Moments later, the kelp began to shrink the perimeter. Inside, the ascendees unleashed trump cards. Sir Star Ring and the other top experts held back none of their power. As Hordeslayer and Rampart flew in as streams of sword energy, the gods were shaken to the core.

What was especially gruish was the manifestation of Zhou Zhengli’s canon, the huge eye. It seemed to be predicting the gods’ every move, as well as all the details of their godly authority. And he was informing everyone about how to deal with thēm. The gods were astonished.

But what shook thēm the most was Xu Qing. His bell was able to restrict all magics. His iron skewer killed any god it hit! The layers of space-time in the area seemed to contain the will of the many heavens.

After the time it takes an incense stick to burn, the kelp plant removed the perimeter. Xu Qing and the squadron continued on their way. All the gods that had ambushed them... were nowhere to be seen. And close examination would reveal that the auras of the squadron members had all improved. They had powered up a bit.

“So,” said Li Mengtu, licking his lips, “it turns out living and healthy gods provide the most delicious ringsource.”

Sir Vilespirit had already recovered from his injuries. “There are a lot of unknowns, but if we stick out a bit, we could attract the attention of some more gods....”

Yuanshan Su looked thoughtful, while Hordeslayer and Rampart seemed itching to fight again. Sir Star Ring’s face was completely expressionless.

As for Zhou Zhengli, he shook his head. “We did well just now, thanks to His Majesty. My foresight is telling me that a True God is behind all of this. There are also multiple Altar Gods in the same group. If we run into a force like that....”

Li Mengtu said nothing.

Xu Qing looked at them calmly. “We continue on as before. We stay cautious and keep under cover. Let’s go.”

Thanks to Zhou Zhengli, everyone gave up on the idea of turning the tables on the gods, and using their status as bait to create their own ambushes. Ringsource was good, but living was better.

If they ended up being targeted by a True God and a host of Altar Gods, then they would definitely be killed. They had been fortunate on their journey so far. The best thing to do going forward was to stay cautious and remain hidden.

And thus, Xu Qing and his squadron disappeared into the universe.

***

In the eastern theater, there were quite a few more god squadrons similar to the one Xu Qing had encountered. Apparently, thēy had been able to remain in hiding this long thanks to outside help. As a result, the cultivators had a very hard time identifying thēm. And if things had gone along as normal, there wouldn’t have been any way to root thēm out easily.

What was more, these gods had godhood, which was a new development. They were not ordinary gods. Thēy had powerful godly authority, and that was evident from the results of their ambushes.

The staging areas of the eastern theater were already descending into disorder. The cultivator army stationed there had no choice but to split up to suppress and contain the incidents.

Before long, the staging areas in the eastern theater were in complete chaos. Within that chaos, and amidst the numerous universes in the eastern theater, there was one universe called the Gracesource Universe. It contained innumerable galaxies, and among those was an unremarkable little galaxy, within which was a very ordinary planet.

The planet was yellow. Looking down at the planet from the starry sky, it was possible to see the earth seething as a huge rift opened up on it. The rift grew wider and wider, and then it started to open up.

It was an eye! Put precisely, this was no planet. It was actually the eye of a god, disguised as a planet, and now it was opening up! Within the golden pupil, it was possible to see an army of gods that numbered no fewer than 10,000!

Perhaps thēy had been there all along, or perhaps thēy had used some special teleportation method to go there. Regardless of how, thēy were there now. Astonishingly, they included gods in the Godfire level, a large number of Altar Gods, many in the peak of that level, and serving as high commanders... there were three True Gods!

One of thēm had a fog obscuring hīs facial features, but hīs godly might caused the surrounding starry sky to ripple and distort. Another was covered from head to toe with fire, and pulsed with an incomparably holy aura. The last was about the same size as a human. Hē was clad in black armor that included a helmet covering hīs entire head. Hē seemed infinitely mysterious.

As soon as the god army thēy commanded arrived... the entire battlefield changed!

The war between the Fourth and Fifth Star Rings was a war of momentum. The scope of the war was like a black and white ink painting, and right now, the black was flowing and the white was seething. They were devouring each other while simultaneously pushing each other away.

Previously, if one could look down on the eastern theater from above, it was full of the white that represented immortal energy. But right now, the conflict between the God Lord and the Immortal Lord, which no one could directly perceive, was changing.

In one small area of the battlefield, the black god energy suddenly became very weak. The mutagen vanished, and the white immortal energy rushed into the area. Meanwhile, an area filled with the white immortal energy was suddenly driven away, to be replaced by the pitch-black of mutagen.

That area was... in the staging areas of the eastern theater! It was a dramatic change!

Because of it, all of the staging areas in the eastern theater suddenly filled with mutagen. Countless cultivator armies were suddenly struck with mutagen, weakening their cultivation bases and infecting them severely.

Godly energy surged, and mutagen went wild. All of the dao flags planted in the universes of the staging areas began to rock back and forth wildly. Cracking sounds rang out. It seemed like the dao flags would start crumbling at any moment. If they did, then it would mean that the cultivators had lost control of the area. And if the eastern theater suffered such a grievous loss, the armies on the front lines would be isolated.

But the cultivator forces rallied. They went all out to protect the dao flags, all in the hopes of buying time.

The gods attacking the Transporter squadrons no longer remained in hiding. They emerged into the open, taking advantage of the mutagen to release an intense tempest of godly might. And they all shot directly toward the nearest dao flags.

At the same time, in many universes, other entities similar to the yellow planet from earlier all opened thēir eyes to reveal armies of gods. Battle raged.

It was impossible to say if the god armies had been lying in wait, or if thēy had taken advantage of the chaos to slip behind enemy lines unnoticed. From the large number of troops involved, the latter seemed like the most likely possibility. Regardless, from the way thēy were taking advantage of the situation, it seemed clear that the gods were the ones taking the initiative to attack. There was no way thēy could have attacked with such precision at the exact moment that there was a change in momentum between the God Lord and the Immortal Lord.

The goal of the attack was obvious: to destroy the dao flags in the universes of the eastern theater’s staging areas, and to turn the entire region into god territory!

***

As the gods appeared everywhere in the staging areas of the eastern theater, there was a spot in the very middle, in a place called the Cloudwatching Universe... where cultivator armies were arrayed in formation.

Every single galaxy there contained a huge army. Every single planet had an army banner on it. The somber and desolate atmosphere grew stronger. This was the location in staging areas of the eastern theater where the high commander banner flew!

All military orders in the eastern theater came from this location. In the middle of that starry sky was an enormous immortal altar that shone with boundless immortal light. And at that spot... an enormous figure sat cross-legged.

He was the highest-ranking high commander, and he was none other than the Fifth Star Ring’s extremely famous Immortal Monarch Silent Dao! He was the second-in-command to Immortal Lord Deepgloom! His cultivation base was at the peak of Lower Immortal! He was an experienced killer, and was known to be the strongest expert among peak Lower Immortals.

In the pursuit of his dao, he had come very close to the great circle. As his eyes opened, they glittered with killing intent.

“They took the bait,” he murmured quietly.

During this war, both gods and immortals had set up very complicated and wide-ranging plans!

The squadrons weren’t the only bait. The dao flags, the cultivators guarding the dao flags, the staging areas of the eastern theater... and even Immortal Monarch Silent Dao himself. They were all bait! The goal was to turn the eastern theater into a massive vortex of flesh and blood. Like a bright lantern on a dark night, it would grab the attention of the army of gods. And it would also be a cover to hide the true plan....

A cultivator with a mysterious origin, an assassin, was heading to the front lines in the Fourth Star Ring to secretly kill the commander of the gods’ eastern army, a peak True God.

Let’s see what happens first. Will you manage to isolate me here and kill me, or... will my mysterious assassin take you out?

Silent Dao’s eyes narrowed as he looked off into the distance.

Who is that mysterious cultivator...? Master picked him and trusts him. And he’s strong enough to kill a True God? There aren’t many people like that... freewebnovel.com

***

Mutagen raged in the staging areas of the eastern theater. It was getting stronger and stronger. The Transporter squadrons were shaken by all the developments. Of the more than one hundred squadrons that had come, most had suffered casualties.

Within the mutagen-filled starry sky, Xu Qing and his squadron all had very serious looks on their faces.

Sounding very grim, Zhou Zhengli said, “Based on what I can tell, about seventy percent of the squadrons... have been wiped out! Those who survived have moved in the direction of the nearest dao flags. What’s coming next is going to be a major offensive by the gods. That means we have a decision to make as well. Do we try to make it to the nearest dao flag? Or... do we keep going?”

Zhou Zhengli looked at Xu Qing. He wasn’t the only one. The other ascendees were all looking at Xu Qing.

Xu Qing surveyed the surroundings quietly. The sudden development had been surprising even to him. Things in the starry sky had changed in an instant. The immortal energy was gone, and mutagen was everywhere. He actually felt somewhat stunned.

Truth be told, he was used to being in places with a lot of mutagen. In fact, it felt familiar. It was very much like the Revered Ancient mainland. He knew that cultivators with powerful cultivation bases could resist mutagen for a time. But if they stayed in such an environment for too long, they would gradually be invaded by it.

What was more... the cultivation base required replenishment after use. And when you absorbed the energy of heaven and earth, and it contained mutagen, then eventually you would show signs of mutation.

Given all that, it seemed that searching for a dao flag wasn’t the best option. Besides, failure to find one could mean death, and he would have no control over that.

As for continuing onward.... Getting out of the staging areas and to the front lines also came with a lot of unknowns. For one thing, he had no idea what they might encounter along the way. What was more, he didn’t know how badly the front lines were infected with mutagen. There was also the possibility of getting lost.

But at least there’s a chance for survival amidst those unknowns. And I’ll have some measure of control! If I stay here, and really do find a dao flag, then it will just mean getting stuck there. And that will be an even more passive position.

After some consideration, his eyes shone with determination. His voice echoed out.

“I want to keep going. I want to reach the front lines of the eastern theater. But if the rest of you want to do something else... I won’t stop you.”

With that, he started moving onward. Li Mengtu and Zhou Zhengli followed immediately. Sir Vilespirit and Yuanshan Su hesitated briefly, during which time Sir Star Ring followed Xu Qing. Hordeslayer and Rampart gritted their teeth and did the same. Finally, Yuanshan Su joined them. Sir Vilespirit sighed inwardly and made the same choice.

As for the other ascendees, the majority made the decision to continue with Xu Qing. Some of them chose not to. Over eighty people had been with Xu Qing during the journey. For the first time, they split up.

Fifty continued on. Thirty went their own way.

It was currently impossible to say which group made the right choice.

Fighting raged in all the universes in the staging areas of the eastern theater. God armies poured forth from various locations, like unstoppable blades surrounded by mutagen. Intense fighting broke out around the dao flags in all the universes.

In some universes, the altars atop which the flags stood were reduced to ashes in an instant. The dao flags were contaminated by mutagen, and crumbled into dust. The cultivator armies in those locations were very unlucky. Some experienced mutation, some were enslaved by the gods, and some just died horrible deaths. It was a brutal scene.

However, in some universes, the altars stood strong. The dao flags continued to emit immortal energy, and the defending cultivators stood against the gods. But a price was paid. The battlefield soon reeked of blood and gore.

Taken in as a whole, the staging areas of the eastern theater were full of endless slaughter. The central army of the eastern theater arrived to provide backup. That army fought back and forth with the army of the gods. They were like dogs snapping at each other. Casualties were inflicted on both sides.

Death dirges rang out constantly! The eastern theater had turned into a brutal, blood-soaked grindstone.

As the grindstone turned, gods and cultivators alike were sucked in, their bones crushed, their flesh pulverized, their souls eradicated. Blood oozed out. And thus, everything became stained with red.

Eventually, it was like a blood-red lantern, flickering on the battlefield between the Fourth and Fifth Star Ring. Gradually... it attracted some attention. However, it was only a dimly flickering light, not enough to attract a lot of attention. The light needed to be brighter. The smell of blood and gore needed to be stronger.

More god armies arrived. More cultivator troops showed up.

Each side had different goals. But all of it served to make the fighting in the eastern theater grow more intense. There was no respect for life in war. There were only ideals and viewpoints that motivated each side to fight and kill.

To the gods, these cultivators were lower beings insulting their superiors. They were trying to overthrow the rule of the gods. If it had been something far, far away thēy might have ignored it. But the Fourth Star Ring was simply too close to the Fifth Star Ring. And the Sixth Star Ring was special. What was more, there was a new God Lord, and that meant thēy needed sacrifices. Because of that, the gods in the Fourth Star Ring had to wage war.

In contrast, the cultivators didn’t think of themselves as lower beings insulting their superiors. They were fighting for freedom. They were fighting to escape slavery. As humans, they were inherently strong-willed. Once they stood up, they would be unyielding! They would never bow down again!

And thus, the slaughter grew increasingly intense.

***

Because of the slaughter and fighting, time flowed a bit differently in the starry sky. Normally speaking, one’s frame of reference related to the planets and universes. Oftentimes, it would take days just to notice a change in the position of such heavenly bodies. In times when there was no war, traveling in the starry sky often seemed very slow-paced, as nothing around you moved. But with a war raging, and danger everywhere, it broke that illusion of stillness.

Zhou Zhengli’s hard work was paying off. His foresight didn’t just relate to matters of life or death. It related to heavenly bodies as well.

“This universe is dying,” Zhou Zhengli said grimly.

Sir Star Ring’s expression was grave. His order and balance, as well as the heaven’s principle that he had acquired in the Helioterra Universe, were all aspects of natural law. As a result, he could sense the same thing even more intensely. “Order is unraveling. Chaos is increasing.”

Xu Qing and the other fifty ascendees felt overwhelmed with danger.

“I can smell the blood...” Sir Vilespirit said. “There’s a massacre going on.”

Thanks to his broken sword, he was very sensitive to auras of death.

Everyone else instinctively looked at Xu Qing.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered. He could never have predicted that someone like himself would end up surpassing everyone else here. After all, Sir Star Ring understood order far better than him. But he was sensitive to mutagen. After all, he had dealt with mutagen from a young age. Besides, Starfire viewed mutagen the way that cultivators viewed spirit energy.

After taking a moment to assess the situation with his senses, Xu Qing said, “The mutagen here is unusually strong. The life... is proliferating dramatically.”

He offered no further explanations. He just sped on his way. Everyone else looked at him, their expressions more somber than ever.

Though he had not offered a detailed explanation, he had made things clear! The stronger the mutagen got, the more dao flags had been destroyed. For life to be proliferating indicated that more and more gods were arriving.

They really had only one option now. They had to get out of the staging areas! That was what everyone was thinking. The situation was so dangerous and serious that everyone was more determined than ever about what to do. And thus, they sped up.

Staying hidden and cautious, they continued toward the border between the staging areas and the front lines of the eastern theater. They ran into a few obstacles. But Xu Qing was like a sharp blade that could cut through anything they faced. Some people sustained injuries, but they were always able to continue onward at top speed.

Maybe they were lucky. Or maybe the gods were so focused on the dao flags that thēy didn’t bother to place many forces in the periphery of the action. Regardless, Xu Qing led everyone onward safely.

Unfortunately... they didn’t stay lucky forever. When they were very close to the border of the staging areas, only about three universes away from the front lines, they ran into something that completely halted their forward progress.

It was a squadron of gods about two hundred strong. There were many in the Godfire level, as well as Altar Gods. In leadership positions were two peak Altar Gods.

Originally, thēy had not been targeting Xu Qing and his people. Thēir original mission had been to serve as support troops. Thēy were simply passing through to serve as reinforcements for an army besieging a dao flag, to boost their morale.

But when the two Altar Gods noticed fluctuations in the surrounding mutagen, thēy didn’t hesitate to take advantage of the situation.

“Did a Transporter squad really make it this far?”

The two peak Altar Gods were actually the same species. Thēy were violet-black from head to toe, with six arms and a fiery, diamond-shaped scale on thēir foreheads. As those scales glittered, the two peak Altar Gods turned expressionlessly to look in the same direction.

“There must be something unusual about these cultivators. They shouldn’t have made it to this point.”

The two of thēm sent out messages of divine will, and thēir squadron changed directions to head toward Xu Qing and his people.

Meanwhile, Xu Qing’s pupils constricted as he sensed the mutagen stirring. Sir Star Ring, Zhou Zhengli, Sir Vilespirit, and the others all sensed the same thing shortly after.

“Some gods have locked onto us!”

“There’s an intense killing intent approaching!”

“The starry sky has been sealed!”

As everyone reacted with varying degrees of shock, Xu Qing said, “Everyone speed up!”

Acting on pure instinct, Xu Qing shot forward with greater speed. Everyone used different ways of following along.

Unfortunately, the surrounding mutagen was going wild, almost like an explosive storm that prevented them from escaping. The unique chanting of the gods filled the area. Their minds blurred, their flesh distorted, and their perceptions were overturned. They were all affected to varying degrees.

Xu Qing threw his hand up. Eyes filling with determination, he called out to Starfire. “I need to borrow your clay fox god form!”

Starfire could tell that it was a moment of crisis, and didn’t hesitate to open hēr mind and let Xu Qing’s divine will in.

Xu Qing currently had a pure immortal body. But he also had a god clone. He just hadn’t brought it to the Fifth Star Ring. But before leaving, he had gained enlightenment of a number of godly authorities. That included the godly authority of sound, the godly authority of blood, as well as his godly poison curse. And there was the godly authority of good luck, not to mention others.

The end result was that Xu Qing was not unfamiliar with gods and their godly magics. In fact, he was extremely familiar with them. The only difference was that his current body wasn’t suitable for such things. He needed a medium to be able to control mutagen! freewebnovel.com

But... things were different with Starfire’s body. That body could be a medium! With that body, Xu Qing could control mutagen.

In terms of god magics, he could imitate them perfectly using Xeno-Immortal School techniques. All in all, he wouldn’t be imitating someone else’s techniques. He would be imitating the magics of his own god body, with which he was extremely familiar.[1]

As for what happened next....

Xu Qing’s eyes glazed with an aggressive light as he stretched his hand out. It was a god technique that Xu Qing had not unleashed in the Fifth Star Ring. But now he was going all out.

The mutagen in the area surged as it became part of Xu Qing’s will. All sound in the area, including the chanting of the gods, ceased. He had seized sound as part of his god magic. Turning it around, he sent the voice of the gods back toward the gods in deadly fashion!

There was more. The mutagen in the area transformed, causing the blood of the gods to seethe. The gods that were chasing them suddenly found thēir god blood going wild. There was also a godly curse. It was a poison that struck with mountain-toppling, sea-draining force.

It was as if a new god had arrived in the world!

All gods had their own personal mutagen ready to release at any time! Mutagen was the manifestation of the aura of a god. And right now, the mutagen filling the staging areas of the eastern theater came from the aloof Gods and spirits, as well as all the other gods in the area.

And in the God Lord’s attempt to create a sense of unity among the various gods, hē had removed hīs will from hīs mutagen, which allowed it to commingle perfectly with the mutagen of the other gods. The result was that as the gods descended on the starry sky, their mutagen worked together to create a shocking godly might.

But if those gods could do that... then Xu Qing could do the same with Starfire’s clay fox body. As the two Altar Gods and thēir host of nearly two hundred god subordinates closed in on Xu Qing and his followers... his godly authority erupted.

The might of the godly authority had Starfire as the basis, but was drawn out by Xu Qing’s will. Back when Xu Qing used his god magics, he had been limited to the constraints of the Godfire level. But Starfire was an Altar God now. Combined with Xu Qing’s control using the Xeno-Immortal School techniques, his god magics were now on the level of an Altar God.

Rumbling sounds swept forth into the hearts and souls of the advancing gods. It became Xu Qing’s godly voice.

“Halt!”

The moment that word echoed out, the approaching gods’ expressions flickered. Only gods could hear that godly voice. Any cultivator who listened to it wouldn’t understand it. All they would hear was a chanting that would fill their bodies and souls with terror.

As Xu Qing spoke in his godly voice, the god blood inside of the gods seethed. Those in the Godfire level trembled. The Altar Gods immediately called on thēir own godly authority to suppress the effects. The gods immediately understood the karma at play.

But there was more. The mutagen around them went wild as a vicious god curse was unleashed. Many of the gods felt sudden sensations of intense crisis. Thēy knew that this entire situation could mean only one thing! And that was... there was a terrifying Altar God here.

However, thēy didn’t know who this Altar God was. All thēy could be certain of was that it wasn’t fake. This was a pure godly voice and true godly authority. What was more... they were full of extraordinary godly might.

The approaching gods slowed down, and the two peak Altar Gods’ eyes glittered. Thēy didn’t hesitate to unleash thēir own godly might into the area. It quickly made contact with the unfamiliar Altar God up ahead, allowing thēm to assess the mutagen at hand. Thēy quickly understood the situation.

And then the godly voice spoke again. “These humans are my prisoners of war.”

Many of the approaching gods chose to stop in place and advance no further. There were rules in place in the army of the gods. For instance, prisoners of war were considered private property. It didn’t matter how many you took, they were yours.

The two peak Altar Gods stopped in place. After all, thēy were on a reinforcement mission, not a mission to seize resources. If these humans hadn’t already been taken prisoner, thēy would obviously attack them. But if they had been taken prisoner by another god already, that was a different story. freewebnovel.com

That said, ever since this war with the Fifth Star Ring began, it had become more common for thēm to encounter situations in which gods had been enslaved. It was always possible that this group of cultivators had done that. Although it would be hard to control a god this perfectly, one of the peak Altar Gods nevertheless stepped through the void to perform a closer inspection.

When Xu Qing sensed the resulting fluctuations in the mutagen, he sighed inside. That said, it wasn’t too much of a surprise. As the Altar God approached through the void, Xu Qing’s eyes glittered coldly.

Sir Vilespirit went all out. He was blood-red from head to toe as he unleashed slaughter with his broken sword, becoming a streak of red that shot with deadly force toward the gods.

In addition to all that, the remaining ascendees from Xu Qing’s squadron, knowing how deadly the situation was, unleashed all sorts of trump cards. In the blink of an eye, the void filled with booms and shock waves. Bloody fighting raged.

Thēy didn’t react visibly in any way. It was almost as if the deaths here were inconsequential to thēm, to the point of being uninteresting.

He pulsed with the powerful aura of a god, causing godly projections to appear around him. Streams of godly authority flickered around him, manifesting a pure godly aura.

But at the same time, immortal fluctuations rolled out from him. His immortal embryo formed, gigantic and pulsing with the pure will of a cultivator. He was manifesting the traits of both gods and immortals, all at the same time! He emerged from the rift to hover in the void.

The gazes of the two peak Altar Gods instantly locked onto him. Then thēir eyes shone with golden glows, as if thēy could see Xu Qing inside and out.

“So, you enslaved a postheaven Altar God, allowing you to manifest Godfolk authority.”

“That said, godly authority this pure is rare indeed.”

“One look makes it all clear.”

The two gods spoke in very emotionless tones. Thēy didn’t seem moved at all. Thēy couldn’t have been more apathetic. This conformed to exactly what Xu Qing would expect of preheaven gods. Given his various dealings with all sorts of gods, he knew how gods could do this. It was... omniscience.

He was right. The moment he stepped out, the peak Altar Gods’ eyes glowed golden, which meant that thēy had activated thēir omniscience! And thēy weren’t just assessing his state, thēy were also attempting to see his past.... Thēy wanted to see his origin!

And that was exactly what Xu Qing had been waiting for! That was exactly why he had walked out as a mixture of immortal and god.

The power of omniscience from the two peak Altar Gods flowed forth with thēir godly might. It came with a nearly paramount pressure, which turned into an almost corporeal light that spread out over Xu Qing.

Godly might was erupting! Omniscience was being unleashed!

Xu Qing shivered. He felt like he was transparent both outside and inside. That included his fleshly body, his immortal embryo, his soul. Nothing could be hidden, not even his past!

Chaotic fighting raged in the area, but he was separated from all that. Everything slowed down, as if the operations of the world, the movement of the starry sky, and everything else was moving in slow motion.

And the two peak Altar Gods’ omniscience was slowly peeling through everything related to Xu Qing, layer by layer. Thēy were peeling away the shell of reality, and rifling through thoughts of the past. Thēy were thoroughly observing Xu Qing.

If thēy succeeded, then thēy would know everything about Xu Qing, and that would indicate... that Xu Qing would have no power to fight back against thēm. That was how the omniscience of the gods worked.

What was more, because this was coming from two peak Altar Gods working together, it would be incredibly difficult for Xu Qing to resist. And so, thēy succeeded in seeing Xu Qing’s history. By means of Xu Qing’s transparent body and soul, thēy saw the Revered Ancient mainland! On that unfamiliar landmass, thēy saw cultivators and gods. And thēy traced the origin back to Sea-Sealing County, and the subterranean palace complex there.

“This is the origin?”

The two peak Altar Gods looked thoughtful as thēy hovered on the battlefield. At the same time thēy suddenly sensed some unknowable danger.

“There’s something... wrong about this god!”

***

Gods were omniscient. But omniscience was relative. To some extent, that was actually the higher star rings’ way of protecting the gods. It made sure that they weren’t invaded by entities stronger than them. After all, superior entities weren’t subject to the omniscience of a god. They could not be sensed or perceived.

When gods looked at such things, it was akin to a mortal looking into a dark room. It wouldn’t be possible to see anything within the pitch-black.

Only people who actually lived in the darkness, and were part of it, would be able to see such things. For instance, the living things in the Revered Ancient mainland, who could simply look up into the sky.

Outside gods, however, would have no way to see or sense any such things. There could be no karma for them to root out. Theoretically speaking, even when these two Altar Gods locked down onto Xu Qing with thēir omniscience and looked into his past and his origin... thēy should have seen his god body but not the origin. The reason was that thēy should have been protected from the origin in question. Thēy should have seen only darkness.

But... someone illuminated the darkness!

The moment Xu Qing’s god clone spoke, the godly authority of fate swelled, and the tattoo on the clone’s back shone brightly. It was a tattoo of a candle! And the candle had just lit up! The light of the flame flashed, instantly becoming a sea of light around Xu Qing’s god clone. As a result, it illuminated everything around it, lighting up the darkness, as well as the omniscience of the Altar Gods....

It forced thēm to see everything! It forced thēm to look deeper into Xu Qing! It forced thēm to witness his origin! It was as Xu Qing had just said!

“Since you’re looking at this origin, you might as well look closely.”

The minds of the two peak Altar Gods reeled. Thēir god souls trembled as if immense weight were crushing down onto thēm, all as an infinitely paramount broken face... appeared within their omniscience. It was as if it had bypassed their defenses and forced them to violate a very strict taboo!

Thēir omniscience had shown them a higher being! It didn’t matter that the higher entity’s eyes were closed. The mere godly might emanating off the entity surpassed anything thēy had ever encountered in thēir lives. Anguished howls erupted from the depths of thēir god souls.

“That... that’s....”

Thēir god bodies writhed. Thēir god souls convulsed. Thēir godly authority melted. And the two peak Altar Gods were filled with unending terror and astonishment. Thēy went mad.

On the most instinctual level, thēy would pay any price possible to escape. Thēy would even burn their own bodies and sever the wills that attached thēm to this place. And that was because thēy could tell that thēy must not stay in this place under any circumstances! And thēy must not be there when this broken face’s eyes opened!

But then the broken face’s eyelashes twitched, as if those eyes were about to open!

That only caused these two Altar Gods to descend further into madness. Thēy immediately took steps to destroy thēir own godly authority and damage thēir god souls to get away. But just as thēy were about to sever the threads of will....

Golden light shone from the forehead of Xu Qing’s god clone, and a golden carving knife emerged. It was a carving knife that contained fate! The moment it appeared, it slashed toward the thread of will that was breaking apart the most quickly!

It looked like it would slash the thread in two, but when it made contact, it actually bolstered it! Fate blessed that will, and from its countless futures, it carved out an ending of death! And thus, the will that had been about to break actually became stronger. It didn’t break. The connection grew stronger, until that god... couldn’t leave!

“YOU!!!” the god shrieked in terror.

At exactly the same moment, the other Altar God’s will actually did break, and the god vanished.

Only one stream of will was left behind. And what awaited that god was the broken face hanging high in the dome of heaven over Revered Ancient. The face’s eyes opened.

Outside the phoenix palace, Xu Qing’s god clone bowed his head and murmured, “Amen!”

The will that had been left behind howled in agony, fury, and madness. Īt tried to reach Xu Qing. But before that could happen, the god became a stream of golden light. A stream of unstoppable gravitational force latched onto īt, and īt was dragged up to the mouth of the broken face.

The broken face’s eyes closed.

Xu Qing’s god clone looked up. “Sadly, I was only strong enough to stop one of them.”

***

Back on the remote edges of the Fifth Star Ring, in the staging areas of the eastern theater, near the front lines, a scream filled the starry sky. The gods all looked over at a scene that shook their god souls to the core!

Both of the two peak Altar Gods were glowing with golden light. But then, one of them went completely and utterly dark. And then, the god disappeared as if being erased from existence.

It wasn’t just the god’s body that disappeared. It was also the soul, the will... and all memories of that god. The god’s past, present, and future disappeared, along with all traces of existence.

The cultivators from the Fifth Star Ring who had seen that god, as well as the gods from the Fourth Star Ring, suddenly had no memory of hīm. That was true death. The gods and ascendees who had seen that Altar God with their own eyes suddenly forgot.

The remaining Altar God’s golden light flickered between light and dark. Hīs eyes turned gray, and hē suddenly turned to flee. Hē wanted to escape this place immediately. Hē didn’t remember hīs companion, nor what hē had seen in hīs omniscience. But the feeling of death that overwhelmed hīm caused hīm to unhesitatingly flee.

Of course, Xu Qing remembered.

As he hovered in the starry sky, his eyes flickering coldly, he said, “Execute them!”

That was a signal based on the plan they had put in place. Upon hearing it, the ascendees’ killing intent skyrocketed. The vast majority of them went all out to kill the surrounding gods.

The kelp plant emerged in full. Ten huge leaves spread out like barriers, splitting the area into two sections. On the inside was the peak Altar God. On the outside were all the other gods! The kelp’s mission was to buy time for the acsendees on the outside to kill the other gods!

Meanwhile, on the inside, Yuanshan Su’s eyes glittered coldly. The endless mountains around her unleashed unrivaled weight, which crushed down onto the fleeing Altar God, stopping hīm from fleeing. Zhou Zhengli was there too. The eye formed from his canon was bloodshot as it emitted soul-crushing weight, a gaze that could cut off the path of all souls! Next was Sir Star Ring, whose countless chains of order swept out as he unleashed heaven’s principle on the Altar God.

This was the might of judgment!
