Sir Vilespirit’s eyes were bloodshot, and his killing intent was at the pinnacle. He was under the control of the broken sword now, and he pulsed with avarice and madness as he streaked toward the Altar God in a red blur.

And Xu Qing used Starfire’s clay fox form to unleash godly authority. Taboo poison. Authority of sound. Blood authority.

***

The godly authorities complemented the ascendees perfectly as they attacked. At that critical moment, the peak Altar God acted on instinct alone to throw out god magics. Unfortunately, hē had paid a heavy price to retreat from within hīs own omniscience, and was badly injured. Next... killing intent erupted!

The tolling of a bell erupted from Xu Qing. As it thrust everything into silence, a black iron skewer emerged! Within that deathly silence, Xu Qing called on the power of his immortal embryo, the might of the immortal palace, and the trump cards of the other cultivators to form... peak strength!

The skewer shot forward! It was a single blow that could execute a god! It ripped through the void, ripped through space-time, and ripped through everything. It shot right up to the peak Altar God and stabbed right into hīs forehead!!

The starry sky shook!

The kelp plant was pushing itself to the limit. But even with the kelp’s help, the dozens of ascendees weren’t a match for so many gods.... The fighting simply wasn’t even. When Xu Qing and the other top ascendees made their move, the kelp plant could just work hard to buy time. It didn’t take long for the kelp’s sealing barrier to start breaking down. The huge leaves were battered away.

The ascendees, despite giving it their all, were so badly wounded they had to fall back.

The isolated area opened up, and the gods who had been temporarily blocked outside were able to rush inside. Except... as the gods entered one by one, they were shocked to the core.

They had already forgotten that they previously had two peak Altar Gods as their leaders. In their minds, they only had a single leader.

But that leader was in horrible condition. Hīs skin was covered with a gruish tattoo that looked like a host of mountain peaks. Those distant mountains contained an incredibly heavy canon that sealed the enemy with the power of 10,000 mountains.

Hē was also wrapped up with a host of chains, each of which glittered with the light of order, and emanated the might of heaven’s principle. Every moment that passed, the chains pulsed with the power of judgment. Hīs chest was a mangled mass, out of which grew a huge eye! The evil, bloodshot eye was the manifestation of Zhou Zhengli’s canon, which suppressed the god soul and cut off all avenues of escape!

On the god’s back was a bright red flower that was the manifestation of Li Mengtu’s canon.

Furthermore, buried in the location of his heart was a broken sword. In fact, the sword pierced right through the Altar God’s heart, where it pulsed with avarice and madness.

There was also a taboo poison curse, manifested as streams of black smoke that covered the god, invading hīm and inflicting excruciating pain.

Beyond all that, an endless voice reached their ears and echoed into their minds, rising and falling with sounds of torment. All of the blood in hīs body was flowing backward, causing the god to slowly wither in on hīmself.

But most importantly of all was the fact that an iron skewer had stabbed into hīs forehead!

Xu Qing had two iron skewers. He had left one behind in the Revered Ancient mainland, with Patriarch Golden Vajra Warrior as the spiritual soul, to stand guard over Plumdark. The other had been forged by the apprentice of Immortal Lord Nineshores in the Fifth Star Ring. It contained Xu Qing’s personal canon, so it could enter overlapping universes and form resonances with multiple space-times! It also had a mote of heaven’s principle, and given all that, the iron skewer’s personhood was extremely high. It also had immense ‘weight.’ It was a weight that even Quasi-Immortals would have to fear and respect!

It could well be said that his second iron skewer was a precious treasure of canon, and the most powerful weapon Xu Qing currently controlled! Its Infinite Timelessness was something no one could tamper with!

When it stabbed into this Altar God, it sealed space-time, cutting hīm off beyond the timescape. Hē was not in the current time! Hē was completely and utterly suppressed!

After the iron skewer stabbed into the god, it glittered brightly. And then, in front of all the other gods, the peak Altar God simply disappeared. Hē was imprisoned in Infinite Timelessness!

The gods were astonished beyond belief. After a brief moment of shocked silence, Xu Qing and the others’ killing intent raged out across the battlefield again.

This had been the plan all along. First, deal with the Altar Gods. Then, go on a rampage! One couldn’t afford blunders when fighting the gods! It was fine to shrink from a fight with them. But if you chose to do battle, you needed to kill them. You had to go all out.

That was especially true in a case like this one. After all, even though Xu Qing and the other top experts had dealt with the peak Altar Gods, the enemy still had a huge advantage. They still had a desperate fight ahead of them!

Preheaven gods had no emotions, but they did have an instinctual desire to remain alive. That obsession to live meant that they would do anything to avoid death. To truly resolve this crisis, they had to kill these cultivators despite their instinctual desire to avoid death.

In the blink of an eye, intense fighting broke out in the starry sky. Blood sprayed everywhere. The blood of gods and the blood of cultivators intermixed and flowed. The stench of gore filled the void. Slaughter turned the area into a living hell. Screams of mourning. Howls of rage. Cries of anguish. The sound of clashing magical techniques, divine abilities, and god magics. The mixture of canon and godly authority. Such things all mixed together. Mad killing took place!

Li Mengtu and Yuanshan Su were splattered with blood from severe injuries. They were nearly spent. That was especially true of Yuanshan Su, whose face was ashen. Her canon was destabilizing. Zhou Zhengli was in similarly bad shape. Blood oozed out of his eyes, ears, nose, and mouth. Sir Vilespirit trembled from head to toe. The flame of his life force was flickering weakly.

Sir Star Ring’s chains of order had lost much of their luster, and he was having a hard time controlling them. Hordeslayer and Rampart flitted about unstably. They were even reaching the point where they couldn’t curse and grumble in their hearts.

Exhaustion and injuries spread like a rising tide. God corpses were piling up, but so were the mangled limbs and disfigured corpses of ascendees. And yet... the slaughter continued.

Xu Qing was like the ambassador of death, bringing a massacre wherever he went. His space-time canon erupted, causing numerous instances of space-time to appear around him. He was like a nightmare for the gods.

But even terrifying nightmares would end upon waking. Xu Qing and his squadron were getting very tired, and thus, it seemed like that awakening would come sooner rather than later.

Thankfully... the instinct to avoid death seemed to be coming even sooner. When about half of the gods had been slaughtered, the survivors began to feel the instinct to flee, rising up from their god souls. After all, their leaders had been captured and mostly killed.

Eventually, one god turned and vanished into the void. All living things have the instinct to seek benefit and avoid harm. That was even truer of the gods. If the two peak Altar Gods were still around, they could use their status as superior gods to compel the others to fight. But now... the inherent cold apathy that existed in the bones of the gods prompted them to flee.

Soon enough, a second god disappeared. As the moments passed, it happened again and again. The gods began dispersing. The scale of the fighting grew smaller. Eventually, silence filled the battlefield. There wasn’t a single god left.

Xu Qing and the survivors hovered in the starry sky. They were completely and utterly spent, in both mind and body. What was more... their numbers had been reduced.

There were no longer over fifty of them. There were now hardly twenty. And they were in bad shape.

However, each and every survivor had an intensely baleful aura, and their eyes were the color of blood. This group had been with Xu Qing on a long journey. They had experienced the incident in the Helioterra Universe, they had seized ringsource with him, they had pillaged the god prison, and they had fought with him.

When they had been given the chance to leave with the other ascendees, they instead chose to stick with Xu Qing. Having survived to this point, they were warriors who had gone through countless trials, and all of them were now elites among elites!

Xu Qing looked around at them for a long moment, then hoarsely said, “Let’s go!”

At that point, Xu Qing stopped using the clay fox form. Turning, he shot off into the distance. No one said a thing. But at the same time, they didn’t waste any time. Turning into beams of prismatic light, they followed him. Together, they made their way off into the starry sky like a pack of wolves!

In that manner, time passed.

The fighting in the eastern theater went on. In fact, it grew more intense. Gods continued to invade from other areas. Cultivator armies that had been waiting in hiding also joined the fighting.

The eastern theater had truly become a grindstone of flesh and blood. One after another, the dao flags in various universes crumbled. Entire armies of gods transformed into corpses.

Countless cultivators were buried in the starry sky, including all of the ascendees who had left Xu Qing and the rest of the squadron. Ascendees were like seeds. But in war, they didn’t count for much. And that was because only the true seeds would end up growing! Those who died were not truly seeds.

The glow of blood grew stronger in the eastern theater. It became like a torch in the night, attracting more and more attention. It seemed as if both sides were getting closer and closer to reaching their goal.

The two peak Altar Gods who had gone missing weren’t very important at all. The fact that the small squadron of gods didn’t make it to the fighting wasn’t even noticed. When bright light shines, dust can’t be seen.

Similarly, as the light grew brighter, no one noticed Xu Qing and his exhausted squadron fleeing into the darkness. Slowly but surely, they approached the border between the staging areas and the front lines of the eastern theater.

The closer they got, the emptier the starry sky became, and the weaker the mutagen. At a certain point, the mutagen disappeared entirely, and they could sense that they were surrounded by immortal energy.

Everyone looked around in surprise. They had left the staging areas. They were now... on the front lines of the eastern theater!

Off in the distance, they could see the massive ramparts that had been erected by the magical techniques of the cultivators. The ramparts went on forever and ever, glittering with bright light.

“We’re finally here,” Zhou Zhengli murmured. His eyes were bloodshot, and he was badly wounded.

For the most part, it was the same with everyone. As they looked at the distant cultivator ramparts, they breathed sighs of relief.

The starry sky here was dazzling, and because the dao flags were all in place, there was no mutagen. The immortal energy was strong. Because of that immortal energy, Xu Qing and the rest of the squadron felt their injuries starting to heal even faster than before. That said, they still weren’t completely safe, so they continued moving forward toward the protective magical techniques.

About two hours later, they were very close to the ramparts. That was when a vast stream of divine will emerged from the ramparts and covered them. Along with the will came a flabbergasted voice.

“Who goes there?”

It spoke into the minds of Xu Qing and the others like heavenly thunder, forcing them to stop in place.

Xu Qing stepped forward. “We’re a squadron from the Department of Acquisitions in the Nineshores Heaven, here on orders from Immortal Lord Nineshores to deliver the ringsource we have acquired to the front lines!”

The border between the staging areas of the eastern theater and the front lines consisted of magnificent, never-ending ramparts. The walls glittered with dazzling light as they spanned galaxies and universes. They served to completely isolate the staging areas from the front lines.

At a certain point along those endless ramparts, Xu Qing’s hoarse voice rang out. The exhaustion in his voice matched the exhaustion that the eighteen surviving members of his squadron couldn’t hide. They stood there quietly as the majestic will from the ramparts scanned them. And they could sense their identity medallions responding to the inspection.

From a distance, they were insignificant in comparison to the ramparts. After their identities had been verified, the will slowly retracted. Then the walls rippled, and an opening appeared. It was a small path.

On the other side of the path, beyond the opening, were over a hundred cultivators, just barely visible, but clearly looking closely at the group. They seemed surprised.

Xu Qing took little note of their facial expressions. He could guess why they were reacting this way. We’re probably the only squadron that made it through.

Without any hesitation, Xu Qing flew onto the path, followed by Zhou Zhengli and everyone else. After they were all on the path, the opening disappeared, and the ramparts went back to the way they were before, glittering and impassable.

***

Inside the ramparts was gentle starlight and strong immortal energy.

After Xu Qing and everyone was present, the more than one hundred cultivators unblurred, making their facial features and expressions clear. Their gazes were those of astonishment and curiosity, leaving Xu Qing and the others feeling like they were rare oddities.

Xu Qing became more convinced than ever of his theory. Looking at the assembled cultivators, he said, “Where do we hand over the ringsource?”

A middle-aged cultivator in black armor stepped forth, looked them over, and finally fixed his gaze on Xu Qing.

“The lieutenant general has summoned you. My squadron will escort you there safely.”

Xu Qing’s heart thumped in his chest. Given his previous experience in cultivator wars, he knew a bit about how the departments and ranks worked.

He was aware that Immortal Lord Deepgloom was in charge of the war effort, and made major strategic decisions. Beneath him were three ministers of war, who commanded the three major war zones, those being the eastern theater, the central theater, and the western theater. Responsibilities in each of the theaters was divided among several lieutenant generals.

In this part of the front lines of the eastern theater, the highest-ranking officer would be the lieutenant general. And now, right as they had arrived, he had summoned them for an audience. This just seemed to confirm Xu Qing’s theory.

Sir Star Ring and the others exchanged glances. Zhou Zhengli’s spirits seemed to lift.

Finally, Xu Qing said, “We shall follow the orders of the lieutenant general!”

The middle-aged cultivator nodded slightly. Then, after a moment of consideration, he instructed some of his subordinate cultivators to give some healing medicinal pills to Xu Qing and his people. After that, they blurred into motion.

Xu Qing and his people followed. And thus, under the protection of this group of cultivators, they made their way through the front lines of the eastern theater toward the lieutenant general’s camp.

After their journey through multiple universes, via many teleportations, moving through the front lines seemed like looking at a scroll painting. Along the way, they saw numerous heavenly bodies being gathered to serve as tents. They were packed densely and were too numerous to count.

Some heavenly bodies were being dragged across a swirling whirlpool that seemed like rivers, which tugged at the starlight to create a dazzling scene. The flame of the life force within them was astounding, and pulsed with an energy that left Xu Qing and the others shocked.

There were also terrifyingly huge dharma statues trudging through the starry sky, dao flags hoisted behind their backs. They pulsed with terrifying pressure as they went about various missions.

Xu Qing also saw numerous suns. Each sun had a huge face on it that seemed to absorb the heat and fire of the sun and turned it into nutrients. After taking in enough nutrients, the faces would fly up and transform into dazzling butterflies that flapped their wings and flew off into distant parts of the starry sky.

Overall, the cultivators seemed to be waiting in combat readiness. The mood was solemn.

If Xu Qing and his squadron had been sent directly to the front lines, they would probably be impressed. But they had just gone through the staging areas and experienced chaos and slaughter. So though these sights were intriguing, they were not shocking. After all, they had gone through a mish-mash of mutagen and immortal energy to get here, not to mention the grindstone of flesh and blood. As a result, this place seemed more like the rear echelon.

As they went along, Xu Qing and his squadron saw a lot of cultivators. Some stuck to themselves, but others stayed in groups. Everyone had responsibilities, and everything was very orderly. The vast majority of cultivators, after noticing Xu Qing and his group, stared at them as they passed.

Xu Qing and his squadron noticed but didn’t react. As they proceeded, they could sense a faint force of rejection coming from the starry sky. It seemed to indicate that they were guests here at the front lines, and had not been completely accepted.

About half a month later, they reached the heavenly body occupied by the lieutenant general.

It was an extremely bright, red-colored sun. It was larger than any sun Xu Qing had ever seen, so much so that the suns from his Inksun Universe seemed like dust in comparison.

It seemed unstable, as if it was constantly sucking in things from the void around it, all while simultaneously ejecting things at top speed. The result was that there was something like a cloud surrounding it. The pressure weighing down on it distorted the starry sky. The starlight in the area bent as if unable to sustain the force. The end result was that the sun seemed like it might explode at any moment and unleash terrifying power. Strangely, the sun actually wasn’t as intensely hot as one might expect.

“That’s a dying sun,” Zhou Zhengli said quietly. “It’s already gone through its primary life cycle, and has become a red giant!”

Everyone else looked at it, their hearts pounding in astonishment. The cultivators who had escorted them on the journey looked deeply at Xu Qing and the others, then clasped hands and left.

Soon, only Xu Qing and his squadron were left in front of the red giant. As the pressure from it weighed down on them, Xu Qing solemnly bowed to it, as did Sir Star Ring and the others.

“Our Acquisitioner squad has come to offer greetings, Lieutenant General!”

Rumbling sounds echoed out from the red giant, and a terrifying aura spread out. The surrounding clouds seethed. Then a black palace appeared, slowly emerging from the red giant into the clouds. A frigid coldness spread from the palace into the starry sky, along with streams of divine will that settled onto Xu Qing and his people.

It was another inspection. Each and every stream of divine will caused Xu Qing and everyone else to shiver mentally. It was immortal will!

The final stream... caused all the others to dim, as if it was far superior to them. Along with it came a calm voice from the hall of the palace.

“You’re the first group, and perhaps the only group, to make it here to deliver the ringsource you acquired. As such, I don’t want to forcibly probe your souls to see what you went through. Instead, I’d like you to simply explain. Tell me how you managed to escape that grindstone of flesh and blood.”

Sir Star Ring and the others instantly got nervous. The use of the word ‘escape’ seemed ominous. They looked at Xu Qing.

Xu Qing’s mind raced. But in the end, he chose to simply tell the truth. And so, he explained their experiences along the way, including why they made the decisions they did. He didn’t go into explicit detail, he just stuck to the basics.

After hearing Xu Qing’s explanation, the divine will of the lieutenant general said nothing. However, one of the other streams of immortal will spoke.

“It must not have been easy for your group to stick together through so many setbacks, and in the end, still reach this point to deliver your ringsource. It counts as a great service. Although the lieutenant general doesn’t wish to probe you with divine will, when it comes to the peak Altar God you encountered... do you have proof to back your claim?”

Xu Qing’s heart and mind stirred. On the surface, it seemed like their story was being questioned. But after everything Xu Qing had experienced in life, he could tell that there was a deeper meaning to the words. Their successful journey counted as a meritorious service, but at the same time, they were being asked to prove what they had done.

The real reason for this caused Xu Qing to look at the surviving members of his squadron. Ascendees all had important backgrounds. For any of them to reach this point would require significant backers, and those backers were now more important than ever.

The key to the whole thing is how he mentioned ‘sticking together.’

After some thought, Xu Qing waved his hand. His canon rippled, and Infinite Timelessness opened. The imprisoned peak Altar God was now visible for everyone to see. It was possible to see wounds inflicted by various types of canon. And the iron skewer embedded in the god’s forehead pulsed with fluctuations of suppression. This explained everything.

Xu Qing immediately said, “I could not have captured this peak Altar God on my own. We worked together!”

Suddenly, Xu Qing heard laughter. It was the lieutenant general in the palace.

“You’re an interesting bunch, I’ll give you that. You experienced a lot of twists and turns crossing the field of battle. It was obviously extremely difficult to deliver the ringsource and accomplish your mission. It definitely counts as a major service.

“Slaughtering a host of gods and capturing a peak Altar God counts as further service. Well then... you might as well stay here in the eastern theater army.”

As the lieutenant general’s voice echoed out, the red giant rumbled, and the black palace sank back down into its depths. All that remained behind was a command medallion that flew over and hovered in front of Xu Qing.

There was also a final bit of divine will that said, “Go to Planet Spirit Restoration and wait for an assignment.”

Xu Qing and the others bowed their heads.

“Yes, sir, Lieutenant General!”

Xu Qing reached out and took the medallion. As soon as he did, the force of rejection from the starry sky vanished. They were no longer just guests.

Xu Qing breathed a sigh of relief. So did Zhou Zhengli, Sir Star Ring, and everyone else. They exchanged glances. Given all that they had experienced, they now felt relief. They had been turned from Acquisitioners into Transporters, and had been sent to the field of battle. That mission had been accomplished.

They had paid a heavy price. They had started out more than a hundred strong. Now... they didn’t even have twenty.

“This is how ascendees are trained,” Zhou Zhengli said quietly. “Only those who survive until the very end can truly become dao seeds.”

After Xu Qing took the medallion, he then handed over the ringsource. Then they left the red giant and disappeared into the starry sky.

After they were gone, the huge red sun continued to emit both mist and bright light. Inside of the sun, in the ancient, pitch-black palace, a sigh drifted out.

“I never imagined the pawns would actually manage to cross the river. And they’re ascendees. Now that I’ve seen them personally, I guess it’s not too surprising they made it this far. The question is whether or not any of them have the potential to become true dao seeds. Or... are they just pale imitations.[1]

“It’s the same with us, after all. With the exception of the esteemed general, all of us are ascendees, and we’re still finding our path. It’s been many years since the Immortal Paragon’s decree, and though immortals like us have proliferated, there has yet to be any new Immortal Lord.”

More sighs could be heard in the palace hall. As time passed, none of the immortals there said anything.

Eventually, the lieutenant general spoke in a hoarse voice. “It’s easy to start a new endeavor. But it’s not as easy to keep it going. That’s how things work in the mortal world, and it’s the same with cultivators in the Fifth Star Ring.”

The immortals present all understood that truth. In fact, they understood it better than most.

It was especially true in the Fifth Star Ring. In the past, the star ring had been controlled by gods, and ruled by a God Paragon. Eventually, the Immortal Paragon struggled into prominence, leading humans from a minor world to carve out a path for cultivators and a dao for immortals. They advanced step by step through countless hardships and tribulations, slaughtering minor worlds and gods along the way.

Ultimately, they crushed the God Paragon, imprisoned the God Lords, and severed the origins of all gods. They enslaved countless members of the Godfolk, and hewed out twelve heavens beyond heaven in the Fifth Star Ring.

Then, in the very middle of it all, they enshrined the Immortal Capital with its crucial mission. And that mission was to eventually turn all of the thirty-six higher star rings into places like the Fifth, in other words, places that belonged to humans and cultivators!

There was no way a task like that could be described as easy. No, it was something extremely difficult! And even more difficult than starting such a task was to continue working on it long-term.

And that was especially true... considering that the person who was originally supposed to be the second Immortal Paragon had perished. Immortal Lord Aurora. When he died, it cast doubt on the future of the entire Fifth Star Ring. After all... with the exception of the Fifth Star Ring and a couple of other very special star rings, all star rings were the home of gods. And though the Fifth Star Ring seemed like a place bursting with life and activity, the reality was that it was already past its zenith and on the decline.

The only way to change that was for a second Immortal Paragon to rise up in the Fifth Star Ring! Before another Immortal Paragon could rise up, there needed to be another Immortal Lord. And that was the reason for all the rigorous training the ascendees went through over all the years.

It was a brutal arrangement. Fostering cultivators who eventually ascended from the Immortal Capital was a process similar to raising venomous bugs in a jar. It didn’t matter what fate or karma had in store, those who died were considered nothing but imitations. Those who lived were the true dao seeds! And those who continued on to the end would be kindred spirits in philosophy!

“I just hope the day will come soon. It doesn't matter which generation that person comes from, as long as they’re human and as long as they’re a cultivator.”

***

Time passed as Xu Qing and the others remained on the front lines of the eastern theater.

In a flash, three months went by. During that time, the grindstone of flesh and blood continued to turn, casting red light onto all of the battlefields in the eastern theater. Xu Qing and the others didn’t know how the war was faring overall. However, the ebb and flow of events on the front lines gave them an idea of how things were going.

The action in the staging areas was reaching a critical point. That much was clear because of the lack of movement among the military forces on the front lines.

On a snowy mountain full of immortal energy on Planet Spirit Restoration, Xu Qing and the rest were gathered around a fire pit.

Snow drifted down calmly from above as Zhou Zhengli said, “It indicates the event is almost complete. Based on the information I’ve been able to gather, there are more small-scale clashes with gods on the true front lines. It seems likely that we’ll be getting our mission soon. That’s the extent of what I’ve been able to learn.”

The snow brought cold with it. However, the heat from the fire pit melted the snow, creating a mist that filled the area.

They were surrounded by snowy mountains in all directions. In fact, if one took in Planet Spirit Restoration as a whole, they would see that it was full of numerous snowy mountains. There were a lot of them. Atop every single mountain, there was a fire pit blazing with red fire. The flames danced, letting out both heat as well as something else very mysterious. Whatever that mysterious power was, it helped cultivators to recover from injuries and rebuild strength.

After spending three months on the planet, Xu Qing and the others had long since recovered. In fact, they had only stayed atop the mountain for the first month. After that, they had scattered, and had spent two months in other places, only returning at specific times to touch bases. Today was their third time meeting up again.

After Zhou Zhengli was done speaking, Li Mengtu took a turn. “The information I got led me in a different direction than Zhou Zhengli. I wanted to find out if anyone else made it through the staging areas in the last few months. None did.”

Li Mengtu knew he wasn’t very good at digging for information, so he had chosen a much simpler task. When he was done with his report, he looked around at the others. Whenever they regrouped, they would share any information they had uncovered, then come up with a new plan before parting ways again. In that way, they were able to gain an understanding of the front lines much more quickly.

Yuanshan Su, Sir Vilespirit, Hordeslayer, Rampart, and everyone else took turns sharing what they had learned.

Finally it was Sir Star Ring’s turn. He looked at Xu Qing. “I looked into those people you mentioned last time we met up, and I learned a thing or two.”

Xu Qing turned to look at Sir Star Ring.

Of course, Xu Qing had gone out just like the rest of them, and had used his own methods of getting information on the front lines. At a certain point, he had noticed some cultivators who seemed to belong to a special army organization. They seemed similar to the Department of Acquisitions, but were very secretive and had very few dealings with anyone outside of their organization.

As a result, Xu Qing wasn’t able to interact with them much. However, he was very curious about them, and had let everyone else know they should pay attention and try to get information if they could.

“They form an auxiliary force in the army, made up of fifty squadrons. They operate on the front lines, specifically, in locations where battles are fought with the gods. They’re called... the Corpsedrainer Division! Their mission is simple. They clear battlefields. They go to front line positions where the bodies of dead gods are located, and they collect ringsource and other loot.

“Similar to Acquisitioners, they can keep a bit for themselves. The more battles are fought, the more active they are. That’s been especially true over the last month, as there have been a lot of skirmishes with the Fourth Star Ring forces. Virtually all of their forces have been sent in that direction.” Looking closely at Xu Qing, Sir Star Ring said, “Why exactly did you want us to pay attention to them?”

Xu Qing looked around thoughtfully at the small group. They had gone through a lot together, so he was very familiar with them at this point.

“It’s been three months since we handed in our ringsource and got sent here to rest and recover,” he said. “During that time, the lieutenant general hasn’t made any arrangements for us.... So I was thinking that, instead of waiting for an assignment, we could take the initiative and find something to do.... Maybe we could even apply for a specific position.

“I’ve almost run out of ringsource to use for cultivation. I’m guessing you’re all in similar positions, right? If we don’t replenish our stock, it’ll affect our cultivation progress.”

In response, Sir Star Ring’s eyes glittered, Zhou Zhengli smiled faintly, Sir Vilespirit licked his lips, and the brothers Hordeslayer and Rampart emitted faint sounds like the humming of swords. Even the normally reserved Yuanshan Su seemed excited. The other ascendees reacted similarly. Their baleful auras pulsed, causing the snowflakes in the sky to turn black.

Li Mengtu was the first to speak. “That’s exactly what I’ve been wanting to do!”

He seemed to have given voice to what everyone was thinking, as their eyes glowed like wolves in a wolf pack. All of these people had fought tooth and nail to ascend from the Immortal Capital. They had gone through all sorts of deadly training, and were like blood fiends who were ruthless to the core. In the three months that had passed, they had been hard-pressed to remain patient. It was only natural that they responded enthusiastically to Xu Qing’s suggestion.

Seeing their reaction prompted a nod from Xu Qing. Not wanting to waste any time, he stood and solemnly took out the command medallion from the lieutenant general. Then his immortal embryo glittered as he sent some immortal will into the medallion. It became a dao voice that caused the medallion to tremble.

“This is Xu Qing, leader of the former Acquisitioner squadron and now Transporter squadron. I would like to submit a petition to the lieutenant general. My squadron is fully recovered and well-rested. We’re in peak condition now. We have been emboldened by seeing our fellow soldiers slaying gods on the front lines, and would thus like to submit an application for a new mission....

“We are willing to go to the battlefields of the front line as a Corpsedrainer squadron. We... would like to continue our previous mission of acquiring ringsource!”

Everyone else stood in anticipation.

However, there was no response from the command medallion. Xu Qing’s immortal will disappeared like a stone ox thrown into the ocean. Everyone, including Xu Qing, stood there waiting patiently.

About an hour passed.... Then the medallion vibrated. Red light shot out from it, surrounding them, and along with it came a stream of majestic immortal will.

“Approved!”

“Yes, sir, Lieutenant General!” Xu Qing said loudly.

Everyone else voiced the same words. The red light shone into the wind and snow like the rising sun!

1. The pawns/river is a reference to Chinese chess. Note: Chinese chess, transliterated xiangqi, translated “elephant chess,” is NOT the game of Go! Go is transliterated weiqi and is directly translated as “encirclement chess,” and it has simple black and white stones that you use to carve out territory on the board. In contrast, Chinese chess (xiangqi) has pieces that correlate to members of an army, similar to international chess. One big difference in Chinese chess is that there’s a ‘river’ in the middle of the board. When a pawn crosses the river, it usually signifies a big change in the game. For one thing, the pawn gains additional abilities when it crosses the river. Beyond that, crossing the river usually signifies an advancement beyond the opening or middlegame. Incidentally, nowadays Chinese chess is much more popular and common than Go. You will see people (usually old guys) playing the game on the street or in the park. Even in overseas Chinese communities, the game is popular. Back when I lived in Chinatown in Manhattan, I remember seeing old dudes playing the game in the park all the time. In fact, here’s a picture I took in a Chinatown park in around 2009 of a bunch of guys gathered around a Chinese chess game. ☜

The war was heating up in the eastern theater. Fighting was breaking out all over the place. Sparks flew. The scale of the fighting wasn’t very large. Most battles were skirmishes involving about a thousand combatants. But the number of battles was growing.

Of course, war had to be judged as a whole. And there was a reason for everything that was happening. It didn’t matter if it was large-scale battles or minor skirmishes, they all played out for specific reasons. And if those various goals were met, then it would build up momentum to reach the biggest goal of all. That was the essence of war. It was like a game.

For example, the information brought in by Xu Qing and everyone else seemed to point to the same conclusion: the event in the staging areas of the eastern theater was over. At the same time, more skirmishes were breaking out on the front lines. Given that... the goal was obvious.

Both gods and cultivators were using the skirmishes to hide their true motives! At the moment, as sparks were flying because of all the skirmishes, there was one battlefield located in an asteroid belt.

The fighting was bloody. Taking in the scene as a whole, rumbling booms echoed out, rubble sprayed everywhere, and mutagen clashed with immortal energy constantly. One side was making an incursion. The other side was trying to stop them. It was a very intense situation.

Beyond the periphery of the fighting, amongst some scattered asteroids, a group of people was observing the battlefield. There were a few hundred of them, all wearing gray and black garments. They looked like vultures, their eyes glittering as they kept a close eye on their surroundings. Clearly, they were ready to fall back if the fighting got too close to them.

One of them, an old man, was talking to some cultivators standing around him.

“I was right, eh? I knew this fight wouldn’t end quickly. My guess is that it’ll keep going for at least another hour. You know, if I hadn’t noticed you a few months ago, and also sensed your command medallion just now, I wouldn’t have called you over here.”

The cultivators around him all had baleful auras that were surprising even to him. That was especially true of their leader, who had the strongest baleful aura of all.

“You know, you’re actually pretty famous for getting through the staging areas to the front lines. But since you’re part of the Logistics Division now, there are some things you need to understand.”

The people around him were, of course, Xu Qing and the other ascendees. After their request for a mission was approved, they had been assigned to this location, and had arrived only about four hours ago. However, before they could get close to the battlefield, this old man had stopped them.

He was also a Corpsedrainer. Being aware of who Xu Qing and the other ascendees were, he had shown them some goodwill by inviting them over.

In response to his words, Xu Qing and Sir Star Ring exchanged a glance, then clasped hands, bowed, and sincerely asked for more information.

The old man nodded. “Technically speaking, we’re part of the Logistics Division. But that’s just the official, nice-sounding version of what we are. As you know, everybody calls us Corpsedrainers!

“Considering we clean up after battles, it only makes sense that we have to wait until the fighting is over before we start working. If we didn’t, then we wouldn’t be Corpsedrainers. We would be actually fighting in the war! Remember, the fighting is done by the army cultivators. We don’t take part. We only go in after the fighting! freewebnovel.com

“That’s because... if we went in too soon, it could affect the strategy and tactics of the army cultivators. What’s more, part of our mission is to make sure that our army cultivators have a path of retreat if they suffer a defeat!”

The old man clearly took his responsibilities very seriously.

Xu Qing and everyone else nodded solemnly. Truth be told, they hadn’t intended to go onto the battlefield. They had just wanted to get close enough to be in the position to get ringsource as quickly as possible. After all, they believed themselves to be quite skilled at acquiring ringsource.

They had quite a bit of experience due to their time in the Department of Acquisitions. During that time, they had managed to meet all their quotas, but had also been able to siphon off plenty of ringsource for their own use. The difference was that they had taken ringsource from living targets before. This would be their first time harvesting it from dead gods.

When the old man saw how attentive Xu Qing and the others were being, he relaxed a bit and cleared his throat.

“Everything I just said is the official position of the army. In reality, we don’t really need to guard the escape routes. And if we do go onto the battlefield, there’s almost no chance we would affect the army.

“Now I’ll tell you the real deal. The truth is that we don’t want to go onto the battlefield too early because, for all we know, it might get us killed. Once the fighting starts to wrap up, things are a lot safer. Of course, it’s hard to predict how things will end in war, so we need to always be ready to evacuate if our side ends up losing.

“You lot are just too young and inexperienced. If I hadn’t stopped you just now, you would have gone too close to the fighting, and that would have put you in a lot of danger. Another thing you should keep in mind is that you should never get into conflicts with the army cultivators, as—”

All of a sudden, Xu Qing’s expression flickered. He, along with Sir Star Ring and the others, all looked over at the battlefield. The old man stopped talking and did the same. They saw a huge swell of immortal energy, and could hear cheering. Then a dao flag was hoisted up.

“Victory!” the old man said, his eyes lighting up. Not bothering to go into any further detail about the rules, he shot forward. “Let’s get to work, everybody!”

As he led the way, the squadron under his command flew forward like vultures who had spread their wings. Xu Qing and the others followed. In short order, they slashed into the asteroid belt like sharp blades.

Within the rubble, they saw god corpses and god blood everywhere, as well as severed limbs and destroyed treasures. There were quite a few cultivator corpses as well.

The cultivator army had already moved on, although a few warriors had remained behind to collect ringsource. The old man and his subordinates didn’t seem surprised by that. They didn’t even glance at the warriors as they swarmed over the unattended corpses. Some cut things apart, some focused on collections, some stored up the gains. They worked together smoothly and with great speed. They were obviously very used to this. Only a few dozen breaths later, they had already cleared much of the battlefield.

The god corpses were collected up, but the cultivator corpses were treated with great respect.

Xu Qing and the others looked on with astonishment. Zhou Zhengli and the other top ascendees suddenly felt great respect. There was no doubt that the old man and his subordinates had pushed their harvesting skills to the point of perfection! Their speed was nothing short of stupefying.

“These people are on a different level when it comes to looting corpses,” someone said. “They’re totally beyond us!”

Xu Qing and the others exchanged glances, then hurried onto the battlefield to start working.

Despite having a background in the Department of Acquisitions, compared to the old man and his people, they couldn’t compete in terms of speed and thoroughness. Furthermore, these gods were dead, so the ringsource in them wasn’t very active. The levels were also much lower than in living gods, which meant that it took a lot of work.

Thankfully, there were plenty of corpses. Obviously, getting a lot of ringsource would involve dealing with a lot of corpses. The Corpsedrainers had their own set of rules. Once someone started working on the corpse of a god, no one would interfere, even if they were taking a long time.

Xu Qing realized that quickly, and made sure to abide by the rules.

And yet, there were still conflicts. They weren’t conflicts between Corpsedrainers, but with the army cultivators. The army cultivators were bossy and domineering, and when it came to collecting the corpses, they were rude and unreasonable. They didn’t make any attempt to hide their disdain of the Corpsedrainers. It made sense considering that their army was the one who had killed these gods....

But there were official arrangements for the resources and battle trophies of war, so there was no grounds for the army cultivators to do much. What usually happened was that after army forces won a battle and moved on, they would leave some people behind to collect some loot, all for the purpose of keeping morale up. Such practices were tacitly approved of.

The Corpsedrainers were used to it, and would usually just rely on their speed to make up for the difference. Xu Qing and the ascendees had just started as Corpsedrainers, so they were clearly not as fast as the others. As a result, they were the first ones the army cultivators targeted.

A few hours later, the massive battlefield was almost totally cleared. The corpses of the cultivators had been attended to properly, and taken away by the army. The corpses of the gods had been collected, with the old man and the Corpsedrainers getting about sixty percent of them. The army cultivators got about thirty percent. The final ten percent... went to Xu Qing and the ascendees.

When the battlefield was cleared, the army cultivators left. Xu Qing and the ascendees were left muttering a bit discontentedly.

Seeing that, the old man came over with a broad smile on his face. “You don’t seem too happy. Feel like you got robbed? You’ll figure things out soon enough. In the end, they did kill these gods, so it’s not unusual at all for them to take some of the corpses. Things will get better for you as you learn to go faster.”

With that, the old man bade farewell and led his subordinates away.

Xu Qing and the ascendees were now alone in the asteroid belt. They didn’t feel any less discontent.

The old man had misjudged them. Their discontent wasn’t because they had performed poorly or were angry. It was true that the army had slain these gods, so it was completely justifiable for them to take the corpses as loot. After all, if the ascendees were in that position, they would be irritated if other people showed up and took the corpses of the gods they had slaughtered. No, they were discontent for a different reason....

“We’re not as fast as the other Corpsedrainers, and we have no right to get in arguments with the army cultivators....”

“Since the Corpsedrainers can only start working after the fighting is over....”

“Maybe we should just go onto the battlefield earlier.”

Everyone exchanged glances, and their eyes were glittering.

The same mysterious light glittered in the eyes of Xu Qing and all the ascendees. They had not done well in this, their first time clearing a battlefield. After they handed in their Corpsedrainer quota, they would hardly have any ringsource left for cultivation purposes.

Everyone slowly looked over at Xu Qing. They were waiting for his final decision.

He scanned the empty battlefield, and then the distant starry sky. Finally, he said, “Entering the field of battle early is definitely an option. But we need to find the right opportunity. And we need to make sure we have a clear assessment of the battle prowess of both sides. Things can change very quickly on the battlefield, and if our timing is wrong, we could end up in a deadly situation. After all, we're not strong enough yet to be able to crush all opposition.”

Xu Qing suppressed the urge to be impulsive. He knew that this was a situation in which hasty decisions weren’t a good idea.

The glow in the eyes of the other ascendees began to fade.

However, that was when Sir Vilespirit licked his lips and said, “Captain... the truth is we’re better at dealing with living gods than dead ones! You can harvest more ringsource from the live ones....”

The glow returned to the eyes of the ascendees. They understood what Sir Vilespirit was getting at. He was suggesting they start hunting gods. They were also thinking about the god prisons they had been to.

When Xu Qing heard someone calling him ‘Captain,’ it left him feeling a bit dazed. It was actually the first time anyone had addressed him that way so far. I wonder what Eldest Brother is up to right now...

Meanwhile, Sir Star Ring said, “You can’t accomplish anything without rules. We’re not Acquisitioners anymore. We’re Corpsedrainers.”

Sir Vilespirit’s eyes glittered as he coldly replied, “And can you really do better than those other Corpsedrainers? They got sixty percent of the corpses! Sir Star Ring, your ‘order’ isn’t going to help at all when it comes to draining corpses!”

Sir Star Ring glared back coldly at Sir Vilespirit. Sir Vilespirit wasn’t about to shrink in the face of that, so he pulsed with a baleful aura and faint Quasi-Immortal fluctuations. Everyone had improved to certain degrees recently. As for Sir Vilespirit, he had broken through into the Quasi-Immortal level. As the two ascendees glared at each other, Xu Qing looked at Zhou Zhengli.

Zhou Zhengli cleared his throat, stepped forward to stand between Sir Star Ring and Sir Vilespirit, and then bowed to Xu Qing.

“Your Majesty, we know your primary concern is keeping us alive. But we’ve made it all the way here to the battlefield. We’ve gone through a lot, and we know that rewards come only with risk. As long as the potential gains are worth it, we don’t mind taking risks. In fact, that’s the best way to get what we need.

“Therefore, what Fellow Daoist Vilespirit just said about targeting the living is true. But so is what Fellow Daoist Star Ring said about rules. I think we could probably find a compromise here.”

Zhou Zhengli licked his lips and continued, “We’re Corpsedrainers, sure. But if we hunted down some gods and turned them into dead bodies, then collected them, well... that wouldn’t be a conflict, would it? We don’t have to look for a battlefield, we can make one. We don’t have to look for corpses, we can make them.”

With that, Zhou Zhengli bowed again to Xu Qing. Sir Vilespirit's eyes glittered as he also bowed. The other ascendees said nothing, but their eyes glittered as they, too, bowed. Sir Star Ring thought about it for a moment, then nodded and looked at Xu Qing.

Xu Qing looked around at them. He knew that everyone present had their own goals and motives. What was more, they were not greenhouse flowers. They had been born amidst foul winds and raining blood. They were running out of ringsource and were getting antsy to devour gods. Given all that....

Xu Qing’s eyes flashed with determination, and he nodded. In response, the other ascendees smiled like wolves that had been let out of their cages. Zhou Zhengli made some final arrangements, and then they scattered. They would use their own various talents to try to find targets, and would send information back for Zhou Zhengli and Sir Star Ring to consider.

As for Xu Qing, he sat down cross-legged on an asteroid to wait.

Half a month passed by. Information continued to pour in from the various ascendees. All of it related to the activities of various gods. However, the vast majority of situations didn’t seem suitable to Xu Qing. Either there were too many gods present, or the scenarios were just too risky.

Roughly a week passed. That was when one of the ascendees named Daoist Bloodcloud sent information about a situation that seemed promising. Sir Star Ring and Zhou Zhengli studied the message to confirm its authenticity, then forwarded the information to Xu Qing.

“Captain, I found a team of scouts about thirty in number. The most powerful is a mid Altar God. Thēy’re definitely Godfolk. I’ve been secretly following thēm for about two days. Thēy come in all shapes and sizes, and thēy seem perfect for our purposes!”

Xu Qing considered it. Then his baleful aura surged as he sent out orders. After that, he stepped out into the void and disappeared. The other ascendees in different areas got the orders, whereupon their eyes glittered. And then, like a pack of vicious wolves, they raced toward the location.

A few days later, near a planet called Graytomb, Xu Qing and the ascendees met up. Daoist Bloodcloud had been waiting for them there. As Xu Qing arrived, flanked by Sir Star Ring and Zhou Zhengli, Daoist Bloodcloud bowed.

“Captain, this group of gods is well-hidden. However, I happen to have a special magic that lets me sense thēm. I followed thēm here, and this is where thēy’ve been for the past few days. In order to avoid detection, I didn’t go onto the planet. But I'm certain that’s where thēy are.”

Sir Star Ring nodded. “I can sense great chaos in the area.”

Zhou Zhengli licked his lips and smiled. “Your Majesty, my canon is informing me that thēy’re still there.”

If the information had been coming from Daoist Bloodcloud alone, Xu Qing would have wanted further proof. But since Sir Star Ring and Zhou Zhengli were corroborating the details, it seemed much more likely to be accurate. As Xu Qing looked at the planet, his immortal embryo stirred, and his canon of space-time spread out. In that way, he was able to confirm the situation on his own as well.

“We strike quickly,” he said in a cold voice. “Collect the ringsource as fast as possible. Everybody... let’s go!”

The ascendees surged with baleful auras as they rushed toward the planet. Over a dozen beams of light shot through the clouds and headed toward the gods at top speed. Xu Qing was among them, and he was going all out to approach the target destination.

There were over thirty gods present, including the Altar God. And upon nearing, the ascendees were able to see what thēy were doing. Thēy were performing some sort of ceremony around an octagonal altar.

Astonishingly, there was a black bowl in the middle of the table. Inside the bowl was blood, and it was bubbling as if boiling. The boiling blood was causing an intense mutagen to form. And it seemed to be building up toward some sort of detonation point.

When Xu Qing and the ascendees arrived, the gods looked up in surprise.

The Altar God’s pupils constricted. “The god altar isn’t complete. The ceremony hasn’t started. The mutagen hasn’t erupted. The foundation is still forming. How could cultivators have shown up already??”

The Altar God was surprised, but acted decisively. Godly authority flared, causing the unfinished altar to burst into flames early. The black bowl of blood suddenly shattered. Massive amounts of mutagen spilled out like roiling black smoke. It was supposed to infect everything in the area. Unfortunately, it wasn’t strong enough, so the effect wasn’t as good as it should have been, making it unclear whether or not a new battlefield could form here.... However, hē had no other options.

At almost the exact same instant that the god aura surged out, the ascendees, who had been holding their longing in check for quite a while now, unleashed everything at their disposal. Down they descended like razor-sharp blades.

Xu Qing extended his hand, and his immortal embryo emerged, blocking out everything as its palm dropped. Its aura shook all of the gods to the core, and immediately covered the effects of the bowl of blood. The black mutagen fell under its power and was crushed. A cracking sound rang out as the mutagen smoke seemed to solidify and then break!

At the same time, the crimson eye manifestation of Zhou Zhengli’s canon opened. Yuanshan Su’s heavy mountains descended. Sir Vilespirit cackled as he rushed forth with killing intent and devilishness. Li Mengtu’s poison swirled while Hordeslayer and Rampart shone with astonishing sword light.

The slaughter was commencing!

***

In the starry sky some distance away from Planet Graytomb, a group of army cultivators were on patrol. They were one of the nine great army corps in the eastern theater’s front lines. They were the Longscale Regiment, who served as vanguard troops when assigned to battle. During peaceful times, they would go on patrol to look for gods in hiding, and to clear areas of mutagen.

There were a bit over a thousand members, organized into battalions of roughly a hundred. Currently, the battalions were seated cross-legged atop enormous green flying ships. The ten flying ships flew the banners of the Longscale Regiment as they sailed majestically through the starry sky.

When the black bowl of blood shattered at Planet Graytomb, the sound of drums suddenly echoed out from the lead ship. The sudden, deafening noise shook the starry sky, and caused all of the cultivators on the ships to open their eyes.

A solemn voice then echoed out. “Gods are erecting an altar to serve as a foundation for a mutagen assault. That is why the god-crushing drums have sounded. Profound. Overlook. Ink. Spirit. Wing. You five battalions will follow the direction of the drums to inspect the area ahead. Find the altar and destroy everything there!”

Five of the flying ships shifted directions and then flew off in the direction indicated.

“Yes, sir!”

In a battlefield in the starry sky, dazzling starlight shone down, and the sound of a very unique drum echoed out, filled with immortal magic that made the void tremble.

They were called the god-crushing drums. They were one of the signature weapons of the patrolling battalions of the Longscale Regiment, and they were designed to flush gods out of hiding. They could sense traces of gods in a wide area, and were very sensitive to mutagen. Guided by the sound of the drums, five ships from the patrol regiment veered off and shot into a specific direction.

The remaining battalions continued on their way to continue inspecting other areas. They would not just sit and wait for the five battalions to complete their mission and return.

And thus, time slipped by. Before the remaining battalions could reach any other locations to inspect, a message came in from the ships that had departed. The person delivering the message sounded a bit flummoxed.

“Exalted one, we’ve followed the drums to Planet Graytomb, where the gods were erecting an altar. However, the only thing here are dead gods.... There’s nothing else. Some unknown party apparently arrived before us and wiped thēm out.”

In the main patrol group was the man in charge of the mission, a middle-aged cultivator with a stern look on his face. He wore a blue-colored suit of scale armor, and he pulsed with the extraordinary fluctuations of a peak Quasi-Immortal.

After receiving the message, he opened his eyes, revealing a thoughtful look. In this relatively large section of the battlefield, the Longscale Regiment was the only group tasked with carrying out patrols. And yet, some unknown party had beaten them to the punch....

After only a moment of consideration, the middle-aged cultivator issued new orders. Shortly after, all of the flying ships changed course and sped through the starry sky toward Planet Graytomb. Before long, ripples spread out through the void outside Planet Graytomb, where the Profound, Overlook, Ink, Spirit, and Wing Battalions waited. Then the rest of the flying ships arrived.

The Quasi-Immortal leader flew off his ship, followed by over a hundred members of his personal guard. Looking like shooting stars, they flew directly toward the planet. After landing... all of them looked around with strange expressions on their faces.

The god altar had clearly been destroyed, and the surroundings were littered with god corpses. The corpses had clearly been sucked dry. It wasn’t a case of them having been killed with fatal blows. They had clearly been milked for all of the ringsource they contained. It had been accomplished very tidily. Not one bit of ringsource was left behind.

The Longscale cultivators exchanged awkward glances. This was definitely not how the Longscale Regiment operated.

The leader looked around at the members of his guard and said, “This looks more like the work of a squadron of Corpsedrainers.... Such efficiency.”

He had merely given voice to what they were all thinking. What they were seeing really did seem like something done by Corpsedrainers. Extracting ringsource was delicate work, and the fact remained that none of them could have accomplished it with such finesse. Work like that took a lot of practice. But then people started questioning the situation.

“But the Corpsedrainers are like vultures. They only show up on big battlefields.”

“You never see them at places like this with only a few dozen god corpses.”

“Maybe it’s the work of scouts from some other regiment. Could they have Corpsedrainers with them? Maybe they’re working together.”

As everyone discussed the situation, the Quasi-Immortal leader looked around at the corpses, studied the altar, and finally fixed his gaze on one corpse in particular.

That was when his eyes suddenly glittered. “That god... is a mid Altar God! Thēy had hidden this place to set up that god altar. But thēy were forced to activate it before thēy were ready. Thēy were obviously in a rush.

“Whoever attacked thēm didn’t sense thēm by means of god-crushing drums. The attackers... were following thēm. To kill an Altar God in such short order, and also remove any evidence of their presence, making it impossible for us to identify thēm... well, it indicates these people are no simpletons.”

No one responded to his words. A moment passed, and the leader looked away from the Altar God corpse.

“Report this matter up the chain of command. It’s probably just some fellow warriors from another regiment who accidentally crossed into our area of operations.”

With that, he flew back up into the starry sky, followed by the others, all the way back to his flying ship. However, along the way, many of his personal guards looked over their shoulders and sighed. They were all thinking similar things.

They crossed into our AO and brought Corpsedrainers with them...?

***

A good distance away from Planet Graytomb was Xu Qing and the other ascendees, who the Longscale Regiment had taken to be fellow warriors who had crossed into their area of operations. They were proceeding along in concealment, all the while talking back and forth as they analyzed how the fight had played out.

“We’re still too slow. The extraction wasn’t fast enough.”

“We might be good at extracting ringsource from living targets, but in the past they were always sealed first. And sealing takes longer than killing.”

“And to get the best results you have to continuously provoke the target....”

“Basically, life extraction is fine under normal circumstances, but on the battlefield, it really is better to deal with corpses!”

“Maybe we should just practice more on the dead bodies. Rapid extraction really is the most suitable for the battlefield.”

At a certain point, Xu Qing interrupted. “From now on, we’ll continue with our assigned Corpsedrainer mission, but at the same time, we’ll do as we just did. We’ll track down suitable god squadrons to practice our extraction techniques!”

Everyone nodded, then scattered to look for new targets.

Soon, Xu Qing was the only one left behind. After watching everyone leave, he found an asteroid where he hewed out a temporary mansion grotto. Once inside, he settled down cross-legged. His plan was to continue absorbing ringsource and push his cultivation base higher. At the same time, he was thinking about the war in the context of everything he had experienced up to this point.

Given how these skirmishes are playing out in the eastern theater, it almost seems like the two sides are playing a complicated game. They both have their own goals. Unfortunately, I don’t have enough information to figure out exactly what those goals are. But one thing is for certain.... Given the scale of the war, and the sacrifices being made, both sides are attempting to accomplish something of great strategic significance!

In order to get a better idea of what was going on, it was necessary to understand the larger trends.

I’m currently an early Quasi-Immortal. If I want to reach the great circle, I’ll need more ringsource. A lot more.... There’s just not enough time. I need to think of ways to speed things up!

Taking out some extracted ringsource, he started absorbing it.

Three months passed in a flash. During that time, the Longscale Regiment experienced several situations similar to what had just played out on Planet Graytomb. Every single time, there were gods in hiding, but before the Longscale patrol could reach them, thēy were wiped out and thēir ringsource extracted. The speed of fighting and extraction only increased. The battlefields were left cleaner and cleaner.

Before long, a rumor started to spread in the Longscale Regiment. Supposedly, a squadron from another regiment had crossed into their area of operations. They were said to be cruel and ruthless. What was more, they were traveling with Corpsedrainers, and whenever they took action, they were quick and deadly.

Over time, the other Corpsedrainer squadrons in the area were getting a bit irritated. What was more, the army leadership eventually noticed what was happening. Unfortunately, nothing anyone did to identify the mysterious squadron actually worked. Though the incidents kept happening, it seemed impossible to identify the perpetrators, so the Longscale Regiment gradually stopped working so hard to find them. Another factor at play was that the war was starting to heat up.

***

On an enormous pure white planet, a small skirmish was playing out involving a few thousand combatants. Booms and screams rang out everywhere. God magics and immortal techniques flared, sending multicolored light shining in all directions. The fighting was getting intense.

On the border of the field of battle was a gigantic white mountain, where a squadron of Corpsedrainers waited. Among them was the same old man Xu Qing had run into a few months before. Xu Qing and his people were there as well, seated cross-legged and keeping an eye on the fighting.

While the other Corpsedrainers were obviously on guard, Xu Qing and the ascendees seemed a bit impatient. Hustling on the side had been quite profitable recently, and they were getting a lot better at their extraction techniques. Their cultivation bases had also improved. However, because more battles were being fought in the war, they had less time for their side hustle, and had to do more official work as Corpsedrainers. They had already been waiting for a long time atop the mountain, yet no side had yet prevailed. Eyes glittering, they began to look over at Xu Qing.

Xu Qing was frowning. The ringsource he had acquired over the past few months had helped his cultivation base a lot, and he was eager to move on to the next battlefield. Unfortunately, there didn’t seem to be any end in sight for this particular skirmish.

After some thought, Xu Qing stood and started walking forward. The other ascendees excitedly got to their feet as well.

The other Corpsedrainers looked over in surprise. That was especially true of the old man who had given Xu Qing advice earlier on. He even opened his mouth to speak. But before he could say anything, Xu Qing burst into motion. Rumbling sounds then echoed out as he became a streak of light that shot like a blade toward the battlefield.

Zhou Zhengli and everyone else followed him without hesitation. They looked like vultures, but at the same time wolves, and it left the other Corpsedrainers on the mountain feeling shaken to the core.

The old man’s eyes widened. “They’re going in early? But—”

He was clearly shocked, but before he could even finish his sentence, Xu Qing and the ascendees reached the battlefield! They charged into the fighting without hesitation! Deafening booms rang out, and shockwaves from magical techniques spread out in all directions. freewebnovel.com

Xu Qing was a blur of afterimages that stopped right in front of the corpse of a Godfire god. He reached out, placed his hand onto the god’s chest, and even as both sides of the conflict continued to fight, he began to extract the ringsource! The corpse of the god withered up in front of him.

Meanwhile, when the combatants noticed what was happening, be they gods or Longscale Regiment cultivators, they looked over in astonishment. No one had ever seen anything like this happening.

As the stunned gods and cultivators looked on, Zhou Zhengli and the other ascendees arrived, spread out, and started finding god corpses.

They started extracting ringsource like crazy! They were fast and skilled, after extracting all the ringsource, they would quickly move on to the next corpse.

Everyone looked on in pure astonishment. The fighting was clearly not over, and yet this group of Corpsedrainers had swooped in right in front of everybody to extract ringsource from the corpses. The cultivators found it strange, but since these people were humans, they didn’t react like the gods. On the other hand, the gods were obviously provoked, and immediately tried to attack them.

However, the Corpsedrainers’ goal was clear. As soon as they met any resistance, they just gave up and moved on to a different god corpse.

Previously, there had been a deadlock on the battlefield, which could have tipped either way. But with these Corpsedrainers here, there were plenty of distractions, and the Longscale Regiment cultivators were quick to take advantage of that. As a result, the gods were forced to take the fighting seriously.

Besides, these Corpsedrainers were extraordinarily strong, and were like fish in water on the battlefield. They were going around like crazy, absorbing ringsource from all the corpses.

If that were all there were to it, it might not have been a big deal. After all, there weren’t even twenty of the Corpsedrainers, and they didn’t affect the fighting much.

But... before long something different happened. It started with Xu Qing. As he was racing toward a god corpse, a peak Godfire god appeared in front of him, who was locked in deadly combat with a Longscale Regiment cultivator.

The god’s eyes were cold and apathetic as hē unleashed god magics, causing the ringsource to seethe within hīm. The Longscale Regiment cultivator’s eyes were bloodshot, and he was about to put everything on the line. That was when the vision of the cultivator and the god blurred.

Xu Qing suddenly appeared right in front of them. Before either could react, Xu Qing reached out and latched his hand down onto the god’s throat. The power of his immortal embryo surged like flood waters, sweeping into the god. A howl of anguish escaped the god’s lips as hē felt hīs life force about to be snuffed out. Then a cracking sound echoed out from the god’s neck, and then hē fell to the ground. The god was a corpse now.

Xu Qing squatted down over the corpse and efficiently extracted the ringsource.

The Longscale Regiment cultivator stared in astonishment. Then his eyes shone with gratitude.

Sir Vilespirit was quick to notice what Xu Qing had done. Licking his lips, he suddenly attacked a god who was fighting a nearby cultivator. The god quickly became a corpse. The other ascendees followed suit, lunging toward the gods like wolves or tigers. If they ran into corpses, they sucked them dry. If they saw enticing targets, they turned them into corpses. If they had to fight, they fought. If they had to launch sneak attacks, they did. If an opponent was too strong, they would rely on life-saving techniques to get away.

In that manner, they became a huge wave sweeping across the battlefield. Though their influence was minimal at first, when they went crazy under Xu Qing’s lead, they soon became the center of attention.

The leaders on both sides saw what was happening. The leader of the gods frowned. In contrast, the leader of the cultivators, who was that same peak Quasi-Immortal from before, looked on with shining eyes.

On the nearby mountain, the other Corpsedrainers, including the old man, were dumbstruck.

“Are they really Corpsedrainers?” one of the squadron members muttered.

“They are. But from what I can see, they kill them first, then drain them....”

They were indeed draining corpses! During the three months that had passed, Xu Qing and the ascendees had learned a lot. It was generally better to drain living gods. But for a number of reasons, it was difficult to do so quickly. Therefore, they had focused their training on corpses. That was the best skill to enhance for use on the battlefield.

After all, battlefields were usually full of corpses. And if an enticing target presented itself that wasn’t a corpse, all they had to do was kill it and turn it into a corpse....

During the three months that had passed, their corpse-draining skills had improved a lot.

The battle on this huge planet was the first time they had acted in the open, and it left all onlookers shocked to the core. The Corpsedrainers on the mountain weren’t the only ones staring in shock. The cultivators on the battlefield were similarly astonished, and suddenly felt less pressure. reewebnovel.com

The fighting had been balanced before, so that meant that whatever pressure left the cultivators was transferred to the gods. Now, the gods not only had to worry about deadly combat with the army cultivators, they also had to worry about being ambushed and drained as corpses.

Xu Qing and the eightteen ascendees roved the battlefield like hungry wolves, or swords shaped like snakes, ready to stab anything they encountered. Wherever they went, corpses were drained dry, and weak gods crumbled. Even the strong gods had to be careful; if they weren’t, they also ran the risk of getting killed.

Naturally, the ascendees only attracted more and more attention. In fact, some of the gods, after being ambushed, forgot about the battle with the Longscale Regiment and instead focused on Xu Qing and the ascendees.

Of course, it went without saying that Xu Qing and the ascendees, given all that they had experienced and survived, were no weaklings. And they had plenty of life-saving magics. In instances where they ran into gods they couldn’t defeat, they just fled as quickly as possible. If they were in a wide, empty space, or were fighting in a dueling environment, then such life-saving magics might not have helped them escape gods this strong. But things were different on a battlefield.

The environment provided all sorts of variables. And even though such variables weren’t necessarily monumental, when they built on each other, they turned into a trend that the gods had to pay attention to.

Unfortunately... the leader of the gods quickly issued orders to try to stabilize thēir position and shore up thēir defenses. The results were middling. Xu Qing and the ascendees were too crafty and too strong. And they knew when to fall back in the face of overwhelming force.

Xu Qing was the best of all. He targeted the Godfire gods, and given that he had a Quasi-Immortal cultivation base, as well as a terrifyingly strong immortal embryo, he could kill such gods with a single blow. In any instances in which he couldn’t drain a corpse on the spot, he just collected the corpse to deal with later.

If the battlefield was a jungle, then the ascendees were predators! And Xu Qing had been developing such skills since he was young. Starfire was drawn out by the excitement of the fighting, and secretly used god magics to absorb the godly authority of the dead gods.

Little Shadow had finally woken up, and was attracted by the mutagen as well as the flesh and blood of the gods. As a result, it instinctively let out emotional fluctuations of hunger and excitement. Xu Qing gave silent approval, and a moment later, the shadow spread out onto the ground to lunge on nearby injured gods.

The leader of the Longscale Regiment took advantage of the developing situation to issue new orders.

“Longscale Regiment, let's finish this fight!” He wanted to take advantage of the variables and the chaos to mount a major offensive. He himself shot forward to attack the leader of the gods, who was a peak Altar God. “Die!”

The battlefield was descending into madness.

On the distant mountaintop, the other Corpsedrainers saw what was happening and were starting to get excited. The old man who had originally given advice to Xu Qing suddenly scowled viciously.

“Let’s go down there too!” he shouted. And with that, he blurred into motion as he headed down the mountain.

The other Corpsedrainers hesitated.

“But the rules—”

“Screw the rules!” the old man roared. “If we don’t get down there, we won’t have a thing to drain!”

The other Corpsedrainers threw caution to the wind and followed. When they reached the battlefield, they weren’t as proficient as Xu Qing and the ascendees. But it was still like adding flowers to the brocade, and it tilted the entire battle further in the direction of the cultivators.

The decisive final moments of the battle had arrived. Booms rang out. Screams filled the air. Gods were being killed, and corpses were being drained.

Within all that chaos, Xu Qing was like a specter, flitting about here and there, attacking ruthlessly and leaving behind no survivors. Starfire and Little Shadow were extremely excited.

Xu Qing stopped in front of a peak Godfire god. The god’s face fell, and hē prepared to fall back. But then Xu Qing’s right hand clamped down onto the top of hīs head. The power of his immortal embryo swept forth. Starfire unleashed a god magic. Little Shadow began to devour hīs flesh and blood.

A god that would have been the subject of devout worship in the Revered Ancient mainland was wiped out in an instant, hīs godly authority seized and hīs corpse half-eaten by Little Shadow. Xu Qing took the remains to drain further at a later time.

Having accomplished that, Xu Qing licked his lips. He had benefited a lot so far, and yet, he still wasn’t satisfied. Godfire gods weren’t enough for his needs. Turning, he looked down the battlefield, his eyes shining with mysterious light.

He was looking to where the peak Quasi-Immortal was fighting the Altar God. Both were going all out trying to kill the other. To fight the leader of the Longscale Regiment, this god was pulsing with a godly aura, and was unleashing god magics that could change the face of heaven and earth.

The ringsource fluctuations... were very enticing.

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed as he projected a message to Starfire and Little Shadow. Then he blurred into motion, heading in the opposite direction and disappearing into the chaos of battle.

Starfire sent out mutagen to cover Xu Qing, causing his immortal aura to disappear. It was replaced by mutagen. His aura was completely hidden. Next, it was Little Shadow’s turn. The shadow covered Xu Qing, making his fleshly body invisible. At the same time, Xu Qing used his space-time to cover himself. Now even his soul was invisible. Using those methods, he made it so that he hardly seemed to exist. In the end... he completely disappeared from the battlefield.

Soon the fight between the two leaders was reaching a critical point. The peak Quasi-Immortal and the peak Altar God were both attacking each other ruthlessly. The Altar God just wanted to get out of this fight. Whether doing so would ultimately change the course of the battle, or whether hē just escaped, it didn’t matter.
