But the leader of the Longscale Regiment wanted the opposite. The cultivators had gained the advantage of the battlefield. If he could keep the Altar God leader locked down for long enough, things would tilt even further in their favor.

The battle intensified. Injuries mounted on both sides. Deafening booms rang out, and the blinding light of god magic and immortal techniques rose high. Casualties mounted. Everyone was resorting to trump cards.

As for the Altar God’s trump card, it was a peak eruption of godly authority, which caused a white sun to form. Instead of emitting heat, however, it emitted frigid coldness and death. Close examination of the sun would reveal that, shockingly, it had innumerable faces on it, and all were distorted and screaming.

As both parties went all out trying to kill each other, an invisible figure crept across the field of battle toward them. It got closer and closer. Soon it was only about 3,000 meters away.

That was when the peak Altar God, who had a humanoid torso but a lower half made of black smoke, turned hīs head, eyes shining with cold apathy. Lifting hīs right hand, hē split the trump card hē had just unleashed, causing a pair of deathly pale suns to appear.

The first blocked the leader of the Longscale Regiment, while the other shot toward that spot 3,000 meters away. All of it happened too quickly.

The terrifying white sun crossed the 3,000 meters in an instant, then exploded. White light spread out, destroying the void, shattering magical laws, and distorting everything.

It also forced the invisible figure out into the open. It was none other than Xu Qing. He tried to fight back, but it did no good. An eruption of godly authority from a peak Altar God was too terrifying. The white light shredded everything to pieces.

Xu Qing writhed as his flesh and blood was ripped apart, as if it might peel off him. At that critical moment, Xu Qing’s eyes shone with determination. Separating his soul, he fell back, hoping to avoid the danger.

And yet, at that exact moment, a host of gods appeared around him. They pounced, unleashing all of their power. The rumbling booms caused many to look in that direction.

Observers on both sides of the conflict saw Xu Qing’s soul and fleshly body ripped to pieces! Zhou Zhengli and the ascendees howled in grief, their eyes bloodshot as they rushed in that direction. Little Shadow became visible. Erupting with emotional fluctuations of madness, it lunged toward the peak Altar God. Starfire did the same, eyes radiating madness. Shē became a stream of god light that shot directly toward the Altar God.

The leader of the Longscale Regiment took advantage of the moment to unleash an immortal magic. It turned into a red moon, which cast a red glow that turned into a gargantuan cloud of sky-obfuscating, land-enshrouding moths. Looking extremely gruish and sinister, they dropped down toward the Altar God. In the blink of an eye, blood-red light filled the battlefield thanks to the never-ending moths.

A sensation of imminent danger filled the Altar God’s heart. Glaring at the Longscale Regiment leader, as well as the cloud of moths, hē suddenly shot backward, all while thrusting hīs palm out in front of hīmself numerous times to unleash a secret magic.

Hīs body quickly withered, becoming very weak. That was the price to pay to use that magic. Latent power erupted, converging in hīs core as sunlight spread out. It was as if hē was transforming into a sun!

Hē was now at his weakest, but by temporarily transforming into a sun, hē could inflict a grievous injury on the leader of the Longscale Regiment. By exhausting hīs strength, hē could create the time and opportunity hē needed to escape. White light shone as hē replaced hīs god body with a sun.

However, that was when something extremely dramatic occurred! The void behind hīm suddenly folded in on itself like a piece of paper. Fluctuations spread out, filling the dome of heaven and causing wild colors to flash.

They were ripples in space! They were flows of time! They were overlapping space-times!

A hand appeared, gripping an iron skewer. And it moved with incomparable speed, in a very gruish fashion, as it stretched out from the overlapping space-time! It appeared right in front of the weakened Altar God’s throat! With blinding speed, unmatchable accuracy, and fluid skill, it slashed through the god’s throat!

What a show of ability!

The god’s skin was flayed. The flesh was opened up. The bones were severed. The skewer came out the other side! In addition, the tolling of a bell echoed out, like a death knell. It happened so quickly that the leader of the gods couldn’t react quickly enough to fight back or put up a defense.

The skewer was incredibly sharp and was made of spectacular materials. In the hands of a skilled wielder, it could unleash incomparable power. Most importantly... the person wielding the skewer, though weaker than the god, was not that much weaker than hīm. And that meant that this sneak attack... was all the more effective!

Hīs eyes went wide as hē looked at hīs own body underneath the shadow of the red moths. For some reason, that body had no head! God blood spurted out of the neck, like a fountain connected it to the red clouds above. The god soul inside the body had been slashed by the skewer, cutting it into two parts.

The red moths smashed down into the body, burrowing into the flesh and destroying it! And then all of it, including hīs will and hīs senses, sped off into the distance. However... what was going off into the distance wasn’t the body. It was the head only!

Hīs head had been grabbed by someone who was racing away! As hīs consciousness faded, hē finally saw who had grabbed hīs head.

It was a young man in a black robe, splattered with god blood. He had violet hair and beautiful facial features. His eyes were incredibly cold. He was... the very same Corpsedrainer that he had just killed!

“You—” hē said hoarsely, but an instant later, hē was sealed. Hīs world turned dark.

The battlefield went quiet.

Xu Qing, who had just escaped with the head of the Altar God, looked completely composed as everyone looked at him. What had been destroyed earlier was only a space-time version of himself. His true form had been in hiding. The gods on the battlefield were astonished. The cultivators were shaken. And then Xu Qing stopped and held up the sealed head. He said nothing. The red glow behind him looked like a moon.

Down on the battlefield, cheering erupted. And then... the cultivator army flowed toward the gods like a mountain-toppling, sea-draining flood.

The blood-red glow in the sky was like an aurora as the countless moths swirled about. It was a beautiful sight. Xu Qing hovered in the air, his hair swirling around him, the head of the god held aloft. That image would remain fixed in the memories of all the cultivators who could see him.

The battle between the gods and the cultivators had been at a deadlock. But when Xu Qing and the ascendees arrived, they became a variable that proved to be the straw that broke the camel’s back. And thus, the balance in the skirmish was changed, and the battle inched toward a conclusion. The sound of slaughter raged as the gods suffered a major defeat in the face of the cultivator onslaught.

Zhou Zhengli, Sir Star Ring, and the other ascendees took advantage of the moment to go crazy in draining corpses.

Xu Qing floated down. As far as he was concerned, getting ringsource was the most important thing right now.

The other group of Corpsedrainers rushed forth like vultures.

About an hour later, the battle was over. The battlefield was covered with god corpses. Though the cultivators had suffered some casualties, it was still a major victory. The gods had been annihilated.

The cultivators felt a mix of exhaustion and exultation as they stood amidst the blood and corpses. All eyes were on Xu Qing and the ascendees as they roved the battlefield draining the corpses of any remaining ringsource. Some of the ascendees had minor injuries, others had more serious wounds. But regardless of how tired or hurt they were, they weren’t slowing down a bit. All were going crazy to collect ringsource.

This time, the Longscale Regiment cultivators didn’t interfere. Their eyes were full of nothing but respect for Xu Qing and the ascendees. Even the old man and the other Corpsedrainers had backed away to let them take the lead. And thus, Xu Qing and the ascendees collected the majority of the ringsource from the thousands of god corpses.

After taking about eighty percent of it, they stopped. The ascendees gathered around Xu Qing, and he looked at the army cultivators, especially the leader.

The leader clasped hands, bowed, and said, “Many thanks!”

Xu Qing returned the salute, then turned and raced off into the distance. Zhou Zhengli and the others followed. They wanted to make haste to the next battlefield.

The people who remained behind watched them go. They could tell that the nineteen of them... had baleful auras, surging blood energy, and down to the last one of them, were vicious wolves.

After everything the ascendees had survived, they could do well on their own. But as a team in an army, they were even more outstanding. About half of them were already Quasi-Immortals, and the rest were extremely close to that point. All had terrifying battle prowess. As a group, they were like a pack of wolves. And as their leader, they had Xu Qing, who was.... the king of the wolves.

***

Time passed. This time, it was several months. During that time, Xu Qing and the ascendees continued to collect ringsource. They kept busy and got better and better. When they appeared at a battlefield, they used their unique methods to make sure there were plenty of corpses available.

Their activities caused their name to spread like wildfire. Eventually, just about all the cultivators in the Longscale Regiment’s area of operations had seen them in action, or at least heard of this terrifying Corpsedrainer squadron.

There were only nineteen of them, but most were Quasi-Immortals, and all of them had plentiful fighting experience. They excelled at using life-saving magics, and could all be considered unparalleled chosen. That said, they lacked the arrogance common among chosen. They had astounding battle prowess, yet didn’t hesitate to use ambushes or assassination techniques. And they were blindingly fast and efficient when it came to draining corpses.

They were taking the reputation of Corpsedrainers to another, much higher level. As a result, the army cultivators’ attitude toward the Corpsedrainers in general was changing.

As for the other Corpsedrainers, they were paying attention to what was happening. Gradually, people started imitating Xu Qing’s group. Although not many succeeded, those who did succeed made a big difference. Gradually, more and more people were following in Xu Qing’s footsteps. Slowly but surely, those Corpsedrainers who followed the new way started becoming so famous that they earned a new nickname.

Now they were called... Undertakers!

As things ran their course, the war in the eastern theater slowly headed toward a critical juncture. The grindstone of flesh and blood was moving at such a fever pitch that the lantern drew attention from all corners. Skirmishes played out constantly on the front line of the eastern theater.

Even the stupidest gods and cultivators could tell that something unusual was going on. Everyone assumed it was the prelude to a huge storm. But in reality, there was another possibility. And that was... without people realizing it, the storm had already passed.

***

In the eastern theater of the Fourth Star Ring, where the mutagen was strong, there was a series of planets that resembled statues. They pulsed with incredible holiness as they floated in the starry sky. There were millions upon millions of them. Ripples spread out in all directions from them. Every single planet was inhabited by gods and their subordinate slave species. Also on the planets were huge beasts, evil god faces, and numerous temples, all of which emanated terrifying godly might. The statue planets and the temples seemed to go on forever.

Nearby was a majestic, endless river of stars that circled the entire area. Occasionally, tentacles would appear from within it.

Chanting sounds from the gods filled that part of the eastern theater. This place was a temporary garrison for the gods.

And in the middle of that garrison were nine enormous altars. All nine were made of countless bones. Some of the bones were just skulls, but there were also bodies with flesh still attached. They came from many species, and while some were cultivators, others were gods. Yet others were from the gods’ slave species. Altogether, they created a very sinister and deathly ambiance.

The fire of the underworld burned on the altars, pale white fire that cast pale halos out in all directions. They were like candles of death, burning silently and without end. The light of each altar overlapped with the other.

In the middle of the nine altars, illuminated by the shapeless, overlapping halos of candle light, was an astonishing item. It was... a huge coffin with no lid. The coffin itself was as large as a planet. And inside of it... was the corpse of a violet god!

This god had three heads and six arms, and was covered with godly striations that made hīm seem unusually noble. And that was because those godly striations wrapped around hīm to form a very mysterious ring!

Unfortunately, the ring had gaps. It wasn’t complete. If that ring were to be completed, then this god would have been... a God Lord!

Among the gods, this particular god was second only to an actual God Lord, which meant that hē definitely wasn’t some anonymous god. Hē was actually the commander-in-chief of the countless gods here in the eastern theater! A peak True God!

But now... hē lay in the coffin as a corpse. On the forehead of each of hīs heads was a ghastly wound that pierced through the soul, destroying īt.

Hē was dead! A month ago, a mysterious cultivator ambushed this god and delivered a fatal blow.[1]

If Xu Qing had been there to witness the scene, he would have realized the truth. And that was... the purpose of the grindstone of flesh and blood in the eastern theater, and the lantern it formed, was almost certainly bait for this particular god! The cultivators in the eastern theater were the bait, and the lantern was there to provide cover for the assassin!

Clearly, the assassination had worked! What was more, if Xu Qing were present to see the marks left by that cultivator, he would find the whole thing very suspicious.

If this plan had been successful, then why was the grindstone of flesh and blood still turning in the eastern theater? In fact, things were getting more intense! It didn’t make sense, unless... the assassination of this commander-in-chief was only one part of the plan being carried out by the cultivators! If that was the case, then this plan was definitely... supremely exceptional!

Near the coffin, in what had previously been empty space filled only with the underworld light, the terrifying aura of numerous gods suddenly spread out. All of thēm were very tall, with impressive godly might and extraordinary physical forms. All of thēm were True God officers among the gods of the eastern theater.

Upon arriving, thēy spread out in a circle around the coffin. Then thēy prostrated to the starry sky above. As thēy offered worship, rumbling filled the starry sky as a rift opened up, as if some immense power had ripped it open.

Godlight spread out from the rift. Within that light it was possible to see a magnificent god kingdom, endless universes, and innumerable gods. And all of thēm... were prostrating. As thēy offered worship, a graceful figure in a long, blue gown appeared, slowly emerging through the godlight.[2]

Hēr facial features were blurred, making them impossible to see clearly. Hēr clothing was extravagant, like all the seas of the Fourth Star Ring combined. Atop hēr head was a phoenix crown covered with numerous pearls. The crown emitted a sound like a phoenix howling in grief, and if you looked closely at the pearls... they were actually eyeballs. Each eyeball came from a different species, specifically, the most beautiful god species. The eyes all blinked at different times. It was gruish yet beautiful.

All of it went to show that this was the daughter of a god, someone with incredibly high status. As shē emerged from the rift, the True Gods around the coffin all bowed to hēr.

“Your Grace Starryeyes.”

The voice of the gods vibrated in the starry sky. It was as if the natural laws of the Fourth Star Ring were doting on this goddess.[3]

The reason was that shē was the newly crowned god emperor’s only child! Among the gods, God Lords were also called god emperors. Hēr father was the highest-ranking officer in the war between the Fifth and Fourth Star Rings, which meant hē was comparable to Immortal Lord Deepgloom.

Normally speaking, Starryeyes would never have come to this place. But now... the god that had been entrusted with a special mission here in the eastern theater had perished before succeeding! And thus, shē had to come, to use the godly authority of the imperial clan to bring the perished commander back as quickly as possible!

With the godly authority in hēr blood, shē could effectuate the return of a perished True God under her father’s command, in a much shorter time. It would only take a few months! Although it would come at a price, it wasn’t more than shē could bear. And that was because it came from the power of hēr father’s godhood!

At the same time, shē had come here with a mission of hēr own. Hēr mission was to stay behind and continue the work being carried out by the perished True God.

That work was only just beginning today.

***

Elsewhere at that exact moment, far from the Fourth Star Ring, on the cultivator’s front line positions, Xu Qing was draining a corpse of ringsource. He suddenly shivered and looked deep into the Fourth Star Ring. He slowly frowned.

“Is that..?” he murmured. For some reason that he couldn’t fathom, he had just sensed something unusual in his heart and soul. It was a lingering sense of fear or a slight trepidation. It was as if something foreordained to occur, something with unstoppable momentum, had suddenly arrived.

1. The assassination was mentioned in chapter 1232. ☜

2. This is only the second time in the novel that we have heard about a ‘god kingdom.’ The first time was in chapter 1196, and even then there was no definition or explanation about exactly what they are. Given how cultivation novels generally work, I think most of us can guess. ☜

3. The term goddess was introduced in chapter 1226. As I mentioned back then, it’s used in this novel to mean ‘daughter of a god.’ ☜

All of it made Xu Qing think about the True God he had imprisoned in the Green Heaven....

To mortals, fate was a mysterious thing that could hardly be comprehended. But to most cultivators who walked a path that defied heaven, there was a point in life in which they had to bow their head to fate. When that happened, they would smile bitterly... and admit that they accepted fate. That was just the helplessness of life. It was a way to add meaning to fickle reality. There was no point in fighting it. It was better to just acclimate to how things worked.

Unfortunately... some living things, for instance gods or immortals, were higher forms of existence. To them, fate was not something mysterious. Nor was it something unperceivable. They could see the evidence of fate, and could even lift the veil covering it. Some could even tamper with it, making certain things uncertain, or uncertain things certain.

Back in the Fifth Star Ring, there had been a very famous god known as the god of pain! Bimo Si! Though hē was not a God Lord, hīs godly authority was special. In fact, it was so special that, if hē encountered a God Lord in hīs heyday, that God Lord would treat hīm with honor.

That was because hīs illusions contained truth! That was why, when hē encountered Xu Qing during hīs attempted return, the unleashing of hīs godly authority caused certain things to change.

Right now, the fear within Xu Qing was like the wings of fate flapping. What he had sensed just now, other than something similar to what he had experienced when fighting the god of pain, was an even more important karma. It was... An old enemy he was very familiar with. It was his older brother, the Crown Prince of Violet and Cyan. It was another terrifying entity who also commanded the power of fate.

Xu Qing had long since been fighting back against him. In fact, due to a destined opportunity in Revered Ancient, he had acquired a very similar godly authority!

That was his carving knife of fate! It could carve out additional fates, and make outside variables become the main reality. It could make fates appear beyond ordinary fate. He didn’t have that carving knife with him. He had left it behind with his god clone, back in Revered Ancient. But the karma was still connected to him.

That was the reason for the thoughtful look on Xu Qing’s face. He was thinking about the True God imprisoned in the Green Heaven, and the pain he had experienced thanks to hīs godly authority. His eyes became very cold.

I went to the front lines and ran into the daughter of a god. The God Lord eventually killed everyone.... Is that what happens next? I run into this goddess?

His eyes narrowed as a fierce coldness filled his heart. Eventually, he looked away from the Fourth Star Ring and focused on the work at hand on the battlefield. Occasionally, the same sensation would strike him.

A month went by.

During that time, Xu Qing went about his usual routine. He drained gods, he worked on cultivation, and he absorbed ringsource. His cultivation base continued to climb. He was now very stable in early Quasi-Immortal.

The lingering sense of fear appeared now and then, but he ignored it. He already knew what he would do about the situation. And so... he waited. He was waiting for ripples in fate. He was waiting for that which was foreordained to present itself to him.

***

The starry sky was like a sea, with waves rippling through it. They were caused by godly voices.

In the eastern theater of the Fourth Star Ring, important things were still happening in the garrison of the gods. The true name of the commander of the army of gods was repeatedly being uttered from the area of the nine altars.

It wasn’t just the prostrating True Gods who were saying the name. The life force of all the countless corpses and bones that made up the nine altars were also calling out. They were all chanting that true name! All of those godly voices gathered around the goddess who hovered above the coffin, whose bloodline power spread out into the void, connecting the ancient to the modern.

The higher star ring cherished the ancient agreement, and thus gave the blessing of power that would call the True God back after death. It lit the path, becoming the guide, and opening the barriers! The aura of returning grew stronger. Godly might grew more majestic, slowly becoming viscous, turning into an actual sea in the starry sky.

Mutagen and godly authority were turning into a god sea! This was the first step of returning.

The commander-in-chief of the gods in the eastern theater was truly on the way to awakening. The eyes of all the other gods present were shining. Clearly, it was time to start the second step of the return. freewebnovel.com

However, that was when something very dramatic happened! An ear-splitting boom shook the starry sky. The nine god altars looked like they might collapse. All of the statue planets and the temples shook violently. It was the same with the river of stars.

The True Gods chanting the true name of their commander-in-chief, plus the goddess above the coffin, were all stunned. The entire area was part of the Fourth Star Ring, and it was full of dense mutagen. It originally was a swath of pitch black. But now... the color white had appeared!

It was the momentum of the immortals! It was a sudden invasion.

The starry sky was transforming. Anyone who looked up with eyes profound enough to see would be able to spot, high in the void, was something that stretched out over both the Fourth and the Fifth Star Ring. Two magnificent entities were there, fighting a battle of momentum.

Immortal Lord Deepgloom had played a game piece in the eastern theater of the gods! Because of this immortal invasion, the entire area became like an ink painting.

Black and white crisscrossed. Ink flowed. Both sides were fighting back and trying to get the upper hand. As the black and white moved, the ink moved, and the battle status changed! Clearly, this incursion of white immortal energy was the result of a lot of preparation. The instant the barriers of the star ring were broken, numerous cultivators started teleporting, pulsing with baleful auras!

In the lead was a grim, middle-aged man who was Immortal Lord Deepgloom’s second-in-command. He was the commander-in-chief of the eastern theater, Immortal Monarch Silent Dao! Astonishingly, he had come straight from the grindstone of flesh and blood to this spot, teleported along with his subordinates. The moment he appeared, pulsing with a baleful aura, his eyes shining so coldly they could freeze universes, he shot... toward the goddess!

The gods were so stunned thēy couldn’t react.

From the look of it, this had been Immortal Lord Deepgloom’s plan all along. The lantern that had been lit in the eastern theater was the distraction. And then the mysterious cultivator assassinated the True God, which drew out the goddess. From beginning to end, the goal had been the goddess!

Goddess Starryeyes was the only child of the God Lord opposed by Immortal Lord Deepgloom. She had hēr father’s bloodline godly authority. If he could capture hēr... then he would gain massive momentum in the war!

This was a battle that surpassed any of the previous battles. Over a hundred True Gods and Lower Immortals participated, along with countless other cultivators and gods. And things... were just getting started! Boundless slaughter spread, shaking universes.

As the cultivators launched their incisive sneak attack, a blow to the gut of the gods’ army... the subject of the attack, the goddess that Immortal Monarch Silent Dao was after... didn’t react at all. Shē just kept chanting the name of the True God!

An instant later, more dramatic things occurred! All of the temples, and all of the statue planets, plus the entire star river, began to glitter, sending out beams of golden light.

Terrifying pressure built up! The starry sky seemed to shatter, as if some veil were suddenly being forcefully lifted away.... A host of spectacular god formations suddenly appeared on the battlefield! There were no less than 1,000,000 of them. And they all erupted at the same time!

Godly might swelled. Mutagen swept out. The cultivators who bore the brunt of it were suppressed. Their minds and hearts trembled as blood sprayed from their mouths. Their souls felt like they were being extracted, and massive weight crushed onto their fleshly bodies. In contrast, the gods were bolstered, and their battle prowess improved. The decline of one side and the improvement to the other was obvious.

At the core of the 1,000,000 formations was the fallen commander-in-chief of the gods. As hē returned, the power of the god formations built up.

This entire thing was a trap! The Immortal Lord had been plotting against the God Lord. But the God Lord had used hīs daughter as bait to plot against the Immortal Lord! Both sides had played game pieces. And now those pieces were clashing!

The slaughter instantly intensified. In the very middle of the battlefield was the goddess, hovering above the coffin, wearing an expression of pure calm.

Immortal Monarch Silent Dao was racing toward hēr. But the god formations were blocking his path and preventing him from entering the very middle of the battlefield.

Then, the void around the goddess blurred as three True Gods stepped out. After surveying the area coldly, thēy stood guard all around hēr.

Starryeyes smiled faintly. Not even looking at the battlefield, shē closed hēr eyes and continued to chant the true name, hēr voice growing continuously ethereal. All shē had to do was successfully call back the commander-in-chief of the eastern theater. The process of awakening would bolster the god formations, and the cultivators would continue to be slaughtered. And then, when the commander-in-chief woke up, the battle... would end in victory for the gods.

As the chanting continued, shē lifted her right hand to hēr forehead. Suddenly, shē shivered from head to toe. Then hēr skin withered, and hēr life force rippled. Hēr blood seemed to burn. Astonishingly, shē... was paying a steep price to speed up the process. Even if shē hērself dropped from the True God level temporarily as a result, it was worth it to speed up the return.

The sense of awakening from the corpse in the coffin grew more intense. This sudden twist put the cultivator force in imminent danger.

Immortal Monarch Silent Dao’s gaze turned razor sharp as he tried to break through the barriers. Unfortunately... the god formations surged, and the lockdown in the central area only grew stronger. What was more, the three True Gods standing guard were bolstering the defenses as well, making it impossible for Immortal Monarch Silent Dao to get in anytime soon. There wasn’t enough time!

In hēr determination, the goddess let hēr cultivation level drop. Then shē spat out a mouthful of god blood, which shē turned into a boundlessly mysterious symbol that pulsed with the aura of the star ring itself. It dropped down into the coffin, where it landed on the chest of the commander-in-chief.

The moment it landed, the goddess’s voice echoed across the battlefield. “Return!”

The starry sky seemed to congeal. Everything turned slow and sluggish, all while a tempest of soundlessness seemed to fill the area. Wind swept from all directions toward the coffin, where it converged on the corpse.

The corpse... suddenly twitched. The eyes slowly opened! The corpse stood! Hīs massive frame pulsed with a terrifying aura, causing countless life forms to tremble. The awakening was complete!

1,000,000 god formations erupted. Countless gods chanted in godly voices. Mutagen swept across the battlefield, and godly voices overwhelmed everything.

The cultivators were completely taken aback.

As for Starryeyes, shē stuck up hēr chin. Hēr bloodline and status, as well as the help shē had provided in the return, ensured that, as shē stood there, the commander-in-chief immediately bowed.

It seemed that everything was over. But then, just as it appeared that the cultivators were going to experience a huge catastrophe, the black mutagen of the gods seethed. A boundless will then erupted from inside.

“He’s not a hē!”[1]

All of a sudden, the gods’ commander-in-chief shivered. Then hē swiveled and thrust hīs fist out toward the goddess! It was only a single fist, but it caused the starry sky to collapse. Boundless and terrifying power very close to that of a God Lord swept forth destructively.

The goddess’s face fell, and hēr pupils constricted. But there was no time for hēr to evade.

It was the same with the three True Gods! The development was simply too unexpected. In the blink of an eye, the three True Gods were ripped to shreds. That single fist caused all of them to explode, even their god souls.

As for Starryeyes, hēr entire body blurred. And then it was just barely possible to see an ancient lamp. The lamp went out, and shē disappeared.

The entire battlefield was thrown into an uproar.

Countless gazes locked onto the commander-in-chief up in midair as hē murmured, “God Lamp Life Substitution?”

Hē looked up. Both gods and cultivators on the battlefield were too stunned to react as hē began laughing. Then... hē began to shine with dazzling light. It wasn’t the gold of the gods. It was... silver!

The light swept out to fill the starry sky. Then a hoarse voice could be heard.

“I am the cultivator Spirit Jade.”

The words struck the battlefield like an earthquake! The gods were stunned, but the cultivators were exuberant. As the words left his mouth, he waved his hand, and the 1,000,000 god formations inverted. Cultivator morale went through the roof.

If Xu Qing had been present, he would have recognized that name. It was the name inscribed on one of the gravestones in the Heroic Immortal Tombs in the Nineshores heaven beyond heaven.[2]

“Life is like a dream, and time is like a song. And the starry sea eventually comes to an end.

“I am Immortal Monarch Spirit Jade. I eradicated a True God and drank hīs blood. I wiped out hīs mark like the turtledove occupying the magpie’s nest. Let’s see what happens in the future.... Will it be hē who returns, or me?

“If hē returns, my corpse will emanate golden light, and later generations can erase the True God from existence. But if it’s me... then silver light will shine, and I will slay gods again!”

***

Immortal Monarch Silent Dao’s expression was calm, as if this wasn’t a surprise at all. Nodding at Spirit Jade, he said, “How’s that body feel for you?”

Spirit Jade grinned. “This isn’t the god I slayed. But to bring me back in the body of this commander-in-chief.... Well, Immortal Lord Deepgloom really wasn’t lying when he said he could make it happen!”

1. Just like in English, the pronouns are pronounced exactly the same. So in reality, this dialogue wouldn’t work when spoken. It only works when you can see the characters.
