2. The name Spirit Jade was previously mentioned in chapter 1202. ☜

In the vast starry sea between the Fourth and Fifth Star Rings, the void rippled as a huge rift cracked open. Two figures flew out from inside. They appeared to be a man and a woman.

The one who looked like a woman was pale in the face, and wore a wrinkled garment that had once been blue, but was now pale. It was as if it had contained a great sea that had dried up. Atop the head of the woman was a phoenix crown, except that phoenix had long since perished, and the pearls made of eyes that had decorated it were as gray as ash.

As for the man, he was a decrepit old god whose cultivation level seemed unstable, and who was covered with an assortment of wounds that were in the middle of healing.

After emerging from the rift, both the man and the woman coughed up huge mouthfuls of blood. It was golden blood that shed bits of mutagen. The old man looked around with eyes that shone with golden light. Seeing the spreading mutagen, the man lifted a hand and clenched it down hard. The mutagen was erased from existence. The same happened to thēir aura and all other evidence of thēir passage.

Having accomplished that, the old god turned to the woman and spoke in a hoarse voice. “Your Grace Starryeyes... this wasn’t your fault. Clearly the cultivators had planned everything out!”

The woman was none other than that only child of the God Lord, Starryeyes, and the man was hēr dao protector. Back when Spirit Jade launched his attack on the battlefield, Starryeyes’ three dao protectors had been killed.

As for Starryeyes, it was only by using the life-saving magic hēr father had given hēr, the God Lamp Life Substitution, that shē managed to escape catastrophe. Unfortunately, shē had drained hērself in the effort to bring back the dead commander-in-chief, so hēr cultivation base had dropped. And so, despite having escaped certain death, shē was still badly hurt.

If it weren’t for the fact that shē had a fourth True God dao protector keeping watch from hiding, who had helped hēr at the last minute, then even hēr God Lamp Life Substitution wouldn’t have been enough to save hēr.

For hēr to escape to this location was really a fluke. But... though shē could accept the drop to hēr life force and cultivation base, shē couldn’t stop thinking about that unforgettable scene.

It was the moment Spirit Jade’s eyes had opened!

“But why was it a cultivator that came back and not the commander-in-chief...?” It was a devastating blow to hēr. Even now, being so far from the battlefield, hēr eyes were blank because of it. “And the war in the eastern theater....”

The old god said, “Your Grace, that immortal was once a peak Lower Immortal, and is now using the body of a True God in the great circle. With battle prowess as terrifying as that, he’s basically as strong as you can get without being a God Lord!

“With an expert as powerful as that to suddenly show up on the battlefield, well, it’s a foregone conclusion how things will end in the eastern theater. You really have to stop worrying about it.

“My injuries are so severe that I could die soon. It’s a struggle simply to stay in the True God level. I won’t be able to keep you safe for much longer, Your Grace.

“Right now... we’re not in the Fourth Star Ring anymore. We’re somewhere between the two star rings. Given the immortal energy here, we’re obviously closer to the cultivators. That’s going to make it even more difficult for us to recover. What’s more, it’s highly likely that the cultivators will be looking for us.

“Your Grace, we’re going to be facing danger from all sides. We need to stay under cover and be very careful as we travel. Until we get back to the Fourth Star Ring, we cannot reveal our true identities! Your safety is of concern to the God Lord hīmself, Your Grace, so... please, pull yourself together!”

Starryeyes said nothing for a moment, but the blankness in hēr eyes faded, to be replaced by coldness. “I hereby promise that if you perish, then after I recover and get help from my father, I’ll personally bring you back!”

The old god nodded in response to hēr words. Then hē closed his eyes, causing hīs body to flash briefly with golden light before turning completely transparent. That will of transparency then expanded to cover the goddess.

The two gods vanished.

***

Days passed.

When Immortal Monarch Spirit Jade returned to the eastern theater in the Fourth Star Ring, the war shifted into high gear. It was like a huge, swelling wave.

Cultivator morale had never been higher. At the same time... the gods were stunned beyond belief. In the past... the gods’ ability to awaken from death was a grace shown by the higher star rings. It was one of the main foundations for the power and strength of the gods. True Gods never really died. As long as the true name of such a god was remembered, then that god could come back.

But what happened in the Fourth Star Ring’s eastern theater completely upended the gods’ perception of reality. There was no doubt... that thēir goddess had been waking up thēir commander-in-chief, only for a cultivator to be the one that woke up!

That indicated that the natural law that was their very foundation had been tampered with by the cultivators! If it happened once, then it could happen twice.... And if the cultivators had that ability, then it meant that they had developed providence, which had once been the reserve power of only the gods! This could change everything!

It also meant that whenever a True God was woken up in the future, this same type of thing could potentially happen. It was a case of the turtledove occupying the magpie’s nest and completely taking over! The gods in the eastern theater were shaken in the most unprecedented way possible.

After all, this entire development meant... that the supposedly eternal laws governing undying True Gods had changed! Considering a cultivator had returned, then... what had happened to the original owner of that god body, the commander-in-chief of the gods’ eastern theater? Hīs return had been tampered with? Therefore, where was hē?

It was completely unknown. And the gods... hated unknowns. Although the event would only specifically affect what happened in the fighting in the eastern theater, it had profound implications for the war in general.

It was easy to imagine what would happen as the news spread. It would certainly cause a storm through the war regions, and beyond that, the Fourth Star Ring as a whole! And that storm was no less significant than the arrival of a new God Lord!

Any spectator would come to the conclusion that this entire thing was a plan hatched by Immortal Lord Deepgloom!

First was the ‘lantern’ in the cultivator’s staging areas. After that was the assassination. Third in line was getting the goddess to come. And then, the goddess was used to awaken the True God, all while a major offensive was launched to distract from what was really going on. From the look of it, everything had been done to make sure that final awakening occurred!

“Now I get it!”

On the front lines in the eastern theater of the Fifth Star Ring, Xu Qing and the ascendees had just finished some Corpsedrainer work, and were stunned to hear the news in a war report. The war report about the events a few days earlier had been spreading far and wide in the eastern theater. It explained everything clearly, and was really improving morale among the cultivators. It also dispelled a lot of the confusion felt by Xu Qing and the ascendees.

“Just what I would expect of Immortal Lord Deepgloom,” Li Mengtu sighed. “He’s not someone known to be constantly hatching plots and schemes, but he’s obviously clever. And then there’s Immortal Monarch Spirit Jade.... I wonder why I’ve never heard of him before.”

The eyes of Sir Star Ring and the other ascendees glittered thoughtfully. What Spirit Jade had accomplished was unimaginably shocking to them.

As for Xu Qing, he just kept thinking about Immortal Monarch Spirit Jade’s epitaph written on his gravestone back at the Heroic Immortal Tombs.

He did it.

Xu Qing was understandably taken aback. However, given what he knew of the gods, he had already reached his own conclusions about the matter. He wasn’t convinced that this was something that would happen a lot. It was the result of some very special plans and circumstances.

Meanwhile, Zhou Zhengli said, “If there’s someone in the Fifth Star Ring known for plots and schemes, it’s Immortal Lord Nineshores.... I wouldn’t be surprised if he’s the one that’s actually behind it all. What’s more, the success of a plan like this... surely involved overcoming many obstacles. I’m afraid it’s not likely to happen again.

“Otherwise, why would Immortal Monarch Spirit Jade be the only one to come back? If it was easily repeatable, then why not bring back a whole bunch of cultivators, have them stay under cover, and then launch a one-time surprise attack?

“But they didn’t do that. They only brought back one cultivator. Though we won a victory, the gods are on guard now. And I’m sure they’ll try to figure out how it happened.”

Everyone clearly took Zhou Zhengli’s assessment seriously.

As for Xu Qing, he looked up at Zhou Zhengli. The two of them were obviously on the same page. However, the success of the operation also caused Xu Qing to think of something else that was very important.

That goddess....

Xu Qing’s pupils constricted.

At almost the exact same moment, Zhou Zhengli said, “And why did they want the goddess there?”

Sir Star Ring and everyone else just considered the question thoughtfully. In contrast, Hordeslayer and Rampart didn’t hesitate to offer their opinion.

“You guys are making this way too complicated. Enough with all the jibber jabber. We two brothers can explain everything. It’s simple. Immortal Lord Deepgloom and the other bigshots were just trying to get the attention of the Fourth Star Ring.”

“You all were talking about the eastern theater being turned into a lantern, right? Well, they just wanted the lantern to shine more brightly.”

Hordeslayer and Rampart weren’t known for being intellectual powerhouses. But their assessment caused Xu Qing to look over at them. Zhou Zhengli and everyone else did the same.

Hordeslayer and Rampart seemed taken aback. They had just been speaking off the cuff....

“If that’s the case,” Zhou Zhengli said, “then... then the ultimate plan for this war must be mind-blowing!”

Zhou Zhengli instinctively looked at Xu Qing. Eyes shining, Xu Qing was about to speak, when out of nowhere, their mission jade slips vibrated. Orders were being sent to everyone on the front lines of the eastern theater.

“All forces will break into small groups and begin a full search of the front lines. Go into all areas, regardless of whether they are full of immortal energy or mutagen.... You will search for... Goddess Starryeyes, the daughter and only child of God Emperor Death Departure! Do not use lethal force!

“Anyone who provides clues leading to hēr capture will be rewarded with 1,000,000 military credits and 10 portions of ringsource!

“Anyone who captures hēr will be rewarded with 10,000,000 military credits and 100 portions of ringsource, will be given the daoist title true monarch, and will also be given... a dao weapon forged by an Immortal Lord!”

Military credits were the main ways cultivators could be promoted in the army. And they were the main currency that could be used to acquire ringsource. freewebnovel.com

Although it wasn’t hard to earn military credits on the battlefield, it would definitely be difficult to get 1,000,000 of them. Normally speaking, getting that many would involve killing ten Altar Gods, or perhaps one peak Altar God. As for 10,000,000... it would be impossible to get that many without killing a True God.

But now, even just evidence leading to the capture of the goddess could bring in 1,000,000, while capturing hēr was worth 10,000,000. The vast majority of cultivators would find such a reward extremely enticing.

That wasn’t even to mention the fact that, in addition to military credits, the reward included ringsource. Ringsource was usually categorized into ‘portions.’ When Xu Qing and the ascendees were in the Department of Acquisitions, their mission requirements usually involved getting 100 portions of ringsource!

Considering that, a reward of 10 portions of ringsource for evidence of the goddess was equivalent to ten percent of their previous mission quota. Meanwhile, capturing the goddess would bring in 100 portions, which was obviously an astonishing amount.

As these orders filtered through the front lines, it caused a big surge of excitement among the army cultivators. Given the ringsource reward, even the most outstanding figures among the cultivators were interested.

But what was most enticing to the high-level cultivators, particularly those in the great circle of Quasi-Immortal, was... the daoist title of true monarch! True monarch was a title reserved for apprentices of Immortal Lords. It was a representation of status, resources, and a bright future. In other words, anyone who captured the goddess would gain an Immortal Lord as a Master!

Add all of those factors together, and it resulted in ninety-nine percent of cultivators being worked up into a frenzy.

The one percent who weren’t very excited by those things were the leadership cultivators who were already Lower Immortals, or army vassals with extremely high cultivation base and status. Yet, even their eyes were currently glittering, and their hearts pounding. That was because of the final item mentioned in the reward for capturing the goddess.

A dao weapon forged by an Immortal Lord! It would be a precious treasure that contained the might of an Immortal Lord! It would be easier to find a phoenix feather or a qilin horn than a treasure as rare as that. Even Lower Immortals would find something like that exciting.

The end result was that the new orders caused a huge sensation on the front lines of the eastern theater. In the blink of an eye, a massive search effort began. All army units and all cultivators, even the Corpsedrainers, took action!

Lower Immortals personally joined in the search, but also sent orders to their subordinates to do the same, while also offering their own rewards for those who reported clues.

Xu Qing and the other ascendees were just as excited.

That was especially true of Sir Vilespirit, whose eyes were completely bloodshot. The broken sword he wielded was his greatest strength, but it was also starting to hold him back. He had to constantly control it; if he failed to do so, then the blade would quickly turn him into nothing more than a puppet. But if he could become the apprentice of an Immortal Lord... then that could all change!

Li Mengtu struggled to control his breathing. He had long since hoped to get rid of the karma of his Master, Poison Monarch. And this mission... could be just the opportunity he was looking for.

Yuanshan Su and other ascendees were thinking similar things. Everyone had their own struggles and dreams that they never talked to others about. Now was their chance to fight for those hopes and dreams!

Hordeslayer and Rampart were particularly excited. Their thoughts were more simplistic than the others. If they could get an Immortal Lord as a Master, then they could envision Xu Qing groveling in front of them as a result.

Even Sir Star Ring’s eyes glittered. This reward was simply too amazing.

Of course, the reward also confirmed their previous speculations. This goddess was very important. That much was obvious considering that it was necessary to capture hēr alive.

Zhou Zhengli was feeling excited, but when he looked over and noticed that Xu Qing didn’t seem to be reacting at all, he forced himself to cool down. But after some thought, he decided that wasn’t the best tactic.

“Everyone, we need to refrain from being impulsive!” The thunderous boom of his voice struck the ascendees to the core.

They looked over. With a solemn expression, Zhou Zhengli continued, “Considering how important this goddess is, it doesn’t matter that shē’s injured.... We cannot afford to look down on hēr! Hēr father is a god. Not just any god. Hē’s God Lord Death Departure!

“This goddess will definitely have a lot of life-saving techniques to employ, and will have no shortage of bodyguards. Granted, the war reports indicated that some of hēr bodyguards died. But I refuse to believe that shē didn’t have backup plans in place! Considering this mission has such a spectacular reward, it goes without saying that it will be very dangerous!”

Yuanshan Su and the others considered his words.

But Sir Vilespirit’s eyes flashed. “That’s absurd! We’re cultivators! We defy the heavens! Since when do things go smoothly for us? Our whole lives are about fighting. We fight people. We fight the heavens. We fight gods!”

Zhou Zhengli snorted coldly. “We’re talking about going up against a True God! If we’re not careful, we could all end up dead.”

Sir Vilespirit laughed coldly and looked at everyone else. Soon, the others began giving their own opinions. It was something they had become accustomed to doing after working together for so long. When facing a new situation, they would discuss all the possibilities and ramifications. In the end, Xu Qing would make a decision based on that.

As they discussed whether or not to participate in the hunt for the goddess, Xu Qing looked off into the starry sky. Within him, Little Shadow was sending some emotional fluctuations....

“Mil... milord... there’s strong.... Very strong perfume!” With some effort, Little Shadow was able to share what it was sensing with Xu Qing.

Within Xu Qing’s soul, he could sense the fluctuations of fate growing stronger. Back when he got the war reports, Xu Qing had already come to the conclusion that his speculations were correct. The scene shown to him by the god of pain was becoming a reality. There really was a goddess on the battlefield. Fate was like a wave, and just as he had predicted, it was bringing the goddess to him....

“Milord, not far now.... Shē’s hidden... but shadow strong, senses, locked tight!” Little Shadow was getting increasingly excited.

Meanwhile, Zhou Zhengli and everyone else were reaching the end of their debate.

“How can you practice cultivation with such fear in your heart?”

“It might be dangerous, but if we’re the ones who find hēr first, think of the military credits!”

“This is pointless, everybody. The front lines are massive. The chances of us finding the goddess are miniscule.”

“It’s like fishing a needle from the sea. The only way we’ll run into this goddess is if it’s foreordained.”

“Therefore....”

All eyes eventually focused on Xu Qing. Even Zhou Zhengli sighed and looked at him, his heart burning.

Xu Qing shifted his gaze away from the starry sky and looked at the companions he had been traveling with for so long now.

“I might have a way to find the goddess,” Xu Qing said calmly. “But people will die.”

Everyone looked at him curiously.

Sir Star Ring gazed at Xu Qing with great meaning. “Before Zhou Zhengli started down this line of reasoning, I didn’t think we had any chance of finding this goddess. But he thinks it’s possible... and now you think it’s possible. It’s my choice how I live and die. If we succeed... we share the reward!”

Sir Vilespirit laughed. “Same for me!”

Li Mengtu, Yuanshan Su, and all the other ascendees thought about it and then agreed to join the effort.

The foolish but seemingly intelligent Hordeslayer and Rampart had started out very excited, but Zhou Zhengli’s arguments had been very convincing to them. Now they were hesitating. But everyone else had already agreed to continue, so they quickly transmitted a conversation between the two of them.

“This Xu fellow says he can find hēr? Is he telling the truth, or lying?”

“He said he ‘might’ have a way! I bet he’s just trying to show off. He said it that way so that he’ll have a good excuse if we don’t find hēr. And if we do find hēr, then he can take all the credit! Hmph! We can play tricks like that as well!”

“That’s so smart, brother!”

The two brothers proudly agreed to face the danger with everyone else!

Seeing that everyone had agreed, Xu Qing’s eyes glittered with determination. Turning, he followed the direction provided by Little Shadow. By tuning in on the fluctuations of fate, he shot off into the starry sky. Sir Star Ring and the others followed.

Time passed. A few days later... a rather small stellar wind drifted through the starry sky of the front lines in the eastern theater. It was full of dust and other unknown particles that made something like a nebula. It was like a long, thin strip, with lightning that crackled occasionally both inside and outside of it.

Nebulae like this weren’t uncommon in the starry sky. Because of the immense weight inside of it, the inanimate objects would clump together, eventually becoming hotter and hotter until a sun formed. Such nebulae formed when suns died. To a certain extent, it was correct to say that a nebula like that was the final breath of a dying sun.

Within this particular nebula was Goddess Starryeyes, the most wanted subject of the massive search effort. The old god was also there. Thēy had withheld no effort to conceal their auras, and had even used the magic of gods to hide in this stellar nebula. Thēy were actually using that final breath of a dying sun to help recover from thēir injuries.

“This magic will conceal our auras,” the old god said. “This location will conceal our energy. It should buy us some time to recover. Unless a Lower Immortal actually came into this nebula, the cultivators shouldn’t be able to find us. Your Grace, have you tried using your bloodline abilities to get in touch with the god emperor?”

Starryeyes was in the middle of doing some breathing exercises. Not bothering to open hēr eyes, shē calmly replied, “I got no response.”

The old god thought for a moment and was about to say something, when all of a sudden, hīs eyes flashed with golden light. He looked outside of the nebula. Out in the starry sky, he saw something rippling. Circular fluctuations rolled out as, astonishingly, a host of cultivators appeared.

They stopped right outside of the nebula. There they hovered, clearly not intending to go anywhere. There were a total of nineteen of them. In the lead was Xu Qing! His eyes glittered brightly as he looked at the majestic nebula.

Inside the nebula, Goddess Starryeyes’ chest tightened. Shē opened hēr eyes and looked out. Somehow, hēr eyes met Xu Qing’s eyes.

The tugging of fate caused Xu Qing’s heart to pound like thunder.

At the same time, Little Shadow was excitedly shouting within him. “God... God Lord’s... bloodline!”

Everything seemed normal in the starry sky! A nebula that was the last breath exhaled by a dying sun drifted along.

Xu Qing and the ascendees hovered next to it. Looking into the nebula, they saw flickering lightning and blurriness. It wasn’t possible to see the interior of the nebula clearly.

Hiding inside the nebula was the old god, whose expression was the same as ever. Hīs cultivation base had been damaged so badly hē had to struggle to remain in the True God level. However, hē fully believed that Quasi-Immortals would be incapable of seeing thēm in thēir hiding spot. It seemed to hīm that these cultivators were simply searching the area. On any other occasion, hē would simply kill them all. But at the moment... the best thing to do was ignore them.

“Your Grace, these humans cannot see us,” hē said.

The cross-legged Goddess Starryeyes’ gaze burned with golden light. After a moment of hesitation, shē suddenly said, “Kill them!”

The old god frowned and turned to look at the goddess. As far as hē was concerned, there was no need to do anything, as it would just expose them to danger.

But the old god’s gaze only caused the goddess’s gaze to turn more serious. Shē obviously knew that staying concealed was the best option. But for some reason, shē got a strange sensation when looking at the cultivators outside of the nebula. It was as if failure to attack and kill these cultivators would bring about some sort of deadly catastrophe upon hēr. It was a strange feeling, and it was extremely strong. Seeing that the old god wasn’t taking immediate action, shē glared at hīm coldly.

“Right now!”

The old god felt that something strange was going on, but hē lifted hīs right hand and made a snatching gesture. The result was that the nebula that was hiding them suddenly seethed into motion. As the nebula was taken control of, it seemed to become a sea of poison.

A wave of dust roared out toward Xu Qing and the others, threatening to instantly engulf them. The shocking power of the wave contained natural and magical laws, as well as unshakable personhood! The void rippled and the starry sky shook as destructive power was unleashed!

The moment the nebula started moving, Xu Qing and the others burst into motion.

Heaven’s principle glittered as Sir Star Ring unleashed chains of order and the canon of balance. He was bolstering everyone! A gruish eye appeared above Zhou Zhengli, linking the souls of everyone present so that they could act in unison. Sir Vilespirit waved his hand, and his bloodthirsty, devilish blade shone with red light as it offered a powerful defense. Li Mengtu’s poison became a mist that filled Yuanshan Su’s heavy mountains....

Everyone else took similar actions. All of the ascendees unleashed trump cards to deal with the incoming nebula.

At the same time, the power of Zhou Zhengli’s gruish eye ensured that they complemented each other perfectly. Thanks to their training and the ringsource they had collected, they had all long since broken into the Quasi-Immortal level.

Combined, they were as powerful as a rocky shoal on a beach. And surrounding them was Xu Qing’s majestic and astonishing immortal embryo! And the canon of space-time stretched over it all like overlapping cliffs! The wave that was the nebula swept forth with destructive force, and then slammed into the rocky shoal.

RUMBLE!

A deafening boom broke the silence.

The attacks of a True God were incomparably terrifying. Even though this was a weakened True God, this nebula attack came with a peak level of pressure. The rocky shoal only lasted for a short time before collapsing.

Everyone was injured to some degree. Some coughed up blood, while others tumbled backward. Despite that, they had managed to defend against the attack of a True God!

They were in ragged shape. They were bleeding, and their cultivation bases were in chaos. Yet they acted with smooth efficiency, and unleashed various life-saving magics. That said, there was no way they could prevent themselves from being stunned. But what stunned them wasn’t the attack. It was... that they had really found the goddess!

Xu Qing had said he could find hēr. But Zhou Zhengli and many others had secretly doubted that he was right. It wasn’t that they didn’t trust him. It was just hard for them to believe it was true. In fact, if the words hadn’t been uttered by Xu Qing himself, they would have refused to believe.

The front lines covered a huge area, so logically speaking, it should have been almost impossible to find the goddess. But now....

Feeling utterly astonished, they looked at the nebula ahead of them. As the attack dissipated, everyone realized that the nebula in front of them was now thinner. In other words, it couldn’t hide its interior as effectively as before.

And now, two figures were just barely visible inside! One was in front of the other!

The one in front looked like an old man, seemingly human, with a golden robe, terrifying fluctuations, and a cold expression. The old man stepped forward, and a screaming wind kicked up, filled with howls of agony and screams that could shake the soul. An aura spread out, creeping along and causing the starry sky to ripple and distort.

Behind the old man was an illusory temple. It was a dilapidated temple, almost a ruin. And through the broken walls, shadows shifted and writhed, as if some vicious beast were lurking inside, or a twisted monster bristling with fangs and claws.

There was a god enshrined in the temple. The god hovered in midair, looking extremely gruish, with spindly legs as thin as tree branches. Īts body was twisted strangely, and it had very long fingers that wriggled like worms. The fingernails were as long as needles, and glinted sharply in the darkness.

Īt seemed to have been severely injured, as it was twisted up in the most freakish manner. Īts torso had seemingly been bent around with great power, while its legs were bent at the waist at a sickening angle, making it seem like they might break off at any moment.

The face of the god was covered with black scales, each of which glittered with a bizarre light that made them seem like countless eyes. The mouth was freakishly huge, with the corners reaching all the way to the ears. And it was filled with razor-sharp fangs. Behind the fangs was a blood-red tongue that twitched back and forth like a living being, like a greedy snake that was ready to strike out and lick up all life in front of it.

Atop the head grew a huge crystal that emitted a faint light. It was irregularly shaped, and seemed to contain endless streams of mysterious, gleaming light. Surrounding the god were faint, violet halos that contained distorted human faces.

This was the godhood of a True God! Within it was a godly will that surpassed natural and magical laws!

Behind the old god was a young woman, who was astoundingly beautiful!

Shē looked exactly like a slender human girl. Hēr embroidered gown was the color of the deep night, and the skirt glittered with darkness. Every line of embroidery seemed to contain countless anguished souls, and every step shē took seemed to cause ghostfire to flicker within the darkness.

Hēr skin was as fair as snow, to the point where it seemed pale, as if shē had spent years out of the sunlight. And shē seemed extremely cold. Hēr facial features were exquisite, almost like a statue made by a master craftsman. Yet the angle of hēr eyebrows seemed to reveal some deep pain or resentment. Then shē frowned ever so slightly, seemingly from a profound fear inside of hēr.

Hēr eyes were like deep, mysterious pools of water, while hēr pupils glowed with a bizarre red light that somehow seemed flirtatious in the darkness. As for hēr lips, they were a stunning red color, almost as if they were covered in blood. And when shē parted those lips to speak, it seemed certain that shē would utter a curse that would damn everyone to myriad tribulations. Hair cascaded down hēr back like a waterfall, and it was a pale, lifeless, silver color.

Surrounding hēr was a faint mist, within which it was just barely possible to see tormented ghost faces. They had fangs and claws, and screamed soundlessly. None dared to get too close to hēr, but merely orbited hēr carefully.

All of it made hēr seem extremely beautiful, but at the same time, profoundly gruish. At the same time, anyone in the starry sky who caught a glimpse of hēr would be stricken with fear by hēr gaze. Shē was like an exquisite spirit who had climbed out of the abyss, combining elements of both dreams and nightmares.

When Xu Qing and the ascendees laid eyes on hēr, their minds reeled! But at the same time, all of them felt the desire to do battle.

Sir Star Ring’s eyes glittered brightly. Sir Vilespirit bristled with baleful energy. Zhou Zhengli’s eyes narrowed. Everyone else reacted similarly.

It was only Hordeslayer and Rampart who reacted differently. They were astonished. We really found hēr?

Both of them were trembling down to their souls.

Xu Qing had remained calm the entire time, yet his gaze... was fixed on the beautiful, gruish goddess who was emerging from the nebula! Goddess Starryeyes looked at all of them before focusing on Xu Qing.

Without the nebula in between, their gazes locked, and all of a sudden, the goddess’ heart filled with intense fear. Hēr eyes glittered with blood-red light, and shē pointed at Xu Qing.

“Cut him down! Pay any price!” Hēr voice echoed with uncharacteristic determination, causing the old god’s eyes to glitter.

Hē had been hēr bodyguard for many years, and had never seen anything like this happen! After the previous defeat on the front lines, shē had been lost, but hadn’t acted like this. But there was no time for hīm to make inquiries. Since hē had chosen to act earlier, hē now had no choice but to erase all traces of thēir presence here. As for these cultivators... hē would kill them all! And it had to happen quickly!

The old god who looked like a human closed hīs eyes. Behind hīm, the temple rumbled, and the god floating inside of it erupted with godly might. It sent the starry sky into chaos, ripping the nebula to shreds as the temple appeared above. It went from illusory to corporeal, and it began to unleash a terrifying mutagen.

That power spread out to lock down the area. Then the god inside of the temple came out into the open! The starry sky transformed dramatically.

Xu Qing had encountered True Gods before. But this was his first time dealing with a True God in the true sense! Bimo Si, the god of pain, had been returning, and not complete. In fact, there were many details about hīm that had been different from hīs complete form. For example, hīs temple, the god inside of it, and hīs godhood....

That god in the temple is nearly cut in half at the waist. That must be the doing of Immortal Monarch Spirit Jade. This god... is already seriously wounded!

Xu Qing shot backward, but his eyes glittered as he focused on the temple. The other ascendees unleashed their cultivation bases as they also fell back.

The temple, meanwhile, rumbled loudly and shone with golden light. Though it was largely crumbling, the godly might from inside was as majestic as a sea. And as the god from inside emerged, intense rumbling sounds filled the area. Mountain-toppling, sea-draining power swept out like a storm.

The starry sky rippled and the void distorted. Xu Qing and the ascendees were shaken to the core. It was like an instinct from their life force, causing their souls to tremble out of control. Fear took root inside of them on the deepest level.

Then a godly voice echoed out.

“Terror!”

The godly voice caused the seed to grow. It bloomed, producing fruit and bringing terror to every corner of their beings. Blood sprayed out of their mouths, as bizarre mutations struck them.

They grew scales all over their bodies, their arms became very skinny, they felt their faces distorting, and they sprouted fangs.... They were all starting to transform to look exactly like this god!

The fruit of terror blossomed within them, causing them to shake violently from fear. It seemed like their souls were being corrupted. If the process completed, they might not be dead, but they would be close to it. And that would be because what was left behind wouldn’t be them. They would simply be believers in the True God to possess as mediums!

That was the real strength of True Gods.

The grievous blow landed by Immortal Monarch Spirit Jade, and the suppression by the immortal will in the area, put this True God at a big disadvantage. The god was struggling to do this. If hē had been dealing with ordinary cultivators, things might have been going better. Hīs weakness wouldn’t have been so obvious.

But Xu Qing and the ascendees were not ordinary cultivators. Therefore, the instant that this True God’s power spread out, Xu Qing and the others unleashed their trump cards.

Whether it was the hypertoxic poison Li Mengtu could utilize after becoming a Quasi-Immortal, or Sir Vilespirit’s mysterious broken blade, or Zhou Zhengli’s eye of foresight... they let loose all of them in a defensive manner. Sir Star Ring, Yuanshan Su, Hordeslayer and Rampart held nothing back.

They suppressed the mutations. Furthermore... their formation did not falter. They stayed tightly organized around Xu Qing.

Each person unleashed a trump card in defense, but not just in self-defense. The trump cards spread out, overlapping and merging together to completely cover Xu Qing! They were like numerous barriers around him! Within those barriers, Xu Qing didn’t need to worry about his own defenses. All he had to do... was attack!

This was the strategy they had devised along the way. Xu Qing was the strongest among them. He was the heart of their team. So they would bolster him. At the moment, their fleshly bodies were mutating, their souls were being corrupted, and their minds were full of terror. But they went all out to form the defenses, whereupon Xu Qing summoned his immortal embryo.

It towered high into the starry sky, the Aurora Immortal Palace glittering within it. The immortal embryo lifted its hand... and smashed it toward the temple.

The starry sky trembled as massive pressure built up. The huge hand of the immortal embryo shot down with astonishing momentum. Just as it was about to hit the temple, the True God emerged from inside.

The twisted frame of the god was about to break at the waist, which was a very bizarre sight. The long, spindly arms then reached up, and the god waved a finger in the direction of the immortal embryo’s hand. The power of a True God erupted.

The wave of that finger caused Xu Qing’s immortal embryo to rumble and blur. Mutagen erupted within it, rapidly spreading out. Before the hand could land, the immortal embryo collapsed. The backlash would have seriously injured Xu Qing, but instead, it was split among the ascendees. Blood sprayed out of their mouths, and their auras vibrated.

Eyes bloodshot, Xu Qing once again formed his immortal embryo.

The True God suddenly vanished, then appeared right in front of the cultivators. That long, skinny finger once again pointed out. A sensation of terror erupted within them, all while the might of the True God weighed down like a destructive mountain.

A rumbling boom echoed out. The blood drained from the faces of Xu Qing and the ascendees. They began to bleed as their bodies withered and their souls distorted from the corruption.

The defenses were starting to melt. Li Mengtu’s poison was thinning. Zhou Zhengli’s eye was shattering. Sir Star Ring’s chains were crumbling. Hordeslayer and Rampart were wailing in agony.

Suddenly, two of the ascendees couldn’t last any longer, and the flames of their life force were extinguished. And yet, they held nothing back, tapping into secret magics to last a bit longer.

The scene playing out caused the True God to frown. Hē was actually in very bad shape, and the attacks from earlier had taken a huge amount of effort. Although these humans were not Lower Immortals, only Quasi-Immortals, they were clearly extraordinary. The person they were defending had the power of an immortal embryo. If hē was at hīs peak, hē could kill this person easily, but right now, all hē felt was a sense of great danger. What was even more important to hīm was that this fight end quickly.

The True God looked in the direction of the goddess, who had been watching this whole time. “Your Grace, let’s work together!”

Starryeyes lifted hēr foot to step forward. But before hēr foot could fall, hēr eyes glittered mysteriously. And instead of taking a step forward, shē actually stepped backward. And then, a teleportation portal appeared beneath hēr feet! The portal activated! Hēr gaze then fell upon Xu Qing, who was the very person that was causing fear to build up within hēr.

Xu Qing looked over with narrowed eyes. He could see what the goddess was doing. “The portal will complete activation in twenty breaths of time!”

Zhou Zhengli, Sir Star Ring, and everyone else reacted with visible shock, just like Xu Qing. Despite the physical pain and corruption to their souls, they were all frowning.

Xu Qing sighed softly. So did everyone else except for Hordeslayer and Rampart. The plan they had come up with on the way was to work together to unleash all of their strongest trump cards. They would create a killing move that would only work once! In reality, it would have been best for them if the goddess did join in and fight next to the True God. Then their killing move wouldn’t be wasted.

But this goddess was very decisive. It didn’t matter that they seemed so weak that all the goddess had to do was join forces with the True God, and they would be killed. Unfortunately... shē wasn’t coming over!

The reality was that they weren’t faking anything. They were really not going to be able to hold out much longer....

At that point, Xu Qing made a snap decision. Killing intent burned in his eyes. His cultivation base raged, and his immortal embryo formed again. And this time... it didn’t just have the Aurora Immortal Palace glittering within it. It had an iron skewer! It was inside the immortal palace, thrumming aggressively.

The canon of all the ascendees bolstered it. Sir Star Ring’s order and balance, combined with heaven’s principle, settled onto the iron skewer. Zhou Zhengli’s eye of foresight flowed around the skewer. Li Mengtu, Yuanshan Su, Sir Vilespirit and all the other ascendees used their canon to add their own effects. Hordeslayer and Rampart turned into swords that merged with the skewer.

With all of their Quasi-Immortal might, the iron skewer pulsed with a glow that illuminated the starry sky. And the addition of Xu Qing’s immortal embryo ensured that the iron skewer was astonishingly mighty.

But things weren’t over yet.... Next, the Green Heaven appeared within the immortal embryo!! Instantly, the starry sky filled with rumbling sounds, and the True God’s face fell.

Just barely visible within the Green Heaven was an astonishing coffin! Inside of that coffin was the god of pain. That god’s godly might had already been extracted and put into the iron skewer, filling it with even more heaven-shaking, earth-shattering momentum.

At this point, things still weren’t over. Xu Qing’s space-time canon and overlapping universes caused a host of images to spring up around the iron skewer. And within every single one of the different space-times, there was another astonishing iron skewer!

As Xu Qing’s eyes glittered with killing intent, he waved his hand, and over a hundred iron skewers stirred. They pierced out of the various instances of space-time, and then appeared on the battlefield, where they combined together!

Over a hundred iron skewers merged to make a nail! The nail had the combined power of all the ascendees, including nineteen canons, Aurora’s power, and Green Heaven’s might. And then, it shot right toward the True God! There was no way to describe how fast it moved. In fact, everyone present saw nothing more than a blur of afterimages that occurred in the past.

But what happened in the present and the future was that the nail stabbed right into the True God! It hit hīm right in hīs injury, at hīs waist where hē was almost cut in half! It stabbed in viciously!

A scream echoed out. The True God trembled as all of the godly might within hīm went into chaos. Hīs temple collapsed, and hīs godhood went weak. God blood poured out of hīm.

But hē was still a True God. The combined trump card of Xu Qing and the ascendees was intended to kill this True God, but even though hē was weak and wounded, that was no easy task. The only way it might have happened would be if this True God was in the middle of returning, similar to what happened with the god of pain.

The result was that this True God was not killed by the nail. However... it did shatter hīs True God cultivation level! Hīs aura weakened, and hīs level dropped! Hīs god magic of terror was diminished, causing the mutations plaguing the ascendees to reverse automatically.

All of this takes a bit of time to describe, but actually happened in the time it takes a spark to fly off a piece of flint. Screaming echoed out as the diminished old god glared with killing intent at the cultivators and prepared to fight back. But then hīs pupils constricted, and hē fell back.

The reason was that... the auras of numerous cultivators were closing in from off in the distance. It was the Longscale Regiment, which Xu Qing and the ascendees had contacted earlier. They were on the way!

The old god rushed toward the teleportation portal being activated by the goddess. Unfortunately... the moment hē started moving, Goddess Starryeyes pointed at Xu Qing.

“Self-detonate and kill him!” shē said. “You won’t be responsible for your own resurrection. My father will guide it! That’s an oath I hereby swear on my own bloodline!”

The old god stopped in place.

The old god had already been badly injured, and had narrowly escaped death at the hands of Immortal Monarch Spirit Jade. While escorting Starryeyes, it had been a difficult challenge simply to stay in the True God level. It was like a dam that had been thrown together to hold back a chaotic maelstrom of water.

Hīs actions moments before had weakened hīm even further, especially dealing with the combined killing move from Xu Qing and the ascendees. That nail had struck hīm in exactly the same spot where hē had been wounded by Immortal Monarch Spirit Jade, and the reverberations were causing the dam to quiver on the verge of collapse.

Hīs temple had crumbled, making it impossible for hīm to maintain hīs True God cultivation level. His godhood was fading and hē was about to drop out of the True God level. Hē was essentially an oil lamp that was about to run out of fuel.

What was more, among the auras of the approaching cultivators were... Lower Immortal auras!

Given that, hīs mission was in grave danger. Hē had originally been planning to flee with Starryeyes and continued to protect hēr. But then Goddess Staryeyes gave orders in hēr godly voice. Shē ordered hīm... to die.

For a short moment, all hē did was look at hēr, a complicated expression on hīs face.

Gods did not have emotions. Hē was aware of that, of course. But perhaps because of hīs cultivation level dropping or perhaps because of hīs serious injury, there were fluctuations in hīs godliness. Because of those fluctuations, hē found hīmself thinking about Starryeyes when shē was a little girl. Hē had watched hēr growing up, rising to great heights step by step. Hē had watched as shē became famous.

Are these emotions? hē wondered. Then hē turned toward Xu Qing and the ascendees, who were racing toward hīm. Heart filling with determination, hē headed toward them.

Golden light shone in hīs eyes, spreading rapidly to become a huge sea. Within that golden sea was terrifying godly might. The old god’s mangled body was visible in the golden light, rapidly expanding, growing larger, aura reaching terrifying levels.

Scattered bits of deafening chanting rang out that could shatter souls. The sound pushed the golden sea even farther in all directions. These were fluctuations that could shatter starry skies and shake universes!

This was hīs... self-detonation! Though hīs cultivation base had dropped and hīs godhood had dimmed, hē... was still a True God! The sound and light was like infinite suns exploding, creating a destructive force that could devastate anything in its path.

It was a light that could illuminate the cosmos. It swept through the stars! It enveloped everything! The cloud was wiped out of existence by it, as were all traces of the passage of Goddess Starryeyes. As a result, nobody present was capable of locking onto hēr to track hēr.

Xu Qing and the ascendees raced in the opposite direction, but weren’t fast enough to escape the golden light. The light swept over everything. Planets were reduced to rubble. The starry sky shattered. Everything became nothing! It didn’t matter that a Lower Immortal aura swept out from the incoming cultivators, sending immortal power into the area to counter the mightiness of the self-detonation.

Xu Qing and the ascendees were too close to avoid it.... It was as if this had been foreordained by fate, and was just happening a bit sooner than expected! Xu Qing’s heart raced as he watched the color gold taking over everything he could see.

He unleashed his cultivation base defensively, sending his immortal embryo out to defend, not just himself, but the ascendees around him. Everyone joined their power together. They resisted as one!

However, as the golden light surged.... His immortal embryo writhed, twisted, and then collapsed. As his fleshly body began to vibrate, numerous space-time instances appeared, out of which different versions of himself emerged. He went all out to fight back.

Sir Star Ring and everyone else went crazy, holding nothing back in the moment of crisis.

It was hard to say how much time passed before the light faded away, and the rumbling ceased. The golden light from the old god’s self-detonation had passed them.

The cultivator army arrived.... The cultivators looked at Xu Qing and the others with respect in their eyes, as well as shock at the sight of the devastation. The commanding officer was an old man who was a Lower Immortal. He looked at the spot where the cloud had been, then at Xu Qing.

“You uncovered clues about the goddess, and then you risked your lives to fight a True God. This... will be reported to my superior. All of you... have performed a great service! Now, go back and... rest up.”

He gave some medicinal pills to them, and then shot off to continue the search. The cultivators under his command gave out medicinal pills as well, then followed him.

Soon, everything was quiet.

Xu Qing hovered in the starry sky, his clothes in shreds, and his face pale. He coughed up a massive mouthful of blood. His fleshly body and soul were weak and exhausted. He turned to look at his companions....

Visible on Sir Star Ring’s forehead was a magical symbol that was currently fading away. It was a life-saving magic his Master had given him. It had obviously been spent and was now useless. He had a host of wounds, all of which were bleeding profusely. He was soaked in blood.

Next to him was Zhou Zhengli, who was trembling. Black blood oozed out of both of his eyes. His eyes... were empty pits. He had been blinded. That was the source of his canon.

Li Mengtu had been ripped in half at the waist, and was unconscious. It was hard to say if he would live. Yuanshan Su was in a similar state. Hordeslayer and Rampart were barely conscious. In the end, they had abandoned their fleshly bodies to become immortal swords, and in that way had barely managed to safeguard their souls. Sir Vilespirit had lost an arm, and his broken sword was covered in cracks. He had sustained serious injuries.

The other ascendees were all in horrible shape. Some were missing limbs or other parts of their bodies, and most were unconscious and in no shape to fight.

In terms of their numbers... they had lost seven people! Those seven had been destroyed in body and soul by the golden light.... That was the disastrous result of them working together and distributing the injury between them. They had numbered nineteen, but now they were only twelve.

Xu Qing looked at the survivors then stared off into the distance. His heart was ice cold as he sent a message to Little Shadow to have it start looking for the goddess again. He was not ready to give up!

Zhou Zhengli, who had lost his eyes, hoarsely said, “I said before... that this would be extremely dangerous. That was a True God, after all. Were it not for the Young Lord, we would have lost more than we did!

“But we’re cultivators. We fight heaven, fight people, and fight gods.... When we perish, it’s simply our dao being dispelled. When you fight against fate, death is nothing abnormal! And it makes it worth it to die alongside a True God!”

Zhou Zhengli smiled, but within that smile was a bit of defiance.

Sir Vilespirit’s eyes were bloodshot as he listened to Zhou Zhengli. Then he said, “Sadly, we didn’t get that goddess!”

His voice seemed full of regret.

Sir Star Ring listened to the two of them. “Xu Qing, you found the goddess once. Can you find her again?”

Xu Qing looked over and met Sir Star Ring’s gaze.

Sir Star Ring’s eyes glowed with killing intent as he continued, “Seven of us died, most of them miserably. Whether it’s for them or for us, I want to catch that goddess! I bet you feel the same, don’t you?”

Sir Star Ring had noted the goddess’s strange actions, and how shē had seemingly restrained hēr own killing intent upon catching sight of Xu Qing.

Xu Qing looked over the group. There were only two who were in fighting condition. Himself and Sir Star Ring.

“The True God’s self-detonation wiped out all traces of hēr passage,” he said. “Shē teleported away leaving no clues behind. Right now... shē’s too far away for my spirit pet to detect.”

Sir Star Ring said nothing in response.

Xu Qing turned to look off into the starry sky. His eyes narrowed. “But... there’s something else I can try.”

Xu Qing pulled out a teleportation jade slip. By making a few adjustments, he transformed it into an entropic teleportation slip. Normal teleportation slips would teleport the user to a specific location. But the entropic variety... were random. They would teleport the user to an unpredictable location. How they worked was really up to fate.

This was the method Xu Qing was thinking of using. He could not sense any traces of the goddess. However, fate had already brought hēr to him. So this time, instead of waiting around, he figured he would take the initiative....

His eyes glowed with a mysterious light. If fate had foreordained everything, then Xu Qing was certain that an entropic teleportation would get him just the result he sought.

With the teleportation jade slip in hand, he looked at Sir Star Ring.

Sir Star Ring looked thoughtfully at the jade slip. He asked no questions. He just walked over to stand next to Xu Qing within the range of the jade slip.

Zhou Zhengli and Sir Vilespirit bowed to the two of them. They were not strong enough to participate in the fight that was to come. They needed time to heal. What was more, the unconscious ascendees required medical treatment. Right now, they had to go to the nearest Longscale Regiment garrison.

Voice hoarse, Zhou Zhengli said, “Young Lord. Sir Star Ring. We’ll wait at the garrison for news of your victory! Capture the goddess!”

Xu Qing nodded and crushed the jade slip. The light of teleportation spread, covering Xu Qing and Sir Star Ring. Rumbling sounds echoed out. The two of them vanished!

Goddess Starryeyes sped along in a black beam of light through the front lines of the eastern theater. Shē wasn’t very far from the territory of the gods. At the same time, he would be strengthened.

All of it turned into a majestic star chart. This was the metal, wood, water, fire, and earth belonging to Xu Qing. The star chart emanated spatial fluctuations, and then... the power of time.

All of this takes a bit of time to describe, but it happened in the time it takes a spark to fly off a piece of flint. And then the iron skewer was right in front of hēr forehead.

A few days later, a handful of rumors struck the eastern theater in the Fifth Star Ring, spreading like a tempest through all of the various armies.

The goddess had been captured! The captors were in a Corpsedrainer squadron attached to the Longscale Regiment. Their leader was Xu Qing! The squadron was under the protection of the Longscale Regiment, who was delivering the goddess to the red giant, where the lieutenant general’s headquarters was located.

The news was explosive. If it had been a Lower Immortal who captured the goddess, or some other high-ranking army leader, then the cultivators in the eastern theater wouldn’t have been so shocked. But... the captors were Corpsedrainers! It was really astonishing news.

After all, the Corpsedrainers didn’t have a very good reputation on the front lines, and they were far below the army cultivators in terms of importance. But now they had accomplished a great deed. It was puzzling and almost inconceivable.
