“You did well....”

As the voice spoke, a solar flare erupted in front of Xu Qing and the ascendees, becoming a brilliant light that illuminated everything in the area. It was like a blazing fire in the middle of the universe.

Within the sea of light, 100,000 silver eyes with vertical pupils opened up. Astonishingly, each of those pupils contained a reflection of the violent clash between the ascendees and the goddess. It was like an overview of the entire event.

Several breaths of time passed, and then the images faded. The 100,000 eyes focused on Xu Qing and the ascendees. Then they looked at Goddess Starryeyes, gripped in Xu Qing’s hand.

A majestic force then locked onto the goddess. Xu Qing released his grip, and Starryeyes was dragged into the sea of light, where shē vanished.

Xu Qing couldn’t help but feel a twinge of regret in his heart. He hadn’t finished extracting all the ringsource. Though it had seemed like the process was going quickly, he had actually been trying to draw the journey out to have more time. The goddess’ ringsource really was different from that of other gods. Though it wasn’t literally endless, it would begin to renew itself each time it seemed like it was about to run out. Though the overall quantity was smaller each time it happened, it was still incomparably pure.

If I could have absorbed it for a bit longer, I could probably break through.

Though he was sighing inside, he also knew that Immortal Lord Deepgloom needed the goddess a lot more than he did. So he suppressed his disappointment.

Thinking about the reward for accomplishing the mission, he bowed deeply. The other ascendees did the same.

A moment later, the ancient voice spoke again. “The reward for finding clues leading to the capture of the goddess was 1,000,000 military credits and 10 portions of ringsource. The reward for capturing the goddess was 10,000,000 military credits and 100 portions of ringsource. You people not only found clues, you also captured the goddess. It can be considered an amazing service!’

Everyone was starting to get excited.

“Xu Qing!” the voice said.

Xu Qing solemnly took a step forward. 100,000 eyes looked at him from within the sea of light.

“In short order, when I deliver this goddess to Immortal Lord Deepgloom, I will submit your official application for the daoist title of true monarch, as well as... your dao weapon! Do you have any requirements for the dao weapon?”

Xu Qing thought about it for a moment, his eyes glittering. Then he clasped hands. “Your humble servant would like to request a dao weapon designed for slaughter!”

“It can be done. I’ll deliver it personally. The reward will be delivered within seven days. You can wait in the flame pagodas here. This star naturally accumulates ringsource, so make good use of it while you can.” The voice faded away.

The 100,000 silver eyes closed, and moments later, the sea of light disappeared. At the same time, twelve pagodas made of lava rose up in the area. The flame pagodas emitted constant pulses of ringsource that caused the canon of Xu Qing and the ascendees to ripple.

Sir Star Ring, Zhou Zhengli, and all the others were visibly moved.

“According to what I heard recently,” Zhou Zhengli said, “this red giant was made using the skulls and god blood of a number of True Gods that Immortal Lord Deepgloom slaughtered years ago! He also put some of his own canon into it. Even a Lower Immortal who practices cultivation here would benefit greatly. Because the star is unstable... no one is permitted to stay here except by invitation!”

Xu Qing nodded. He looked at the ascendees, and it was plain to see how difficult this mission had been for all of them.

With a serious expression on his face, he bowed to them. “I can’t share the title of true monarch, but I can share all the other rewards, including the ringsource and the military credits! As for the Immortal Lord’s dao weapon, though it’s being given to me, it can be our communal property!”

Zhou Zhengli looked back at him solemnly. Sir Star Ring said nothing. Li Mengtu grinned, and Sir Vilespirit cleared his throat. Yuanshan Su looked down. The others reacted similarly. They all bowed back. Hordeslayer and Rampart seemed somewhat excited, as if having Xu Qing bow to them was a reward in and of itself.

After that, Xu Qing turned and entered his flame pagoda. Everyone else entered their own respective pagodas to start working on cultivation. And that was how the days passed.

As they waited for their reward, and as the goddess was delivered to Immortal Lord Deepgloom, the black and white color that was superimposed over the battlefield of the Fourth and Fifth Star Rings constantly shifted. It was clear... that the white color that represented the immortals was advancing, while the black mutagen was falling back.

The change affected the front lines in all the theaters of war. Clearly, the cultivators had gained the upper hand. The deadlock between God Emperor Death Departure and Immortal Lord Deepgloom had been broken.

Two majestic figures within the black and the white were looking at each other.

And then... a voice spoke. “Deepgloom, you should know that if I lose control of the front lines, then this war will reach another level. It will be a battle between a God Paragon and an Immortal Paragon. Are you people ready for that...?”

***

In the middle of the Fourth Star Ring, far from the battlefield, the mutagen levels were very high. On the edge of the starry sky there, a god flew along, with an ancient aura and a physical frame as large as an asteroid. Hē was panting for breath, and had nearly passed out. Hē seemed almost to be moving forward on instinct alone. Hē was moving in a very specific direction, as if hē was being drawn there. Perhaps hē was returning there.

Inside of that god, where the heart had once been, there was an empty cavity in which two people sat cross-legged. One was a man, the other was a woman. At a certain point, the woman opened her eyes, cast her senses outside, and then spoke in a soft voice.

“We’re almost there, husband....”

The man opened his eyes and nodded. “The lantern on the front lines really did attract a lot of attention. Unfortunately... we need to stay even more hidden going forward.”

Were Xu Qing present, he would recognize these two people instantly. They were Young Lord Aurora and his daoist partner, Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix!

Six days flew by in a flash. As the day the lieutenant general had mentioned approached, Xu Qing and the ascendees worked on their cultivation in their respective flame pagodas. The ringsource gathered by the red giant wasn’t as pure as that from the goddess, but was still very beneficial as they healed from their injuries. In the six days that passed, most of them ended up recovering fully.

Xu Qing was particularly benefited. The ringsource from the red giant was of great help in pushing his immortal embryo toward completion. It formed a great complement to the ringsource he had collected from the goddess, making it easier to absorb. The advancement of his immortal embryo put him on the very cusp of mid Quasi-Immortal.

As it turns out, cultivation on the battlefield really is more efficient.

Inside the flame pagoda, Xu Qing opened his eyes. They glowed as if heavenly bodies swirled within them, making him seem extraordinarily refined. Combined with his extraordinary good looks, he really embodied the spirit of what it meant to be an immortal.

Sadly... this ringsource is too placid. If I didn’t have the purer kind from the goddess to balance it out, it wouldn’t be as good for healing purposes.

Xu Qing still regretted not being able to make better use of the goddess. It wasn’t that he had never harvested ringsource from a True God before. In fact, he currently had a True God in his heaven beyond heaven, and he would occasionally extract ringsource from it. But Starryeyes’ ringsource was just much more pure.

The daughter of a god emperor. The blood of a God Lord.... They’re really extraordinary.

Just thinking about extracting ringsource from that goddess caused Xu Qing to lick his lips. That pure level of ringsource was really perfect for him! It could even be called incomparable.

Unfortunately, he had already turned the goddess in for the mission, so all he could do was suppress his disappointment and settle down to work on his cultivation. But right then...

A solar flare erupted on the red giant! Intense rumbling sounds echoed out as the boundless sea of light swept out to cover the entire star, sending out infinite glowing light. That light swept over Xu Qing’s flame pagoda, and after it was gone, so was the pagoda.

A boundless power swept through the sea of light, causing a huge silver eye to appear right in front of Xu Qing. The eye opened!

Trembling, Xu Qing stood, his expression solemn as he bowed to the silver eye. “Well met, Lieutenant General!”

The silver eye regarded Xu Qing for a moment, and then that most ancient voice echoed within the sea of light.

“Here is your reward.”

As the voice drifted out, ten pieces of glittering jade drifted out, rectangular in shape and glowing with light. There was also a medallion with military credits in it. The ten pieces of jade pulsed with ringsource, and their swirling light made them look like jewels. The military credit medallion looked ordinary in nature, but its contents were astonishing.

“This is the reward for providing clues leading to the capture of the goddess. Ten portions of ringsource and 1,000,000 military credits!”

Next came 100 pieces of jade and ten military credit medallions. The contrast between the first reward and the second was clear, and the latter simply pulsed with dazzling, multicolored light. If these items were displayed in public, they would cause countless cultivators to go crazy with longing.

“This is the reward for capturing the goddess alive!”

Xu Qing looked at it all, his eyes glittering. Forcing himself to remain calm, he stood there quietly.

“As for the title of true monarch....” The silver eye suddenly seemed to become more solemn. “There are some things you need to understand. Apprentices of Immortal Lords are true monarchs. Here in the Fifth Star Ring, the dao of immortals was established by the Immortal Paragon. By refining countless gods into spirit lineaments and natural law, destiny aura was formed.

“The Immortal Paragon enjoys fifty percent of the destiny aura, while the eleven Immortal Lords have forty percent and the true monarchs get the remaining ten percent! Those who use destiny aura are blessed by the destiny aura, and receive the protection of the star ring.”

Xu Qing’s gaze sharpened. He had known about true monarchs being the apprentices of Immortal Lords. But he didn’t know very much about destiny aura, so this new information was intriguing.

The ancient voice spoke again, and this time it boomed like thunder.

“Xu Qing! This crystal has been provided to you by Immortal Lord Deepgloom. It was formed from the destiny aura of the Fifth Star Ring. Imprint it with divine will, and the star ring itself will bless you with a name!”

Golden threads emerged, combining in front of Xu Qing to form a finger-nail sized golden crystal! It looked similar to the godhood of True Gods that Xu Qing had seen, but there were some differences.

Xu Qing instinctively looked at it, and the moment he did, he felt like he could see the entire Fifth Star Ring spinning. He saw infinite universes, boundless starry skies, and numerous heavens beyond heaven. He was just about to put his mark on the crystal... when all of a sudden, within the Fifth Star Ring inside the crystal, next to the eleven active heavens beyond heaven, light glittered brightly. It came from what had once been the Aurora heaven beyond heaven.

The word ‘Green’ was forming there. Green light erupted from it, sweeping across universes.

The silver eye uttered an expression of surprise. “Is the issue of Aurora Heaven’s title being settled now?”

Xu Qing looked dazed. When he finally cleared his head, he saw that there was an additional word on the crystal.

Green!

Upon seeing that word... it was as if countless species had joined voices to speak a title that echoed in Xu Qing’s ears.

True Monarch Green Aurora!

It was closely linked to Xu Qing’s providence! At that moment, Xu Qing felt a close connection to the Fifth Star Ring appear within himself. He was now more closely linked to the Fifth Star Ring than ever before. Now, wherever he went, he knew that he would be able to sense the Fifth Star Ring calling to him.

This is destiny aura.... Xu Qing thought.

At the same time, his cultivation base received an augmentation from the destiny aura of the Fifth Star Ring, causing him to instantly achieve a breakthrough! Rumbling sounds filled him as his immortal embryo appeared behind him, towering over the red giant. Instantly, a tempestuous vortex formed, as an immortal will glittered into the starry sky. Just like the tempest, his cultivation base raged to new heights.

He instantly broke past the limits of early Quasi-Immortal and entered... mid Quasi-Immortal! The moment he entered mid Quasi-Immortal, he could sense immortal energy as vast as a sea roiling within him. His hair whipped about, and the pressure he radiated vastly surpassed anything from before.

Just barely, he could sense an immortal reserve within him. That immortal reserve was the foundation upon which to control his own fate. As of that moment, Xu Qing’s eyes started shining with silver light! That was one of the hallmarks of immortals!

After Xu Qing was bolstered by the destiny aura, achieving a cultivation base breakthrough, it became possible to see a figure clad in a daoist robe, standing in the huge silver eye in front of him. It was a middle-aged cultivator who seemed threatening without being angry. His daoist robe was blue, he pulsed with an immortal energy, and his eyes seemed to contain universes and star domains.

He was the lieutenant general of the eastern theater. He stepped out into the open and stood in front of Xu Qing, looking at him with glittering eyes.

Xu Qing took a deep breath to calm himself, then prepared to bow.

The lieutenant general shook his head and sent out a gentle force that prevented Xu Qing from bowing.

“You have the title true monarch. If you were a Lower Immortal, I would need to bow to you. And even though you’re not a Lower Immortal yet, we have equal status, so there’s no need for you to bow. When you eventually leave this battlefield, you will be able to select an Immortal Lord as your Master!”

Xu Qing knew that he should follow the rules of the Fifth Star Ring, so he made no further attempt to bow. However, he still made a sincere expression of gratitude. “Many thanks for your support and guidance, Lieutenant General. I, Xu Qing, will never forget it.”

The lieutenant general nodded approvingly. “You earned it and deserve it. Now we come to the final reward for capturing the goddess. The Immortal Lord’s dao weapon!”

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered. This... was what he had been waiting for this entire time! The ringsource and the military credits would be useful. But things like that could be acquired by other means. Even the title of true monarch was really just a change in status. What Xu Qing cared the most about right now was battle prowess! And the dao weapon of an Immortal Lord would definitely improve his battle prowess and make him more lethal!

When the lieutenant general saw how focused Xu Qing was on the dao weapon, he smiled faintly. With the wave of his hand, he sent a host of silver streams of light flying out of his sleeve and up into the void overhead.

Xu Qing’s pupils constricted as he looked up. The silver threads entered the sea of light above. A brief rumbling sound echoed out, and then some red dots appeared above. The red dots seemed to blossom, turning into a host of red flowers. Finally, they combined, seemingly filling the entire sea of light, until the dome of heaven was the color of blood.

Immense pressure seemed to form above, and then rifts began to open up. Gradually, the rifts connected and combined, creating a huge, irregularly shaped opening! It snaked through the canopy of heaven for over 3,000,000 meters. Blood-red mist poured down from it like a waterfall.

Within that turbid wave of mist was a blade of bone, ghastly white and pulsing with fiendishness. It looked like an inverted crescent moon, shining like blood! It was covered with countless inscriptions that seemed natural, but at the same time, the work of craftsmanship. Maybe they were both.[1]

As the blade descended, the sea of light in the area shrank down and formed into a vortex.

What was especially bizarre was that the spatial rifts that had opened up, upon being filled with the bright red light of the blade, seemed to transform into thousands upon thousands of writhing karma threads. Their interactions became restraining magical law that controlled the blade light, making it a deadly arc that could sever reincarnation itself.

“This blade was used by Immortal Lord Deepgloom after he and other Immortal Lords joined forces to slaughter the last God Lord in the Fifth Star Ring. It’s a precious treasure made from the fingernail of that God Lord! That God Lord’s godhood was that of slaughter, and thus, this blade... can unleash astonishing levels of slaughter!”

It seemed like the blade could hear his words; as it descended, it vibrated and released a thrumming sound. That mere thrumming sent all starlight tumbling away from it. The sound summoned countless discarnate souls that the blade had destroyed, and they materialized around it like an army of demonic monsters. However, they didn’t dare to wail or howl; they turned into a mottled fog of blood that surrounded the blade.

The edge of the blade sliced space as it passed, leaving behind wounds like those inflicted by a ravenous animal. This was the dao weapon of an Immortal Lord!

Xu Qing was astonished. Acting on instinct, he reached out to grab the blade! The moment his hand closed around the hilt, he felt like he could hear gods howling in the starry sky, a sound which could pierce through all universes. All of a sudden, Xu Qing’s view of the world became the color of rust. A terrifying aura spread out that caused his scalp to go numb.

“You have been given all of your rewards. Half a month from now, an important event will take place. According to the treaty that has been agreed upon between God Lord Death Departure of the Fourth Star Ring and Immortal Lord Deepgloom, there will be a hostage exchange!

“Since you were the one to capture the goddess, the Immortal Lord has decreed... that you will be the one to hand her over, Xu Qing! It will happen on the front lines of the eastern theater. And my entire army will be there to keep you safe!”

1. The characters used to describe this blade are often rendered as machete or scimitar. They literally just mean curved blade, although they could also be rendered in other ways, such as crooked blade or even bent blade. Considering the description of it being like an inverted crescent moon, I feel like it’s supposed to be something akin to a sickle or falx as opposed to a straight-bladed weapon. Here are some examples of what I mean. There is never a super clear description, though, so in the end, it’s up to your imagination. That said... (minor spoilers): later descriptions indicate that the blade is only about 5 inches long, so using something like “scimitar” or “machete” doesn’t seem appropriate. Because of that, I’m going to render it as blade, or occasionally curved blade as a reminder of its shape. ☜

God Emperor Death Departure and Immortal Lord Deepgloom had agreed to a hostage exchange treaty.... That was not something Xu Qing had anticipated would happen, much less that the Immortal Lord would assign him to be the escort.

As the lieutenant general explained things, a thoughtful look appeared in Xu Qing’s eyes. Previously, he had come to the conclusion that the goddess was important because of the blood of the imperial clan that ran in hēr veins, and how it contained the godhood power of hēr father, God Emperor Death Departure. Capturing hēr could give the Immortal Lord a much deeper understanding of how to deal with Death Departure’s godhood. By extension, that would enable him to gain an advantage in the war. But now... the goddess was being returned.

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed. He gripped the blade as he listened to the lieutenant general. When it was appropriate for him to speak, he said, “Lieutenant General, is there any chance you know why the exalted Immortal Lord has agreed to a hostage exchange with the god emperor?”

The lieutenant general glanced out at the starry sky briefly. “Because God Emperor Death Departure made a few concessions that we Fifth Star Ring cultivators simply couldn’t reject!”

Xu Qing was instantly curious about what sort of concessions could have been offered that were impossible to reject, and would even prompt the Immortal Lord to give back Goddess Starryeyes.

“To begin with,” continued the lieutenant general, “God Emperor Death Departure offered to return five Lower Immortals who were captured by the Fourth Star Ring but not killed. That was the first concession.

“Of those five Lower Immortals, one was Immortal Lord Deepgloom’s last apprentice, who had patrolled the border with him for 10,000 years. He performed astounding services on the battlefield, and specialized in assassinations. Several years ago, the gods laid a cunning trap that resulted in his capture. All attempts to rescue him failed, and he suffered years of torture.

“The other four aren’t as important, but have still performed amazing services for the Fifth Star Ring. All of them were doomed to be tortured to death, but now we have a chance to get them back. So that’s the first concession offered by God Emperor Death Departure.

“But there’s a second concession, and as I said, the Fifth Star Ring simply couldn’t reject it. Even the Immortal Lord fully approved.... It’s a roaming universe!” The lieutenant general’s eyes gleamed as he looked at Xu Qing. “You’re an ascendee, so though you know a bit about history, your understanding is not comprehensive.

“Countless years ago here in the Fifth Star Ring, during the war between cultivators and local gods, the fighting was intense. The slaughter that was carried out shook the heavens and toppled the earth. In the end, the Immortal Paragon and the God Paragon fought each other, and it nearly destroyed the Fifth Star Ring. Many starry skies were ripped out of place and turned into roaming universes that left the Fifth Star Ring.

“Years later, the Immortal Lords were given a mission to go out, find the roaming universes, and bring them back. The ultimate goal was... to make the Fifth Star Ring whole again! If the Fifth Star Ring were whole, then the natural and magical laws, as well as the destiny aura, would reach the ultimate peak.

“Over the years, most of the roaming universes have been found and brought back. But the biggest of them all has been missing the entire time. Because of that, the Fifth Star Ring has never truly been complete.

“God Emperor Death Departure’s second concession is to return that final roaming universe! If we get it, then the Fifth Star Ring will finally be whole. The natural and magical laws will be complete, and the destiny aura will flourish. It will benefit all living beings. Now, do you really think we could reject an offer like that?”

The lieutenant general looked at Xu Qing.

Xu Qing was visibly moved. And then a seemingly outrageous thought occurred to him. “Don’t tell me that... the Immortal Lord knew all along that God Emperor Death Departure had the roaming universe, and that’s why he captured Goddess Starryeyes?”

The lieutenant general’s eyes glittered with profound light, but he didn’t answer the question. Instead, he lifted his hand to reveal a silver jade stone. It radiated scintillating light, as well as a robust immortal energy. Just barely visible within the jade stone was some sort of mysterious bubble.

When Xu Qing laid eyes on the bubble, he shivered from head to toe. He felt his canon stirring, as well as his immortal embryo. It was as if... that bubble contained the boundless will of the entire Fifth Star Ring. The destiny aura he had acquired seemed to thrum in resonance with it.

“Is that...?” Xu Qing whispered.

“This is a Fifth Ring Immortal Pill! Because it’s so closely linked to destiny aura, only true monarchs can be given them. If an ordinary cultivator consumed it, they would die. But a true monarch can use it to increase their chances of successfully breaking through to Lower Immortal! The Immortal Lord will give this pill to you as a reward after you successfully escort Goddess Starryeyes to the handover!”

Xu Qing looked at the jade stone and struggled to control his breathing. He could feel the destiny aura within him resonating, and felt his immortal embryo trembling. All of that made it very obvious that this pill... would be very useful to him! The lieutenant general was still talking, and his voice seemed to be tinged with a bit of regret.

“Xu Qing, Immortal Lord Deepgloom... cares a lot about you. The army will be present during the handover, and the Immortal Lord will be closely observing. So you shouldn’t be in much danger. In fact, for all intents and purposes, the hostage exchange could be handled by anybody.

“What’s more, regardless of who does it, they’ll receive the gratitude of the five Lower Immortals who we’re getting back. Having good relationships like that will vastly improve the reputation of anyone, and will make that person the envy of the entire army. After this matter, you will have the qualifications and experience necessary to lead an entire army!”

The lieutenant general waved his hand, sending the jade stone flying over to Xu Qing. It stopped in front of him and hovered there.

Xu Qing looked at it, then took a deep breath and said, “The Immortal Lord’s orders are understood and will be followed!”

The lieutenant general nodded, and without another word, he turned and walked into the silver eye. The eye glittered, and the sea of light vanished. Everything went back to normal. Xu Qing was back inside the flame pagoda, as if nothing at all had just happened. The eye vanished.

However, the silver jade stone remained behind, glittering brightly in front of him, pulsing with ringsource and a strong immortal energy. Xu Qing just stood there for a moment analyzing the pros and cons.

This... is not something that happened in the illusion created by the god of pain.... The hostage exchange seems reasonable, but.... freewebnovel.com

He got the feeling things weren’t so simple. Whether it was the Immortal Lord’s scheme, or the deal to return the roaming universe, or everything that led up to the moment.... Everything just seemed to have gone too smoothly.

In fact, it’s going so smoothly... that it almost seems like God Lord Death Departure is taking the initiative to cooperate.

That possibility caused Xu Qing’s pupils to constrict.

Considering this is a God Lord, I could see hīm being in a passive position occasionally. But for hīm to constantly be in the passive position seems very unusual!

Xu Qing frowned. That said, someone with an Immortal Lord cultivation base would see and know things that he himself couldn’t comprehend. When he thought back to the momentum of the war, and considered what an Immortal Lord could do, he had to admit there was the possibility he was overlooking something.

So if both sides are in on this thing, what is the ultimate point?

Even after thinking about it for a while, Xu Qing couldn’t come up with a good theory. He looked at his reward items, then settled his thoughts and sent a message via divine will to Sir Star Ring and the others. Before long, the various dao seeds opened their eyes and emerged from their flame pagodas. Full of anticipation, they proceeded to Xu Qing’s flame pagoda. Upon entering, they saw the reward items.

Sir Star Ring and Zhou Zhengli were the most experienced and knowledgeable, and they looked dazed.

“This is the ringsource and the military credits delivered by the lieutenant general,” Xu Qing said.

They had already agreed how to split up the rewards. Because Xu Qing had led the search and been the one to actually capture Goddess Starryeyes, he got forty percent. Sir Star Ring had participated in the final fight, so he got ten percent. The remainder was split between the other ten ascendees! That was the arrangement for both ringsource and military credits.

After the rewards were distributed, everyone left, their hearts filled with excitement. Nobody had any misgivings about Xu Qing getting the biggest share. Having worked so closely with him for so long, they knew that it was only his battle prowess that had brought them to this point.

Xu Qing also felt that the split was fair. Without the help of the other ascendees, it would have been impossible for him to defeat the True God and capture Goddess Starryeyes.

After they were done splitting the rewards, Xu Qing told them about the hostage exchange. He also explained his suspicions and speculations. Everyone else listened with various thoughtful expressions on their faces. This was their custom. When they ran into an issue, they would confer and analyze the situation from different perspectives.

“What Xu Qing says makes a lot of sense. The hostage exchange probably won’t be very dangerous. In terms of the larger picture, my guess is that the Immortal Lord doesn’t want the war getting even worse!”

“If the war expanded, or shifted too much in our favor, the other side might get more God Lords involved. The opposite would be true. And who knows, it’s even possible the Immortal Paragon would have to step in....”

“That would be the final battle!”

“This whole thing is a game being played between an Immortal Lord and a God Lord. And it’s all about momentum....”

“Yes, but there’s something strange going on here. What exactly is Immortal Lord Deepgloom trying to accomplish?”

“Who cares what he’s planning? We should just do it. We two brothers can conquer any obstacle!”

Everyone had their say. Xu Qing listened to all the opinions and considered how they related to his own analysis. Eventually, he looked at Zhou Zhengli. During their time together, Xu Qing had come to trust Zhou Zhengli's judgement.

Zhou Zhengli frowned as he looked back at Xu Qing. After some hesitation, he kneaded the bridge of his nose. “Young Lord, and all you other Fellow Daoists, there’s one possibility none of you mentioned.... What if the hostage exchange is actually part of the ‘lantern’ that’s been lit?”

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered. “If that’s the case, then it would mean the lantern in the eastern theater isn’t shining brightly enough. If the hostage exchange is meant to brighten the lantern, then... there must still be hidden forces at work on the battlefield. And those forces... are in the Fourth Star Ring!”

Xu Qing’s words struck all of them like a tempest.

***

Time passed, and the day of the hostage exchange approached.

Xu Qing and the others had agreed to stay vigilant. Xu Qing was ready. He had taken a few days to get familiar with the new dao weapon. And he had used the ringsource from the red giant to stabilize his place within mid Quasi-Immortal. He was at his peak.

The atmosphere had changed recently. Every few days, army cultivators would cross the starry sky and set up camp around the red giant. More and more cultivators came. Things were getting increasingly tense.

Although Xu Qing and the ascendees couldn’t see what was happening on the front lines, the same thing was happening there. Both cultivators and gods were gathering into larger groups. They were consolidating their battle prowess.

The white and black in the eastern theater continued to intertwine. A storm was coming!

One day, when it was only about two hours before the hostage exchange was to occur, the bleak sound of a horn echoed outside of the red giant. It pierced through the starry sky, reaching the ears of countless cultivators.

Xu Qing opened his eyes. A sea of light glittered in front of him, whereupon a familiar figure appeared, bound tightly with fetters.

It was Goddess Starryeyes! Shē had been treated well in hēr time away from Xu Qing. Hēr ringsource had been largely replenished, and hēr skin was lustrous again. Considering what the Immortal Lord was planning, there had been no need to torment hēr. In fact... hēr perfume was stronger than ever.

Xu Qing looked at hēr. Eyes glittering, he licked his lips.

Goddess Starryeyes looked back at him, her legs trembling. In fact, shē was shaking from head to toe, as if shē were looking at... a nightmare.

In a flame pagoda by the red giant, an immortal and a god were apparently linked by predestination.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered. Starryeyes’ expression was one of despair. Shē had assumed that this human shē hated so much would actually say something to hēr. So shē wanted to say something first.

“You—”

Shē had no chance to finish what shē was going to say. Xu Qing was not a fan of wasting time, so before shē could finish, he reached toward hēr....

It was as if a gravitational force latched onto Starryeyes and dragged hēr toward Xu Qing. When shē arrived, his hand latched onto a very familiar location. Hēr throat!

The moment his hand clamped down, shē felt terror explode within hēr. Acting with instinctive speed, Xu Qing began to drain hēr ringsource. As the ringsource flowed out, shē felt that same sensation, like hēr soul was being extracted.

The ringsource flowed into Xu Qing’s hand to nourish his immortal embryo, his soul, and everything else about him. A sensation he had not experienced in some time filled him, and his mood immediately improved. It was a flavor he had sighed about many times in the past few days. Now that he could experience it again, his cultivation base rotated rapidly, and the silver light in his eyes glittered.

Pain once again struck Starryeyes, filling hēr body and soul. Shē was in a nightmare again, and the mental stability shē had worked so hard to recover was once again upturned. Venomous hatred appeared in hēr again, and this time, it was dozens of times stronger than before.

Xu Qing recognized the look in hēr eyes. He ignored it and continued to extract the ringsource. It lasted for about an hour.

At that point, Starryeyes’ skin was no longer lustrous. It was anemic again. All the ringsource shē had built back up was gone. Shē was extremely listless.

Xu Qing was satisfied. He released his hand, whereupon the limp Starryeyes sagged in front of him. Shē was weak physically, but the hatred in hēr heart was extremely intense, and shē glared murderously at him. But only a moment later, shē took a deep breath and closed hēr eyes. When shē opened them again, the venom was gone, having been replaced with bitterness.

“I met your Immortal Lord,” shē said. “You people got what you want. With the exchange at hand, I can understand why you’re not willing to give up. I can’t stop you from extracting my ringsource. After all, gods and immortals are polar opposites. When one of you immortals falls into our hands, they can’t avoid torment. I understand all that. From an objective perspective, there is no enmity between the two of us. In the final analysis, the reason you captured me is that my god magic wasn’t pure enough!”

Hēr voice was hoarse and a bit self-deprecating. During hēr recent days in captivity, shē had thought through many things.

This was the first time Xu Qing had ever seen Starryeyes behave like this. He looked at the goddess. Shē looked back at him calmly.

“Before, you couldn’t hide your hatred,” he said suddenly. “That was because you were in despair and thought you were going to die. Now you’re masking it because you have hope. You don’t want to take any risks. But you’re also worried you might anger me, and that I’ll kill you, transforming your hope back into despair.”

Starryeye’s pupils constricted.

“The exchange is upon us,” he said calmly. “You and I both know that I can’t kill you. In other words, you can stop trying so hard to seem weak. I can tell how much you hate me. And there’s no need for you to explain what you plan to do after you get back. You’re not going to forget this or let it go. That said, I’m glad you reminded me of something....”

Eyes narrowing, Xu Qing extended his right hand, and the power of extreme metal glittered, turning into golden threads. Next, the power of wood bolstered it. After that came water, fire, and earth. The five extremes turned into a cage! Time made the seal, and space was the justification, making the cage even more profound. And finally... Xu Qing’s space-time descended. It made the lock for the cage!

Rumbling sounds surrounded Starryeyes as shē was imprisoned in the illusory cage.

Yet Xu Qing didn’t think that was enough. He extended his hand, and the weight of heaven’s principle caused the cage to materialize.

Then Starryeyes’ expression flickered as Xu Qing performed a double-handed incantation gesture and then touched his forehead. His immortal embryo unleashed majestic immortal energy as it exhaled the Aurora Immortal Palace.

The cage overlapped! Rumbling sounds echoed out, and Starryeyes’ face fell. And yet, things weren’t over yet.

After the cage was made with the eight extremes, Xu Qing’s ninth extreme appeared, the canon of parallelism. As the overlaps appeared, the power of numerous space-times became chains that could restrain gods. They shot out of nowhere toward Starryeyes.

A shrill scream echoed out as dozens of chains flowed from different space-times to pierce into the goddess’ scapulas! Starryeyes wanted to struggle, but hēr every attempt just caused the chains to glitter with immortal inscriptions. A profoundly irritating sensation swept through hēr like a storm, wiping away the veneer of weakness. Boundless, unending hatred suddenly erupted again within hēr.

“I’m going to kill you, Xu Qing! And not just you. All your loved ones! All your relatives! All your friends! They’ll all die miserably because of you!!”

Xu Qing looked at the goddess expressionlessly, all while assessing hēr ringsource. He soon realized that, thanks to the stimulation of the cage and chains, more ringsource had appeared within hēr. Nodding in satisfaction, he reached out to extract it.

Now Starryeyes realized that he had been doing it all on purpose to provoke hēr into producing more ringsource. All of a sudden, shē thought back to the terrifying memories of hēr original journey with him.

“You’re a nightmare!” shē screamed shrilly. “You’re not an immortal! You’re a devil!!”

When shē finally took a breath, Xu Qing spoke. “I’m very curious,” he said calmly, “about why you continuously produce ringsource after being drained.”

He sliced his fingernail across hēr pale forehead and, eyes glittering, sent some divine will into hēr. It passed through the blood, flesh, and bones, all the way into the godhood in hēr god soul.... He had tried something similar in the past, but had failed due to his low cultivation base.

Now his cultivation base had reached a higher level. What was more, Xu Qing was convinced that the Immortal Lord must have left traces behind of his own search for information. He wanted to see if he could find such clues, and learn more about Starryeyes’ secrets. This time... things were working a lot more smoothly. And so, it didn’t take long after he sent his divine will into hēr god soul, he found the clues.

Xu Qing’s previous probing was too weak to do anything. But now he saw the damage that had been done by the Immortal Lord! As a result, Xu Qing’s divine will was able to enter easily.

As he went deeper, he sensed that there was something ahead that wasn’t illusory. It was material. It was something... crystalized! It looked like it was something made of destiny aura, but at the same time, wasn’t. There was something mysterious swirling in it. At the same time, it was covered with cracks....

It looked like it was on the verge of collapsing. But at the same time, it gave Xu Qing the sensation he was looking at the entire Fourth Star Ring. Terrifying pressure radiated out of it.

Xu Qing was initially stunned, but after a bit of hesitation, he decisively sent his divine will inside! The crystal suddenly started rumbling, and a majestic, indescribable force swept outward, eradicating everything in its path.

Xu Qing’s divine will collapsed, and his fingers were shoved away from her neck. At the same time, the provocation caused new power to surge within Starryeyes, who looked up at him, hēr pupils transformed into a vortex of stars.

“You actually tried to take the godly authority my father gave to me!” shē roared in a voice like thunder. It wasn’t actually hēr original voice, but rather, a chaotic combination of countless voices that became a godly voice.

Suddenly, nine bolts of golden lightning appeared around hēr, which shot toward Xu Qing. However, just as they touched him, they were shattered by some ancient will coming from the goddess. Starryeyes sagged listlessly, all while gasping for breath.

Xu Qing instantly identified the mysterious will. It contained boundless immortal energy that surpassed that of a Lower Immortal.

It’s a sealing mark left inside of hēr by the Immortal Lord!

Xu Qing looked thoughtfully at the tip of his index finger. There was a black spot there that was fading away. Looking at it closely, it was clear that the spot was made up of countless intricate golden designs. Looking at it seemed like looking at the destruction and rebirth of countless planets.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered. This is the secret of hēr never-ending ringsource.

***

In the outside world, the hostage exchange was about to happen, and the lieutenant general was speaking into the minds of all cultivators.

“The time has come! Men, move out!”

A rumbling sound emerged from the red giant that could shake starry skies! It... was about to leave! And the entire massive army camped in the area was going with it.

The sight of it was astonishing. The starry sky trembled, universes shook, and star regions distorted. A massive teleportation the size of an entire star region... was beginning.

The incredibly important hostage exchange was taking place in the eastern theater between the Fourth and Fifth Star Rings, in a place filled with innumerable asteroids. There was also dust that formed stellar storms which covered everything.

There was black and white roiling in all parts. Within the black part, there were unending gods, all of them pulsing with so much black mutagen that it was corporeal. There were so many gods that the starry sky almost couldn’t take it, and rifts were starting to break open.

Within the white color were numerous cultivator armies, all of them brimming with somber auras and immortal energy. Each and every cultivator in the massive group was an accomplished killer.

There weren’t just troops gathered from the front lines of the eastern theater. All of the armies were there, united. That included Immortal Monarch Silent Dao and the newly returned Spirit Jade.... Everyone was there!

Above the armies was the chaotic mixture of black and white, wherein thunder boomed. Up there, it was just possible to see two blurry figures who emanated pressure onto everyone else. As the two sides faced off, the starry sky on the cultivator side rippled as... the red giant and the armies that had camped around it appeared!

Its arrival attracted the attention of all the immortals and gods!

Inside the giant red star, Xu Qing sat cross-legged in his fire pagoda.

“Xu Qing, bring out the captive goddess!”

Upon hearing that, Xu Qing calmly stood. Grabbing the chains of canon, he dragged the cage... out of the fire pagoda.

The moment Xu Qing emerged from the flame pagoda, the black mutagen of the host of gods fluctuated so violently the starry sky shook. All eyes were fixed on him there by the red giant, including those of both gods and immortals. And then, all gazes shifted from Xu Qing to the cage he was dragging behind him.

Gazes could have weight, especially those of the gods. It was weight that could crush down on the body and suppress the soul. In an instant, Xu Qing felt like his soul was about to be shredded. The gazes of the immortals opposed that. So as the pressure from the gods built, the immortals looked over and dispelled the pressure.

Xu Qing proceeded, surrounded by loud rumbling sounds as the void rippled, shook, became clear, and then collapsed, over and over again. His face was completely expressionless as he continued to drag the cage forward. Soon he was beyond the borders of the red star, where he stopped and looked around coldly.

This spot was in between the Fourth and Fifth Star Rings, and had once been a battlefield. Because of the blue stellar clouds in the area, it was known as... the Blue Wastes!

Black and white filled the sky, while blue clouds swirled everywhere. The shattered remains of the planets that stretched out endlessly looked like the hulking spines of huge beasts. The surfaces of shattered planets had strange markings crawling across them that looked like bulging veins. The faceoff between the gods and immortals made the markings pulse, which in turn caused the shattered planets to glitter with rippling blood-red light.

Beauty and majesty coexisted! That was the backdrop for the scene!

Framed against that backdrop was an army of cultivators organized in ranks that seemed to conform to the overall structure of the entire Fifth Star Ring. It was so majestic and massive that the army seemed to never end. Seen from afar, it looked like dots organized neatly on a chart, but closer examination would reveal that each dot was made of 10,000 troops!

In the middle of it all was an enormous war drum covered with designs of gobblewocks and heaveneaters. When Xu Qing stopped moving forward, the drum echoed out with a thunderous roar.

On the other side of the same backdrop was the army of gods with their mutagen. They had numerous planets, shrunken down and covered with flesh, that spat out endless mutagen. Atop each of those planets were hosts of gods. Their forces also seemed to go on without end.

Behind that were enormous conglomerations of mutated flesh and blood that looked like bows made of space rock, with strings made of starry rivers. They were taut... and thrummed with a sound that made the atmosphere very tense.

What was more, there were golden shooting stars that flew back and forth on the side of the gods, following mysterious orbital paths that formed a defensive barrier. Whenever the sound of the cultivators’ drums threatened to invade the territory of the gods, black holes would appear on that barrier, and would swallow up the sound and the light that tried to pass them.

It was a dramatic and majestic sight. What was even shocking to the immortals and gods was the vast area overhead. That... was where a scroll painting and a godly river were at odds.

On the side of the scroll painting was the majestic figure of Immortal Lord Deepgloom, who commanded everything around him. Stretching out behind him was the scroll painting that covered half of a star region, its gilded designs featuring magical laws of heaven and earth.

Opposite of him in the black river of the gods was God Lord Death Departure, seated in a throne forged from the shattered remnants of countless universes. As the sharp tips of his fingernails pointed down, the water of the river froze.

Few people could see the two of them clearly. But the pressure they exuded was clearly sensed by all living beings. They were both looking at the same spot! It was the location in the very middle of this ancient battlefield, where the exchange was to take place.

There, the clouds swirled to reveal an enormous, majestic altar!

The altar was made from 360 coffins and 360 huge trees. The coffins were made from devil copper, and were covered with peeling rust, beneath which were symbols scrawled in blood. Whenever the stellar wind blew, the coffins would leak black mist that caused terrifying gruish figures to appear.

The trees were made from immortal crystal. Silver immortal symbols flowed across their surfaces, all of which pulsed with an incomparable and boundless power of life force. Whenever black mist would pulse out of the coffins, the immortal trees would produce the spirits of heroic immortals to wage war against it.

This jointly built altar was the spot where the hostage exchange would take place!

Even after all of the wars Xu Qing had participated in, this scene was still shocking, and he had to stop and take it in for a moment before continuing on his way. He left the red giant and entered the starry sky. The cage he dragged behind him left a dark red streak in the starry sky as he approached the altar.

On the side of the gods, the golden barrier shimmered, and as countless cultivators looked on, a god emerged. The god actually resembled a middle-aged human, except with a vastly larger fleshly body, being around 20-25 meters tall.

Hīs facial features were beautiful, and hē had long violet hair that swayed around hīm. Hē wore a golden suit of armor that perfectly accentuated hīs perfect physique. In terms of level... that had been determined by the nature of the exchange.

Hē was a peak Altar God. Hē came out with five emaciated old men with dull facial expressions, who were bound like captive dogs. All five of the old men were crisscrossed with cuts and bruises. They were wan and sallow, their life force faded and dull. Obviously, they had suffered torment in their years of captivity. These were the human cultivators who had performed meritorious deeds in the service of the Fifth Star Ring.

When the cultivators saw them, their emotions swelled, and the sound of the war drum became louder.

The pretty god sensed that, and with cold, apathetic eyes, hē jerked the rope binding the necks of the five captive cultivators. The five old men trembled, the pain obviously severe as the rope seemed about to break their necks. Hē looked at Xu Qing.

The atmosphere instantly grew even more tense.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered with coldness. Though he didn’t know these five Lower Immortals, based on what the lieutenant general had told him, he knew that they had performed great services. What was more, he could tell that this pretty god was trying to provoke him.

Lifting his hand, he opened the cage of canon, then transformed it into a chain that bound Starryeyes’ arms and legs. Next, he dragged hēr out into the open and clasped his hand down onto hēr neck. As all the gods and even the god emperor watched, he started extracting ringsource!

Starryeyes shivered, and was instantly dragged out of unconsciousness by the pain.

The gods erupted into anger. Killing intent surged. To the gods, seeing Xu Qing extract ringsource from their goddess, right in front of them, was an unspeakable insult!

The pretty god looked at Xu Qing, then expressionlessly loosened the rope binding the five humans. Xu Qing also relaxed his hand and stopped the extraction process. Pulling on the chain, he placed Starryeyes in front of him.

Both sides proceeded toward the altar.

Every step Xu Qing took caused brilliant lotuses of light to spread out beneath his feet. His cultivation base stirred to its absolute peak.

As Starryeyes proceeded, the void around hēr contracted. God blood dripped out, but didn’t dissipate. Instead, it floated behind her like a path of bloody planets born in the void. Shē grew weaker with each step shē took, until walking forward became difficult. The chains around hēr feet tightened more and more, causing pain to stab through hēr. The clank of the chains were like cold winds blowing through the Nine Serenities, and made hēr think back to the pain shē had experienced. Perhaps because of all that animosity, hēr hair began to crumble and fall down like stardust.

Behind hēr, Xu Qing looked calm, but the truth was that his guard was up, and he was ready for something unexpected to happen. He actually felt uneasy.

Although he could sense the protection offered by countless gazes, as well as the pounding of the drum, after his discussion with his squadron, he felt that there had to be another reason why he had been selected for this assignment. And there was one distinct possibility that he kept thinking about....

If Starryeyes was aware this exchange was going to happen, then considering how much shē hates me... wouldn’t shē make additional demands?

He looked at the staggering goddess in front of him, and his eyes narrowed.

The moments ticked by as Xu Qing prodded Starryeyes forward. Soon, both he and the pretty god entered the asteroid belt on the way to the altar. Eventually... they were in the middle of the asteroid belt, only about 30,000 meters away from the altar.

Starryeyes suddenly spun in place. Because of the mutagen in the area, hēr eyes had regained some of the golden fire that had been extinguished before. “Every bit of ringsource you take from me will be a star that pierces your life force and turns into the biggest curse you can imagine, something that you’ll regret for the rest of your life!”

Xu Qing didn’t reply. He jerked the chain, causing immortal symbols to appear on it and release the power to extract ringsource. Starryeyes grunted as ringsource flowed out of hēr wounds. Shē staggered over a small asteroid. The black surface of the asteroid wriggled, causing the rust-colored stains covering hēr robes to grow more prominent.

Xu Qing’s daoist robe swirled despite there being no wind, as a vortex of stellar clouds began to spin around him counter-clockwise.

The ringsource coming out of Starryeye’s wounds flowed into the vortex, becoming specks of brightness like moonlight.

Then Xu Qing quietly said, “Keep your mouth shut.”

Starryeyes glared at Xu Qing, then gritted hēr teeth and tried to hurry onward. Xu Qing tugged back on the chains.

In that manner, Xu Qing controlled how quickly they covered the 3,000-meter distance to the altar. Upon arriving, he was able to get a closer look at the pretty god and the five cultivators.

He suddenly felt even more uneasy than before. Eyes flashing, he reached out and grabbed Starryeyes. Ignoring hēr struggles, he once again clamped his hand onto hēr throat.

Then he viciously extracted hēr ringsource. This time, he exerted far more force than before. After draining hēr, he eased up. But this time, the ringsource didn’t start coming back. It stopped. It was as if shē was about to become a corpse, so there was no need to continue.

The process was more painful to Starryeyes than anything from before, to the point where hēr mind was on the verge of breaking.

The gods seethed. Countless roars echoed out, and immense pressure weighed down. The pretty god’s face hardened, and hē rushed forward. The cultivators also stirred due to Xu Qing’s sudden action. It looked like something big was about to happen between the two sides.

Meanwhile, Starryeyes was struggling violently. Perhaps because of the mutagen, or perhaps because of secret assistance from somewhere, shē suddenly unleashed a terrifying power, as well as a scream that caused Xu Qing’s hand to shake.

All of a sudden, the chains binding hēr shattered. Shē was free! The weakened goddess had no time to think rationally. Shē just raced away, becoming a stream of light that disappeared behind the pretty god. Shē was returning to the camp of the gods!

Xu Qing scowled at hēr retreating figure and suddenly said, “You can run, but we’ll meet again!”

Starryeyes looked over hēr shoulder on the way back to the gods. Glaring at Xu Qing with the golden color of god blood in hēr eyes, shē forced herself to simply grind hēr teeth.

“You’re right, we’ll meet again soon! I’ve hated you this entire time, Xu Qing. Did you really think you were in control? What a joke! Don’t you realize that you are the point of this exchange? You’re the point of the treaty between my father and your Immortal Lord. And it was my idea!”

Because of the current situation, Xu Qing was able to tell how much of what shē was saying was true. All of the emotion on his face suddenly vanished.

“So that’s how it is.” Xu Qing waved his hand, and everything Starryeyes could see vanished like a popping bubble.

Shē was back at his side, with his hand clamped around hēr throat, still 3,000 meters away from the altar! Hēr jaw dropped as waves of fury battered hēr heart. Pupils constricting, shē incredulously said, “A True God’s illusory region? How could you have a True God’s illusory region??”

Xu Qing didn’t answer. Quickly sealing Starryeyes, he turned and sped in the opposite direction.

In the depths of the voice, an exclamation of surprise echoed out, and then the god river which had been frozen by God Emperor Death Departure’s fingernail suddenly turned into a host of icy chunks that flew up into the starry sky. Someone who could surpass space-time would see those chunks of ice turn into the eyes of a god, looking down on everything.

“Your side violated the treaty, Deepgloom.”

The voice surpassed any heavenly sound, any type of dao will, and exceeded all natural and magical laws. It was like the chanting of infinite gods, with mightiness that shattered starry skies, enveloped all living beings, eradicated all manner of things, and even shattered universes. Endless black flesh and blood emerged from the shattered fragments, then proliferated like mad, turning the entire world into something gruish.

The person who spoke was none other than... God Emperor Death Departure! Hē sat on an imperial throne made of countless universes, and hīs eyes were currently open, with hīs divine will filling every block of shattered ice so that it seemed like many heavens were looking down.

All cultivators shivered in their hearts and minds, and the flames of their life force flickered as if they might go out. The actual immortals were not spared!

The countless chunks of rubble that filled the ancient battlefield began vibrating. Countless eyes from corpses that had been there for endless years floated up, transformed by the will of the God Lord into a huge river. All of a sudden, the lids of the 360 coffins in the central altar opened. Black energy poured out of them, creating space-time ripples that could rip apart the souls of gods.

All of that happened because of one thing said by a God Lord!

Xu Qing was hit particularly hard since he was right at the edge of the altar. His mind went blank, and he suddenly lost all ability to sense anything. It was as if... he had become a piece of dust. Compared to a God Lord, right now... he really was like nothing more than dust.

As dramatic things seemed about to unfold, a cold voice suddenly spread out from the scroll painting that opposed the God Lord.

“So what if the treaty was violated?”

That voice caused more dramatic things to happen in the starry sky. The shattered ice, the crystals that had formed, the godly might and mutagen, and even the infinite and gruish proliferations of flesh, all went still. They became a boundless black mist that shot toward the painting, converging on the index finger of the Immortal Lord who sat cross-legged within it.

It vanished. A mere afterglow remained on the fingertip, which turned into a ring of black ice.

The Immortal Lord flicked his finger. The black ice melted, becoming a white flame that danced about, leaving faint burn marks like stardust.

Just like that, the battlefield changed again. The coffins’ lids shut, and the space-time ripples were erased. The crystal river tumbled back and became a sea of flames that spread out, filled with immortal energy. The cultivators’ minds cleared, and they unhesitatingly beat their war drums. The sound of it filled the starry sky.

Xu Qing regained his senses, and didn’t hesitate for a moment to flee. He wouldn’t be so quick to believe the Fifth Star Ring had sold him out. For one thing, he didn’t believe that he was important enough to be sold out. After everything that had happened, it still seemed to him like there was some other secret at play during this exchange. It seemed more likely that his presence had simply been to ensure that the exchange started off smoothly....

Even as that thought coalesced in his mind, the godly river in the starry sky seethed. Within it, God Lord Death Departure slowly rose, reaching such a great height it seemed like the starry sky couldn’t accommodate hīm.

A mountain-toppling, sea-draining godly might filled hīs voice as hē said, “You violated the treaty for the sake of a Quasi-Immortal?”

The person to answer hīm wasn’t Immortal Lord Deepgloom. Rather, it was Immortal Monarch Silent Dao, who strode out of the crowd of cultivators.

Standing in front of the army, he looked at the godly river and said, “God Emperor Death Departure, given your level, there’s no need to continue with the facade. This isn’t about a Quasi-Immortal. You just added a stipulation to the agreement because you wanted my Master to believe your story. Since my Master is here, you’ve achieved your goal.

“What you really want to do is pin down my Master here so that you can fully open the rift that you’ve been secretly preparing in the western theater. You see... my Master long since realized what was happening over there, and has made arrangements. Given your godly omniscience, you surely know about all that.”

In response to these words, the God Lord said nothing and didn’t even react.

“On the other hand, we have a different goal. We wanted you over here, God Lord, so that we would have a chance... to send you back to where you came from! After we kill you, the war will reach a new level.... Thus, in some ways, you’re correct. However, after we kill you, there will be balance between the two sides. So who cares if the fighting kicks back in full force?

“That’s why my Master agreed to your concessions. It was because, at that time, he wasn’t completely sure he could deal with your godhood. But now he knows he can control it, and therefore, this entire exchange was set up... to kill you!”

As his words echoed out, the cultivators’ war drums pounded even more loudly, stirring the spirits of all the warriors. The gods, meanwhile, sank into silence.

In the godly river, the God Lord stared at Immortal Lord Deepgloom in the scroll painting. “Deepgloom, it seems you really do know the secrets of my godhood. That’s why you had your apprentice explain all that, instead of doing so yourself. Unfortunately, you came to this realization too late. You cultivators believe yourselves to be infallible. You make all sorts of plans and schemes, but did you really think I wouldn’t find out about them?”

The godly river seethed as the god emperor’s godly might spread out in all directions. “I knew all about your secret ‘lantern’ in the eastern theater. I also know how you assassinated my officer here. I saw right through your plan to kidnap my daughter. And, of course, I was aware of how you covet my godhood!”

As hē spoke those words, hē strode out of the godly river and toward the scroll painting. Every step hē took caused the starry sky to crack, filled the battlefield with rumbling sounds, and shook universes.

“That’s why I just went along with what you wanted. I pretended to not know. I let you bring my daughter here, using hēr to make sure I could get to you. You were plotting against me, Deepgloom, but I was also plotting against you! You thought you could use my daughter to probe my godly authority. But the reality is that I was using hēr to probe your canon.

“That is why I offered the roaming universe as a concession. I knew you couldn’t refuse that. All I had to do was see hēr and speak a word to hēr. In that manner, I could confirm everything about hēr, and that includes all of the results of my plot. Now, you know about my godhood, and I know about your canon. Deepgloom... how do you think you can beat me now?”

As the god emperor’s voice shook universes, he unleashed the canon of cultivators, causing an ever-changing mask to appear between his fingers. The mask shifted back and forth between faces that were men and women, old people and youngsters. It displayed different ages and cultivation bases, but all of them were smiling with joy.

The God Lord looked at the mask and sighed in admiration. “Immortal canon really is extraordinary. To imitate godhood... and then use that to carve a new path, a second route to ringsource! As for you, Deepgloom, your canon... is unexpected. It’s not about slaughter, but about hope. You gather the hope of all living things to defend, to cherish, and to remember. You turn all that into a safeguard, by means of war and killing!”

Though there was admiration in the God Lord’s eyes, an instant later, hē smiled and flicked hīs finger. Black energy proliferated, filling the mask and causing the joy on all the living beings' faces to change. Instead of smiling, they were wailing in despair! The sound of howling rose up.

Astonishingly, hē was infecting Immortal Lord Deepgloom’s canon! Boundless blackness erupted from beneath hīs feet, rumbling out to fill the area with mutagen. The entire battlefield was infected.

Then God Emperor Death Departure took another step forward and entered Immortal Lord Deepgloom’s scroll painting.

“Now we’ll see if you kill me or if I cut you down!”

White and black inverted. The scroll painting blurred. A battle started raging that could not be perceived.

Fighting instantly broke out between the two armies! The array of dots that were the cultivators became like a wave of fire. Countless magical treasures were unleashed, resulting in a dazzling, multicolored display. reewebnovel.com

The red giant stirred into motion, transforming into a burning ball of true fire and instantly covered any nearby gods and mutagen.

Battle flags flapped and war drums shook the soul! The sound could shatter planets as dust swept out and turned everything into a gauzy blur.

On the gods’ side, bowstrings twanged as countless streams of destructive and infectious godlight headed toward the cultivators like shooting stars. Their defensive barrier rippled, releasing ravenous vortexes. Countless roving stars on the side of the Fifth Star Ring were thrown off of their orbital tracks. An infinitude of gods rushed forth.

In an instant, the battlefield turned into a grindstone of flesh and blood that sent blood spurting everywhere. Extra bits of might would occasionally shoot out from the scroll painting. Those from the Immortal Lord were like ink stains. Every single one turned into a massive stream of sword will that headed toward the gods. Whatever gods it encountered would simply explode. But the gory chunks would then be frozen by the God Lord’s godly might, then turned into millions upon millions of immortal-slaying spears that would shoot into the army of cultivators.

Blood flew everywhere. Black and white no longer intersected, but rather, were physical things that clashed violently. Space-time fractured, rifts spread out, and universes were born and destroyed.

It was the same on the central altar, where the devil copper and the immortal trees were separating from each other! One coffin of devil copper after another collapsed, becoming black mist that would turn into the faces of huge gods that devoured everything in the area. As for the huge immortal trees, when they shattered, they would turn into karma threads that swept across the battlefield and destroyed any god they touched.

The battlefield instantly devolved into chaos! Space was shaken, time was influenced, and space-time seemed like it might shatter.

As that moment of crisis built, Xu Qing fled at top speed! He was doing everything in his power to make his way off into the distance.

But then, the pretty god behind him who had been the one supposedly handling the hostage transfer, looked at him with golden light in hīs eyes, and inhaled deeply.... The five human cultivators around hīm suddenly shivered, and then the color drained out of them as their true features were revealed. They were five corpses that had been turned into gods!

They had long since died. As of now, they were simply god puppets! But when the pretty god inhaled, they collapsed into dust, and all of the ringsource in them was sucked right into the pretty god.

As a result, the pretty god’s cultivation level rose into the level of True God! Then hē shot right toward Xu Qing! Hē was to rescue Starryeyes and also kill Xu Qing! Earlier, hē had been very close to accomplishing that. But just before hē did, Xu Qing realized what was going on and fled. Then the fighting broke out, and hē realized hē was in danger of failing to accomplish hīs mission. Now was the time for hīm to turn things around!
